uvāca mahātmanā brahmaṇā kalpitam pūrvam purāṇam laiṅgam uttamam grantha koṭi pramāṇam tu catur lakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte vyāsaiḥ sarva antareṣu vai ca eva brahma ādau dvāpara ādiṣu liṅgam ekādaśam proktam mayā vyāsāt śrutam ca tat asya ekādaśa sāhasre grantha mānam iha dvijāḥ tasmāt saṃkṣepāt vakṣye na śrutam vistareṇa yat catur lakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte kṛṣṇadvaipāyanena tu atra ekādaśa sāhasraiḥ kathitaḥ liṅga saṃbhavaḥ sargaḥ prādhānikaḥ paścāt prākṛtaḥ vaikṛtāni ca aṇḍasya asya ca saṃbhūti raṇḍasya āvaraṇa aṣṭakam aṇḍa udbhava tvam śarvasya rajaḥ guṇa samāśrayāt viṣṇu tvam kāla rudra tvam śayanam ca apsu tasya ca prajāpatīnām sargaḥ ca pṛthivī uddharaṇam tathā brahmaṇaḥ ca divārātram āyuṣaḥ gaṇanam punar divyam ca mānuṣam varṣam ārṣam vai dhrauvyam eva ca pitryam pitṛāṇām saṃbhūti dharmaḥ ca āśramiṇām tathā mahā ākhyā aṣṭakam hi rudrasya kathitam rodana antare brahma viṣṇu vivādaḥ ca punar liṅgasya saṃbhavaḥ śilādasya tapaḥ ca eva vṛtrāreḥ darśanam tathā śilāda śakra saṃvādaḥ padmayoni tvam eva ca bhavasya darśanam ca eva tiṣyeṣu ācārya śiṣyayoḥ vyāsa avatārāḥ ca tathā kalpa manvantarāṇi ca kalpa tvam ca eva kalpānām ākhyā bhedeṣu anukramāt kalpeṣu kalpe vārāhe vārāha tvam hareḥ tathā punar liṅga udbhavaḥ ca eva ṛṣi madhye pinākinaḥ liṅgasya ārādhanam snāna vidhānam śauca lakṣaṇam vārāṇasyāḥ ca mahātmyam kṣetra māhātmya varṇanam bhuvi rudra ālayānām tu saṃkhyā viṣṇoḥ gṛhasya ca antarikṣe tathā aṇḍe asmin deva āyatana varṇanam dakṣasya patanam bhūmau punar svārociṣe antare dakṣa śāpaḥ ca dakṣasya śāpa mokṣaḥ tathā eva ca kailāsa varṇanam ca eva yogaḥ pāśupataḥ tathā saṃdhyāṃśaka pramāṇam ca saṃdhyā vṛttam bhavasya ca udvāhaḥ śaṃkarasya atha putra utpādanam eva ca maithuna atiprasaṅgeṇa vināśaḥ jagatām bhayam śāpaḥ satyā kṛtaḥ devān purā viṣṇum ca pālitam grahaṇa ādiṣu kāleṣu snāpya liṅgam phalam tathā pativratāyāḥ ca ākhyānam paśu pāśa vicāraṇā pravṛtti lakṣaṇam jñānam nivṛtti adhikṛtā tathā vasiṣṭha tanaya utpattiḥ vāsiṣṭhānām mahātmanām munīnām vaṃśa vistāraḥ rājñām śakteḥ vināśanam suta śokaḥ vasiṣṭhasya arundhatyāḥ pralāpanam snuṣāyāḥ preṣaṇam ca eva garbha sthasya vacaḥ tathā parāśarasya avatāraḥ vyāsasya ca śukasya ca ca kṛtaḥ vai śakti sūnunā devatā parama artham tu vijñānam ca prasādataḥ purāṇa karaṇam ca eva pulastyasya ājñayā guroḥ bhuvanānām pramāṇam ca grahāṇām jyotiṣām gatiḥ jīvat śrāddha vidhānam ca śrāddha arhāḥ śrāddham eva ca nāndī śrāddha vidhānam ca tathā adhyayana lakṣaṇam pañcayajña prabhāvaḥ ca pañcayajña vidhiḥ tathā rajasvalānām vṛttiḥ ca vṛttyā putra viśiṣṭa tā bhojya abhojya vidhānam ca sarveṣām eva varṇinām narakāṇām svarūpam ca daṇḍaḥ karma anurūpataḥ svargi nārakiṇām puṃsām cihnam janma antareṣu ca nānāvidhāni dānāni pretarāja puram tathā pañcākṣarasya atha rudra māhātmyam eva ca śvetasya mṛtyoḥ saṃvādaḥ śveta arthe kāla nāśanam devadāru vane śaṃbhoḥ praveśaḥ śaṃkarasya tu sudarśanasya ca ākhyānam krama saṃnyāsa lakṣaṇam śraddhā sāddhyā atha rudraḥ tu kathitam brahmaṇā tadā brahmaṇaḥ paramam jñānam ādātum mīna tā hareḥ sarva avasthāsu viṣṇoḥ ca jananam līlayā eva tu rudra prasādāt viṣṇoḥ ca jiṣṇoḥ ca eva tu saṃbhavaḥ manthāna dhāraṇa arthāya hareḥ kūrma tvam eva ca saṃkarṣaṇasya ca utpattiḥ kauśikyāḥ ca punarbhavaḥ yadūnām ca eva saṃbhūtiḥ yādava tvam hareḥ svayam bāla bhāve hareḥ krīḍā putra artham saṃkara arcanam nārasya ca tathā utpattiḥ kapāle vaiṣṇavāt harāt bhū bhāra nigraha arthe tu rudrasya ārādhanam hareḥ devāsure purā labdhaḥ bhṛgu śāpaḥ ca viṣṇunā kṛṣṇa tve dvārakāyāḥ tu nilayaḥ mādhavasya tu labdhaḥ hitāya śāpaḥ tu durvāsasya ānanāt hareḥ vṛṣṇi andhaka vināśāya śāpaḥ piṇḍāra vāsinām anyonyam vivāde vṛṣṇi vigrahaḥ līlayā ca eva kṛṣṇena sva kulasya ca saṃhṛtiḥ purā andhaka agni dakṣāṇām śakra ibha mṛga rūpiṇām madanasya ādidevasya brahmaṇaḥ ca amara arīṇām halāhalasya daityasya kṛtā avajñā pinākinā viṣṇoḥ vara āyudha avāptiḥ tathā rudrasya ceṣṭitam hareḥ pitāmahasya atha śakrasya ca mahātmanaḥ bhūmau rudrasya lokam ca pātāle hāṭakeśvaram tapasām lakṣaṇam ca eva dvijānām vaibhavam tathā sarva mūrtīnām liṅga mūrteḥ viśeṣataḥ liṅge asmin ānupūrvyeṇa vistareṇa anukīrtyate etat jñātvā purāṇasya saṃkṣepam kīrtayet tu yaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge anukramaṇikāvarṇanam nāma dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca aliṅgaḥ liṅga mūlam tu avyaktam liṅgam ucyate aliṅgaḥ śivaḥ iti uktaḥ liṅgam śaivam iti smṛtam aguṇam dhruvam akṣayyam aliṅgam śiva lakṣaṇam gandha varṇa rasaiḥ yuktam śabda sparśa ādi lakṣaṇam jagat yonim mahābhūtam sthūlam sūkṣmam dvijottamāḥ vigrahaḥ jagatām liṅgam āliṅgāt abhavat svayam saptadhā ca aṣṭadhā ca eva tathā ekādaśadhā punar liṅgāni aliṅgasya tathā māyayā vitatāni tu tebhyaḥ pradhānadevānām trayam āsīt śiva ātmakam ekena eva hṛtam viśvam vyāptam tu evam śivena tu aliṅgam ca eva liṅgam ca liṅga aliṅgāni mūrtayaḥ aliṅgī bhagavant bījī saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ bījam yoniḥ ca nirbījam nirbījaḥ bījam ucyate bīja yoni pradhānānām ātma ākhyā vartate tu iha viśuddhaḥ iyam tathā rudraḥ purāṇe śivaḥ ucyate śivena dṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ śaivī samabhavat dvijāḥ sarga ādau sā guṇaiḥ yuktā purā vyaktā svabhāvāt avyakta ādi viśeṣa antam viśvam tasyāḥ samucchritam viśva dhātrī tu ajā ākhyā ca śaivī sā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā tām ajām lohitām śuklām kṛṣṇām ekā bahu prajām janitrīm anuśete sma juṣamāṇaḥ svarūpiṇīm tām eva ajām ajaḥ anyaḥ tu bhukta bhogām jahāti ca ajā janitrī jagatām sā ajena samadhiṣṭhitā prādurbabhūva sa mahān puruṣa adhiṣṭhitasya ca ajā ājñayā pradhānasya sarga kāle guṇaiḥ tribhiḥ sisṛkṣayā codyamānaḥ praviśya avyaktam avyayam vyakta sṛṣṭim vikurute ca ātma na adhiṣṭhitaḥ mahant mahataḥ tu tathā vṛttiḥ tena eva ca āvṛtaḥ samyak ahaṅkāraḥ tamaḥ adhikaḥ ahaṅkārāt śabda mātram tasmāt ākāśam avyayam sa śabdam āvṛṇot paścāt ākāśam śabda kāraṇam tanmātrāt bhūta sargaḥ ca dvijāḥ tu evam prakīrtitaḥ sparśa mātram tathā ākāśāt tasmāt vāyuḥ mahān mune tasmāt ca rūpa mātram tu tatas agniḥ ca rasaḥ tatas rasāt apaḥ śubhāḥ tābhyaḥ gandha mātram dharā tatas āvṛṇot hi tathā ākāśam sparśa mātram dvijottamāḥ āvṛṇot rūpa mātram tu vāyuḥ vāti kriyā ātmakaḥ āvṛṇot rasa mātram vai devaḥ sākṣāt vibhāvasuḥ āvṛṇvānāḥ gandha mātram apaḥ sarva rasa ātmakāḥ sā pañca guṇā tasmāt eka ūnāḥ rasa saṃbhavāḥ triguṇaḥ bhagavān vahniḥ dviguṇaḥ sparśa saṃbhavaḥ pañca buddhīndriyāṇi asya pañca karmedriyāṇi tu śabda ādīnām avāpti artham manaḥ ca eva ubhaya ātmakam mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ hi aṇḍam utpādayanti ca jala budbuda vat tasmāt avatīrṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ aṇḍam daśaguṇena eva vāriṇā prāvṛtam bahis apaḥ daśaguṇena eva tad brāhye tejasā vṛtāḥ tejaḥ daśaguṇena eva bāhyatas vāyunā vṛtam vāyuḥ daśaguṇena eva bāhyatas nabhasā vṛtaḥ ākāśena āvṛtaḥ vāyuḥ ahaṅkāreṇa śabda jaḥ mahantā a śabda hetuḥ vai pradhānena āvṛtaḥ svayam sapta aṇḍa āvaraṇāni āhuḥ tasya ātmā kamalāsanaḥ koṭi koṭi yutāni atra ca aṇḍāni kathitāni tu sṛṣṭāḥ pradhānena tadā labdhvā śaṃbhoḥ tu saṃnidhim mādikartā ca bhūtānām saṃhartā paripālakaḥ tasmāt maheśvaraḥ devaḥ brahmanā adhipatiḥ śivaḥ sadāśivaḥ bhavaḥ viṣṇuḥ brahmā sarvātmakaḥ yatas eka daṇḍe tathā lokāḥ ime kartā pitāmahaḥ prākṛtaḥ kathitaḥ tu eṣa puruṣa adhiṣṭhitaḥ mayā sargaḥ ca abuddhi pūrvaḥ tu dvijāḥ prāthamikaḥ śubhaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge prākṛtaprāthamikasargakathanam nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sargasya tādṛśī rātriḥ prākṛtasya samāsanaḥ divā sṛṣṭim vikurute rajanyām pralayam vibhuḥ divā vikṛtayaḥ sarve vikārāḥ viśva devatāḥ prajānām patayaḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ ahar tu tasya vaikalpaḥ rātriḥ tādṛgvidhā smṛtā catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vatsarāṇām kṛtam dvijāḥ tāvacchatī ca vai saṃdhyā saṃdhyā aṃśaḥ ca kṛtasya tu tri śartā dviśatā saṃdhyā tathā ca ekaśatā kramāt aṃśakaḥ ṣaṭśatam tasmāt kṛta saṃdhyāṃśakam vinā tretā dvāpara tiṣyāṇām kṛtasya kathayāmi vaḥ nimeṣa pañcadaśakā kāṣṭhā svasthā asya suvratāḥ martyasya ca akṣṇoḥ tamyāḥ ca tatas triṃśatikā kalā kalā triṃśatikaḥ viprāḥ muhūrtaḥ iti kalpitaḥ muhūrta pañcadaśikā rajanī tādṛśam tu ahar pitrya rātri ahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgaḥ tayoḥ punar kṛṣṇapakṣaḥ tu ahar teṣām śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī triṃśat ye mānuṣāḥ māsāḥ pitryaḥ māsaḥ tu saḥ smṛtaḥ śatāni trīṇi māsānām ṣaṣṭyā ca api adhikāni vai pitryaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ hi eṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate mānupena eva mānana varṣāṇām yat śatam bhavet pitṇām trīṇi varṣāṇi saṃkhyātāni iha tāni vai daśa vai dvi adhikāḥ māsāḥ vitṛ saṃkhyā iha saṃsmṛtā laukikena eva mānena abdaḥ yaḥ mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ divye rātri ahanī varṣam pravi bhāgaḥ tayoḥ punar ahar tatra udagayanam rātriḥ syāt dakṣiṇāyanam ete rātri ahanī divye prasaṃkhyāte viśeṣataḥ triṃśat yāni tu varṣāṇi divyaḥ māsaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ mānuṣam tu śatam viprāḥ divya māsāḥ trayaḥ tu te daśa ca eva tathā ahāni divyaḥ hi eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ trīṇi ṣaṣṭi varṣāṇi yāni tu divyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ hi eṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ trīṇi varṣa sahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi pramāṇāt triṃśat anyāni varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣi vatsaraḥ nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām mānuṣāṇi tu triśat tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām mānuṣāṇi tu varṣāṇām tat śatam jñeyam divyaḥ hi eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ trīṇi eva niyutāni āhuḥ varṣāṇām mānuṣāṇi tu ṣaṣṭiḥ ca eva sahasrāṇi saṃkhyātāni tu saṃkhyayā divyam varṣa sahasram tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyā vidaḥ janāḥ pūrvam kṛta yugam nāma tatas tretā vidhīyate dvārapaḥ ca kaliḥ ca eva yugāni etāni suvratāḥ atha saṃvatsarāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ sahasrāṇām śatāni āsan caturdaśa ca saṃkhyayā catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi tathā anyāni kṛtam yugam tathā daśa sahasrāṇām varṣāṇām śata saṃkhyayā aśītiḥ ca sahasrāṇi kāla sretā yugasya ca sapta eva niyutāni āhuḥ varṣāṇām mānuṣāṇi tu viṃśatiḥ ca sahasrāṇi kālaḥ tu dvāparasya ca tathā śata sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām trīṇi saṃkhyayā sahasrāṇi kālaḥ kali yugasya tu evam catur yugaḥ kālaḥ ṛte saṃdhyāṃśakāt smṛtaḥ niyutāni eva ṣaṭtriṃśat niraṃśāni tu tāni vai catvāriṃśat tathā trīṇi niyutāni iha saṃkhyayā viṃśatiḥ ca sahasrāmi saṃdhyāṃśaḥ ca caturyugaḥ evam catur yuga ākhyānām sādhakā hi ekasaptatiḥ manvantarasya saṃkhyā ca varṣa agreṇa prakīrtitā triṃśat koṭayaḥ tu varṣāṇām mānuṣeṇa dvijottamāḥ saptaṣaṣṭiḥ tathā anyāni niyutāni adhikāni tu viṃśatiḥ ca sahasrāṇi kālaḥ yam adhikam vinā manvantarasya saṃkhyā eṣā laiṅge ismin kīrtitā dvijāḥ niśā ante sṛjate lokān naśyante niśi jantavaḥ tatra vaimānikānām tu aṣṭāviṃśati koṭayaḥ manvantareṣu vai saṃkhyā sāṃtareṣu yathā tathā trīṇi koṭi śatāni āsan koṭayaḥ dvinavatiḥ tathā tu vai viprāḥ sahasrāṇām tu saptatiḥ punar tathā aṣṭa sāhasram sarvatra eva samāsatas koṭīnām dve sahasre tu aṣṭau koṭi śatāni tu dviṣāṣṭiḥ ca tathā koṭayaḥ niyutāni ca saptatiḥ varṣāṇām aṣṭa sāhasram brāhmam vai brahmaṇaḥ yugam savanānām sahasram tu trividham triguṇam tathā brahmaṇaḥ tu tathā proktaḥ kālaḥ kāla ātmanaḥ prabho ṛtuḥ vahniḥ havyavāhaḥ sāvitraḥ śuddhaḥ eva ca uśikaḥ kuśikaḥ ca eva gāndhāraḥ muni sattamāḥ bhaḥ ca tathā ṣaḍjaḥ majjālīyaḥ ca madhyamaḥ vairājaḥ vai niṣādaḥ ca mukhyaḥ vai meghavāhanaḥ pañcamāḥ citrakaḥ ca eva ākūtiḥ jñānaḥ eva ca manaḥ sudarśaḥ bṛṃhaḥ ca tathā vai śvetalohitaḥ raktaḥ ca pītavāsāḥ ca asitaḥ sarva rūpakaḥ evam kalpāḥ tu saṃkhyātāḥ brahmaṇaḥ avyakta janmanaḥ koṭi koṭi sahasrāṇi kalpānām muni sattamāḥ gatāni tāvat śeṣāṇi aharniśyāni vai punar para ante vai vikārāṇi vikāram yānti viśvatas vikārasya śivasya ājñā vaśena eva tu saṃhṛtiḥ sādharmyeṇa avatiṣṭhete pradhāna puruṣau ubhau guṇānām ca eva vaiṣamye viprāḥ sṛṣṭiḥ iti smṛtā sāmye layaḥ guṇānām tu tayoḥ hetuḥ maheśvaraḥ līlayā devadevena sargāḥ tu īdṛgvidhāḥ kṛtāḥ a saṃkhyātāḥ ca saṃkṣepāt pradhānāt anvadhiṣṭhitāt asaṃkhyātāḥ ca kalpa ākhyāḥ hi asaṃkhyatāḥ pitāmahāḥ harayaḥ ca api asaṃkhyātāḥ tu ekaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ pradhāna ādi pravṛttāni līlayā prākṛtāni tu aprākṛtasya tasya ādiḥ madhya antam na asti ca ātmanaḥ pitāmahasya atha paraḥ parārdha dvaya saṃmitaḥ divā sṛṣṭam tu yat sarvam niśi naśyati ca asya tat rātrau ca ekārṇave brahma naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame suṣvāpa aṃbhāsi yaḥ tasmāt nārāyaṇaḥ iti smṛtaḥ śarvarī ante prabuddhaḥ vai dṛṣṭvā śūnyam carācaram sraṣṭum tadā matim cakre brahmā brahma vidām varaḥ udakaiḥ āplutām kṣmām tām samādāya sanātanaḥ pūrvavat sthāpayāmāsa vārāham rūpam āsthitaḥ nadīnada samudrān ca pūrvavat ca akarot prabhuḥ dharāyām saḥ cinot sarvān girīn dagdhān purā agninā bhūḥ ādyān caturaḥ lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat sraṣṭum ca bhagavant cakre tadā sraṣṭā punar matim iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sṛṣṭiprāraṃbhavarṇanam nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca yadā sraṣṭum matim cakre mohaḥ ca āsīt mahātmanaḥ tamaḥ mohaḥ mahāmaḥ hastāmisraḥ ca andha saṃjñitaḥ avidyā pañcadhā hi eṣā prādurbhūtā svayambhoḥ asādhakaḥ iti smṛtvā sargaḥ mukhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ abhyamanyata saḥ anyam vai nagāḥ mukhya udbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ arvāksrotaḥ anugrahaḥ ca tathā bhūta ādikaḥ punar saptamaḥ mānuṣaḥ viprāḥ aṣṭamaḥ anugrahaḥ smṛtaḥ navamaḥ ca eva kaumāraḥ prākṛtāḥ vaikṛtāḥ tu ime purastāt asṛjat devaḥ sanandam sanakam tathā sanātanam muni śreṣṭhāḥ naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param dakṣam atrim vasiṣṭham ca saḥ asṛjat yoga vidyayā navā ete brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ brahma jñāḥ brāhmaṇa uttamāḥ brahma vādinaḥ eva ete brahmaṇaḥ sadṛśāḥ smṛtāḥ ṛbhum sanatkumāram ca sasarja ādau sanātanaḥ ha vakṣye bhāryā kulam teṣām munīnām agrajanmanām samāsatas muni śreṣṭhāḥ prajā saṃbhūtim eva ca śatarūpām tu vai rājñim virājam asṛjat prabhuḥ svāyaṃbhuvāt tu vai rājñī śatarūpā tu a yoni jā lebhe putra dvayam puṇyā tathā kanyā dvayam ca sā uttānapādaḥ hi avaraḥ dhīmān jyeṣṭhaḥ priyaṃvrataḥ jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā tu ākūtiḥ prasūtiḥ ca anujā smṛtā upayeme tadā ākūtim ruciḥ nāma prajāpatiḥ prasūtim bhagavān dakṣaḥ loka dhātrīm ca yoginīm dakṣiṇā sahitam yajñam ākūtiḥ suṣuve tathā dakṣiṇā ājanayāmāsa divyāḥ dvādaśa putrikāḥ prasūtiḥ suṣuve dakṣāt caturviśati kanyakāḥ śraddhām lakṣmīm dhṛtim puṣṭim tuṣṭim medhām kriyām tathā buddhi lajjām vapuḥśāntim siddhim kīrti mahā tapāḥ khyātim śānti ca saṃbhūtim smṛitm prītim kṣamām tathā sannatim ca anasūyām ca ūrjām svāhām surāraṇim svadhām ca eva mahābhāgām pradadau ca yathākramam śraddhā ādyāḥ ca eva kīrti antāḥ trayodaśa sudārikāḥ dharmam prajāpatim jagmuḥ patim parama durlabhāḥ upayeme bhṛguḥ dhīmān khyātim tām bhārgava araṇim saṃbhūtim ca marīciḥ tu smṛtim ca eva aṅgirāḥ muniḥ prītim pulastyaḥ puṇya ātmā kṣamām tām pulahaḥ muniḥ kratuḥ ca saṃnatim dhīmān atriḥ tām ca anasūyakām ūrjām vasiṣṭhaḥ bhagavān variṣṭhaḥ vārija īkṣaṇām vibhāvasuḥ tathā svāhām svadhām vai pitaraḥ tathā putrīkṛtā satī yā sā mānasī śiva saṃbhavā dakṣā ima jagantām dhātrī rudram eva āsthitā patim dṛṣṭvā sarga ādau kanaka aṇḍa jaḥ vibhajasva iti ca āha ādau yadā jātā tadā abhavat tasyāḥ ca eva aṃśa jāḥ sarvāḥ striyaḥ tribhuvane tathā ekādaśāvidhāḥ rudrāḥ tasya ca aṃśa udbhavāḥ tathā strī liṅgam akhilam sā vai pulliṅgam nīlalohitaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā bhagavān brahmā dakṣam ālokya suvratām bhajasva dhātrīm jagatām mama api ca tava api ca praśastā tava kāntā iyam syāt putrī viśva mātṛkā tasmāt putrī satī nāmnā te eṣā ca bhaviṣyati labdhvā putrīm dadau sākṣāt satīm rudrāya sādaram dharmasya patnyaḥ śraddhā ādyāḥ kīrtitāḥ vai trayodaśa śrutaḥ tu daṇḍaḥ samayaḥ bodhaḥ ca eva mahā dyutiḥ kṣemam sukham yaśaḥ ca eva dharma putrāḥ ca tāsu vai dharmasya vai kriyāyām tu daṇḍaḥ samayaḥ eva ca bhṛgu patnī ca suṣuve khyātiḥ viṣṇoḥ priyām śriyam dhātāram ca vidhātāram meroḥ jāmātarau sutau prabhūtiḥ nāma yā patnī marīceḥ suṣuve sutau pūrṇamāsam tu mārīcam tatas kanyā catuṣṭayam tuṣṭiḥ jyeṣṭhā ca vai dṛṣṭiḥ kṛṣiḥ ca apacitiḥ tathā kṣamā ca suṣuve putrān putrīm ca pulahāt śubhām kardamam ca varīyāṃsam sahiṣṇum muni sattamāḥ tathā kanaka pītām sa pīvarīm pṛthivī samām prītau pulastyaḥ ca tathā janayāmāsa vai sutān dattorṇam vedabāhum ca putrīm ca anyām dṛṣadvatīm putrāṇām ṣaṣṭi sāhasram saṃnatiḥ suṣuve śubhā kratoḥ tu bhāryā sarve te vālakhilyāḥ iti śrutāḥ sinīvālīm kuhūm ca eva rākām ca anumatim tathā smṛtiḥ ca suṣuve patnī muneḥ ca aṅgirasaḥ tathā atreḥ bhāryā anasūyā vai suṣuve ṣaṣ prajāḥ tu yāḥ tāsu ekā kanyakā nāmnā śrutuḥ sā sūnu pañcakam somaḥ ca vai śrutiḥ ṣaṣṭhī pañca ātreyāḥ tu sūnavaḥ ūrjā vasiṣṭhāt vai lebhe sutān ca suta vatsalā jyāyasī puṇḍarīkākṣān vāsiṣṭhān vara locanā rajaḥ suhotraḥ bāhuḥ ca savanaḥ ca anaghaḥ tathā yaḥ ca abhimānāḥ bhagavān bhava ātmā paitāmahaḥ vahniḥ asuḥ prajānām svāhā ca tasmāt suṣuve sutānām trayam trayāṇām jagatām hitāya iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge prajāsṛṣṭivarṇanam nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca pavamānaḥ pāvakaḥ ca śuciḥ agniḥ ca te smṛtāḥ nirmarthyaḥ pavamānaḥ tu vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ śuciḥ sauraḥ tu vijñeyaḥ svāhā putrāḥ trayaḥ tu te putraiḥ pautraiḥ tu iha eteṣām saṃkhyā saṃkṣepāt smṛtā prajānām patayaḥ sarve sarve rudra ātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ ayajvānaḥ ca yajvānaḥ pitaraḥ prīti mānasāḥ māgniṣvāttāḥ ca yajvānaḥ śeṣāḥ barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ menām tu mānasīm teṣām janayāmāsa vai svadhā menā mānasā loka viśrutā asūta menā mainākam kraiñcam tasya anujām umām gaṅgām haimavatīm jajñe bhava aṅga āśleṣa pāvanīm dharaṇīm janayāmāsa mānasīm yajña yājinīm pitaraḥ amṛtapāḥ proktāḥ teṣām ca eva iha vistaraḥ ṛṣīṇām ca kulam sarvam śṛṇudhvam tat su vistaram vadāmi pṛthak adhyāya saṃsthitam vaḥ tat ūrdhvatas dākṣāyaṇi sati yātā pārśvam rudrasya pārvatī paścāt dakṣam vinindya eṣā patim lebhe bhavam tathā tām dhyātvā vyasṛjat rudrān anekān nīlalohitaḥ yācitaḥ muni śārdūlāḥ brahmanā prahasan kṣaṇāt tān dṛṣṭvā vividhān rudrān nirmalān nīlalohitān prāha namaḥ astu vaḥ mahādevāḥ trinetrāḥ nīla lohitāḥ sarva jñāḥ sarva gāḥ dīrghāḥ hrasvāḥ vāmanakāḥ śubhāḥ hiraṇya keśāḥ dṛṣṭi ghnāḥ nityāḥ buddhāḥ ca nirmalāḥ nirdvandvāḥ vīta rāgāḥ ca viśva ātmānaḥ bhavātama jāḥ evam stutvā tadā ca āha bhavam śivam pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tadā bhagavān kanaka aṇḍa jaḥ mṛtyu hīnāḥ vibho sraṣṭum mṛtyu yuktāḥ sṛja prabho tatas tam āha bhagavān na hi me tādṛśī sthitiḥ sa tvam sṛja yathākāmam mṛtyu yuktāḥ prajāḥ prabho labdhvā sasarja sakalam śaṃkarāt ca turānanaḥ śaṃkaraḥ api tadā rudrauḥ nivṛtta ātmā hi adhiṣṭhitaḥ sthāṇu tvam tasya vai viprāḥ śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ niṣkalasya ātmanaḥ śaṃbhoḥ sva icchā dhṛta śarīriṇaḥ śam rudraḥ sarva bhūtānām karoti ghṛṇayā yatas śaṅkaraḥ ca aprayatnena tad ātmā yoga vidyayā aṇoḥ tu viṣaya tyāgaḥ saṃsāra bhayāt kramāt vairāgyāt jāyate puṃsaḥ virāgaḥ darśana antare viguṇa tyāgaḥ vijñānasya avicārataḥ tasya ca asya ca saṃdhānam prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ dharmaḥ jñānam ca vairāgyam aiśvaryam śaṃkarāt iha saḥ eva śaṅkaraḥ sākṣāt pinākī nīlalohitaḥ ye śaṅkara āśritāḥ sarve mucyante te na saṃśayaḥ na gacchanti eva narakam pāpiṣṭhāḥ api dāruṇam āśritāḥ śaṅkaram tasmāt prāpnuvanti ca śaśvatam ūcuḥ māyā antāḥ ca eva ghora adya hi aṣṭaviṃśatiḥ eva ca koṭayaḥ narakāṇām tu pacyante tāsu pāpinaḥ śritāḥ śivam śivam śaṃkaram nīlalohitam āśrayam sarva bhūtānām avyayam jagatām patim puruṣam paramātmānam puru hūtam puruṣṭutam tamasā kālarudra ākhyam rajasā kanaka aṇḍa jam karmaṇā akarmaṇā vā api śrotum kautūhalam hi naḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ prabhāvam śaṃkarasya ādyam saṃkṣepāt sarva darśiṇaḥ yoginaḥ sarva tattva jñāḥ param vairāgyam āsthitāḥ prāṇāyāma ādibhiḥ ca aṣṭa sādhanaiḥ sahacāriṇaḥ karuṇā ādi guṇa upetāḥ kṛtvā api vividhāni te prasādāt jāyate jñānam jñānāt yogaḥ pravartate yogena jāyate muktiḥ prasādāt ākhilam tatas ūcuḥ masādāḥ di ādi vijñānam svarūpam vaktum arhasi divyam māheśvaram ca eva yogam yoga vidām vara katham karoti bhagavān cintayā rahitaḥ śivaḥ prasādam yoga mārgeṇa kasmin kāle nṛṇām vibhuḥ uvāca devānām ca ṛṣīṇām ca pitṝṇām saṃnidhau purā śailādinā tu kathitam śṛṇvantu brahma sūnave vyāsa avatārāṇi tathā dvāpara ante ca suvratāḥ yoga ācārya avatārāṇi tathā tiṣye tu śūlinaḥ tatra tatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāḥ cātvāraḥ śama bhājanāḥ praśīṣyāḥ bahavaḥ teṣām prasīdati evam īśvaraḥ evam krama āgatam jñānam mukhāt eva nṛṇām vibhoḥ vaiśya antam brāhmaṇa ādyam hi ghṛṇayā ca anurūpatas ūcuḥ dvāpare dvāpare vyāsāḥ ke vai kutra antareṣu vai uvāca śṛṇvantu kalpe vārāhe dvijāḥ vaivasvata antare vyāsān ca sāṃpratam rudrān tathā sarva antareṣu vai vedānām ca purāṇānām tathā jñāna pradarśakān yathākramam pravakṣyāmi sarva āvarteṣu sāpratam kratuḥ satyaḥ bhārgavaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ mṛtyuḥ śatakratuḥ dhīmant vasiṣṭhaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ sārasvataḥ tridhāmā ca trivṛtaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ śatatejāḥ svayam dharmaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrutaḥ tarakṣuḥ ca aruṇiḥ dhīmān tathā devaḥ gṛtañjayaḥ tṛṇābinduḥ muniḥ rukṣaḥ śaktiḥ śākteyaḥ uttaraḥ jātūkarṇyaḥ hariḥ sākṣāt kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ vyāsāḥ tu ete ca śṛṇvantu kalau yogeśvarān kramāt asaṃkhyātāḥ hi kalpeṣu vibhoḥ sarva antareṣu ca kalau rudra avatārāṇām vyāsānām kila gauravāt avatārān pravakṣyāmi tathā sarva antareṣu vai ūcuḥ manvantarāṇi vārāhe vaktum arhasi sāṃpratam uvāca manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ tu ādyaḥ tatas svārociṣaḥ dvijāḥ uttamaḥ tāmasaḥ ca eva raivatāḥ cākṣuṣaḥ tathā vaivasvataḥ ca sāvarṇiḥ dharmaḥ sāvarṇikaḥ punar piśaṅgaḥ ca apiśaṅga ābhaḥ śabalaḥ varṇakaḥ tathā aukāra antāḥ akāra ādyāḥ manavaḥ parīkīrtitāḥ śvetaḥ pāṇḍuḥ tathā raktaḥ tāmrāḥ patiḥ ca kāpilaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śyāmaḥ tathā dhūmraḥ sudhūmraḥ ca dvijottamāḥ apiśaṅgaḥ piśaṅgaḥ ca tri varṇaḥ śabalaḥ tathā śubhāḥ svara ātmānaḥ samākhyātāḥ ca antara īśāḥ samāsatas tu samatīteṣu kalpeṣu tathā ca anāgateṣu vai vārāhaḥ sāṃpratam jñeyaḥ saptama antarataḥ kramāt yoga avatārān ca vibhoḥ śiṣyāṇām saṃtatiḥ tathā saṃprekṣya sarva kāleṣu tathā āvartteṣu yoginām ādye śvetaḥ kalau rudrāḥ sutāraḥ madanaḥ tathā suhotraḥ kaṅkaṇaḥ ca eva logākṣiḥ muni sattamāḥ jaigīṣavyaḥ mahā tejāḥ bhagavān dadhivāhanaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ ca muniḥ dhīmān ugraḥ catriḥ subālakaḥ bhṛt mālī aṭṭahāsaḥ ca dārukaḥ lāṅgalī tathā mahākāya muniḥ śūlī daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ svayam sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśaḥ jagadguruḥ yoga ācārya avatārāḥ ye sarva āvarteṣu suvratāḥ vyāsāḥ ca evam muni śreṣṭhāḥ dvāpare dvāpare tu ime yoga īśvarāṇām catvāraḥ śiṣyāḥ pratyekam avyayāḥ śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaṇḍī ca śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ dundubhiḥ śatarūpaḥ ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumant tathā mahā asuraḥ ca vikeśaḥ ca vipāśaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraḥ ca sudhāmā virajāḥ tathā meghaḥ sārasvataḥ tathā suvāhanaḥ muni śreṣṭhaḥ meghavāhaḥ mahā dyutiḥ kapilaḥ ca āsuriḥ ca eva tathā pañcāśikhaḥ muniḥ vālkalaḥ ca mahā yogī dharma ātmānaḥ mahā ojasaḥ parāśaraḥ ca gargaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ tathā balabandhu niṃrāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgaḥ tapodhanaḥ lambodaraḥ ca lambaḥ ca laṃbākṣaḥ laṃbakeśakaḥ sudhāmā kāśyapaḥ ca eva vāsiṣṭhaḥ virajāḥ tathā atriḥ devasadaḥ ca eva śravaṇaḥ atha śraviṣṭhakaḥ kuṇiḥ ca kuṇibāhuḥ ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ kaśyapaḥ upi uśanāḥ ca eva cyavanaḥ atha bṛhaspatiḥ vācaḥśravāḥ sudhakiḥ ca śyāvāśvaḥ ca yatīśvaraḥ nābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ logākṣiḥ kuthumiḥ tathā plakṣaḥ dālbhyāyāṇiḥ ca eva ketumant gopanaḥ tathā bhallāvī madhupiṅgaḥ ca śvetaketuḥ tāponidhiḥ śālihotra ugniveśaḥ ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaḥ ca kumbhaḥ ca eva pravāhaṅkaḥ ulūkaḥ vidyutaḥ ca eva maṇḍūkaḥ hi āśvalāyanaḥ akṣapādaḥ kumāraḥ ca ulukaḥ vatsaḥ eva ca śiṣyāḥ tu ete mahātmānaḥ sarva āvarteṣu yoginām vimalāḥ brahma bhūyiṣṭhāḥ jñāna yoga parāyaṇāḥ ete pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ śiṣyāḥ praśiṣyāḥ ca eteṣām śataśas utha sahasraśas prāpya pāśupatam yogam rudra lokāya saṃsthitāḥ deva ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ teṣām pati tvāt sarva īśaḥ bhavaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ tena praṇītaḥ rudreṇa paśūnām patinā dvijāḥ yogaḥ pāśupataḥ jñeyaḥ parāvara vibhūtaye iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge manuvyāsa yogeśvaratacchiṣyakathanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca saṃkṣepataḥ pravakṣyāmi yoga sthānāni sāṃpratam tāni śivena eva hitāya jagantām dvijāḥ prasādasya svarūpam yat sva saṃvedyam dvijottamāḥ vaktum na śakyam brahma ādyaiḥ kramaśas jāyate nṛṇām yoga śabdena nirvāṇam māheśam padam ucyate tasya hetuḥ ṛṣeḥ jñānam jñānam tasya prasādāt nirdahet pāpam nirudhya viṣayān sadā sādhanāni aṣṭadhā ca asya kathitāni iha siddhaye tṛtīyam āsanam proktam prāṇāyāmaḥ tatas param pratyāhāram pañcamaḥ vai dhāraṇā ca tatas parā dhyānam saptamam iti uktam samādhiḥ tu aṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ahiṃsā prathamaḥ hetuḥ yamasya yaminām varāḥ niyamasya api vai mūlam yamaḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ ātma vat sarva bhūtānām hitāya eva pravartanam ahiṃsā eṣā samākhyātā yā ca ātma jñāna siddhi dā dṛṣṭam śrutam ca anubhitam sva anubhūtam yathārthāt na aślīlam kīrtayet evam brāhmaṇānām iti śrutiḥ anādānam para svānām āpadi api vicārāt manasā karmaṇā vācā tat astā iyam samāsatas maithunasya apravṛttiḥ hi manaḥ vāc kāya karmaṇā brahmacaryam iti proktam yatīnām brahmacāriṇām iha vaikhānasānām ca vidārāṇām viśeṣataḥ sa dārāṇām gṛhastha nām tathā eva ca vadāmi vaḥ sva dāre vidhivat kṛtvā nivṛttiḥ ca anyatas sadā manasā karmaṇā vācā brahmacaryam iti smṛtam medhyā sva nārā saṃbhogam kṛtvā snānam samācaret evam gṛhasthaḥ yukta ātmā brahmacārī na saṃśayaḥ vidhinā yādṛśī hiṃsā sātva hiṃsā iti smṛtā striyaḥ sadā parityājyāḥ saṅgam na eva ca kārayet kuṇapeṣu yathā citta tathā kuryāt vicakṣaṇaḥ viṣ mūtra utsarga kāleṣu bahis bhūmau yathā matiḥ tathā kāryā ratau ca api sva dāre ca anyatas kutas aṅgāra sadṛśī nārī ghṛta kumbha samaḥ pumān tasmāt na ariṣu saṃsargam dūratas parivarjayet bhogena tṛptiḥ na eva asti viṣayāṇām vicārataḥ tasmāt virāgaḥ kartavyaḥ manasā karmaṇā girā na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā iva bhūyas eva abhivardhate tasmāt tyāgaḥ sadā kāryaḥ tu amṛta tvāya yoginā tyogena eva amṛta tvam hi śruti smṛti vidām varāḥ karmaṇā prajayā na asti dravyeṇa dvijasattamāḥ tasmāt virāgaḥ kartavyaḥ manaḥ vāc kāya karmaṇā yamāḥ saṃkṣepāt proktāḥ niyamān ca vadāmi vaḥ śaucam ijyā tapaḥ dānam svādhyāya upastha nigrahaḥ vrata upavāsa maunam ca snānam ca niyamāḥ daśa niyamaḥ syāt anīhā ca śaucam tuṣṭiḥ tapaḥ tathā mantraḥ śiva praṇīdhānam padmaka ādyam tathā āsanam bāhyam ābhyantaram proktam śaucam ābhyantaram varam bāhya śaucena yuktaḥ san tathā ca abhyantaram caret āgneyam vāruṇam brāhmam kartavyam śiva pūjakaiḥ snānam vidhānataḥ samyak paścāt ābhyam taram caret mṛdā ālipya tīrtha toyeṣu sarvadā śaivalāḥ jhaṣakāḥ matsyāḥ sattvāḥ matsya upajīvinaḥ sadā avagādyaḥ salile viśuddhāḥ kim dvijottamāḥ tasmāt ābhyantaram śaucam sadā kāryam vidhānāt snātvā sakṛt ālipya bhāvatas suvairāgya mṛdā śuddhaḥ śaucam evam prakīrtitam śuddhasya siddhayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ na eva aśuddhasya siddhayaḥ nyāyena āgatayā vṛttyā saṃtuṣṭaḥ yaḥ tu suvrataḥ saṃtoṣaḥ tasya satatam atīta arthasya ca asmṛtiḥ cāndrāyaṇa ādi nipuṇasya pāṃsi su śubhāni ca svādhyāyaḥ tu japaḥ proktaḥ praṇavasya tridhā smṛtaḥ vācikaḥ ca adhamaḥ mukhyaḥ upāṃśuḥ ca uttama uttamaḥ mānasaḥ vistareṇa eva kalpe pañca akṣare smṛtaḥ tathā śiva praṇīdhānam manaḥ vāc kāya karmaṇā śiva jñānam guroḥ bhaktiḥ acalā su pratiṣṭhitā nigrahaḥ hi apahṛtya āśu prasaktāni indriyāṇi ca viṣayeṣu samāsena pratyāhāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ cittasya dhāraṇā proktā sthāna bandhaḥ samāsatas tasyāḥ svāsthyena dhyānam ca samādhiḥ ca vicārāt samādhiḥ sarva hetuḥ ca prāṇāyāmaḥ iti smṛtaḥ prāṇa apāna nirodhaḥ tu prāṇāyāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ prāṇāyāmasya mānam tu mātrā dvādaśakam smṛtam nīcaḥ dvādaśa mātraḥ tu uddhātaḥ dvādaśaḥ smṛtaḥ mukhyaḥ tu yaḥ tris uddhātaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat mātraḥ ucyate romāñca dhvani saṃviddha sva aṅgamaḥ u ṭana kampanam bhramaṇam sveda janyā sā saṃvid mūrchā bhavet yadā tadā uttama uttamaḥ proktaḥ praṇāyāmaḥ su śobhanaḥ ibhaḥ vā śarabhaḥ vā api durādharṣaḥ atha kesarī tathā sa mariṇaḥ asvasthaḥ durādharṣaḥ ca yoginām yathā eva mṛgarāj nāgaḥ śarabhaḥ vā api durmadaḥ kāla antara vaśāt yogāt damyate parama ādarāt manaḥ vāc kāya jān doṣān kartuḥ deham ca rakṣati saṃyuktasya tathā samyak prāṇāyāmena dhīmataḥ doṣāt tasmāt ca naśyanti niśvāsaḥ tena jīryate prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti divyāḥ śānti ādayaḥ kramāt ca bhāve catuṣṭayasya iha proktā śāntiḥ iha dvijāḥ sahaja āgantukānām ca pāpānām śāntīḥ ucyate praśāntiḥ saṃyamaḥ samyak vacasām iti saṃsmṛtā prakāśaḥ dīptiḥ iti uktaḥ sarvatas sarvadā dvijāḥ prasādaḥ iti saṃproktaḥ svānte tu iha catuṣṭaye prāṇaḥ apānaḥ samānaḥ ca udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca nāgaḥ kūrmaḥ tu kṛkalaḥ devadattaḥ dhanañjayaḥ eteṣām yaḥ prasādaḥ tu marutām iti saṃsmṛtaḥ prayāṇam kurute tasmāt vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti smṛtaḥ apānayati apānaḥ tu āhāra ādīn krameṇa ca vyānaḥ vyānāmayati aṅgam vyādhi ādīnām prakopakaḥ udvejayati marmāṇi udānaḥ ayam praṅkīrtitaḥ samam nayati gātrāṇi samānaḥ pañca vāyavaḥ udgāre nāgaḥ ākhyātaḥ kūrmaḥ unmīlane tu saḥ kṛkalaḥ kṣutakāya eva devadattaḥ vijṛṃbhaṇe dhanañjayaḥ mahā ghoṣaḥ sarvagaḥ sa mṛte api hi iti yaḥ daśa vāyūnām prāṇāyāmena sidhyati prasādaḥ asya turīyā tu saṃjñā viprāḥ catuṣṭaye khyātiḥ saṃvīt tatas paścāt īśvaraḥ matiḥ eva ca buddhyāḥ etāḥ dvijāḥ saṃjñāḥ mahataḥ parikīrtitāḥ asyāḥ buddheḥ prasādaḥ tu prāṇāyāmena siddhi ati visvaraḥ visvarībhāvaḥ dvandvānām muni sattamāḥ agrajaḥ sarva tattvānām mahān yaḥ parimāṇāt yad pramāṇa guhā prajñā manaḥ tu manute yatas bṛha tvāt bṛṃhaṇa tvāt ca brahmā brahma vidām varāḥ sarva karmāṇi bhoga artham yat cinoti citiḥ smṛtā khyāyate yat tu iti khyātiḥ jñāna ādibhiḥ anekaśas sarva tattva adhipaḥ sarvam vijānāti yat īśvaraḥ asyāḥ buddheḥ prasādaḥ tu prāṇāyāmena siddhi ati doṣān vinirdahet sarvān prāṇāyāmāt asau yamī pātakam dhāraṇābhiḥ tu pratyāhāreṇa nirdahet viṣayān viṣa vat dhyātvā dhyānena anīśvarān guṇān samādhinā yati śreṣṭhāḥ prajñā vṛddhim vivardhayet sthānam labdhvā eva kurvīta yoga aṣṭāṅgāni vai kramāt agni abhyāse jale vā api śuṣka parṇa caye tathā jantu vyāpte śmaśāne ca jīrṇa goṣṭe catuṣpathe na ācaret deha bādhāyām daurmanasya ādi saṃbhave darpaṇa udara saṃkāśe kṛṣṇa agaru su dhūpite nānā puṣpa samākīrṇe vitāna upari śobhite sama āsana sthaḥ yoga aṅgāni abhyaset hṛṣitaḥ svayam praṇipatya gurum paścāt bhavam devīm vināyakam yogi īśvarān sa śiṣyān ca yogam yuñjīta yoga vid hastam badhvā padmam ardhāsanam tu vā sama jānuḥ tathā dhīmān eka jānuḥ atha api vā samam dṛḍha āsanaḥ bhūtvā saṃhṛtya caraṇau ubhau saṃvṛta āsya upabaddha akṣaḥ uraḥ viṣṭabhya ca agratas pārṣṇibhyām vṛṣaṇau rakṣan tathā prajananam punar kiṃcid unnāmita śira dantaiḥ dantān na saṃspṛśet saṃprekṣya nāsikā agrām svam diśaḥ ca an avalokayan oṃkāra vācyam paramam śuddham dīpa śikhā ākṛtim dhyāyet vai puṇḍarīkasya karṇikāyām samāhitaḥ tri aṅgule ca aṣṭakoṇam vā pañcakoṇam atha api vā trikoṇam ca tathā āgneyam saumyam sauram sva śaktibhiḥ āgneyam ca tatas sauram saumyam evam vidhānāt agneḥ adhas prakalpya evam dharma ādīnām catuṣṭayam guṇa trayam krameṇa eva maṇḍala upari bhāvayet nābhau vā atha gale vā api śrū madhye vā yathāvidhi phalikāyām vā mūrdhani dhyānam samācaret dbidale ṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre krameṇa tu daśa are vā ṣaāḍasre vā catur asre smaret śivam dvādaśa āditya saṃkāśe candra bimba same api vā āgnivarṇe atha vā vidyut valaya ābhe samāhitaḥ nīlalohita bimbe vā yogī dhyānam maheśvaram hṛdi dhyāyet nābhi padme sadāśivam candracūḍam lalāṭe tu śrū madhye śaṃkaram svayam divye ca śāśvata sthāne śiva dhyānam samabhyaset nirmalam niṣkalam brahma su śāntam jñāna rūpiṇam alakṣaṇam anirdeśyam aṇoḥ alpataram śubham kaivalyam ca eva nirvāṇam niḥśreyasam anūpamam mahānandam parānandam yogānandam anāmayam heya upādeya rahitam sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataram śivam atīndriyam anābhāsam param tattvam parātparam nābhau sadāśivam ca api sarva deva ātmakam vibhum deha madhye śivam devam śuddha jñāna mayam vibhum tat kanyasena eva mārgeṇa ca udghātena api śaṃkaram dvātrīṃśat recayet dhīmān hṛdi nābhau samāhitaḥ recakam pūrakam tyaktvā kumbhakam ca dvijottamāḥ ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān sākṣāt samarase sthitaḥ dhāraṇā dvādaśa āyāmā dhyānam dvādaśa dhāraṇam dhyānam dvādaśakam yāvat samādhiḥ rabhidhīyate athavā jñāninām viprāḥ saṃparkāt eva jāyate prayatnāt vā tayoḥ cirāt vā hi acirāt dvijāḥ yoga antarāyāḥ ta jāyante yuñjataḥ punar iti śrī liṅge mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge aṣṭāṅgayoganirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca mālasyam prathamam paścāt vyādhi pīḍā prajāyate pramādaḥ saṃśaya sthāne cittasya iha anavasthitiḥ aśraddhā darśanam bhrāntiḥ duḥkham ca trividham tatas daśadhā abhiprajāyante muneḥ yoga antarāyakāḥ ālasyam ca apravṛttiḥ ca guru tvāt kāya acittayoḥ vyādhayaḥ dhātu vaiṣamyāt karma jāḥ doṣa jāḥ tathā pramādaḥ tu sādhanānām mabhāvanam idam vijñānam sthāna saṃśayaḥ aśraddhā bhāva rahitā vṛttiḥ vai sādhaneṣu ca sādhye cittasya hi gurau jñāna ācāra śiva ādiṣu anātmani ātma vijñānam ajñānāt tasya saṃnidhau icchā vighātāt saṃkṣobhaḥ cetasaḥ tat udāhṛtam tamasā rajasā ca eva saṃspṛṣṭam durmanaḥ smṛtam haṭhāt svīkaraṇam kṛtvā yogya ayogya vivekāt pranaṣṭeṣu antarāyeṣu dvijāḥ paścāt hi yoginaḥ pratibhā prathamā siddhiḥ dvitīyā śravaṇā smṛtā hi vārttā tṛtīyā vipra indrāḥ turīyā ca iha darśanā āsvādā pañcamā proktā vedanā ṣaṣṭhikā smṛtā su alpa ṣaṣ siddhi saṃtyāgāt siddhi dāḥ siddhayaḥ muneḥ sūkṣme vyavahita itīte viprakṛṣṭe tu anāgate sarvatra sarvadā jñānam pratibhā anukrameṇa tu śravaṇāt sarva śabdānām aprayatnena yoginaḥ hrasva dīrgha pluta ādīnām guhyānām śravaṇāt api sparśasya adhigamaḥ yaḥ tu vedanā tu upapāditā darśanāt divya rūpāṇām darśanam ca aprayatnataḥ vārtā ca divya gandhānām tanmātrāḥ buddhi saṃvidā jagati asmin hi deha stham catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇam samam aupasagiṅkam eteṣu guṇeṣu guṇitam dvijāḥ paiśāce pārthivam ca āpyam rākṣasāṇām pure dvijāḥ tu taijasam proktam gāndharve śvasana ātmakam madhye ca aṣṭa dvitīye ca tathā ṣoḍaśa rūpakam catvāriṃśat pañcame tu bhūtamātrā ātmakam smṛtam tathā aṣṭacatvāriṃśat ca ṣaṭpañcāśatī tathā eva ca catuḥ ṣaṣṭi guṇam brāhmam labhate dvijasattamāḥ sthūlatā hrasvatā bālyam vārddhakyam yauvanam tathā nānā jāti svarūpam ca caturbhiḥ dehadhāraṇam pārthiva aṃśam vinā nityam surabhiḥ gandha saṃyutaḥ etat aṣṭaguṇam proktam aiśvaryam pārthivam mahat tat tat rasa anvitam tasya trayāṇām dehadhāraṇam bhāṇḍam vinā atha hastena jala piṇḍasya dhāraṇam agni nigrahaṇam haste smṛti mātreṇa ca āgamaḥ bhasmībhūta vinirmāṇam yathāpūrvam sa kāmatas dvābhyām rūpa viniṣpattiḥ vinā taiḥ tribhiḥ ātmanaḥ caturviṃśa ātmakam hi etat taijasam muni puṃgavāḥ manogati tvam bhūtānām antar nivasanam tathā laghu tvam ca guru tvam ca pāṇibhyām vāyu dhāraṇam chāyā vihīna niṣpattiḥ indriyāṇām ca darśanam dūre ca śabda grahaṇam sarva śabdāḥ vagāhanam tanmātra liṅga grahaṇam sarva prāṇini darśanam yata akāma upalabdhiḥ ca yathākāma vinirgamaḥ kāma anurūpa nirmāṇam vaśi tvam priya darśanam saṃsāra darśanam ca eva mānasam guṇa lakṣaṇam chedanam tāḍanam bandham saṃsāra parivartanam sarva bhūta prasādaḥ ca mṛtyu kāla jayaḥ tathā prājāpatyam idam proktam āha ṅkārikam uttamam akāraṇa jagat sṛṣṭiḥ tathā anugrahaḥ eva ca asādṛśyam idam vyaktam nirmāṇam ca pṛthak pṛthak etāvat tattvam iti uktam prādhānyam vaiṣṇavam padam brahmaṇā tad guṇam śakyam vettum anyaiḥ na śakyate vidyate tad param śaivam viṣṇunā na avagamyate asaṃkhyeya guṇam śuddham kaḥ jānīyāt śiva ātmakam vyutthāne siddhayaḥ ca etāḥ hi upasargāḥ ca kīrtitāḥ nāśa atiśaya tām jñātvā viṣayeṣu bhayeṣu ca vaitṛṣṇyam puruṣe khyātam guṇa vaitṛṣṇyam ucyate vairāgyeṇa eva saṃtyājyāḥ siddhayaḥ ca aupasargikāḥ athavā anugraha artham ca līlā artham vā tadā muniḥ kvacid bhūmim parityajya hi ākāśe krīḍate śriyā udgiret ca kvacid vedān sūkṣmān arthān samāsatas kvacid daṇḍaka bandham tu sahasraśas mṛga pakṣi samūhasya ruta jñānam ca vindati bahunā atra kim uktena vijñānāni sahasraśas abhyāsena eva vijñānam viśuddham ca sthiram bhavet tejaḥ rūpāṇi sarvāṇi sarvam paśyati yoga vid deva bimbāni anekāni vimānāni sahasraśas brahma viṣṇu indra yama agni varuṇa ādikān graha nakṣatra tārāḥ ca bhuvanāni sahasraśas pātāla tala saṃsthāḥ ca samādhi sthaḥ sa paśyati prasāda amṛta pūrṇena sattva pātra sthitena tu tamaḥ nihatya puruṣaḥ paśyāti hi atmani īśvaram tasya prasādāt dharmaḥ ca aiśvaryam jñānam eva ca vairāgyam apavargaḥ ca na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na śakyaḥ vistaraḥ vaktum varṣāṇām ayutaiḥ api yoge pāśupate niṣṭhā sthātavyam ca muni īśvarāḥ iti śrī liṅgapurāṇe pūrva bhāge yogāntarāyakathanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca satām jita ātmanām sākṣāt dvijātīnām dvijottamāḥ dharma jñānām ca sādhūnām ācāryāṇām śivatmanām dayāvatām dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ tathā ca eva tapasvinām saṃnyāsinām viraktānām jñāninām vaśaga ātmanām dāninām ca eva dāntānām trayāṇām satya vadinām alubdhānām sayogānām śruti smṛti vidām dvijāḥ śrauta smārta aviruddhānām prasīdati maheśvaraḥ sāyujyam brahmaṇaḥ yāti tena saṃtaḥ pracakṣate daśa ātmake ye viṣaye sādhane ca aṣṭa lakṣaṇe na krudhyānti na hṛṣyanti jita ātmānaḥ tu te smṛtāḥ sāmānyeṣu ca dravyeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca brahma kṣatra viśe yasmāt yuktāḥ tasmāt dvijātayaḥ varṇa āśrameṣu yuktasya svarga ādi sukha kāriṇaḥ vidyāyāḥ sādhanāt sādhu brahmacārī guroḥ hitaḥ kriyāṇām sādhanāt ca eva gṛhasthaḥ sādhuḥ ucyate sādhanāt tapasaḥ araṇye sādhuḥ vaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ yatamānaḥ yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛtaḥ yogasya sādhanāt evam āśrama dharmāṇām sādhanāt sādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ kuśala kuśalam karma dharma adharmau iti smṛtau dhāraṇa arthe mahān hi eṣa dharma śabdaḥ prakīrtitaḥ atra iṣṭa prāpakaḥ dharmaḥ ācāryaiḥ upadiśyate adharmaḥ ca aniṣṭa phalaḥ hi ācaryaiḥ upadiśyate vṛddhāḥ ca a lolupāḥ ca eva ātmavantaḥ hi a dāṃbhikāḥ samyak vinītāḥ ṛjavaḥ tān ācāryan pracakṣate bhācinoti ca śāstra arthān ācāryaḥ tena ca ucyate vijñeyam śravaṇāt śrautam smaraṇāt smārtam ucyate ijyā veda ātmakam śrautam smārtam varṇa āśrama ātmakam dṛṣṭvā anurūpam artham yaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ na eva api gūhati yathā dṛṣṭa pravādaḥ tu satyam laiṅge atra paṭhyate ahiṃsā sarvatas śāntiḥ tapaḥ iti abhidhīyate ātma vat sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ hitāya ahitāya ca vartate tu asakṛt dhṛttiḥ kṛtsnā hi eṣā dayā smṛtā yat yat iṣṭatamam dravyam nyāyena eva āgatam kramāt tat tat guṇavate deyam dātuḥ tat dāna lakṣaṇam kāruṇyāt sarva bhūtebhyaḥ saṃvibhāgaḥ tu madhyamaḥ śruti smṛtibhyām vihitaḥ dharmaḥ varṇa āśrama ātmakaḥ śiṣṭa ācāra aviruddhaḥ ca sa dharmaḥ sādhuḥ ucyate māyā karma phala tyāgī śiva ātmā pariḥ ketataḥ ātma artham vā para artham vā indriyāṇi iha yasya vai anudvignaḥ hi aniṣṭeṣu tathā iṣṭān na abhinandati prīti tāpa viṣādebhyaḥ vinivṛttiḥ virakta tā saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇām nyāsaḥ kṛtānām akṛtaiḥ saha kuśala akuśalānām tu prahāṇam nyāsaḥ ucyate cetana acetana anya tva vijñānam jñānam vacyate evam tu jñāna yuktasya śraddhā yuktasya śaṃkaraḥ prasīdati na saṃdehaḥ dharmaḥ ca ayam dvijottamāḥ jñānam adhyāpanam homaḥ dhyānam yajñaḥ tapaḥ śrutam cāndrāyaṇa sahasraiḥ ca prājāpatya śataiḥ tathā māsa upavāsaiḥ ca anyaiḥ vā bhaktiḥ muni vara uttamāḥ bhaktānām darśanāt eva nṛṇām svarga ādayaḥ dvijāḥ brahma viṣṇu suredrāṇām tathā anyeṣām api sthitiḥ bhavena ca tathā proktam saṃprekṣya umām pinākinā devyai devena madhuram vārāṇasyām purā dvijāḥ avimukte samāsīnāḥ rudreṇa paramātmanā rudrāṇī rudram āha idam labdhvā vārāṇasīm purīm uvāca kena vaśyaḥ mahādeva pūjyaḥ dṛśyaḥ tvam īśvaraḥ uvāca niśamya vacanam tasyāḥ tathā hi ālokya vārvatīm ha bāla indu tilakaḥ pūrṇa indu vadanām hasan smṛtvā atha menayā patnyā gireḥ gām kathitām purā devī labdhā purī ramyā tvayā yat praṣṭum arhasi sthāna artham kathitam mātrā vismṛtā iha vilāsini purā pitāmahena api pṛṣṭaḥ praśravatām vare yathā tvayā adya vai pṛṣṭaḥ draṣṭum brahmatmakam tu aham śvete śvetena varṇena dṛṣṭvā kalpe tu mām śubhe sadyojātam tathā rakte raktam vāmam pitāmahaḥ pīte tatpuruṣam pītam aghore kṛṣṇam īśvaram īśānam viśvarūpa ākhyaḥ viśvarūpam tat āha mām uvāca dṛṣṭaḥ mayā tvam gāyatryā devadeva maheśvara kena vaśyaḥ mahādeva dhyeyaḥ kutra ghṛṇā nidhe dṛśyaḥ pūjyaḥ tathā devyā vaktum arhasi śaṃkara śrī bhagavant uvāca dhyeyaḥ liṅge tvayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā payasām nidhau pūjyaḥ pañcāsya rūpeṇa pavitraiḥ pañcabhiḥ dvijaiḥ bhava bhaktyā adya dṛṣṭaḥ uham tvayā aṇḍaja jagadguro saḥ upi mām āha bhāva artham dattam tasmai mayā purā bhāvam bhāvena deveśi dṛṣṭavan mām hṛdi īśvaram tasmāt tu śraddhayā vaśyaḥ dṛśyaḥ śreṣṭha gireḥ sute pūjyaḥ liṅge na saṃdehaḥ sarvadā śraddhayā dvijaiḥ śraddhā dharmaḥ paraḥ sūkṣmāḥ śraddhā jñānam hutam tapaḥ śraddhā svargaḥ ca mokṣaḥ ca dṛśyā uham śraddhayā sadā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bhaktibhāvakathanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham vai dṛṣṭavān brahmā sadyojātam maheśvaram vāmadevam mahātmānam purāṇa puruṣottamam uvāca ekonatriṃśakaḥ kalpaḥ vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ tasmin tat paramam dhyānam dhyāyataḥ brahmanaḥ tadā utpannaḥ tu śikhā yuktaḥ kumāraḥ śveta lohitaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā puruṣam śrīmān brahmā vai viśvatomukhaḥ hṛdi kṛtvā mahātmānam brahma rūpiṇam īśvaram dhyāna yogāt param jñātvā vavande devam īśvaram tatas asya pārśvatas śvetāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ mahā yaśāḥ śiṣyāḥ te vai mahātmānaḥ yaiḥ tat brahma sadā āvṛtam tasya agre śveta varṇa ābhaḥ śvetaḥ nāma mahā muniḥ prapannāḥ parayā bhaktyā gṛṇantaḥ brahma śāśvatam tasmāt viśveśvaram devam ye prapadyanti vai dvijāḥ prāṇāyāma pare bhūtvā brahma tatpara mānasāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sadyojātamāhatmyam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca dhyāyataḥ putra kāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ mahā tejāḥ kumāraḥ rakta bhūṣaṇaḥ sa tam dṛṣṭvā mahātmānam kumāram rakta vāsasam param dhyānam samāśritya bubudhe devam īśvaram tathā stutaḥ mahādevaḥ brahmanā parameśvaraḥ dhyāyatā putra kāmena pitāmahaiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ paramayā bhaktyā stutaḥ ca brahma purvakam vetsyase mām prasaṃkhyātam loka dhātāram īśvaram tatas tasya mahātmānaḥ catvāraḥ te kumārakāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ mahātmānaḥ viśuddhāḥ brahma varcasaḥ virajāḥ ca vibāhuḥ ca viśokaḥ viśvabhāvanaḥ brahmaṇyāḥ brahmaṇaḥ tulyāḥ vīrāḥ adhyavasāyinaḥ rakta ambara dharāḥ sarve rakta mālya anulepanāḥ rakta kuṅkuma lipta aṅgāḥ rakta bhasma anulepanāḥ gṛṇantaḥ ca mahātmānaḥ brahma tat vāmadaivikam anugraha artham lokānām śiṣyāṇām hita kāmyayā dharma upadeśam akhilam kṛtvā te brahmaṇaḥ priyāḥ ye api ca anye dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ yuñjānāḥ vāmam īśvaram prapaśyanti mahādevam tad bhaktāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ te sarve pāpa nirmuktāḥ vimalāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vāmadevamāhātmyam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ekatriṃśattamaḥ kalpaḥ pītavāsāḥ iti smṛtaḥ brahma yatra mahābhāgaḥ pīta vāsāḥ babhūva ha dhyāyataḥ putra kāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ mahā tejāḥ kumāraḥ pītagandha anulipta aṅgaḥ pīta mālya ambaraḥ yuvā hema yajñopavītaḥ ca pīta uṣṇīṣaḥ mahā bhujaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā dhyāna saṃyuktaḥ brahmā loka maheśvaram manasā loka dhātāram prapede śaraṇam vibhum tatas dhyāna gataḥ tatra brahmā māheśvarīm varām gām viśva rūpām dadṛśe maheśvara mukhāt cyutām catuṣpadām catur vaktrām catur hastām catuḥstanīm catur netrām catuḥśṛṅgīm catur daṃṣṭrām catur makhīm dvātriṃśat guṇa saṃyuktā amī śvarīm sarvatomukhām sa tām dṛṣṭvā mahā tejāḥ mahādevīm maheśvarīm matīḥ smṛtiḥ buddhiḥ iti gāyamānaḥ punar punar mahādevī sā atiṣṭhat prāñjaliḥ vibhum viśvam āvṛtya yogena jagant sarvam vaśīkuru atha tām āha deveśaḥ rudrāṇī tvam bhaviṣyasi brāhmaṇānām hita arthāya parama arthā bhaviṣyasi tathā enām putra kāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ pradadau devadeveśaḥ catuṣpādām jagadguruḥ tatas tām dhyāna yogena viditvā parameśvarīm gāyatrīm tu tatas raudrīm dhyātvā brahman anuyantritaḥ iti etām vaidīkīm vidya raudrīm gāyatrim īritām japitvā tu mahādevīm brahmā loka namaskṛtām aiśvaryam jñāna saṃpattim vairāgyam ca dadau prabhuḥ tatas asya pārśvatas divyāḥ pradurbhūtāḥ kumārakāḥ pīta mālya ambara dharāḥ pīta sraj anulepanāḥ pīta ābha uṣṇīṣa śirasaḥ pīta āsyāḥ pīta mūrdhajāḥ yoga ātmānaḥ te pohlādāḥ brāhmaṇānām hita eṣiṇaḥ dharma yoga bala upetāḥ munīnām upadiśya mahā yogam praviṣṭāḥ te maheśvaram niyata ātmānaḥ dhyāna yuktāḥ jita indriyāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge tatpuruṣamāhātmyam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sraṣṭu kāmaḥ prajāḥ brahmā cintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ samabhava dvarṇaḥ dhyāyataḥ parama uṣṭhinaḥ atha apaśyat mahā tejāḥ prādurbhūtam kumārakam kṛṣṇa varṇam mahā vīryam dīpyamānam sva tejasā kṛṣṇa ambara dhara uṣṇīṣam kṛṣṇa yajña upavītinam kṛṣṇena maulinā yuktām kṛṣṇa sraj anulepanam sa tam dṛṣṭvā mahātmānam aghoram ghora vikramam vavande devadeveśam adbhutam kṛṣṇa piṅgalam prāṇāyāma paraḥ śrīmān hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram tathā vai dhyāyamānasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ atha asya pārśvatas kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇa sraj anulepanāḥ catvāraḥ tu mahātmānaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ kumārakāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇa śikhaḥ ca eva kṛṣṇa āsyaḥ upāsitvā mahā yogam śiṣyebhyaḥ pradaduḥ punar yogena yogasam pannāḥ praviśya manasā śivam amalam nirguṇam syānam praviṣṭāḥ viśvam īśvaram evam etena yogena ye api ca anye manīṣiṇaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge aghorotpattivarṇanam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tatas tā asmin gate kalpe kṛṣṇa varṇe bhayānake tuṣṭāva devadeveśam brahmā tam brahma rūpiṇam anugṛhya tatas tuṣṭaḥ brahmāna mavadat haraḥ anena eva tu rūpeṇa saṃharāmi na saṃśayaḥ brahmahatyā ādikān ghorān tathā anyān api pātakān hīnān ca eva mahābhāga tathā eva vividhāni api mānasānim su tīkṣṇāni vācikāni pitāmaha kāyikāni sumiśrāṇi tathā prāsaṃgikāni ca buddhi pūrvam kṛtāni eva sahaja āgantukāni ca mātṛ deha uttha tāni evam pitṛ dehe ca pātakam saṃharāmi na saṃdehaḥ sarvam pātaka jam vibho caturguṇam buddhi pūrve krodhāt aṣṭaguṇam smṛtam vīra hā lakṣa mātreṇa bhrūṇa hā koṭim abhyaset mātṛ hā niyutam japtvā śuddhyate na atra saṃśayaḥ go ghnaḥ ca eva kṛtaghnaḥ ca strī ghnaḥ pāpa yutaḥ naraḥ asnāta āśī sahasreṇa ajapī ca tathā dvijaḥ a huta āśī sahasreṇa a dātā ca viśuddhyā ati brāhmaṇa sva apahartā ca svarṇa steyī nara adhamaḥ niyutam mānasam japtvā mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ rataḥ vā api mātṛ ghnaḥ vā nara adhamaḥ samparkāt pāpinām pāpam tad samam paribhāṣitam saṃsargāt pātakī lakṣam japet vai mānasam dhiyā upāṃśu yat caturdhā vai vācikam ca aṣṭadhā japet pātakāt ardham eva syāt upapātakinām smṛtam tad ardham kevale pāpe na atra kāryā vicāraṇā kṛtvā caja gurutalpam pāpa kṛt brāhmaṇaḥ yadi rudragāyatryā grāhyam go mūtram kāpilam dvijāḥ śuktam iti ājyam kāpilam saṃharet budhaḥ āpyāyasva iti ca kṣīram ca āharet gavyam dadhi navam sākṣāt kāpilam vai pitāmahaiḥ ekasthām hema pātre vā kṛtvā aghoreṇa rājate tāmre vā padma pātre vā pālāśe vā dale śubhe sa kūrcam sarva ratna āḍhyam kṣiptvā tatra eva kāñcanam japet lakṣam aghora ākhyam hutvā ca eva ghṛta ādibhiḥ hutvā avoreṇa deveśam snātvā aghoreṇa vai dvijāḥ aṣṭa droṇa ghṛtena eva snāpya paścāt viśodhya ca ahorātra uṣitaḥ snātaḥ pibet kūrcam śiva agratas evam kṛtvā kṛtaghnaḥ api brahma hā bhrūṇa hā tathā ca madyapaḥ vṛṣalī saktaḥ para dāra vidharṣakaḥ brahma sva hā tathā go ghnaḥ mātṛ hā pitṛ hā tathā tathā anyāni ca pāpāni mānasāni dvijaḥ yadi vācikāni tathā anyāni kāyikāni sahasraśas iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge aghoreśamahātmyam pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha anyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ kalpaḥ vartate muni puṃgavāḥ viśvarūpaḥ iti khyātaḥ nāmnaḥ parama adbhutaḥ vinivṛtte tu saṃhāre punar sṛṣṭe carācare brahmaṇaḥ putra kāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ prādurbhūtā mahā nādā viśva rūpā sarasvatī viśva mālya ambara dharā viśva yajña upavītinī viśva uṣṇīṣā viśva gandhā viśva mātā mahoṣṭhikā tathāvidham sa bhagavant īśānam parameśvaram śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam atha tam manasā dhyātvā yukta ātmā vai pitāmahaḥ vavande devam īśānam sarva īśam sarva gam prabhum namaḥ astu sarva vidyānām īśāna parameśvara namaḥ astu sarva bhūtānām īśāna vṛṣavāhana oṃkāra mūrte deveśa sadyojāta namaḥ namaḥ vāmadeva namaḥ tubhyam jyeṣṭhāya vara dāya ca namaḥ vikaraṇāya eva kāla varṇāya varṇine balāya balinām nityam sadā vikaraṇāya te sarva bhūta īśvara īśāya bhūtānām damanāya ca mahātmane jyeṣṭhāya ca eva śreṣṭhāya rudrāya vara dāya ca śrāvayet vā dvijān śrāddhe sa yāti paramām gatim evam dhyāna gatam tatra praṇamantam pitāmaham uvāca bhagavant īśaḥ prītaḥ aham te kim icchasi tatas tu praṇataḥ bhūtvā vāc viśuddham maheśvaram uvāca bhagavān rudram prītam prītena cetasā yat idam viśva rūpam te viśva gauḥ śreyāḥ īśvarā kā eṣā bhagavatī devī catuṣpādā caturmukhā catur śṛṅgī catur vattrā catur daṃṣṭrā catuḥstanī catur hastā catur netrā viśva rūpā katham smṛtā kiṃnāma gotrā kasya iyam kiṃvīryā ca api karmataḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā devadevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ prāha deva vṛṣam brahmā brahmāṇam ca ātma saṃbhavam rahasyam sarva mantrāṇām pāvanam puṣṭi vardhanam śṛṇuṣva etat param guhyam ādi sarge yathā tathā tvattaḥ parataram deva viṣṇunā tat padam śubham vaikuṇṭhena viśuddhena mama vāma aṅga jena vā śatam śata sahasrāṇām atītāḥ ye svayaṃbhuvaḥ purastāt te deveśaiḥ tat śṛṇuṣva mahāmate māṇḍavya gotraḥ tapasā mama putra tvam āgataḥ tvayi yogam ca sāṃkhyam ca tapaḥ vidyā vidhi kriyāḥ ṛtam satyam dayā brahma ahiṃsā sat matiḥ kṣamā dhyānam dhyeyam damaḥ śāntiḥ vidyā avidyāḥ matiḥ dhṛtiḥ kāntiḥ nitiḥ prathā medhā lajjā dṛṣṭiḥ sarasvatī tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā ca eva prasādaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ dvātriṃśat suguṇā hi eṣā dvātriṃśa akṣara saṃjñayā viṣṇoḥ bhagavantaḥ ca api tathā anyeṣām api prabho sā eṣā bhagavatī devī mad prasūtiḥ pratiṣṭhitā caturmukhā jagat yoniḥ prakṛtiḥ gauḥ pratiṣṭhitā gaurī māyā ca vidyā ca kṛṣṇā haimavatī iti ca pradhānam prakṛtiḥ ca eva yām āhuḥ tattva cintakāḥ ajām ekām lohitām śukla kṛṣṇām viśva prajām sṛjamānām sarūpām mām viddhi tām viśva rūpam gāyatrīm gām viśva rūpām hi buddhyā tatas ca pārśva gāḥ devyāḥ sarva rūpa kumārakāḥ jaṭī muṇḍī śikhaṇḍi ca ardhamuṇḍaḥ ca jajñire dharma upadeśam akhilam kṛtvā yoga mayam dṛḍham śiṣṭāḥ ca niyata ātmānaḥ praviṣṭāḥ rudram īśvaram iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge īśānamāhātmyakathanam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ evam saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ sadya ādīnām samudbhavaḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet vā dvijottamān sa yāti brahma sāyujyam prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ ūcuḥ katham liṅgam abhūt liṅge samabhyarcyaḥ sa śaṃkaraḥ kim liṅgam kaḥ tathā liṅgī sūta vaktum iha arhasi uvāca evam devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ praṇipatya pitāmaham apṛcchan bhagavant liṅgam katham āsīt iti svayam kim liṅgam kaḥ tathā liṅgī saḥ upi āha ca pitāmahaḥ uvāca pradhānam liṅgam ākhyātam liṅgī ca parameśvaraḥ rakṣā artham ambudhau mahyam viṣṇoḥ tu āsīt sura uttamāḥ sthiti kāle tadā pūrṇe tatas pratyāhṛte tathā śuṣke ca sthāvare sarvasmin tu anāvṛṣṭyā ca sarvaśas paśavaḥ mānuṣāḥ vṛkṣāḥ piśācāḥ piśita aśanāḥ gandharva ādyāḥ krameṇa eva nirdagdhāḥ bhānu bhānubhiḥ suṣvāpa ambhasi yoga ātmā nirmalaḥ nirupaplavaḥ sahasra śīrṣā viśva ātmā sahasra akṣaḥ sahasra pād hiraṇyagarbhaḥ rajasā tamasā śaṅkaraḥ svayam kāla ātmā kālānābhaḥ tu śuklaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tu nirguṇaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sarva ātmā sat asat mayaḥ tathābhūtam aham dṛṣṭvā śayānam paṅkaja īkṣaṇam tadā hasta prahāreṇa tīvreṇa sa dṛḍhena tu prabuddhaḥ ūhīya śayanāt samāsīnaḥ kṣaṇam vaśī mām agre saṃsthitam bhāsa adhyāsitaḥ bhagavant hariḥ ha ca utthāya bhagavant hasan mām madhuram sakṛt svāgatam svāgatam vatsa pitāmaha mahā dyute tasya tat vacanam śrutvā smita pūrvam sura ṛṣabhāḥ bhāṣase vatsa vatsaiḥ iti sarga saṃhāra kāraṇam mām iha antar smitam kṛtvā guruḥ śiṣyam iva anagha prakartāram jagatām sākṣāt prakṛtyāḥ ca pravartakam sanātanam ajam viṣṇum viriñcim viśva saṃbhavam viśva ātmānam vidhātāram dhātāram paṅkaja īkṣaṇam bhartā hartā bhavān aṅgāt avatīrṇaḥ mama avyayāt vismṛtaḥ asi jagannātham nārāyaṇam anāmayam puruṣam paramātmānam puru hūtam puruṣṭutam viṣṇum acyutam īśānam viśvasya prabhava udbhavam tava aparādhaḥ na asti atra mama māyā kṛtam tu idam aham eva param jyotiḥ parama ātmā tu aham vibhuḥ yat yad dṛṣṭam śrutam sarvam jagati asmin carācaram mayā sṛṣṭam purā vyaktam caturviśatikam svayam nitya antāḥ hi aṇavaḥ baddhāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ krodha udbhava ādayaḥ prasādāt hi bhavān aṇḍāni anekāni iha līlayā sṛṣṭā buddhiḥ mayā tasyām ahaṅkāraḥ tridhā tatas tanmātra pañcakam tasmāt manaḥ ṣaṣṭha indriyāṇi ca ākāśa ādīni bhūtāni bhautikāni ca līlayā āvayoḥ ca abhavat yuddham su ghoram roma harṣaṇam ca jvālā mālā sahasra āḍhyam kāla anala śata upamam mohitam prāha mām atra parikṣāvaḥ agni saṃbhavam evam vyāhṛtya viśvātmā sva rūpam akarot tadā vārāham aham api āśu haṃsa tvam prāptavan surāḥ tadā prabhṛti mām āhuḥ ṛṃhasam haṃsaḥ virāj iti haṃsa haṃsa iti yaḥ brūyāt mām haṃsaḥ sa bhaviṣyati su śvetaḥ hi anala akṣaḥ ca viśvatas pakṣa saṃyutaḥ manaḥ nila javaḥ bhūtvā gataḥ ham ca ūrdhvatas surāḥ nārāyaṇaḥ api viśvātmā nīlāñjana caya upamam daśa yojana vistīrṇam śata yojanam āyatam meru parvata varṣmāṇam gaura tīkṣṇa agra daṃṣṭriṇam kāla āditya sama ābhāsam dīrgha ghoṇam mahā svaram hrasva pādam vicitra aṅgam jaitram dṛḍham anaupamam vārāham asitam rūpam āsthāya gatavān adhas evam varṣa sahasram tu tvaran viṣṇuḥ adhas gataḥ na apaśyat alpam api asya mūlam liṅgasya sūkaraḥ śrāntaḥ hi a dṛṣṭvā tasya antam ahaṃkārāt adhas gataḥ tathā eva bhagavant viṣṇuḥ śrāntaḥ saṃtrasta locanaḥ samāgataḥ mayā sārdham praṇipatya mahāmanāḥ māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhoḥ tasthau saṃvigna mānasaḥ pṛṣṭhatas pārśvatas ca eva ca agratas parameśvaram praṇipatya mayā sārdham sasmāra kim idam tu iti tadā samabhavat tatra nādaḥ vai śabda lakṣaṇaḥ om om iti sura śreṣṭhāḥ su vyaktaḥ pluta lakṣaṇaḥ liṅgasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tadā apaśyat sanātanam ādya varṇa makāram tu ukāram ca uttare tatas makāram madhyatas ca eva nāda antam tasya ca ūm iti sūrya maṇḍala vat dṛṣṭvā varṇam ādyam tu dakṣiṇe uttare pāvaka prakhyam ukāram puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ śītāṃśu maṇḍala prakhyam makāram madhyamam tathā turīya atītam amṛtam niṣkalam nirupaplavam nirdvandvam kevalam śūnyam bāhya abhyantara varjitam ādi madhya anta rahitam ānandasya api kāraṇam mātrāḥ tisraḥ tu ardha mātram nāda ākhyam brahma saṃjñitam ṛk yajuḥ sāma vedāḥ vai mātrā rūpeṇa mādhavaḥ veda śabdebhyaḥ eva īśam viśvātmānam acintayat tadā abhavat ṛṣiḥ vedaḥ ṛṣeḥ sāratamam śubham tena eva ṛṣiṇā viṣṇuḥ jñātavan parameśvaram a prāpya tam nivartante vācyaḥ tu eka akṣareṇa saḥ eka akṣareṇa tat vāci amṛtam parama kāraṇam eka akṣarāt akāra ākhyaḥ bhagavān kanaka aṇḍa jaḥ eka akṣarāt ukāra ākhyaḥ hariḥ parama kāraṇam eka akṣarāt makāra ākhyaḥ bhagavant nīlalohitaḥ makāra ākhyaḥ vibhuḥ vījī hi akāraḥ bījam ucyate ukāra ākhyaḥ hariḥ yoniḥ pradhāna puruṣa īśvaraḥ bījī ca bījam tad yoniḥ nāda ākhyaḥ ca maheśvaraḥ bījī vibhajya ca ātmānam sva icchāyā tu vyavasthitaḥ asya liṅgāt abhūt bījam akāraḥ bījīnaḥ prabhoḥ sauvarṇam abhavat ca aṇḍam āveṣṭya ādyam tat akṣaram aneka abdam tathā ca apsu divyam aṇḍam vyavasthitam aṇḍam apsu sthitam sākṣāt ādi ākhyena īśvareṇa tu tasya aṇḍasya śubham haimam kapālam ca ūrddhva saṃsthitam jajñe yat dyauḥ tad aparam pṛthivī pañca lakṣaṇā tasmāt aṇḍa udbhavaḥ jajñe tu akāra ākhyaḥ caturmukhaḥ sa sraṣṭā sarva lokānām saḥ eva trividhaḥ prabhuḥ evam om om iti proktam iti āhuḥ yajuṣām varāḥ yajuṣām vacanam śrutvā ṛcaḥ sāmāni sādaram tatas vijñāya deveśam yathāvat śruti sambhavaiḥ āvayoḥ stuti saṃtuṣṭaḥ liṅge tasmin nirañjanaḥ divyam śabda mayam rūpam āsthāya prahasan sthitaḥ akāraḥ tasya mūrdhā tu lalāṭam dīrgham ucyate ikāraḥ dakṣiṇam netram īkāraḥ vāma locanam ukāraḥ dakṣiṇam śrotram ūkāraḥ vāmam ucyate ṛkāraḥ dakṣiṇam tasya kapolam parameṣṭhinaḥ vāmam kapolam ṝkāraḥ ḷ ḷ nāsā puṭe ubhe ekāram oṣṭham ūrddhvaḥ ca ekāraḥ tu adharaḥ vibhoḥ kādi pañca akṣarāṇi asya pañca hastāni dakṣiṇe madhya ādi pañca akṣarāṇi evam pañca hastāni vāmatas tathā pakāram udaram tasya phakāraḥ pārśvam ucyate bakāraḥ vāma pārśvam vai bhakāram skandham asya tat makāram hṛdayam śaṃbhoḥ mahādevasya yogīnaḥ yakāra ādi sakāra antam vibhoḥ vai sapta dhātavaḥ hakāraḥ ātma rūpam vai kṣakāraḥ krodhaḥ ucyate tam dṛṣṭvā umayā sārdham bhagavantam maheśvaram praṇamya bhagavān viṣṇuḥ punar ca apaśyat ūrddhvatas oṃkāra prabhavam mantram kalā pañcaka saṃyutam śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam subha aṣṭatriṃśat akṣaram gāyatrī prabhavam mantram haritam vaśya kārakam caturviṃśati varṇa āḍhyam catuṣkalam anuttamam atharvam asitam mantram kalā aṣṭaka samāyutam yajurveda samāyuktam pañcatriṃśat śubha akṣaram kalā aṣṭaka samāyuktam su śvetam śāntikam tathā trayodaśa kalā yuktam bāla ādyaiḥ saha lohitam sama udbhavam jagatī ādyam vṛddhi saṃhāra kāraṇam varṇāḥ ṣaṣ adhikāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ asya mantra varasya tu pañca mantrān tathā labdhvā jajāpa bhagavant hariḥ atha dṛṣṭvā kalā varṇam ṛc yajuḥ sāma rūpiṇam īśānam īśa mukuṭam puruṣa āsyam purātanam aghora hṛdayam hṛdyam vāma guhyam sadāśivam sadyas pādam mahādevam mahā bhogi indra bhūṣaṇam viśvatas pāda vadanam viśvatas akṣi karam śivam tuṣṭāva punar iṣṭābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ vara dam aśviram iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge liṅgodbhavaḥ nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ eka akṣarāya rudrāya akārāya ātma rūpiṇe ukārāya ādi devāya vidyā dehāya vai namaḥ tṛtīyāya makārāya śivāya paramātmane sūrya agni soma varṇāya yajamānāya vai namaḥ agnaye rudra rūpāya rudrāṇām pataye namaḥ śivāya śiva mantrāya sadyojātāya vedhase vāmāya vāmadevāya vara dāya amṛtāya te aghorāya ati ghorāya sadyojātāya raṃhase īśānāya śmaśānāya ativegāya vegine namaḥ astu śrutipādāya ūrdhvaliṅgāya liṅgine hema liṅgāya hemāya vāri liṅgāya ca ambhase śivāya śiva liṅgāya vyāpine vyoma vyāpine pṛthivyai ca antarikṣāya pṛthivī vyāpine namaḥ anantāya virupāya ananta anāmayāya ca śāśvatāya variṣṭhāya vāri garbhāya yogine acetanāya cintyāya cetanā āyāsa hāriṇe arūpāya surūpāya anaṅgāya aṅga hāriṇe śvetāya śveta varṇāya tuhinādri carāya ca su śvetāya suvaktrāya namaḥ śvetaśikhāya ca śveta āsyāya mahā āsyāya namaḥ te śveta lohita sutārāya viśiṣṭāya namaḥ dundubhine hara śatarūpa virupāya namaḥ ketumate sadā ṛddhi śoka viśokāya pinākāya kapardine vipāśāya supāśāya namaḥ te pāśa nāśine suhotrāya haviṣyāya subrahmaṇyāya sūriṇe kaṅkāya kaṅka rūpāya kaṅkaṇī kṛta pannaga sanatkumāra sāraṅga māraṇāya mahātmane loka akṣiṇe tridhāmāya namaḥ virajase sadā śaṅkhapālāya śaṅkhāya rajase tamase namaḥ suvāhāya vivāhāya vivāda vara dāya ca namaḥ śivāya rudrāya pradhānāya namaḥ namaḥ saṃsārāya namaḥ tubhyam namaḥ saṃsāra hetave mokṣāya mokṣa rūpāya mokṣa kartre namaḥ namaḥ ātmane ṛṣaye tubhyam svāmine viṣṇave namaḥ namaḥ bhagavate tubhyam nāgānām pataye namaḥ oṃkārāya namaḥ tubhyam sarvajñāya namaḥ namaḥ sarvāya ca namaḥ tubhyam namaḥ nārāyaṇāya ca mahādevāya devānām īśvarāya namaḥ namaḥ śarvāya ca namaḥ tubhyam satyāya śamanāya ca brahmaṇe ca eva bhūtānām sarvajñāya namaḥ namaḥ mahātmane namaḥ tubhyam prajñā rūpāya vai namaḥ citaye citi rūpāya smṛti rūpāya vai namaḥ jñānāya jñāna gamyāya namaḥ te saṃvide sadā śikharāya namaḥ te nalikaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ ardha nārī śarīrāya avyaktāya namaḥ namaḥ ekādaśa vibhedāya sthāṇave te namaḥ sadā namaḥ somāya sūryāya bhavāya bhava hāriṇe yaśaskarāya devāya śaṃkarāya īśvarāya ca namaḥ umbikā adhipataye umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ nīla keśāya vittāya śitikaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ kapardine namaḥ te nāga aṅga ābharaṇāya ca hartre kartre namaḥ namaḥ vīra rāma atirāmāya rāma nāthāya te vibho namaḥ rājā dhirājāya rājñām adhigatāya te namaḥ pāla adhipataye namaḥ namaḥ keyūra bhūṣāya gopate te namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ śrīkaṇṭha nāthāya namaḥ likuca pāṇaye sāraṅgāya namaḥ tubhyam rājahaṃsāya te namaḥ sarpa kuṇḍala mālāya kaṭisūtrīkṛta ahine virarāma iti saṃstutvā brahmaṇā sahitaḥ hariḥ etat stotra varam puṇyam sarva pāpa praṇāśanam yaḥ paṭhet śrāvayet vā api brāhmaṇān vedapāragān tasmāt japet paṭhet nityam śrāvayet brāhmaṇān śubhān sarva pāpa viśuddhi artham viṣṇunā paribhāṣitam iti liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge viṣṇustavaḥ nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca paśyatām mām mahādevam bhayam sarvam vimucyatām yuvām prasūtau gātrābhyām mama pūrvam mahā balau ayam me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ vāme pārśve ca me viṣṇuḥ viśvātmā hṛdaya udbhavaḥ evam uktvā tu tam viṣṇum karābhyām parameśvaraḥ pasparśa subhagābhyām tu kṛpayā tu kṛpā nidhiḥ tatas prahṛṣṭa manasā praṇipatya maheśvaram prāha nārāyaṇaḥ nātham liṅga stham liṅga varjitam devaḥ pradattavān devāḥ sva ātmani avyabhicāriṇīm brahmaṇe viṣṇave ca eva śraddhām śītāṃśu bhūṣaṇaḥ jānubhyām avanīm gatvā punar nārāyaṇaḥ svayam praṇipatya ca viśveśam prāha mandataram vaśī iha āgataḥ bhavān yasmāt vivāda śamanāya āvayoḥ praṇipatya sthitam mūrdhnā kṛta añjali puṭam smayan śrī mahādevaḥ uvāca pralaya sthiti sargāṇām kartā tvam dharaṇī pate tridhā bhinnaḥ hi aham viṣṇo brahma viṣṇu bhava ākhyayā sarga rakṣā laya guṇaiḥ niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ saṃmoham tyaja bho viṣṇo pālaya enam pitāmaham tadā drakṣyasi mām ca evam saḥ api drakṣyati padmajaḥ tadā prabhṛti lokeṣu liṅga arccā su pratiṣṭhitā liṅga vediḥ mahādevī liṅgam sākṣāt maheśvaraḥ sa yāti śivatām vipraḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge viṣṇuprabodhaḥ nāma ekonāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ bhavam ca dṛṣṭavan tena brahmaṇā puruṣottamaḥ etat sarvam viśeṣeṇa sāṃpratam vaktum arhasi uvāca mayam āsīt ekārṇavam ghoram avibhāgam tamaḥ mayam ca nārāyaṇa mukha udgīrṇa sarva ātmā puruṣottamaḥ aṣṭa bāhuḥ mahā vakṣāḥ lokānām yoniḥ ucyate evam tatra śayanena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā mad ārāmeṇa krīḍā artham līlayā akliṣṭa karmaṇā śata yojana vistīrṇam taruṇa āditya sannibham vajra daṇḍam mahā utsedham nābhau sṛṣṭam tu puṣkaram tasya evam krīḍamānasya samīpam devamīḍhuṣaḥ caturvaktraḥ viśāla akṣaḥ samāgamya yadṛcchayā krīḍamānam ca padmena dṛṣṭvā brahmā śubha īkṣaṇam provāca kaḥ bhavān śete hi āśritaḥ mavyam aṃbhasām atha tasya acyutaḥ śrutvā brahmanaḥ tu śubham vacaḥ dyauḥ antarikṣam bhūḥ ca eva param padam aham bhuvaḥ tam evam uktvā bhagavant viṣṇuḥ punar atha abravīt kaḥ tvam khalu samāyātaḥ samīpam bhagavān kutas kva vā bhūyas ca gantavyam kaḥ ca vā te pratiśrayaḥ evam bruvantam vaikuṇṭham pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhoḥ a vijñāya janārdanam māyayā mohitam devam avijñātam mahātmanaḥ yathā bhavān tathā eva aham ādikartā prajāpatiḥ sa vismayam vacaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ loka tantriṇaḥ anujñātaḥ ca te nātha vaikuṇṭhaḥ viśva saṃbhavaḥ kautūhalāt mahā yogī praviṣṭaḥ brahmaṇaḥ mukham imān aṣṭādaśa dvīpān sa samudrān sa parvatān praviśya su mahā tejāḥ cāturvarṇya samākulān brahmaṇaḥ tu udare dṛṣṭvā sarvān viṣṇuḥ mahā bhujaḥ aṭitvā vividhān lokān viṣṇuḥ nānāvidha āśrayān tatas varṣa sahasra ante na antam hi dadṛśaḥ yadā nārāyaṇaḥ jagat dhātā pitāmaham atha abravīt bhagavān ādiḥ aṅkaḥ ca madhyam kālaḥ diśaḥ nabhaḥ evam uktvā abravīt bhūyas pitāmaham idam hariḥ bhagavān evam eva aham śāśvatam hi mama udaram tatas prāhlādinīm vāṇīm śrutvā tasya abhinandya ca śrīpateḥ udaram bhūyas praviveśa pitāmahaḥ paryaṭitvā tu devasya dadṛśe antam na vai hareḥ jñātvā gatim tasya pitāmahasya dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pidhāya viṣṇuḥ tatas dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pihitāni samīkṣya vai sūkṣmam kṛtvā ātmanaḥ rūpam nābhyām dvāram avindata padma sūtra anusārā ima ca anvapaśyat pitāmahaḥ ujjahāra ātmanaḥ rūpam puṣkarāt caturānanaḥ brahmā svayambhuḥ bhagavān jagadyoniḥ pitāmahaḥ kutas api aparimeya ātmā bhūtānām prabhuḥ iśvaraḥ śūlapāṇiḥ mahādevaḥ hema vīra ambara chadaḥ śīghram vikramataḥ tasya udbhūtāḥ tūrṇam ākāśe pṛthulāḥ toya bindavaḥ ati uṣṇaḥ ca atiśatiḥ ca vāyuḥ tatra vavau punar tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam brahmā viṣṇum abhāṣata ap bindavaḥ ca śīta uṣṇāḥ kampayanti ambujam bhṛśam etat me saṃśayam brūhi kim vā tu anyat cikīrṣasi śrutvā apratima karmā hi bhagavān asura antakṛt kim nu khalu atra me nābhau bhūtam anyat kṛta ālayam kim mayā ca kṛtam deva yat mām priyam anuttamam bhāṣase puruṣa śreṣṭha kimartham brūhi tattvataḥ evam bruvāṇam deveśam lokayātrā anugam tatas brahmā vedanidhiḥ prabhuḥ yaḥ asau te udaram pūrvam praviṣṭaḥ aham tvad icchayā yathā mama udare lokāḥ sarve dṛṣṭāḥ tvayā prabho tathā eva dṛṣṭāḥ kārtsnyena mayā lokāḥ tava udare tvayā matsara bhāvena mām vaśīkartum icchatā āśu dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pihitāni samantataḥ mā abhūt te manasaḥ alpaḥ api vyāghātaḥ ayam kathaṃcana iti eṣā anugatiḥ viṣṇo kāryāṇām aupasarpiṇī yat mayā anantaram kāryam brūhi kim karavāṇi aham tatas param ameya ātmā hiraṇyakaśipoḥ ripuḥ anavadyām priyām iṣṭām śivām vāṇīm pitāmahāt na hi evam īdṛśam kāryam mayā adhyavasitam tava tvām bodhayitu kāmena krīḍā pūrvam yadṛcchayā āśu dvārāṇi sarvāṇi ghāṭitāni mayā ātmanaḥ na te anyathā avagantavyam mānyaḥ pūjyaḥ ca me bhavān sarvam marṣaya kalyāṇa yat mayā apakṛtam tava na aham bhavantam śaknomi soḍhum tejaḥ mayam gurum sa tvam ca naḥ mahā yogī tvam īḍyaḥ praṇava ātmakaḥ adya prabhṛti sarva īśaḥ śveta uṣṇīṣa vibhūṣitaḥ tatas sa bhagavant devaḥ varam da tvā kirīṭine evam bhavatu ca iti uktvā prīta ātmā gata matsaraḥ saṃnamatha āyāntam bāla arka ābham mahā ānanam bhavam atyadbhutam dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇam atha abravīt aprameyaḥ mahā vaktraḥ daṃṣṭrī dhvasta śiroruhaḥ daśa bāhuḥ trisūla aṅkaḥ nayanaiḥ viśvatas sthitaḥ loka prabhuḥ svayam sākṣāt vikṛtaḥ muñjamekhalī kaḥ khalu eṣa pumān viṣṇo tejaḥ rāśiḥ mahā dyutiḥ vyāpya sarvāḥ diśaḥ dyām ca itas eva abhivartate mahatā ākāśe pi utthitāḥ ca jalaśayāḥ ghrāṇa jena ca vātena kaṃpyamānam tvayā saha samāgataḥ bhavān īśaḥ hi anādiḥ ca anta kṛt prabhuḥ bhavān aham ca stotreṇa upatiṣṭhāva go dhvajam tatas kruddhaḥ ambujābhākṣam brahmā provāca keśavam brahmānam loka kartāram mām na vetsi sanātanam tasya tat krodha jam vākyam śrutvā hariḥ abhāṣata mā mā evam vada kalyāṇa parivādam mahātmanaḥ hetuḥ asya atha jagataḥ purāṇapuruṣaḥ avyayaḥ bījī khalu eṣa bījānām jyotiḥ ekaḥ prakāśate bāla krīḍanakaiḥ devaḥ krīḍate śaṃkaraḥ svayam mama ca etāni nāmāni nityam prasava dharmiṇaḥ yaḥ kaḥ saḥ iti duḥkha ārtaiḥ dṛśyate yatibhiḥ śivaḥ eṣa bījī bhavān bījam aham yoniḥ sanātanaḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ viśvātmā brahmā viṣṇum apṛcchata bhavān yoniḥ aham bījam katham bījī maheśvaraḥ jñātvā ca vividha utpattim brahmaṇaḥ loka tantriṇaḥ imam parama sādṛśyam praśram abhyavadat hariḥ mahataḥ paramam dhāma śivam adhyātminām padam mama yonau samāyuktam tat bījam kāla paryayāt hiraṇmayam akūpāre yonau aṇḍam ajāyata śatāni daśa varṣāṇā maṇḍam apsu pratiṣṭhitam kapālam ekam dyauḥ jajñe kapālam aparam kṣitiḥ mātāra arka idu nakṣatram śūnyam lokam avekṣya ca priyadarśanāḥ tu yatayaḥ yatīnām pūrvajāḥ tava bhuvana anala saṃkāśāḥ padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇāḥ śrīmān sanatkumāraḥ ca ṛbhuḥ ca eva ūrdhva retasau utpannāḥ sama kālam te buddhyā atīndriya darśanāḥ utpannāḥ pratibhā ātmānaḥ jagatām sthiti hetavaḥ na ārapsyante ca karmāṇi tāpa traya vivarjitāḥ alpa saukhyam bahu kleśam jarā śoka samanvitām maraṇam ca eva saṃbhavaḥ ca punar punar viditvā ca āgamam sarvam avaśyam bhavitavyatām ṛbhum sanatkumāram ca dṛṣṭvā tava vaśe sthitau trayaḥ tu trīn guṇān hitvā ca ātmajāḥ sanaka ādayaḥ tatas teṣu pravṛtteṣu sanaka ādiṣu vai triṣu bhaviṣyasi vimūḍhaḥ tvam māyayā śaṃkarasya tu evam kalpe tu vaivṛtte saṃjñā naśyati te anagha yalpe śeṣāṇi bhūtāni sūkṣmāṇi pārthivāni ca sarveṣām hi aiśvarā māyā samudāhṛtā jñātvā ca īśvara sadbhāvam jñātvā mām ambuja īkṣaṇam mahādevam mahābhūtam bhūtānām vara dam prabhum tvām ca mām ca eva saṃkruddhaḥ niḥśvāsāt nirdahet ayam evam jñātvā mahā yogam abhyuttiṣṭhan mahā balam mama tvām agratas kṛtvā stoṣyāmi anala saprabham iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge brahmaprabodhanam nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca brahmaṇam agratas kṛtvā tatas sa garuḍadhvajaḥ uvāca namaḥ kṣetra adhipataye bījine śūline namaḥ sumeṇḍhrāya arcya meṇḍhrāya daṇḍine rūkṣa retase namaḥ jyeṣṭhāya śreṣṭhāya pūrvāya prathamāya ca namaḥ mānyāya pūjyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ ca namaḥ te hi mad ādīnām bhūtānām prabhave namaḥ vedānām prabhave ca eva smṛtīnām prabhave namaḥ prabhave karma dānānām dravyāṇām prabhave namaḥ namaḥ dhruva nibaddhānām ṛṣīṇām prabhave namaḥ ṛkṣāṇām prabhave tubhyam grahāṇām prabhave namaḥ vaidyuta aśani meghānām garjita prabhave namaḥ mahā udadhīnām prabhave dvīpānām prabhave namaḥ adrīṇām prabhave ca eva varṣāṇām prabhave namaḥ namaḥ nadīnām prabhave nadānām prabhave namaḥ mahauṣadhīnām prabhave vṛkṣāṇām prabhave namaḥ dharmavṛkṣāya dharmāya sthitīnām prabhave namaḥ namaḥ rasānām prabhave ratnānām prabhave namaḥ prabhave ca eva lavānām prabhave namaḥ ahorātra ardha māsānām māsānām prabhave namaḥ ṛtūnām prabhave tubhyam saṃkhyāyāḥ prabhave namaḥ namaḥ purāṇa prabhave sargāṇām prabhave namaḥ kalpa udaya nibandhānām vātānām prabhave namaḥ mantrāṇām prabhave tubhyam mantra adhipataye namaḥ pitṝṇām pataye ca eva paśūnām pataye namaḥ vāc vṛṣāya namaḥ tubhyam purāṇa vṛṣabhāya ca namaḥ paśūnām pataye govṛṣa indra dhvajāya ca prajāpatīnām pataye siddhīnām pataye namaḥ daitya dānava saṃghānām rakṣasām pataye namaḥ gandharvāṇām ca pataye yakṣāṇām pataye namaḥ garuḍa uraga sarpāṇām pakṣiṇām pataye namaḥ sarva guhya piśācānām guhya adhipataye namaḥ gokarṇāya ca goptre ca śaṅkukarṇāya vai namaḥ varāhāya aprameyāya ṛkṣāya virajāya ca namaḥ surāṇām pataye gaṇānām pataye namaḥ ambhasām pataye ca eva ojasām pataye namaḥ namaḥ astu lakṣmīpataye śrīpāya kṣitipāya ca bala abala samūhāya akṣobhya kṣobhaṇāya ca dīpta śṛṅga eka śṛṅgāya vṛṣabhāya kakudmine atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya vai namaḥ suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hi ajitāya ca vara dāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane namaḥ bhavāya devāya ijyāya yājakāya ca pratyudīrṇāya dīptāya tattvāya atiguṇāya ca namaḥ pāśāya śastrāya namaḥ tu ābharaṇāya ca hutāya upahūtāya prahuta prāśitāya ca namostu yaṣṭāya pūrtāya agniṣṭoma dvijāya ca namaḥ ca eva dakṣiṇa avabhṛthāya ca ahiṃsāya apralobhāya paśu mantra auṣadhāya ca namaḥ puṣṭi pradānāya suśīlāya suśīline atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya te namaḥ suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hi ajitāya ca vara dāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane namaḥ ca indriya patrāṇām lelihānāya sragviṇe viśvāya viśvarūpāya viśvatas śirase namaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādāya rudrāya apratimāya ca namaḥ siddhāya medhyāya iṣṭāya ijyā parasmai ca su vīrāya su ghorāya akṣobhya kṣobhaṇāya ca su prajāya sumedhāya dīptāya bhāskarāya ca namaḥ buddhāya śuddhāya vistṛtāya matāya ca namaḥ sthūlāya sūkṣmāya dṛśya adṛśyāya sarvaśas namaḥ te vakra keśāya ūru vakṣaḥ śikhāya ca virupa akṣāya liṅgāya piṅgalāya mahā ojase vṛṣṭi ghnāya namaḥ ca eva namaḥ saumya īkṣaṇāya ca namaḥ dhūmrāya śvetāya kṛṣṇāya lohitāya ca piśitāya piśaṅgāya pītāya ca niṣaṅgiṇe namaḥ te saviśeṣāya nirviśeṣāya vai namaḥ namaḥ pūjyāya upajīvyāya vai namaḥ namaḥ kṣemyāya vṛddhāya vatsalāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ bhūtāya satyāya satya asatyāya vai namaḥ mahā saṃdhyā abhra varṇāya cāru dīptāya dīkṣiṇe apramāṇāya sarvāya avyayāya amarāya ca namaḥ rūpāya gandhāya śāśvatāya akṣatāya ca purastāt bṛṃhate ca eva vibhrāntāya kṛtāya ca tarkya atarkya śarīrāya baline raṃhasāya ca sikatyāya pravāhyāya sthitāya prasṛtāya ca te kulālāya namaḥ te śaśi khaṇḍine cekitānāya tuṣṭāya namaḥ te nihitāya ca namaḥ kṣāntāya dāntāya vajra saṃhananāya ca rakṣaḥ ghnāya viṣa ghnāya śitikaṇṭha ūrdhva manyave lelihāya kṛtāntāya tigma āyudha dharāya ca anāmayāya sarvāya mahākālāya vai namaḥ praṇava praṇava īśāya bhaga netra antakāya ca mṛgavyādhāya dakṣāya dakṣa yajña antakāya ca sarva bhūta ātma bhūtāya sarva īśa ati śayāya ca pūṣa danta vināśāya bhaga netra antakāya ca kāma dāya variṣṭhāya kāma aṅga dahanāya ca daityānām antaka īśāya daitya āktanda karāya ca hima ghnāya ca tīkṣṇāya ārdra carma dharāya ca śmaśāna rati nityāya namaḥ astu ulmuka dhārīṇe namaḥ te prāṇa pālāya muṇḍa mālā dharāya ca prahīṇa śokaiḥ vividhaiḥ bhūtaiḥ parivṛtāya ca nara nārī śarīrāya devyāḥ priya karāya ca jaṭine muṇḍine ca eva vyāla yajña upavītine namaḥ astu nṛtya śīlāya upanṛtya priyāya ca manyave gīta śīlāya munibhiḥ gāyate namaḥ tigmāya apriyāya priyāya ca vibhīṣaṇāya bhīṣmāya bhaga pramathanāya ca siddha saṃgha anugītāya mahābhāgāya vai namaḥ namaḥ mukta aṭṭahāsāya kṣveḍita āsphoṭitāya ca namaḥ mṛḍāya śvasate dhāvate adhiṣṭhite namaḥ valgate krīḍate ca eva lamba udara śarīriṇe namaḥ akṛtyāya kṛtyāya muṇḍāya kīkaṭāya ca namaḥ unmatta dehāya kiṅkiṇīkāya vai namaḥ namaḥ vikṛta veṣāya krūrāya amarṣaṇāya ca aprameyāya goptre ca dīptāya anirguṇāya ca vāma priyāya vāmāya cūḍāmaṇi dharāya ca sarveṣām siddhi yogānām adhiṣṭhānam tava udaram madhye antarikṣam vistīrṇam tārā gaṇa vibhūṣitam svāteḥ pathaḥ iva ābhāti śrīmān hāraḥ tava urasi diśaḥ daśa bhujāḥ tubhyam keyūra aṅgada bhūṣitāḥ vistīrṇa pariṇāhaḥ ca nīlāñjana caya upamaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ te śobhate śrīmān hemasūtra vibhūṣitaḥ daṃṣṭra karālam durdharṣam anaupamyam mukham tathā padma mālā kṛta uṣṇīṣam śiraḥ dyauḥ śobhate adhikam akṣara antara niṣpandāt guṇān etān viduḥ budhāḥ pureśayaḥ guhā vāsī khecaraḥ rajanīcaraḥ haya śīrṣā payaḥ dhātā vidhātā bhūtabhāvanaḥ bṛhat rathaḥ bhīma karmā bṛhat kīrtiḥ dhanañjayaḥ ghaṇṭā priyaḥ dhvajī chatrī pinākī dhvaji vipatiḥ kavacī pāṭṭiśī khaṅgī dhanuḥ hastaḥ paraśvadhī tvām prasādya purā asmābhiḥ dviṣantaḥ nihatāḥ yudhi sadā arṇava ambhaḥ tvam piban api na tṛpyase krodha ākāraḥ prasanna ātmā kāma daḥ kāmagaḥ priyaḥ brahmacāri ca agādhaḥ ca brahmaṇyaḥ śiṣṭa pūjitaḥ devānām akṣayaḥ kośaḥ tvayā yajñaḥ prakalpitaḥ bhavān īśaḥ anādimān tvam ca sarva lokānām tvam brahma kartā ādisargaḥ sāṃkhyāḥ prakṛtyāḥ paramam tvām viditvā kṣīṇa dhyānāḥ tvām amṛtyum viśanti yogāḥ ca tvām dhyāyinaḥ nitya siddham jñātam vā yogān saṃtyajante punar tān te māhātmyam apārasya mahātmanaḥ uvāca śrāvayet vā dvijān vidvān śṛṇuyāt vā samāhitaḥ aśvamedha ayutam kṛtvā yat phalam tat avāpnuyāt pāpa ācāraḥ api yaḥ martyaḥ śṛṇuyāt śiva saṃnidhau śrāddhe vā daivike kārye yajñe vā avabhṛtha antike iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge brahmaviṣṇustutiḥ nāma ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atyanta avanatau dṛṣṭvā madhu piṅga āyata īkṣaṇaḥ umāpatiḥ virūpākṣaḥ dakṣa yajña vināśanaḥ pinākī khaṇḍaparaśuḥ su prītaḥ tu trilocanaḥ tatas sa bhagavān devaḥ śrutvā vāc amṛtam tayoḥ jānan api mahādevaḥ kriḍā pūrvam atha abravīt asmin ghore mahā plave tau ūcatuḥ mahātmanau saṃnirīkṣya parasparam vibho rudra mahāmāyaḥ icchayā vām kṛtau tvayā uvāca bhagavān devaḥ madhuram ślakṣṇayā girā bho bho hiraṇya garbha tvām tvām ca kṛṣṇa bravīmi aham prītaḥ aham anayā bhaktyā śāśvata akṣara yuktayā yuvābhyām kim dadāmi adya varāṇām varam īpsitam atha uvāca mahābhāgaḥ viṣṇuḥ bhavam idam vacaḥ tat evam svasti te vatsa gamiṣyāmi ambuja īkṣaṇa evam uktvā tu bhagavant brahmāṇam ca api śaṃkaraḥ anugṛhya aspṛśat devaḥ brahmānam parameśvaraḥ ca prāha hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam evam uktvā tu bhagavant tatas ntardhānam īśvaraḥ avāpya saṃjñām govindāt padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ prajāḥ sraṣṭu manāḥ cakre tapaḥ ugram pitāmahaḥ tatas dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhāt krodhaḥ hi ajāyata krodha āviṣṭasya netrābhyām prāpatan aśru bindavaḥ mahābhāgāḥ mahā sattvāḥ svastikaiḥ api alaṅkṛtāḥ prakīrṇa keśāḥ sarpāḥ te prādurbhūtāḥ mahā viṣāḥ sarpān tān agrajān dṛṣṭvā brahmā ātmānam anindayat loka vaināśikā jajñe ādāḥ veve prajā mama tasya tīvrā abhavat mūrcchā krodha amarṣa samudbhavā mūrchā abhiparitāpena jahau prāṇān prajāpatiḥ tasya apratima vīryasya dehāt kāruṇya pūrvakam ye rudrāḥ te khalu prāṇāḥ ye prāṇāḥ te tad ātmakāḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇavatām jñeyāḥ sarva bhūteṣu avasthitāḥ prāṇān tasya dadau bhūyas triśūlī nīlalohitaḥ praṇamya saṃsthitaḥ apaśyat gāyatryā viśvam īśvaram sarva loka mayam devam dṛṣṭvā stutvā pitāmahaḥ uvāca vacanam śarvam sadya ādi tvam katham vibho iti śrī laṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge rudrotpattivarṇanam nāma dvāviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca brahmarūpī prabodha artham brahmānam prāha sa smitam śveta uṣṇīṣaḥ śveta mālyaḥ śveta ambara dharaḥ sitaḥ śveta asthiḥ śveta romā ca śveta asṛj śveta lohitaḥ mad prasūtā ca deveśī śvetāṅgā śvetalohitā śveta varṇā tadā hi āsīt gāyatrī brahma saṃjñitā vijñātaḥ svena tapasā sadyojāta tvam āgataḥ tasmāt guhya tvam āpannam ye vetsyām dvijātayaḥ yadā ca eva punar tu āsīt lohitaḥ nāma nāma taḥ tadā lohita māṃsa asthi lohita kṣīra sambhavā lohita akṣī stanavatī gāyatrī gauḥ prakīrtitā ca mahā sattva tvayā aham niyata ātmanā tatas ca vāmadeva iti khyātim yātaḥ asmi bhū tale ye ca api vāmadeva tvām jñāsyanti iha dvijātayaḥ mad prasūtā ca deveśī pītāṅgī pītalohitā pīta varṇā tadā hi asīt gāyatrī brahma saṃjñitā yasmāt aham taiḥ vijñātaḥ yoga tatpara mānasaiḥ tatra tatpuruṣa tvena vijñātaḥ aham tvayā punar ye mām rudram ca rudrāṇīm gāyatrīm vedamātaram tapasā yuktāḥ vimalāḥ brahma saṃgatāḥ yadā aham punar eva āsam kṛṣṇa varṇaḥ bhayānakaḥ mad kṛtena ca varṇena saṃkalpaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ucyate tatra aham kāla saṃkāśaḥ kālaḥ loka prakālakaḥ mad prasūtā ca gāyatrī kṛṣṇa aṅgā kṛṣṇa lohitā tadā āsīt brahma saṃjñitā teṣām aghoraḥ śāntaḥ ca bhaviṣyāmi aham avyayaḥ tadā api aham tvayā jñātaḥ parameṇa samādhinā viśva rūpā ca saṃvṛttā gāyatrī loka dhāriṇī tasmin viśva tvam āpannam ye mām vetsyānti bhū tale teṣām śivaḥ ca saumyaḥ ca bhaviṣyāmi sadā eva hi yasmāt ca viśvarūpaḥ vai kalpaḥ ayam samudāhṛtaḥ ṣaṣ rūpā tathā ca iyam sāvitrī samudāhṛtā sarvarūpā tathā ca ime saṃvṛttāḥ mama putrakāḥ catvāraḥ te mayā khyātāḥ putra vai loka saṃmatāḥ yasmāt ca sarva vaṇa tvam prajānām ca bhaviṣyati mokṣaḥ dharmaḥ tathā arthaḥ ca kāmaḥ ca iti catuṣṭayam bhūta grāmāḥ ca catvāraḥ āśramāḥ ca tathā eva ca dharmasya pādāḥ catvāraḥ catvāraḥ mama putrakāḥ aṣṭa akṣara sthitaḥ lokaḥ sthānesthāne tat akṣaram bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar mahaḥ ca eva pādāḥ catvāraḥ eva ca viṣṇu lokaḥ smṛtam sthānam punarāvṛtti durlabham rudra lokaḥ smṛtaḥ tasmāt padam tat yoginām śubham nirmamāḥ nirahaṃkārāḥ kāma krodha vi virjitāḥ drakṣyanti tat dvijāḥ yuktāḥ dhyāna tatpara mānasāḥ yasmāt catuṣpadā hi eṣā tvayā dṛṣṭā sarasvatī pāda antam viṣṇu lokam vai kaumāram śāntam uttamam aumam māheśvaram ca eva tasmāt dṛṣṭā catuṣpadā tasmāt tu paśavaḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti catuṣpadāḥ tatas ca eṣām bhaviṣyanti catvāraḥ te payodharāḥ jīvaḥ prāṇabhṛtām brahman punar pīta stanāḥ smṛtāḥ tasmāt soma mayam ca eva amṛtam jīva saṃjñitam catuṣpādāḥ bhaviṣyanti śveta tvam ca asya tena tat yasmāt ca eva kriyā bhūtvā dvipadā ca maheśvarī dṛṣṭā punar tathā eva eṣā sāvitrī loka bhāvinī tasmāt ca dvipadāḥ sarve dvi stanāḥ ca narāḥ śubhāḥ tasmāt ca iyam ajā bhūtvā sarva varṇā maheśvarī yā vai dṛṣṭā mahā sattvā sarva bhūta dharā tvayā tasmāt ca viśva rūpa tvam prajānām vai bhaviṣyati ajaḥ ca eva mahā tejāḥ viśva rūpaḥ bhaviṣyati amogha retāḥ sarvatra mukhe ca asya hutāśanaḥ tasmāt sarva gataḥ medhyaḥ puśu rūpī hutāśanaḥ tapasā ye mām drakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ rajas tamobhyām nirmuktāḥ tyaktvā mānuṣyakam vapuḥ praṇamya prayataḥ bhūtvā punar āha pitāmahaḥ viśva ātmānam hi sarvam tvām gāyatryāḥ tava ca īśvara tasmāt vidvān hi viśva tvam asyāḥ ca asya mahātmanaḥ sa yāti brahma sāyujyam vacanāt brahyaṇaḥ prabhoḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca punar praṇamya deveśam rudram āha prajāpatiḥ kasyām vā yuga saṃbhūtyām drakṣyanti iha dvajatayaḥ namaḥ te vai mahādeva śakyaḥ draṣṭum dvijātibhiḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā śarvaḥ saṃprekṣya tam puras smayan prāha mahādevaḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāmasam bhavaḥ śrī bhagavant uvāca na śakyam mānavaiḥ draṣṭum ṛte dhyānāt aham tu iha anugraha artham lokānām brāhmaṇānām hitāya ca tadā aham brāhmaṇa arthāya kalau tasmin yuga antike bhaviṣyāmi śikhā yuktaḥ śvetaḥ nāma mahā muniḥ tatra śiṣyāḥ śikhā yuktāḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā mama śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaḥ ca eva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ catvāraḥ tu mahātmānaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ tatas te brahma bhūyiṣṭhāḥ dṛṣṭvā brahma gatim parām mad sa mīpam gamiṣyanti dhyāna yoga parāyaṇāḥ tadā loka hita arthāya sutāraḥ nāma nāmnaḥ bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin śiṣya anugraha kāmyayā tatra api mama te śiṣyāḥ nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ dundubhiḥ śatarūpaḥ ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumant tadā prāpya yogam tathā dhyānam sthāpya brahma ca bhū tale tṛtīye dvāpare ca eva yadā vyāsaḥ tu bhārgavaḥ vikośaḥ ca vikeśaḥ ca vipāśaḥ śāpanāśanaḥ caturthe dvāpare ca eva yadā vyāsaḥ aṅgirāḥ smṛtaḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi suhotraḥ nāma nāmataḥ tatra api mama te putrāḥ catvāraḥ api tapodhanāḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ bhaviṣyanti yoga ātmānaḥ dṛḍha vratāḥ prāpya yoga gatim sūkṣmām vimalāḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ tadā ca api bhaviṣyāmi kaṅkaḥ nāma mahā tapāḥ anugraha artham lokānām yoga ātmā eka kalā gatiḥ catvāraḥ tu mahābhāgāḥ vimalāḥ śuddha yonayaḥ śiṣyāḥ mama bhaviṣyanti yoga ātmānaḥ dṛḍha vratāḥ vibhuḥ sanatkumāraḥ ca nirmamāḥ nirahaṃkṛtāḥ parīvarte punar ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyuḥ vyāsaḥ yadā vibhuḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi logākṣīḥ nāma nāmataḥ tatra api mama te śiṣyāḥ yoga ātmānāḥ dṛḍha vratāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahābhāgāḥ catvāraḥ loka saṃmatāḥ sudhāmā virajāḥ ca eva śaṅkhapād rajaḥ eva ca yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ sarve vai dagdha kilbiṣāḥ mahā tejāḥ prathitaḥ pūrva janmani jaigīṣavyaḥ vibhuḥ khyātaḥ sarveṣām yoginām varaḥ sārasvataḥ ca meghaḥ ca megha vāhaḥ su vāhanaḥ te api tena eva mārgeṇa dhyāna yoga parāyaṇāḥ gamiṣyānti mahātmānaḥ rudra lokam nirāmayam vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṣṭame vyāsaḥ parīvarte bhaviṣyati yadā tadā bhaviṣyāmi nāmnā aham dadhivāhanaḥ tatra api mama te putrāḥ yoga ātmānaḥ dṛḍha vratāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahā yogāḥ yeṣām na asti samaḥ bhuvī kapilaḥ ca āsuriḥ ca eva tathā pañcaśikhaḥ muniḥ bāṣkalaḥ ca mahā yogī dharma ātmānaḥ mahā ojasaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam jñāninaḥ dagdha akilbiṣāḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi ṛṣabhaḥ nāma nāmataḥ parāśaraḥ ca gargaḥ ca bhārgava aṅgirasau tadā bhaviṣyanti mahātmānaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ sarve tapaḥ bala utkṛṣṭāḥ śāpa anugraha kovidāḥ daśame dvāpare vyāsaḥ tripād vai nāma nāmnaḥ yadā bhaviṣyate vipraḥ tadā aham bhavitā muniḥ nāmnā bhṛgoḥ tu śikharam prathitam deva pūjitam tatra api mama te putrāḥ bhaviṣyanti dṛḍha vratāḥ yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ tapaḥ yoga samanvitāḥ rudra lokam gamiṣyanti tapasā dagdha kilbiṣāḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi gaṅgādvāre kalau tathā ugraḥ nāma mahā tejāḥ sarva lokeṣu viśrutaḥ lambodaraḥ ca lambākṣaḥ lambakeśaḥ pralambakaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokam gatāḥ hi te dvādaśe parivarte tu śatatejāḥ yadā muniḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi kalau iha yuga antike haitukam vanam āsādya atriḥ nāmnā pariśrutaḥ tatra api mama te putrāḥ bhasma snāna anulepanāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahā yogāḥ rudra loka parāyaṇāḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokam gatāḥ hi te dharmaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ nāma vyāsaḥ tu bhavitā yadā tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi vāliḥ nāma mahā muniḥ sudhāmā kāśyapaḥ ca eva vāsiṣṭhaḥ virajāḥ ta thā prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokam gatāḥ hi te tatra api punar eva aham bhaviṣyāmi yuga antike vaṃśe tu aṅgirasām śreṣṭhe gautamaḥ nāma nāmataḥ bhaviṣyati mahā puṇyam gautamam nāma tat vanam atriḥ devasadaḥ ca eva śravaṇaḥ atha śraviṣṭhakaḥ yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ sarve yoga samanvitāḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokāya te gatāḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi nāmnā vedaśirāḥ dvijaḥ bhaviṣyati mahā vīryam vedaśīrṣaḥ ca parvataḥ himavat pṛṣṭham āsādya sarasvatyām naga uttame kuṇiḥ ca kuṇibāhuḥ
