ca kuśarīraḥ kunetra kaḥ yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ sarve te div ūrdhvaretasaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokāya te gatāḥ vyāsaḥ yuge ṣoḍaśe tu yadā devaḥ bhaviṣyati tatra yoga pradānāya bhaktānām ca yata ātmanām tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi gokarṇaḥ nāma nāmataḥ bhaviṣyati su puṇyam ca gokarṇam nāma tat vanam kāśyapaḥ hi uśanāḥ ca eva cyavanaḥ utha bṛhaspatiḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam gantāraḥ rudram eva hi yadā bhaviṣyati vyāsaḥ nāmnā devakṛtam jayaḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi guhāvāsī iti nāmataḥ siddha kṣetram mahā puṇyam bhaviṣyati mahālayam tatra api mama te putrāḥ yoga jñāḥ brahma vādinaḥ bhaviṣyanti mahātmānaḥ nirmamāḥ nirahaṅkṛtāḥ teṣām śata sahasram tu śiṣyāṇām dhyāna yoginām bhaviṣyanti tadā kāle sarve te dhyāna yuñjakāḥ yoga abhyāsa ratāḥ ca eva hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram mahālaye padam nyastam dṛṣṭvā yānti śivam padam dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya vimalāḥ śuddha buddhayaḥ mama prasādāt yāsyanti rudra lokam gata jvarāḥ gatvā mahālayam puṇyam dṛṣṭvā māheśvaram padam tīrṇaḥ tārayate jantuḥ daśa pūrvān daśa uttarān mānam ekaviṃśam tu tārayitvā mahālaye mama prasādāt yāsyanti rudra lokam gata jvarāḥ tadā ṛtañjayaḥ nāma vyāsaḥ tu bhavitā muniḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi śikhaṇḍi nāma nāmnaḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ vanam ca api yatra siddha niṣevitam vācaśravāḥ ṛcakiḥ ca śyāvāśvaḥ ca yatīśvaraḥ yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ sarve te vedapāragāḥ prapya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokāya saṃvṛtāḥ vyāsaḥ tu bhavitā nāmnā bharadvājaḥ mahā muniḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi jaṭāmālī ca nāmataḥ hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ lokākṣī kuthumī tathā īśvarāḥ yoga dharmāṇaḥ sarve te hi ūrdhvaretasaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokāya saṃsthitāḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi aṭṭahāsaḥ tu nāmataḥ aṭṭahāsa priyāḥ ca eva bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ tatra eva himavat pṛṣṭhe aṭṭahāsaḥ mahā giriḥ deva dānavam yakṣa indra siddhi acāraṇa sevitaḥ yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ dhyāyinaḥ niyata vratāḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokāya te gatāḥ vācaśravāḥ smṛtaḥ vyāsaḥ yadā saḥ ṛṣi sattamaḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi dārukaḥ nāma nāmnaḥ tasmāt bhaviṣyate puṇyam devadāru vanam śubham plakṣaḥ dārbhāyaṇiḥ ca eva ketumant gautamaḥ tathā yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ niyatāḥ ūrdhvaretasaḥ naiṣṭhikam vratam āsthāya rudra lokāya te gatāḥ dvāviṃśe parivarte tu vyāsaḥ śuṣmāyaṇaḥ yadā tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi vārāṇasyām mahā muniḥ nāmnā vai lāṅgalī bhīmaḥ yatra devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ tatra api mama te putrāḥ bhaviṣyanti su dhārmikāḥ bhallaviḥ madhupiṅgaḥ ca śvetaketuḥ kuśaḥ tathā prāpya māheśvaram yogam te api dhyāna parāyaṇāḥ vimalāḥ brahma bhūyiṣṭhāḥ rudra lokāya saṃsthitāḥ parivarte trayoviṃśe tṛṇabinduḥ yadā muniḥ vyāsaḥ hi bhavitā brahman tadā aham bhavitā punar śvetaḥ nāma mahā kāyaḥ muni putraḥ tu dhārmikaḥ tatra api mama te śiṣyāḥ bhaviṣyanti tapasvinaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokāya te gataḥ parivarte caturviṃśe vyāsaḥ ṛkṣaḥ yadā vibho śūlī nāma mahā yogī naimiṣe deva vandite tatra api mama te śiṣyāḥ bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ śālihotra ugniveśaḥ ca nāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ te api tena eva mārgeṇa rudra lokāya saṃsthitāḥ pañcaviṃśe punar prāpte parivarte krama āgate vāsiṣṭhaḥ tu yadā vyāsaḥ śaktiḥ nāmnā bhaviṣyati tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaḥ ca kubhāṇḍaḥ ca pravāhakaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam amṛta tvāya te gatāḥ paḍviṃśe parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ parā śaraḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi sahiṣṇuḥ nāma nāmataḥ tatra api mama te putrāḥ bhaviṣyanti su dhārmikāḥ ulūkaḥ vidyutaḥ ca eva śambūkaḥ hi āśvalāyanaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yugam rudra lokāya te gatāḥ jātūkarṇyaḥ yadā vyāsaḥ bhaviṣyati tapodhanaḥ tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi somaśarmā dvijottamaḥ prabhāsa tīrtham āsādya yoga ātmā yoga viśrutaḥ tatra api mama te śiṣyāḥ bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ akṣapādaḥ kumāraḥ ca ulūkaḥ vatsaḥ eva ca yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ vimalāḥ śuddha buddhayaḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam rudra lokam tatas gatāḥ aṣṭāviṃśe punar prāpte parivarte krama āgate parāśara sutaḥ śrīmān viṣṇuḥ lokapitāmahaḥ yadā bhaviṣyati vyāsaḥ nāmnā dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ tadā ṣaṣṭhena ca aṃśena kṛṣṇaḥ puruṣa sattamaḥ vasudevāt yaduśreṣṭhaḥ vāsudevaḥ bhaviṣyati tadā api aham bhaviṣyāmi yoga ātmā yoga māyayā loka vismayana arthāya brahmacāri śarīrakaḥ śmaśāne mṛtam utsṛṣṭam dṛṣṭvā kāyam anāthakam brāhmaṇānām hita arthāya praviṣṭaḥ yoga māyayā divyām meru guhām puṇyām tvayā sārdham ca viṣṇunā bhaviṣyāmi tadā brahman lakulī nāma nāmnaḥ kāya avatāraḥ iti evam siddha kṣetram ca vai tadā yoga ātmānaḥ mahātmānaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ prāpya māheśvaram yogam vimalāḥ hi ūrdhvaretasaḥ ete pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ liṅga arcana ratāḥ nityam bāhya abhyantarāt sthitāḥ bhaktyā mayi ca yogena dhyāna niṣṭhā jita indriyāḥ saṃsāra bandha cheda artham jñāna mārga prakāśakam svarūpa jñāna siddhi artham yogam pāśupatam mahat yoga mārgāḥ aneke ca jñāna mārgāḥ tu anekaśas na nivṛttim upāyānti vinā pañcākṣarīm kvacid eka aham yaḥ pumān samyak caret pāśupata vratam na sāṃkhye pañcarātre vā na prāpnoti gatim kadā manu ādi kṛṣṇa paryantam aṣṭa āviśan dyuga kramāt tatra śruti samūhānām vibhāgaḥ dharma lakṣaṇaḥ bhaviṣyati tadā kalpe kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ yadā uvāca niśamya evam mahā tejāḥ mahādevena kīrtitam rudra avatāram bhagavant praṇipatya maheśvaram tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ punar prāha ca śaṃkaram uvāca sarve viṣṇu mayāḥ devāḥ sarve viṣṇu mayāḥ gaṇāḥ na hi viṣṇu samā kācid gatiḥ anyā vidhīyate iti evam satatam vedāḥ gāyanti na atra saṃśayaḥ uvāca niśamya vacanam tasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ pūjā prakāraṇam tasmai tam ālokya āha śaṃkaraḥ bhavān nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva śakraḥ sākṣāt sura uttamaḥ munayaḥ ca sadā liṅgam saṃpūjya vidhi pūrvakam svam svam padam vibho prāptāḥ tasmāt saṃpūjayanti te liṅga arcanam vinā niṣṭhā na asti tasmāt janārdanaḥ iti evam uktvā brahmāṇam anugṛhya mabha īśvaraḥ punar saṃprekṣya deveśam tatra eva antaradhīyata tam uddiśya tadā brahmā namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ sraṣṭum tu aśeṣam bhagavant labdha saṃjñaḥ tu śaṃkarāt iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge caturviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham pūjyaḥ mahādevaḥ liṅga mūrtiḥ maheśvaraḥ vaktum arhasi ca naḥ romaharṣaṇa sāṃpratam uvāca devyā pṛṣṭaḥ mahādevaḥ kailāse tām naga ātmajām aṅka sthām āha deveśaḥ liṅga arcana vidhim kramāt tadā pārśve sthitaḥ nandī śālaṅkāyanaka ātmajaḥ śrutvā akhilam purā prāha brahma putrāya suvratāḥ sanatkumārāya śubham liṅga arcana vidhim param tasmāt vyāsaḥ mahā tejāḥ śrutavan śruti saṃmitam snāna yoga upacāram ca yathā śailādeḥ mukhāt śrutavan tat pravakṣyāmi snāna ādyam ca arcana vidhim uvāca atha snāna vidhim vakṣye brāhmaṇānām hitāya ca sarva pāpa haram sākṣāt śivena kathitam purā anena vidhinā snātvā sakṛt pūjya ca śaṅkaram trividham snānam ākhyātam devadevena śaṃbhunā hitāya brāhmaṇa ādyānām caturmukha suta uttama vāruṇam puratas kṛtvā tatas ca āgneyam uttamam mantrasnānam tatas kṛtvā pūjayet parameśvaram bhāva duṣṭaḥ ami asi snātvā bhasmanā ca na śuddhi ati sarit saraḥ taḍāgeṣu sarveṣu āpralayam naraḥ snātvā api bhāva duṣṭaḥ ced na śuvyati na saṃśayaḥ nṛṇām hi citta kamalam prabuddham abhavat yadā prasuptam tamasā jñāna bhānoḥ bhāsā tadā suciḥ mṛd śakṛt ti ca snāna artham bhasitam tathā ādāya tīre niḥkṣipya snāna tīrthe kuśāni ca prakṣālya ācamya pādau ca malam dehāt viśodhya ca uddhṛtā asi iti mantreṇa punar deham viśodhayet mṛdā ādāya tatas ca anyat vastram strātvā hi anulbaṇam gandha dvārām durādharṣām iti mantreṇa mantra vid śukla vastra parīdhānaḥ bhūtvā snānam samācaret sarva pāpa viśuddhi artham āvāhya varuṇam tathā tad toye bhānu soma agni maṇḍalam ca smaret vaśī śṛṅgeṇa parṇa puṭakaiḥ pālaśaiḥ kṣālitaiḥ tathā tad tad mantra adhidevānām svarūpam ca ṛṣīn smaran evam hi ca abhiṣicya atha sva mūrdhni payasā dvijāḥ dhyāyet ca tryambakam devam hṛdi pañca āsyam aśviram ācamya ācamanam kuryāt sva sūtra uktam samīkṣya ca pavitra hastaḥ su āsīnaḥ śucau deśe yathāvidhi abhyukṣya sa kuśam ca api dakṣiṇena kareṇa tu pradakṣiṇam tatas kuryāt viṃsā pāpa praśāntaye evam saṃkṣepāt proktam snāna ācamaṃnam uttamam sarveṣām brāhmaṇānām tu hita arthe dvijasattamāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge snānavidhiḥ nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ āvāha yet tatas devīm gāyatrīm vedamātaram maheśvarīm pādyam ācamanīyam ca tasyāḥ ca arghyam pradāpayet prāṇāyāma trayam kṛtvā samāsīnaḥ sthite api vā sahasram vā tad ardham vā śatam aṣṭa uttaram tu vā gāyatrīm praṇavena eva trividheṣu ekam ācarat prācyā ālokya abhivandya īśām gāyatrīm vedamātaram kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā prārthayet bhāskaram tathā abhivandya punar sūryam brahmānam ca vidhānāt tathā saurāṇi sūktāni ṛk yajuḥ sāma jāni ca japtvā pradakṣiṇam paścāt tris kṛtvā ca vibhāvasoḥ ātmānam ca antar ātmānam paramātmānam eva ca abhivandya punar sūryam brahmāṇam ca vibhāvasum munīn pitṝn yathānyāyam sva nāmnā āvāhayet tatas sarvān āvā hayāmi iti devān āvāhya sarvatas tarpayet vidhinā paścāt prāc mukhaḥ vā hi udak mukhaḥ devānām puṣpa toyena ṛṣīṇām tu kuśa ambhasā yajña upavīti devānām nivītī ṛṣi tarpaṇam prācīnāvīti vipra idra pitṝṇām tarpayet kramāt ṛṣīn kaniṣṭhā aṅgulinā śrotriyaḥ sarva siddhaye pitṝn tu tarpayot vidvāḥ dākṣiṇa aṅguṣṭhakena tu devayajñam ca mānuṣyam bhūtayajñam tathā eva ca pitṛ yajñam ca pūta ātmā yajña karma parāyaṇaḥ sva śākhā adhyayanam vipra brahmayajñaḥ iti smṛtaḥ sarveṣām eva bhūtānām bali dānam vidhānataḥ sa dārān sarva tattva jñān brāhmaṇān vedapāragān pitṝn uddiśya yat dattam pitṛ yajñaḥ saḥ ucyate evam pañca mahāyajñān kuryāt sarva artha siddhaye sarveṣām śṛṇu yajñānām brahmayajñaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ brahmayajñena tuṣyanti sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ brahmā ca bhagavant viṣṇuḥ śaṃkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ vedāḥ ca pitaraḥ sarve na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yāvat tu adṛṣṭam abhavat uṭajānām chadam naraḥ prācyām udīcyām ca tathā prāñc udīcyām atha api vā prīti artham ca ṛcām viprāḥ tris pītvā plāvya plāvya ca yajuṣām parimṛjya evam dvis prakṣālya ca prīti artham sāmavedānām upaspṛśya ca mūrdhāni spṛśet atharva vedānām netre ca aṅgirasām tathā nāsike brāhmaṇaḥ aṅgānām kṣālya kṣālya ca vāriṇā aṣṭādaśa purāṇānām brahma ādyānām tathā eva ca tathā ca upapurāṇānām saura ādīnām yathākramam puṇyānām itihāsānām śaiva ādīnām tathā eva ca śrotre spṛśet hi tuṣṭi artham hṛd deśyam tu tatas spṛśet kalpa ādīnām tu sarveṣām kalpa vid kalpa vittamāḥ evam ācamya ca āstīrya darbha piñjūli ātmanaḥ kṛtvā pāṇi tale dhīmān ātmanaḥ dakṣiṇa uttaram vidhivat brahmayajñam ca kuryāt sūtrī samāhitaḥ a kṛtvā ca muniḥ pañca mahāyajñān dvijottamaḥ bhuktvā ca sūkarāṇām tu yonau vai jāyate naraḥ brahmayajñāt atha snānam kṛtvā ādau sarvathā ātmanaḥ tīrtham saṃgṛhya vidhivat praviśet śibiram vaśī bahis eva gṛhāt pādau hastau prakṣālya vāriṇā jyotiḥ agniḥ tathā sāyam samyak ca anudite mṛṣā na asti satya samam yasmāt asatyam pātakam ca yat īśānena śiras deśam mukham tatpuruṣeṇa ca uraḥ deśam aghoreṇa guhyam vām eva suvratāḥ sadyena pādau sarva aṅgam praṇavena abhiṣecayet tatas prakṣālayet pādam hastam brahmā vidām varaḥ mantrasnānam tatas kuryāt āpohiṣṭhā ādibhiḥ kramāt puṇyaiḥ ca eva tathā mantraiḥ ṛc yajuḥ samā sambhavaiḥ dvijānām tu hitāya evam kathitam snānam adya te saṃkṣipya yaḥ sakṛt kuryāt saḥ yāti paramam padam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge pañcayajñavidhānam nāma ṣāḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca vakṣyāmi śṛṇu saṃkṣopāt liṅga arcana vidhi kramam vaktum varṣa śatena api na śakyam vistareṇa yat evam snātvā yathānyāyam pūjā sthānam praviśya ca prāṇāyāma trayam kṛtvā dhyāyet devam tryambakam sarva ābharaṇa saṃyuktam citra ambara vibhūṣitam tasya rūpam samāśritya dāhana plāvana ādībhiḥ śaivīm tanum samāḥ sthāya pūjayet palameśvaram sūtre namaḥ śivāya iti chandāṃsi parame śubhe mantrāṇi sūkṣma rūpā ima saṃsthitāni yatas tatas dravyāṇi śodhayet paścāt kṣālana prokṣaṇa ādibhiḥ ca eva pramavena vidhīyate prokṣaṇī ca arghya pātram ca pādya pātram anukramat tathā hi ācamanīya artham kalpitam pātram eva ca sthāpayet vidhinā dhīmān avaguṇṭhya yathāvidhi teṣu teṣu atha sarveṣu kṣipet toyam suśītalam praṇavena kṣipet teṣu dravyāṇi ālokya buddhimān cūṇayitvā yathānyāyam kṣipet ācamanīyake evam sarveṣu pātreṣu dāpayet candanam tathā karpūram ca yathānyāyam puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca kuśa agram akṣatān ca eva yava vrīhi tilāni ca mājya siddhārtha puṣpāṇi bhasitam ca arghya pātrake dāpayet prokṣaṇī pātre bhasitam praṇavena ca nyaset pañcākṣaram ca eva gāyatrīm rudra devatām atha saṃprokṣayet paścāt dravyāṇi praṇavena tu prokṣaṇī pātra saṃsthena īśāna ādyaiḥ ca pañcabhiḥ pārśvatas devadevasya nandīnam mām samarcayet tridaśeśvaram puṣpa mālā dharam saumyam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam uttare ca ātmanaḥ puṇyām bhāryām ca marutām śubhām suyaśām suvratām ca ambā pāda maṇḍana tatparām evam pūjya praviśya antar bhavanam parameṣṭhinaḥ dattvā puṣpa añjalim bhaktyā pañca mūrdhasu pañcabhiḥ skandam vināyakam devīm liṅga śuddhim ca kārayet japtvā sarvāṇi mantrāṇi praṇava ādi namentakam kalpayet āsanam paścāt padma ākhyam praṇavena tat tasya pūrva dalam sākṣāt daṇima āmayam akṣaram laghimā dakṣiṇam ca eva mahimā paścimam tathā prāptiḥ tathā uttaram patram prākāmyam pāvakasya tu īśitvam naiṛtam pattram vaśitvam vāyugocare sarvajña tvam tathā aiśānyam karṇikā somaḥ ucyate somasya adhas tathā sūryaḥ tasya adhas pāvakaḥ svayam mahā ātma trayam tatas ca ūrdhvam tasya ante śiva pīṭhikā sadyojātam prapadyāmi iti āvāhya parameśvaram īśānaḥ sarva vidyānām iti mantreṇa pūjayet pādyam ācamanīyam ca vibhoḥ ca arghyam pradāpayet snāpayet vidhinā rudram gandha candana vāriṇā śuddhim kṛtvā yathānyāyam sita vastreṇa sādhakaḥ kuśa apāmārga karpūra jātipuṣpaka campakaiḥ bhaiḥ āpūrya puṣpaiḥ su śubhaiḥ candana ādyaiḥ ca tat jalam suvarṇa kalaśena atha tathā vai rājatena vā tāmreṇa padma patreṇa pālāśena dalena vā mantrāṇi te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarva artha siddhaye yaiḥ liṅgam sakṛt api evam snāpya mucyeta mānavaḥ pavamānena mantra jñāḥ tathā vāmīyakena ca rudreṇa nīlarudreṇa śrī su ktena śubhena ca hotāreṇa atha śirasā artharveṇa śubhena ca śāntyā ca atha punar śāntyā bhāruṇḍena aruṇena ca sāmnā tu bṛhaccandreṇa viṣṇunā virūpākṣeṇa skandena śata ṛgbhiḥ śivaiḥ tathā snāpayet devadeveśam sarva pāpa praśāntaye vastram śivopavītam ca tathā hi ācamanīyakam gandham puṣpam tathā dhūpam dīpam annam krameṇa tu mukuṭam ca śubham channam tathā vai bhūṣaṇāni ca tatas sphaṭika saṃkāśam dave niṣkalam akṣaram kāraṇam sarva devānām sarva loka mayam param ādi madhya anta rahitam bheṣajam bhava rogiṇām dattvā atha puṣpāṇi pādayoḥ tu vikīrya ca pravakṣyāmi liṅga arcanam iha adya te iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge liṅgārcanavidhiḥ nāma saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca āgneyam sauram amṛtam biṃbiṃ bhāvyam tatas upari guṇatrayam ca hṛdaye tathā ca ā tma trayam kramāt tasya upari mahādevam niṣkalam sakala ākṛtim kāntā ardha rūḍha deham ca pūjayet dhyāna vidyayā tasmāt dhyeyam tathā dhyānam yajamānaḥ prayojanam yājyam yajñena yajate yajamānaḥ tu saḥ smṛtaḥ pradhānapuruṣa īśānam yāthātathyam prapadyate iha ṣaḍviśakaḥ dhyeyaḥ dhyātā vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ mahant tathā tu ahaṅkāram tanmātram pañcakam punar pañca eva tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca manaḥ ca pañca bhūtāni śivaḥ ṣaḍviṃśakaḥ tatas hiraṇyagarbham rudraḥ asau janayāmāsa śaṃkaraḥ viśva adhikaḥ ca viśvātmā viśvarūpaḥ iti smṛtaḥ vinā yathā hi pitaram mātaram tanayāḥ tu iha kartā yadi mahādevaḥ paramātmā maheśvaraḥ uvāca kālaḥ karoti sakalam kālam kalayate sadā niṣkalam ca manaḥ sarvam manyate saḥ api niṣkalaḥ vinā ākāśam jagat na eva vinā kṣmām vāyunā vinā tejasā vāriṇā ca eva yajamānam tathā vinā bhānunā śāśinā lokaḥ tasya etāḥ tanavaḥ prabhoḥ sūkṣmam vadanti ṛṣayaḥ yat na vācyam dvijottamāḥ na bhetavyam tathā tasmāt jñātvā ānandam pinākinaḥ namaskāreṇa satatam gauravāt parameṣṭhinaḥ puruṣaḥ vai mahādevaḥ maheśānaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ saṃsāra hetuḥ saṃsāraḥ mokṣa hetuḥ ca nirvṛtiḥ cintā bahuvidhā khyātā sā ekatra parameṣṭhinā su niṣṭhā iti atra kathitā rudram rodrī na saṃśayaḥ pā indrā ca aindre tathā saumyā some nārāyaṇe tathā sūryaḥ vahnau ca sarveṣām sarvatra evam vicārāt sā eva aham sā ham iti evam dvidhā saṃsthāpya bhāvatas bhaktā asau na asti yaḥ tasmāt cintā brāhmī na saṃśayaḥ tyājyam grāhmam alabhyam ca kṛtyam ca akṛtyam eva ca samākhyātam evam abhyarcanam kramāt ābhyantara arcakāḥ pūjyāḥ namaskāra ādibhiḥ tathā virūpāḥ vikṛtāḥ ca api na nindyāḥ brahma vādinaḥ na parīkṣyāḥ vijānatā tasmāt sevyāḥ namaskāryāḥ sadā brahma vidaḥ tathā varṇa āśrama vinirmuktāḥ varṇa āśrama parāyaṇaiḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivārcanatattvasaṃkhyādivarṇanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ idānīm śrotum icchāmi purā dāru vane vibho pravṛttam tat vanasthānām tapasā bhāvitātmanām katham dāru vanam prāptaḥ bhagavān nīlalohitaḥ vikṛtam rūpam āsthāya ca ūrdhvaretāḥ diś ambaraḥ uvāca tasya tat vacanam śrutvā śruti sāra vidām varaḥ śilāda sūnuḥ bhagavān prāha kiṃcid bhavam hasan uvāca tuṣṭi artham devadevasya sa dāra tanaya agnayaḥ tuṣṭaḥ rudraḥ jagannāthaḥ cekitānaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ dhūrjaṭiḥ parameśānaḥ bhagavant nīlalohitaḥ pravṛtti lakṣaṇam jñānam jñātum dāru vanaukasām parīkṣā artham jagannāthāḥ śraddhayā krīḍayā ca saḥ nivṛtti lakṣaṇa jñāna pratiṣṭhā artham ca śaṅkaraḥ devadāru vana sthānām pravṛtti jñāna cetasām vikṛtam rūpam āsthāya digvāsāḥ viṣama īkṣaṇaḥ mugdhaḥ dvi hastaḥ kṛṣṇa aṅgaḥ divyam dāru vanam yayau bhra vilāsam ca gānam ca cakāra atīva sundaraḥ saṃprokṣya nārī vṛndam vai muhur muhur anaṅga hā aṃnaga vṛddhim akarot atīva madhura ākṛtiḥ vane tam puruṣam dṛṣṭvā vikṛtam nīla lohitam striyaḥ pativratāḥ ca api tam eva anvayuḥ ādarāt vana uṭaja dvāra gatāḥ ca nāryaḥ visrasta vastra ābharaṇāḥ viceṣṭāḥ dṛṣṭvā kāścid bhavam nāryaḥ mada ghūrṇita locanāḥ hyaḥ tāḥ ca api bhrū vilāsam pracakrire atha dṛṣṭvā aparāḥ nāryaḥ kiñcid prahasita ānanāḥ kiṃcid visrasta vasanāḥ srasta kāñcī guṇāḥ jaguḥ kāścid tadā tam vipine tu dṛṣṭvā vipra aṅganāḥ srasta nava aṃśukam vā svān svān vicitrān valayān pravidhya mada anvitāḥ bandhu janān ca jagmuḥ kācid tadā tam na viveda dṛṣṭvā vivāsanā srasta mahā aṃśukā ca śākhā vicitrān viṭapān prasiddhān mada anvitāḥ bandhu janān tathā anyāḥ kāścid jaguḥ tam nanṛtiḥ nipetuḥ ca dharā tale niṣeduḥ gaja vat ca anyā provāca dvija puṃgavāḥ anyonyam sa smitam prekṣya ca āliliṅguḥ samantataḥ kaḥ bhavān iti ca āhuḥ tam āsyatām iti ca aparāḥ viparitāḥ nipetuḥ vai visrasta aṃśuka mūrdhajāḥ pativratāḥ pitīnām tu saṃnidhau bhava māyayā dṛṣṭvā śrutvā bhavaḥ tāsām ceṣṭā vākyāni ca avyayaḥ śubham vā api aśubham vā api na uktavan parameśvaraḥ dṛṣṭvā nārī kulam viprāḥ tathābhūtam ca śaṃkaram atīva paruṣam vākyam jajalpuḥ te muni īśvarāḥ tapāṃsi teṣām sarveṣām pratyāhanyanta śaṅkare yathā āditya prakāśeṇa tārakāḥ nabhasi sthitāḥ śrūyate ṛṣi śāpena brahmaṇaḥ tu mahātmanaḥ samṛddha śreyasām yoniḥ yajñāḥ vai nāśam āptavan bhṛgoḥ api ca śāpena viṣṇuḥ parama vīryavān prādurbhāvān daśa prāptaḥ duḥkhitaḥ ca sadā kṛtaḥ indrasya api ca dharma jña chinnam sa vṛṣaṇam purā ṛṣiṇā gautamena urvyām kruddhena vinipātitam garbha vāsaḥ vasūnām ca śāpena vihitaḥ tathā bhīṣām ca eva śāpena nahuṣaḥ sarpa tām gataḥ kṣīrodaḥ ca samudra usau nivāsaḥ sarvadā hareḥ dvitīyaḥ ca amṛta ādhāraḥ hi apeyaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ avimukteśvaram prāpya vārāṇasyām janārdanaḥ bhṛṣṭvā īśam devadevam tryambakam śraddhayā parayā yuktaḥ deha āśleṣa amṛtena vai niṣiktena svayam devaḥ kṣīreṇa madhusūdanaḥ kṣīrodam pūrvavat cakrenivāsam ca ātmanaḥ prabhuḥ dharmaḥ ca eva tathā śaptaḥ māṇḍavyena mahātmanā vṛṣṇayaḥ ca eva kṛṣṇena durvāsa ādyaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ rāghavaḥ sa anujaḥ śca api durvāsena mahātmanā śrīvatsaḥ ca muneḥ pāda patanāt tasya dhīmataḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ viprāṇām vaśam āgatāḥ te api dāru vanāt tasmāt prātar saṃvigna mānasāḥ pitāmaham mahātmānam āsīnam parama āsane gatvā vijñāpayāmāsuḥ pravṛttam akhilam vibhoḥ śubhe dāru vane tasmin munayaḥ kṣīṇa cetasaḥ saḥ upi saṃcintya manasā kṣaṇāt eva pitāmahaḥ teṣām pravṛttam akhilam puṇye dāru vane purā utthāya prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā praṇipatya bhavāya ca uvāca sa tvaram brahmā munīn dāru vana ālayān vṛthak kṛtam yatas viprāḥ yuṣmābhiḥ bhāgya varjitaiḥ yaḥ tu dāru vane tasmin liṅgī dṛṣṭaḥ api aliṅgibhiḥ yuṣmābhiḥ vikṛta ākāraḥ saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ hirūpāḥ ca surūpāḥ ca malināḥ ca api apaṇḍitāḥ purā bhūmau dvijāgryeṇa jitāḥ hi atithi pūjayā anyathā nā asti saṃtartum gṛhasthaiḥ ca dvijottamaiḥ tyaktvā ca atithi pūjām tām ātmanaḥ bhuvi śodhanam gṛhasthaḥ api purā jetum sudarśanaḥ iti śrutaḥ pratijñām akarot jāyām bhāryām āha pativratām tvayā vai na avamantvāya gṛhe hi atithayaḥ sadā sarve eva svayam sākṣāt atithiḥ yat pinākadhṛk evam uktvā atha saṃtaptā vivaśā sā pativratā tasyāḥ tat vacanam śrutvā punar prāha sudarśanaḥ deyam sarvam śivāya ārye śivaḥ eva atithiḥ svayam tasmāt sarve pūjanīyāḥ sarve api atithayaḥ sadā evam uktā tadā bhartrā bhāryā tasya pativratā śeṣām iva ājñām ādāya mūrdhnā sā prācarat tadā parīkṣitum tathā śraddhām tayoḥ sākṣāt dvijottamāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā ācārca yāmāsa sa argha ādyaiḥ anaghā dvijam saṃpūjitaḥ tayā tām tu prāha dharmaḥ dvijaḥ svayam bhadre kutas patiḥ dhīmān tava bhartā sudarśanaḥ sā ca lajjā āvṛtā nārī smarantī kathitam purā niveditum kila ātmānam tasmai pateḥ iha ājñayā etasmin antare bhartā tasyāḥ nāryāḥ sudarśanaḥ gṛha dvāram gataḥ dhīmān tām uvāca mahā muniḥ sudarśanaḥ tatas prāha su prahṛṣṭaḥ dvijottamaḥ bhuṅkṣya ca enām yata ākāmam gamiṣya iham dvijottama hṛṣṭaḥ atha darśayām āsa sva ātmānam dharmarāj svayam eṣā na bhuktā vipra indraiḥ manasā api su śobhanā mayā ca eṣā na saṃdehaḥ śraddhām jñātum iha āgataḥ tasmāt tathā pūjanīyāḥ sarve hi atithayaḥ sadā bahunā atra kim uktena bhāgya hīnāḥ dvijottamāḥ tam eva śaraṇam tūrṇam gantum arhatha śaṃkaram tasya tat vacanam śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ brāhmaṇa ṛṣabhāḥ brahmānam abhivandya ārtāḥ procuḥ ākulita īkṣaṇāḥ ūcuḥ na apekṣitam mahābhāga jīvitam vikṛtāḥ striyaḥ śaptaḥ ca sarvagaḥ śūlī pinākī nīlalohitaḥ ajñānāt śāpa jā śaktiḥ kuṇṭhita āsya nirīkṣaṇāt draṣṭum vai devadeveśam ugram bhīmam kapardinam uvāca ādau vedān adhītya eva śraddhayā ca guroḥ sadā dvijottamāḥ grahaṇa antam hi vā vidvān atha dvādaśa vārṣikam snātvā āhṛtya ca dārān vai putrān utpādya suvratān agniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ ca iṣṭvā yajñaiḥ yajñeśvaram vibhum pūjayet paramātmānam prāpya araṇyam vibhāvasau muniḥ dvādaśa varṣam vā varṣa mātram atha api vā pakṣa dvādaśakam vā api dina dvādaśakam tu vā kṣīra bhuj saṃyutaḥ śāntaḥ sarvān saṃpūjayet surān yajet evam juhuyāt agnau yajña pātrāṇi mantratas sva dhanam sakalam ca eva brāhmaṇebyaḥ viśaṅkayā nikṛtya keśān sa śikhān uvapītam visṛjya ca pañcabhiḥ juhuyāt apsu bhūḥ svāhā iti vicakṣaṇaḥ vratena anaśanena api toya vṛttyā api vā punar parṇa vṛttyā payaḥ vṛttyā phala vṛttyā api vā yatiḥ evam jīvanmṛtaḥ no ced ṣaṣ māsāt vatsarāt tu vā prasthāna ādikam āyāsam sva dehasya ceret yatiḥ mahā śiva sāyujyam āpnoti karmaṇā api evam ācaran iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ekonatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca evam uktāḥ tadā tena brahmaṇā brāhmaṇa ṣabhāḥ śvetasya ca kathām puṇyā mapṛcchan parama ṛṣayaḥ uvāca śvetaḥ nāma muniḥ śrīmān gata āyūḥ giri gahvare rudrādhyāyena puṇyena namaste ityādinā dvijāḥ tatas kālaḥ mahā tejāḥ kāla prāptam dvijottamam śvetaḥ api dṛṣṭvā tam kālam kāla prāptaḥ api śaṃkaram pūjayāmāsa puṇya ātmā tryambakam anusmaran kim kariṣyati me mṛtyuḥ mṛtyoḥ mṛtyuḥ aham yatas tam dṛṣṭvā sa smitam prāha śvetam loka bhayaṃkaraḥ mā ehi ehi śvetā ca anena vidhinā kim phalam tava rudraḥ vā bhagavant viṣṇuḥ brahmā vā jagat īśvaraḥ netum yasya utthitaḥ ca aham yama lokam kṣaṇena vai tam prāha ca mahādevam kālam saṃprekṣya vai dṛśā netreṇa bāṣpa miśreṇa saṃbhrāntena samākulaḥ uvāca tvayā kim kāla no nāthaḥ ca asti ced vi vṛṣadhvajaḥ atīva bhava bhaktānām madvidhānām mahātmanām tatas niśamya kupitaḥ tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ bhayaṅkaraḥ śrutvā śvetasya tat vākyam pāśa hastaḥ bhaya āvahaḥ siṃhanādam mahat kṛtvā ca āsphāṭya ca muhur muhur babandha ca munim kālaḥ kāla prāptam tam āha ca mayā baddhaḥ asi viprarṣe śvetam netum yama ālayam niśceṣṭaḥ asau mahādevaḥ katham pūjyaḥ maheśvaraḥ tatas sadāśivaḥ svayam dvijam nihantum āgatam tryambakaḥ ambayā samam sa nandinā gaṇeśvaraiḥ sasarja jīvitam kṣaṇāt bhavam nirīkṣya vai bhayāt papāta ca āśu vai balī muneḥ tu saṃnidhau dvijāḥ nirīkṣaṇena vai mṛtam bhavasya vipra puṃgavāḥ vineduḥ uccam īśvarāḥ sura īśvarāḥ maheśvaram praṇemuḥ aṃbikām umām muni īśvarāḥ tu harṣitāḥ su śobhanam su śītalam su puṣpa varṣam ambarāt aho nirīkṣya ca antakam mṛtam tadā su vismitaḥ śilā aśana ātmajaḥ avyayam śivam praṇamya śaṃkaram uvāca bāla dhīḥ mṛtaḥ prasīda ca iti vai muneḥ maheśvaram maheśvarasya ca anugaḥ gaṇeśvaraḥ kṣaṇāt gūḍha śarīram hi dhvasta dṛṣṭvā antakam kṣaṇāt tasmāt mṛtyuṃjayam ca eva bhaktyā dvijāḥ uvāca evam uktāḥ tadā tena brahmaṇā brahma vādinaḥ uvāca na dānena muni śreṣṭhāḥ tapasā ca na vidyayā prasāde na eva sā bhaktiḥ śive parama kāraṇe sa dāra tanayāḥ śrāntāḥ praṇemuḥ ca pitāmaham tasmāt pāśupatā bhaktiḥ dharma kāma artha siddhi dā kṣayam jaghāna pādena vajra asthi tvam ca labdhavān śvetena api gatena āsyam mṛtyoḥ muni vareṇa tu iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tān uvāca mahābhāgān bhagavant ātma mūḥ svayam devadāru vana sthān tu tapasā pāvaka prabhān uvāca devānām ca ṛṣīnām ca pitṝṇām ca eva sa prabhuḥ saṃharati eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ eṣa ca eva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjati ekaḥ sva tejasā eṣa cakrī ca vajrī ca śrīvatsa kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ rudrasya mūrtayaḥ tu etāḥ ye abhidhyāyānti paṇḍitāḥ catur asram bahis ca antar aṣṭa asram piṇḍikā āśraye mudarśanam yogyam evam liṅgam prapūjayet tamaḥ hi agniḥ rajaḥ brahmā sattvam viṣṇuḥ prakāśakam mūrtiḥ ekā sthitā ca asya mūrtayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ tasmāt hi devadeveśam īśānam prabhum avyayam liṅgam kṛtvā yathānyāyam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutam aṅguṣṭha mātram su śubham su vṛttam sarva saṃmatam tathā aṣṭa asram vā su vṛttam maṇḍalam divyam sarva kāma phala pradam vedikā dviguṇā tasya samā vā sarva saṃmatā ca paṭṭikā ca samantāt vai yava mātrā dvijottamāḥ sauvarṇam rājatam śailam kṛtvā tāmra mayam tathā mahā vedikāyāḥ ca vistāram triguṇam vai samantataḥ vartulam catur asram vā ṣaṣ asram vā tris asrakam samantāt nirvraṇam śubhram lakṣaṇaiḥ tat su līkṣitam pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyam pūjā lakṣaṇa saṃyutam secayet ca tatas liṅgam pavitraiḥ pañcabhiḥ śubhaiḥ samāhitāḥ pūjayadhvam sa putrāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ sarve prāñjalayaḥ bhūtvā śūlapāṇim prapadyata tatas drakṣyatha deveśam durdaśama kṛtātmabhiḥ yam dṛṣṭvā sarvam ajñānam adharmaḥ ca praṇaśyati tatas pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā brahmāṇam amita ojasam saṃprasthitāḥ vanaukāḥ te devadāru vanam tatas brahmaṇā kathitam yathā sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu parvatānām guhāsu ca nadīnām ca vivikteṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu ca śaivāla śobhanāḥ kecid kecid antar jaleśayāḥ kecid darbha avakāśāḥ tu pādāṅguṣṭha agra dhiṣṭhitāḥ dantolūkhalinaḥ tu anye aśmakuṭṭāḥ tathā pare sthāna vīrāsanāḥ tu anye mṛgacaryā ratāḥ pare tapasā pūjayā ca mahā dhiyaḥ tatas teṣām prasāda artham bhaktānām anukaṃpayā devadāru vanam prāptaḥ prasannaḥ parameśvaraḥ bhasma pāṃsu upadigdha aṅgaḥ nagnaḥ vikṛta lakṣaṇaḥ kvacid nṛtyati śṛṅgāram kvacid rauti muhur muhur bhaikṣyam yācate ca punar punar māyām kṛtvā tathārūpām devaḥ tad vanām āgataḥ tatas te munayaḥ sarve tuṣṭuvuḥ ca samāhitāḥ sa patnīkāḥ mahābhāgāḥ sa putrāḥ sa paricchadāḥ ajñānāt devadeveśaiḥ yat asmābhiḥ anuṣṭhitam karmaṇā manasā vācā tat sarvam kṣantum arhasi caritāni guhyāni gahanāni ca brahma ādīnām ca devānām durvijñe yāni te hara stuvānti tvām mahātmānaḥ devadevam maheśvaram ananta bala vīryāya bhūtānām pataye namaḥ saṃhartre ca piśaṅgāya avyayāya vyayāya ca gaṅgā salila dhārāya ādhārāya guṇa ātmane tryambakāya trinetrāya triśūla vara dhāriṇe śaṅkarāya vṛṣāṅkāya gaṇānām pataye namaḥ daṇḍa hastāya kālāya pāśa hastāya vai namaḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca yat ajñānāt yadi vijñānāt yat kiñcid kurute naraḥ evam stutvā tu munayaḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥ antarātmabhiḥ tapasā yuktaḥ paśyāmaḥ tvām yathā purā tatas devaḥ prasanna ātmā svam eva āsthāya śaṃkaraḥ rūpam tryakṣam ca saṃdraṣṭum divyam cakṣuḥ adāt prabhuḥ labdha dṛṣṭyā tayā dṛṣṭvā devadevam tryambakam punar tuṣṭuvuḥ īśānam devadāru vanaukasaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ namaḥ digvāsase nityam kṛtāntāya triśuline arūpāya surūpāya viśvarūpāya te namaḥ kaṭaṅkaṭāya rudrāya svāhākārāya vai namaḥ nityam khaṇḍāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namaḥ namaḥ nīlakaṇṭhāya devāya citā bhasma aṅga dhāriṇe tvam brahmā sarva devānām rudrāṇām nīlalohitaḥ ātmā ca sarva bhūtānām sāṃkhyaiḥ puruṣaḥ ucyate parvatānām mahā meruḥ nakṣatrāṇām ca candramāḥ ṛṣīṇām ca vasiṣṭhaḥ tvam devānām vāsavaḥ tathā oṃkāraḥ sarva vedānām śreṣṭha sāma ca sāmasu āraṇyānām paśūnām ca siṃhaḥ tvam parameśvaraḥ grāmyāṇām ṛṣabhaḥ ca asi bhagavān loka pūjitaḥ tvām eva tatra paśyāmaḥ brahmaṇā kathitam tathā kāmaḥ krodhaḥ ca lobhaḥ ca viṣādaḥ madaḥ eva ca mahā saṃharaṇe prāpte tvayā deva kṛtātmanā karam lalāṭe saṃvidhya vahniḥ utpāditaḥ tvayā tena agninā tadā lokāḥ arcirbhiḥ sarvatas vṛtāḥ yāni ca anyāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca naḥ dahyamānānām trātā bhava sureśvara tvam ca loka hita arthāya bhūtāni pariṣiñcasi maheśvara mahābhāgā prabho śubha nirīkṣaka ājñāpaya vayam nātha kartāraḥ vacanam tava bhūta koṭi sahasreṣu rūpa koṭi śateṣu ca iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ro-0 r ro-0 stutim śrutvā stutaḥ teṣām idam vacanam abravīt yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api yuṣmābhiḥ kīrtitam stavam śrāvayet vā dvijān vipraḥ gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt vakṣyāmi vaḥ hitam puṇyam bhaktānām muni puṃgavāḥ strī liṅgam akhilam devī prakṛtiḥ mama deha jā puṃlliṅgam puruṣaḥ viprāḥ mama deha samudbhavaḥ ubhābhyām eva vai sṛṣṭiḥ mama viprāḥ na saṃśayaḥ bāla unmatta viceṣṭam tu mad param brahma avādinam ye hi mām bhasma niratāḥ bhasmanā dagdha kilbiṣāḥ yathā ukta kāriṇaḥ dāntāḥ viprāḥ dhyāna parāyaṇāḥ acayanti mahādevam vāc manaḥ kāya saṃyatāḥ bhasma vratāḥ ca muṇḍāḥ ca vratinaḥ viśva rūpiṇaḥ na haset na apriyam brūyāt amutra iha hita arthavān yaḥ tāḥ nindati mūḍha ātmā mahādevam sa nindati yaḥ tu etān pūjayet nityam sa pūjayati śaṃkaram evam eṣa mahādevaḥ lokānām hita kāmyayā yuge yuge mahāyogī krīḍate bhasma guṇṭhitaḥ atulam iha mahā bhaya praṇāśa hetum śiva kathitam paramam padam viditvā tatas pramuditāḥ viprāḥ śrutvā ivam kathitam tadā gandha udakaiḥ su śuddhaiḥ ca kuśa puṣpa vimiśritaiḥ ardha nārī śarīrāya sāṃkhyayoga pravartine megha vāhana kṛṣṇāya gaja carma nivāsine bhū ajina uttarīyāya vyāla yajña upavītine tatas tān sa munīn prītaḥ pratyuvāca maheśvaraḥ prītaḥ u ḥ asmi tapasā vaḥ varam vṛṇuta suvratāḥ bhṛgu aṅgirāḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca viśvāmitraḥ tathā eva ca marīciḥ kaśyapaḥ kaṇvaḥ saṃvartaḥ ca mahā tapāḥ tatas teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavant parameśvaraḥ sa smitam prāham saṃprekṣya sarvān muni varān tadā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bāge ṛṣivākyam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī bhagavant uvāca agniḥ hi aham soma kartā somaḥ ca agnim upāśritaḥ bhasmanā vīryam āsthāya bhūtāni piraṣiñcati agni kāryam ca yaḥ kṛtvā kariṣyati triyāyuṣam bhakṣaṇāt sarva pāpānām bhasma iti parikīrtitam mapāḥ pitaraḥ jñeyāḥ devāḥ vai soma saṃbhavāḥ agnīṣoma ātmakam sarvam jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam mama agniḥ mahā tejāḥ somaḥ ca eṣā mahā aṃbikā mā agniḥ ca somaḥ ca prakṛtyā puruṣaḥ svayam sva vīryam vapuṣā ca eva dhārayāmi iti vai sthitiḥ tadā prabhṛti lokeṣu rakṣā artham aśubheṣu ca bhasmanā kriyate rakṣā sūtikānām gṛheṣu ca bhasma asnāna aviśuddha ātmā jita krodaḥ jita indriyaḥ matam pāśupatam yogam kāpilam ca eva nirmitam śeṣāḥ ca āśrāmiṇaḥ sarve paścāt sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā sṛṣṭiḥ eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā lajjā moha bhaya ātmakā ye ca anye mānavāḥ loke sarve jāyanti avāsasaḥ taiḥ eva saṃvṛtaiḥ guptaḥ na vastram kāraṇam smṛtam kṣamā dhṛtiḥ ahiṃsā ca vairāgyam ca eva sarvaśas yadi akārya sahasrāṇi kṛtvā yaḥ snāti bhasmanā tasmai dyatna paraḥ bhūtvā tri kālam api yaḥ sadā bhasmanā kurute snānam gāṇapatyam sa gacchati samāhṛtya kratūn sarvān gṛhītvā vratam uttamam dhyāyanti ye mahādevam līlā sadbhāva bhāvitāḥ uttareṇa ārya panthānam te amṛta tvam avāpnuyuḥ dakṣiṇena ca panthānam ye śmaśānāni bhejire icchā kāma avasāyi tvam tathā prākāmyam eva ca īkṣiṇena ca panthānam ye śmaśānāni bhejire indra ādayaḥ tathā devāḥ kāmika vratam āsthā etāḥ imam pāśupatam dhyāyan sarva pāpa praṇāśanam yaḥ paṭhet ca śuciḥ bhūtvā śraddadhānaḥ jita indriyaḥ te sarve munayaḥ śrutvā vasiṣṭha ādyāḥ dvijottamāḥ bhasma pāṇḍura digdha aṅgāḥ babhūvuḥ vigata spṛhāḥ rudra lokāya kalpa ante saṃsthitāḥ śiva tejasā tasmāt na nindyāḥ pūjyāḥ ca vikṛtāḥ malināḥ api rūpa anvitāḥ ca vipra indrāḥ sadā yogin indra śaṅkayā bahunā kim pralāpena bhava bhaktāḥ dvijottamāḥ saṃpūjyāḥ sarva yatnena śiva vat na atra saṃśayaḥ malināḥ ca eva vipra indrāḥ bhava bhaktāḥ dṛḍha vratāḥ nārāyaṇam tathā loke rudra bhaktyā na saṃśayaḥ jaṭinaḥ muṇḍinaḥ ca eva nagnāḥ nānā prakāriṇaḥ saṃpūjyāḥ śiva vat nityam manasā karmaṇā girā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge yogi praśaṃsā nāma cutastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ katham jaghāna rājānam kṣupam pādena suvrata vajra asthi tvam katham lebhe mahādevāt mahā tapāḥ uvāca brahma putraḥ mahā tejāḥ rājā kṣupaḥ iti smṛtaḥ cirāt tayoḥ prasaṃgāt vai vādaḥ kṣupa dadhīcayoḥ abha vat kṣatriya śreṣṭhaḥ vipraḥ eva iti viśrutaḥ aṣṭānām lokapālānām vapuḥ dhārayate nṛpaḥ tasmāt tvayā mahābhāga cyāvaneya sadā hi aham dadhīcaḥ cyāvaniḥ ca ugraḥ gauravāt ātmanaḥ dvijaḥ atāḍayat kṣupam mūrdhni dadhīcaḥ vāma muṣṭinā ciccheda vajroṇa ca tam dadhīcam balavān kṣupaḥ labdham vajram ca kārya artham vajrimā coditaḥ prabhuḥ yathā vajradharaḥ śrīmān balavān tamasā anvitaḥ śukrā upi saṃdhayāmāsa tāḍitam kuliśena tam yogāt etya dadhīcasya deham dehabhṛtām varaḥ saṃdhāya pūrvavat deham dadhīcasya āha bhārgavaḥ saṃpūjya pūjyam brahma ādyaiḥ devadevam nirañjanam mṛta saṃjīvanam tasmāt labdham etat mayā dvija na asti mṛtyu bhayam śambhoḥ bhaktānām iha sarvatas mṛtasaṃjīvani ca api śaivam adya vadāmi te indriyeṣu tathā anyeṣu deveṣu ca gaṇeṣu ca puṣpeṣu gandha vat sūkṣmaḥ su gāndhiḥ parameśvaraḥ viṣṇoḥ pitāmahasya api munīnām ca mahā mune indrasya api ca devānām tasmāt vai puṣṭi vardhanaḥ tam devam amṛtam rudram karmaṇā tapasā tathā satyena anena mukṣīyān mṛtyu pāśāt bhavaḥ svayam mṛtasaṃjīvanīḥ mantraḥ mayā labdhaḥ tu śaṃkarāt japtvā hutvā abhimantrya evam jalam pītvā divāniśam liṅgasya saṃnidhau dhyātvā na asti mṛtyu bhayam dvija tasya tat vacanam śrutvā tapasā ārādhya śaṃkaram evam ārādhya deveśam dadhīcaḥ muni sattamaḥ atāḍayat ca adīna tām ca kṣupā dadhīcasya tadā prabhāvam harim mukundam indrānujam prekṣya tadā ambuja akṣam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge kṣupābidhanṛpaparābhavavarṇanam nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pūjayā tasya saṃtuṣṭaḥ bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ śrī bhūmi sahitaḥ śrīmān śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ kirīṭī padma hastaḥ ca sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ pīta ambaraḥ ca bhagavant devaiḥ daityaiḥ ca saṃvṛtaḥ divyena darśanena eva dṛṣṭvā devam janārdanam tuṣṭāva pāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ praṇamya garuḍadhvajam tvam ādiḥ tvam anādiḥ ca prakṛtiḥ tvam janārdanaḥ puruṣaḥ tvam jagannāthaḥ viṣṇuḥ viśveśvaraḥ bhavān brahmā asi mahant tathā ca bhūtādiḥ tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca tvayā eva adhiṣṭhitāni eva viśvamūrte maheśvara prasīda tvam jagannātha śaraṇyam śaraṇam gataḥ vaikuṇṭha śaure sarvajña vāsudeva mahā bhuja saṃkarṣaṇa mahābhāga pradyumna puruṣottama aniruddha mahāviṣṇo sadā viṣṇo namaḥ astu te adhas ca dharmaḥ deveśa jñānam vairāgyam eva ca aiśvaryam āsanasya asya pāda rūpeṇa suvrataiḥ vāsāṃsi sāgarāḥ sapta diśaḥ ayutān gaṇān tāni sarvāṇi sahasā dadāha muni sattamaḥ tasya dehe hareḥ sākṣāt apaśyat dvijasattamaḥ dadhīcaḥ bhagavān vipraḥ devatānām gaṇān pṛthak rudrāṇām koṭayaḥ ca eva gaṇānām koṭayaḥ tadā aṇḍānām mahā bāho vicārataḥ vijñānānām sahasrāṇi durvijñeyāni mādhava brahmānam ca tathā rudram divyām dṛṣṭim dadāmi te iti uktvā darśayāmāsa sva tanau nikhilam muniḥ māyayā hi anayā kim vā mantra śaktyā atha nārāyaṇam ca tam bārayāmāsa niśceṣṭam padmayoniḥ jagadguruḥ jagāma bhagavant viṣṇuḥ praṇipatya mahā munim chupaḥ duḥkha āturaḥ bhūtvā saṃpūjya ca muni īśvaram dadhīcam abhivandya āśu prārthayāmāsa uttamān rudra kopa agninā devāḥ sa deva indrāḥ muni īśvaraiḥ dhvastāḥ bhavantu devena viṣṇunā ca samanvitāḥ evam śaptvā kṣupam prekṣya punar āha dvijottamaḥ devaiḥ ca pūjyāḥ rāja indra nṛpaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ gaṇaiḥ brāhmaṇāḥ eva rāja indra balinaḥ prabhaviṣṇavaḥ iti uktvā sva uṭajam vipraḥ praviveśa mahā dyutiḥ sthāneśvaram anuprāpya śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt kathitaḥ tava saṃkṣepāt vivādaḥ kṣupa dadhīcayoḥ yaḥ idam kīrtayoḥ divyam vivādam kṣupa dadhīcayoḥ jitvā apamṛtyum dehānte brahma lokam prayāti saḥ yaḥ idam kīrtya saṃgrāmam praviśet tasya sarvadā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge kṣupadadhīcisaṃvādaḥ nāma ṣaṭratriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca prajā kāmaḥ śilādaḥ bhūt pitā mama mahā mune śilādam āha tuṣṭaḥ asmi varayasva varān iti tatas praṇamya deveśam sahasrākṣam saha amaraiḥ provāca muni śārdūlaiḥ kṛta añjali puṭaḥ harim uvāca uvāca putram dāsyāmi viprarṣe yoni jam mṛtyu saṃyutam te na dāsyāmi mṛtyu hīnāḥ na santi vai saḥ api devaḥ svayam brahmā mṛtyu hīnaḥ na ca īśvaraḥ yoni jaḥ ca mahā tejāḥ ca aṇḍa jaḥ padma sambhavaḥ maheśvara aṅga jaḥ ca eva bhavānyāḥ tanayaḥ prabhuḥ tasya api āyuḥ samākhyātam parārdha dvaya saṃmitam koṭi koṭi sahasrāṇi ahar bhūtāni yāni vai samatītāni kalpānām tāvat śeṣā para traye parityaja āśām vipra indraiḥ gṛhāṇa ātma samam sutam uvāca tasya tat vacanam śrutvā pitā me loka viśrutaḥ śilādaḥ iti puṇya ātmā punar prāha śacīpatim uvāca maheśvara aṅga yoni tvam śrutam vai brahmaṇaḥ mayā purā mahā indra dāyādāt gadataḥ ca asya pūrvajāt nāradāt vai mahā bāho katham atra āśu naḥ vada dākṣāyaṇī sā dakṣaḥ api devaḥ padmodbhava ātmajaḥ uvāca sthāne saṃśayitum vipra tava vakṣyāmi kāraṇam kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttam brahmanaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ sasarja sakalam dhyātvā brahmāṇam parameśvaraḥ nārāyaṇaḥ mahādevam bahu mānena sa ādaram dṛṣṭvā bhāvam mahādevaḥ hareḥ sva ātmani śaṅkaraḥ tadā tam kalpam āhuḥ vai meghavāhana saṃjñayā hiraṇyagarbhaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā tasya deha udbhavaḥ tadā janārdana sutaḥ prāha tapasā prāpya śaṃkaram te vāma aṅga jaḥ viṣṇuḥ dakṣiṇa aṅga bhavaḥ hi aham nārāyaṇāt api vibho bhaktā uham te śaṃkara tadā atha labdhvā bhagavant bhavāt sarva ātma tām kṣaṇāt ekārṇava ālaye śubhre tu andhakāre su dāruṇe jagat āvāsa hṛdayam dadarśa puruṣam tu ajaḥ ananta bhoga śayyāyām śāyinam paṅkaja īkṣaṇam sarva ābharaṇa saṃyuktam śaśi maṇḍala saṃnibham śrīvatsa lakṣaṇam devam prasanna āsyam janārdanam ramā mṛdu kara ambhoja sparśa rakta pada ambujam paramātmānam īśānam tamasā kāla rūpiṇam rajasā sarva lokānām sarga līlā pravartakam sattvena sarva bhūtānām sthāpakam parameśvaram sarva ātmānam mahātmānam paramātmānam īśvaram kṣīrārṇave amṛta maye śāyinam yoganidrayā tam dṛṣṭvā prāha vai brahmā bhagavantam janārdanam grasāmi tvām prasādena yathāpūrvam bhavān aham udaikṣata mahā bāhuḥ smitam īṣat cakāra saḥ viveśa ca aṇḍa jam tam tu grastaḥ tena mahātmanā sṛṣṭaḥ tena hariḥ prekṣya sthitaḥ tasya atha saṃnidhau vikṛtam rūpam āsthāya purā datta varaḥ tayoḥ āgacchat yatra vai viṣṇuḥ viśvātmā parameśvaraḥ prasādam atulam kartum brahmanaḥ ca hareḥ prabhuḥ paśyatām bhavam devam kālāgni sadṛśam prabhum praṇematuḥ ca vara dam bahu mānena dūratas iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge brahmaṇaḥ vara pradānam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śrī viṣṇuḥ uvāca parameśaḥ jagannāthaḥ śaṅkaraḥ tu eṣa sarvagaḥ āvayoḥ akhilasya īśaḥ śaraṇam ca maheśvaraḥ mama vāma aṅga jaḥ brahman śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ mām āhuḥ ṛṣayaḥ prekṣya pradhānam prakṛtim tathā evam āhuḥ mahādevam āvayoḥ api kāraṇam atha ambhasā plutām bhūmīm samādhāya janārdanaḥ pūrvavat sthāpayāmāsa vārāham rūpam āsthitaḥ nadīnada samudrān ca pūrvavat ca akarot prabhuḥ dharāyām saḥ ucinot sarvān bhūdharān bhūdhara ākṛtiḥ bhūḥ ādyān caturaḥ lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat sraṣṭum ca bhagavān cakre matim matimatām varaḥ mukhyam ca tairyagyonyam caṃ daivikam mānuṣam tathā vibhuḥ ca anugraham tatra purastāt asṛjat devaḥ sanandam sanakam tathā sanātanam satām śreṣṭham naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param dakṣam atrim vasiṣṭham ca sā usṛjat yoga vidyayā bhum sanatkumāram ca sasarja ādau sanātanaḥ evam mukhya ādikān sṛṣṭvā padmayoniḥ śila aśana yuga dharmān aśeṣān ca kalpayāmāsa viśvasṛj iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vaiṣṇavakathanam nāma aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śrutvā śakreṇa kathitam pitā mama mahā muniḥ punar papraccha deveśam praṇamya racita añjaliḥ uvāca śacīpate jagannātha sahasrākṣa maheśvaraḥ vaktum arhasi me sarvam sāṃpratam praṇatāya me uvāca tasya tat vacanam śrutvā śilādasya mahātmanaḥ vyājahāra yathādṛṣṭam yuga dharmam su vistaram uvāca ādyam kṛta yugam viddhi tatas tretā yugam mune dvāparam tiṣyam iti ete catvāraḥ tu samāsatas sattvam kṛtam rajaḥ tretā dvāparam ca rajaḥ tamaḥ dhyānam param kṛta yuge tretāyām yajñaḥ ucyate catvāri ca sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tat kṛtam yugam tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ catvāri ca sahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi śilāśana tatas kṛta yuge tasmin saṃdhyāṃśe ca gate tu vai bhavati yuga dharmaḥ tu sarvatas kṛta ardham dvāparam viddhi tad ardham tiṣyam ucyate triśatī dviśatī saṃdhyā tathā ca ekaśatī mune saṃdhyāṃśaṅkam tathā api evam kalpeṣu evam yuge yuge ādye kṛta yuge dharmaḥ catuṣpādaḥ sanātanaḥ tri pāda hīnaḥ tiṣye tu sattā mātreṇa dhiṣṭhitaḥ tu mithuna utpattiḥ vṛttiḥ sākṣāt rasā ullasā prajāḥ tṛptāḥ sadā sarvāḥ sarva ānandāḥ ca bhoginaḥ adhama uttama tā tāsām na viśeṣāḥ prajāḥ śubhāḥ tulyam āyuḥ sukham rūpam tāsām tasmin kṛte yuge tāsām prītiḥ na ca dvandvam na dveṣaḥ na asti ca klamaḥ parvata udadhi vāsinyaḥ hi aniketa āśrayāḥ tu tāḥ viśokāḥ sattva bahulāḥ ekānta bahulāḥ tathā tāḥ vai niṣkāma cāriṇyaḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ apravṛttiḥ kṛta yuge karmaṇoḥ śubha pāpayoḥ varṇa āśrama vyavasthā ca tava āsīt na ca saṃkaraḥ rasollāsaḥ naśyate dvijaiḥ tasyām siddhau pranaṣṭāyām anyā siddhiḥ prajāyate apām saukṣmye pratigate tadā megha ātmanā tu vai sakṛt eva tathā vṛṣṭyā saṃyukte pṛthivī tale prādurāsan tadā tāsām vṛkṣāḥ te gṛha saṃjñitāḥ tatas kālena mahatā tāsām eva viparyayāt tāsām tu tena tad kāla bhāvinā praṇaśyanti tatas sarve vṛkṣāḥ te gṛha saṃjñitāḥ tatas teṣu pranaṣṭeṣu vibhrāntāḥ mā eṣunā udbhavāḥ api dhyāyanti tām siddhim satya abidhyāyinaḥ tadā prādurbabhūvuḥ tāsām tu vṛkṣāḥ te gṛha saṃjñitāḥ vastrāṇi te prasūyante phalāni ābharaṇāni ca teṣu eva jāyate tāsām gandha varṇa rasa anvitam amākṣikam mahī vīryam puṭakepuṭake madhu hṛṣṭa puṣṭāḥ tayā siddhyā prajāḥ vai tatas kāla antareṇa eva punar lobha āvṛtāḥ tu tāḥ vṛkṣān tān paryagṛhṇanti madhu vā mākṣikam balāt tāsām tena upacāreṇa punar lobha kṛtena vai pranaṣṭāḥ madhunā sārdham kalpavṛkṣāḥ kvacid kvacid tasyām eva alpa śiṣṭāyām siddhyām kāla vaśāt tadā āvartanāt tu tretāyām dvandvāni abhyutthitāni vai śīta varṣā tapaiḥ tīvraiḥ tatas tāḥ duḥkhitāḥ bhṛśam dvandvaiḥ saṃpīḍyamānāḥ ca cakruḥ āvaraṇāni tu kṛta dvaṃdva pratīghātāḥ ketanāni girau tatas pūrvam nikāma cārāḥ tāḥ hi aniketāḥ atha avasan yathāyogam yathāprīti niketeṣu avasan punar kṛtvā dvandva upaghātān tān vṛtti upāyam a cintayan naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārdham kalpavṛkṣeṣu vai tadā vivāda vyākulāḥ tāḥ vai prajāḥ tṛṣṇā kṣudhā arditāḥ vārtāyāḥ sādhakā api anyā vṛṣṭiḥ tāsām nikāmāt tāsām vṛṣṭi udaka ādīni hi abhavan nimna gāni tu abhavan vṛṣṭi saṃtatyā srota sthānāni nimnagāḥ evam nadyaḥ pravṛttāḥ tu dvitīye vṛṣṭi sarjane ye punar tad apām stokāḥ patitāḥ pṛthi vītale pām bhūmeḥ ca saṃyogāt oṣadhyaḥ tāḥ tadā abhavan atha alpa kṛṣṭāḥ ca anuptāḥ grāmya āraṇyāḥ caturdaśa ṛtu puṣpa phalāḥ ca eva vṛkṣa gulmāḥ ca jajñire prādurbhūtāni ca etāni vṛkṣa jāti auṣadhāni ca tatas punar abhūt tāsām rāgaḥ lobhaḥ ca sarvaśas avaśyam bhāvinā arthena tretā yuga vaśena ca tatas tāḥ paryaguhṇanta nadī kṣetrāṇi parvatān viparyayeṇa ca oṣadhyaḥ pranaṣṭāḥ tāḥ caturdaśa matvā dharām praviṣṭāḥ tāḥ iti auṣadhīḥ pitāmahaḥ tadā prabhṛti ca oṣadhyaḥ phaālakṛṣṭāḥ tu itas tatas mārtā kṛṣim samāyātāḥ prayatnataḥ mātā vṛttiḥ samākhyātā kṛṣi kāma prayatnāt anyathā jīvitam tāsām na asti tretā yuga atyaye tatra api jagṛhuḥ sarve ca anyonyam krodha mūrcchitāḥ maryādāyāḥ pratiṣṭhā artham jñātvā tat akhilam vubhuḥ sasarja kṣatriyān trātum kṣatāt kamalasaṃbhavaḥ varṇa āśrama pratiṣṭhām ca cakāra svena tejasā vṛttena vṛttinā vṛttam viśvātmā nirmame svayam paśu yajñam na sevante kecid tatra api suvratāḥ balāt viṣṇuḥ tadā yajñam akarot sarva dṛś kramāt dvijāḥ tadā praśaṃsanti tatas tu āhiṃsakam mune dvāpareṣu api vartante mati bhedāḥ tadā nṛṇām manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrāt vārttā prasidhyati tadā tu sarva bhūtānām kāya kleśa vaśāt kramāt lobhaḥ bhṛtiḥ vaṇij yuddham tattvānām aviniścayaḥ veda śākhā praṇayanam dharmāṇām saṃkaraḥ tathā varṇa āśrama paridhvaṃsaḥ kāma dveṣau tathā eva ca vedaḥ vyāsaiḥ caturdhā tu vyasyate dvāpara ādiṣu saṃkṣayāt āyuṣaḥ ca eva vyasyate dvāpareṣu saḥ hi ṛṣi putraiḥ punar bhedāḥ bhidyante dṛṣṭi vibhramaiḥ saṃhitāḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāmnām saṃhanyante manīṣibhiḥ sāmānyāḥ vaikṛtāḥ ca eva draṣṭṛbhiḥ taiḥ pṛthak pṛthak brāhmaṇam kalpasūtrāṇi mantra pravacanāni ca itihāsa purāṇāni bhidyante kāla gauravāt brāhmam pādmam vaiṣṇavam ca śaivam bhāgavatam tathā bhaviṣyam nāradīyam ca mārkaṇḍeyam atas param āgneyam brahmavaivartam laiṅgam vārāham eva ca skāndam tathā ca brahmāṇḍam teṣām bhedaḥ prakathyate laiṅgam ekādaśavidham prabhinnam dvāpare śubham manu atri viṣṇu hārīta yājñavalkya uśanāḥ uṅgirāḥ yama āpastamba saṃvartāḥ kātyāyana bṛhaspatī parāśara vyāsa śaṅkha likhitāḥ dakṣa gautamau śātātapaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca evamādyauḥ sahasraśas avṛṣṭiḥ maraṇam ca eva tathā vyādhi ādi upadravāḥ nirvedāt jāyate teṣām duḥkha mokṣa vicāraṇā vicāraṇāt ca vairāgyam vairāgyāt doṣa darśanam doṣāṇām darśanāt ca eva dvāpare jñāna saṃbhavaḥ eṣā rajaḥ tamaḥ yuktā vṛttiḥ vai dvāpare smṛtā dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā pramaśyati kalau yuge iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tiṣye māyām asūyām ca vadham ca eva tapasvinām anāvṛṣṭi bhayam ghoram deśānām ca viparyayaḥ na prāmāṇyam śruteḥ asti nṛṇām ca adharma sevanam adhārmikāḥ tu anācārāḥ mahā kopa alpa cetasaḥ anṛtam bruvate lubdhāḥ tiṣye jātāḥ ca duṣprajāḥ duriṣṭaiḥ duradhītaiḥ ca durācāraiḥ durāgamaiḥ viprāṇām karma doṣeṇa prajānām jāyate bhayam na adhīyante tadā vedān na yajanti dvijātayaḥ utsīdanti narāḥ ca eva kṣatriyāḥ ca viśaḥ kramāt śūdrāṇām mantra yogena saṃbandhaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha rājānaḥ śūdra bhūyiṣṭhāḥ brāhmaṇān bādhayanti te bhrūṇahatyā vīra hatyā prajāyante prajāsu vai śūdrāḥ ca brāhmaṇa ācārāḥ sudra ācārāḥ ca brāhmaṇāḥ rāja vṛtti sthitāḥ caurāḥ caura ācārāḥ ca pārthivāḥ varṇa āśrama pratiṣṭhānaḥ jāyate nṛṣu sarvatas tadā svalpa phalā bhūmiḥ kvacid ca api mahā phalā a rakṣitāraḥ hartāraḥ pārthivāḥ ca śilaśana śūdrāḥ vai jñāninaḥ sarve brāhmaṇaiḥ abhivanditāḥ a kṣatriyāḥ ca rājānaḥ viprāḥ śudra upajīvinaḥ mad āsana sthāḥ dvijān dṛṣṭvā na calanti alpabuddhayaḥ tāḍayanti dvijendrān ca śudrāḥ vai su alpabuddhayaḥ nidhāya vai hastam karṇam śudrasya vai dvijāḥ ucca āsana sthān śūdrān ca dvija madhye dvijarṣabha jñātvā na hiṃsate rājā kalau kāla vaśena tu puṣpaiḥ ca vāsitaiḥ ca eva tathā anyaiḥ magalaiḥ śubhaiḥ śūdrān abhyarcayanti alpa śruta bhāgya bala anvitāḥ sevā avasaram ālekya dvāre tiṣṭhanti vai dvijāḥ hana sthān samāvṛtya śudrān śūdra upajīvinaḥ tapaḥ yajña phalānām ca vikretāraḥ dvijottamāḥ puruṣa alpam bahu strīkam yuga ante samupasthite kalau devaḥ mahādevaḥ śaṃkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ prakāśate pratiṣṭhā artham dharmasya vikṛta ākṛtiḥ ye tam viprāḥ niṣevante yena kena api śaṃkaram śvāpada prabala tvam ca gavām ca eva parikṣayaḥ sādhūnām vinivṛttiḥ ca vedyā tasmin yuga kṣaye tadā sūkṣmaḥ mahā udarkaḥ durlabhaḥ dāna mūlavān arākṣitāraḥ hartāraḥ balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ yuga anteṣu bhaviṣyanti sva rakṣaṇa parāyaṇāḥ aṭṭa śūlāḥ janapadāḥ śiva śūlāḥ catuṣpathāḥ pramadāḥ keśa śūlinyaḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge citra varṣī tadā devaḥ yadā prāhuḥ yuga kṣayam kuśīla caryāḥ pāṣaṇḍaiḥ vṛthak rūpaiḥ samāvṛtāḥ na avyāhṛta krūra vākyaḥ na ārjavī na anasūyakaḥ na kṛte pratikartā ca yuga kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati nindakāḥ ca eva patitāḥ yuga antasya ca nṛpa śūnyā vasumatī na ca dhānya dhana āvṛtā maṇḍalāni bhaviṣyanti deśeṣu nagareṣu ca alpa udakā ca alpa phalā bhaviṣyati vasuṃdharā goptāraḥ ca api agoptāraḥ saṃbhaviṣyanti aśāsanāḥ hartāraḥ para vittānām para dāra pradharṣakāḥ kāma ātmānaḥ durātmānaḥ hi adhamāḥ sāhasa priyāḥ pranaṣṭa ceṣṭanāḥ puṃsaḥ mukta keśāḥ ca śūlinaḥ janāḥ ṣoḍaśa varṣāḥ ca prajāyante yuga kṣaye śukla danta ajina akṣāḥ ca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāya vāsasaḥ śūdrāḥ dharmam cariṣyānti yuga ante samupastite sasya caurāḥ bhaviṣyanti dṛḍha caila abhi lāṣiṇaḥ kaṭi mūṣaka sarpāḥ ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān subhikṣam kṣemam ārogyam sāmarthyam durlabham tadā pratipatsyante deśān kṣudh bhaya pīḍitāḥ duḥkhena abhiplutānām ca parama āyuḥ śatam tadā dṛśyante na ca dṛśyante vedāḥ kali yuge akhilāḥ utsīdanti tadā kevala adharma pīḍitāḥ nirgranthāḥ kāpālī bahulāḥ tu iha veda vikrayiṇaḥ ca anye tīrtha vikrayiṇaḥ pare varṇa āśramāṇām ye ca anye pāṣaṇḍāḥ paripanthinaḥ adhīyante tadā vedān śūdrāḥ dharma artha kovidāḥ yajante ca aśvamedhena rājānaḥ śūdra yonayaḥ upadravān tathā anyonyam sādhayanti tadā prajāḥ duḥkha prabhūtam alpa āyuḥ deha utsādaḥ sa roga tā tasmāt āyuḥ balam rūpam kilam prāpya prahīyate śruti smṛti uditam dharmam ye sūyakāḥ tretāyām vārṣikaḥ dharmaḥ dvāpare māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ yathākleśam caran prājñaḥ tat ahnā prāpnute kalau eṣā kali yuga avasthā saṃdhyāṃśam tu nibodha me yuge yuge ca hīyante trīn trīn pādān tu siddhayaḥ yuga svabhāvāḥ saṃdhyāḥ tu tiṣṭhanti iha tu pādaśas saṃdhyā svabhāvāḥ sva aṃśeṣu pādaśas te pratiṣṭhitāḥ evam sandhyāṃśake kāle saṃprāpte tu yuga antike teṣām śāstā hi asādhūnām bhūtānām nidana utthitaḥ mānavasya tu sa iṃśena pūrvam svāyaṃbhuva intare samāḥ sa viṃśatiḥ pūrṇā paryaṭan vai vasuṃdharām anukarṣan sa vai senām sa vāji ratha kuñjarām pragṛhīta āyudhaiḥ vipraiḥ śataśas utha sahasraśas sa hatvā sarvaśas ca eva rājñaḥ tān śūdra yoni jān pākhaṇḍān tu tatas sarvān niḥśeṣam kṛtavan prabhuḥ na atyartham dhārmikāḥ ye ca tān sarvān hanti sarvatas varṇa vyatyāsa jātāḥ ca ye ca tān anujīvinaḥ adhṛṣyaḥ sarva bhūtānām cacāra atha vasuṃdharām pūrva janmani viṣṇoḥ tu pramitiḥ nāma vīryavān dvātriṃśe abhyudite varṣe viṃśatiḥ samāḥ vinighnan sarva bhūtāni śata śotha sahasraśas kṛtvā bīja avaśeṣām tu pṛthivīm krūra karmaṇaḥ sa sādhayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśas tān adhārmikān gaṅgā yamunayoḥ madhye sthitim prāptaḥ saha anugaḥ tatas vyatīte kāle tu sa amātyaḥ sa haisanikaḥ utsādya pārthivān sarvān mlecchān ca eva sahasraśas tatra saṃdhyāṃśake kāle saṃprāpte tu yuga antike sthitāsu alpa avaśiṣṭāsu prajāsu iha kvacid kvacid apragrahāḥ tatas tāḥ vai lobha āviṣṭāḥ tu kṛtsnaśas prajāḥ tāḥ vai tatas sarvāḥ paraspara bhaya arditāḥ vyākulāḥ ca paribhrāntāḥ tyaktvā dārān gṛhāni ca svān prāṇān an apekṣantaḥ niṣkāruṇyāḥ su duḥkhitāḥ nirmaryādāḥ niḥsnehāḥ nirapatrapāḥ naṣṭe dharme pratihatāḥ hrasvakāḥ pañcaviṃśakāḥ hitvā putrān ca dārān ca vivāda vyākula indriyāḥ anāvṛṣṭi hatāḥ ca eva vārttām utsṛjya dūratas sarit sāgara kūpān te sevante parvatān tathā cari pattra ajina dharāḥ niṣkriyāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ varṇa āśrama paribhraṣṭāḥ saṃkaṭam ghoram āstaitāḥ evam kaṣṭam anuprāptāḥ alpa śeṣāḥ prajāḥ tadā jarā vyādhi kṣudhā āviṣṭāḥ duḥkhāt nirveda mānasāḥ vicāraṇā tu nirvedāt sāmya avasthā vicāraṇā sāmya avasthā ātmakaḥ bodhaḥ saṃbodhāt dharma śīla tā arūpa śama yuktāḥ tu kali śiṣṭāḥ hi vai svayam ahorātrāt tadā tāsām yugam tu parivartate citta saṃmohanam kṛtvā tāsām vai supta matta vat utpannāḥ kali śiṣṭāḥ tu prajāḥ kārtayugāḥ tadā tiṣṭhanti ca iha ye siddhāḥ adṛṣṭāḥ vicaranti ca brahma kṣatra viśaḥ śudrāḥ bīja artham ye smṛtāḥ iha teṣām saptarṣayaḥ dharmam kathayanti itare api ca varṇa āśrama ācāra yutam śraitam smārtam dvidhā tu yam śrauta smārta kṛtānām ca dharme saptarṣi darśite yathā dāva pradagdheṣu tṛṇoṣu iha tatas kṣitau vanānām prathamam vṛṣṭyā teṣām mūleṣu saṃbhavaḥ tathā kārtayugānām tu kali jeṣu iha saṃbhavaḥ sukham āyuḥ balam rūpam dharmaḥ ūrathaḥ kāmaḥ eva ca yugeṣu etāni hīyante trīn trīn pādan krameṇa tu sa saṃdhyāṃśeṣu hīyante yugānām dharma siddhayaḥ iti eṣā pratisiddhiḥ vai kīrtitā eṣā krameṇu tu catur yugānām sarveṣām anena eva tu sādhanam eṣā catur yuga āvṛttiḥ ā sahasrāt guṇīkṛtā brahmaṇaḥ tat ahar proktam rātriḥ ca etāvatī smṛtā anārjavam jaḍībhāvaḥ bhūtānām āyugakṣayāt etat eva tu sarveṣām yugānām lakṣaṇam smṛtam catur yugānām ca guṇitā hi ekasaptatiḥ pañcaviṃśat parīmitāḥ na nyūnāḥ na adhikāḥ tathā tathā kalpāḥ yugaiḥ sārdham bhavanti saha sa kṣaṇaiḥ manvantarāṇām sarveṣām etat eva tu lakṣaṇam yatā yugānām parivartanāni cira pravṛttāni yuga svabhāvāt tathā tu saṃtiṣṭhati jīva lokaḥ kṣaya udayābhyām parivartamānaḥ iti etat lakṣaṇam proktam yugānām vai samāsatas atīta anāgatānām hi sarva manvantareṣu vai manvantareṇa ca ekena sarvāṇi eva antarāṇi ca anāgateṣu tadvat ca takaḥ kāryaḥ vijānatā manvantareṣu sarveṣu atīta anāgateṣu iha devāḥ hi aṣṭavidhāḥ ye ca ye ca manvantara īśvarāḥ evam varṇa āśramāṇām tu pravibhāgaḥ yuge yuge varṇa āśrama vibhāgāḥ ca yugāni yuga siddhayaḥ yugānām parimāṇam te kathitam hi prasaṅgataḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge caturyugaparimāṇam nāma catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ punar sasarja bhagavān prabhraṣṭāḥ pūrva vat prajāḥ tadā dharā ambhasi vyāptāḥ hi apaḥ vahnau samīraṇe vahniḥ samīraṇaḥ ca eva vyomni tanmātra saṃyutaḥ indriyāṇi daśa eka ca tanmātrāṇi dvijottama ahaṅkāram anuprāpya pralīnāḥ tad kṣaṇāt aho abhimānaḥ tadā tatra mahantam vyāpya vai kṣaṇāt tatas sṛṣṭiḥ abhūt tasmāt pūrvavat puruṣāt śivāt atha sṛṣṭāḥ tadā tasya manasā tena mānasāḥ duścaram vicacāra īśam samuddiśya tapaḥ svayam tuṣṭaḥ tu tapasā tasya bhavaḥ jñātvā sa vāñchitam atha ardha mātrām kalyāṇīm ātmanaḥ parameśvarīm bubhuje yoga mārgeṇa vṛddhi artham jagatām śivaḥ tasyām harim ca brahmāṇam sasarja parameśvaraḥ viśveśvaraḥ tu viśvātmā ca astrām pāśupatam tathā tasmāt brahmā mahādevyāḥ ca aṃśa jaḥ ca hariḥ tathā aṇḍa jaḥ padmajaḥ ca eva bhava aṅga bhavaḥ eva ca parārdham brahmanaḥ yāvat tāvat bhūtiḥ samāsatas vairāgyam brahmaṇaḥ vakṣye tama udbhūtam samāsatas nārāyaṇaḥ api bhagavant bridhā kṛtvā tmanaḥ stanum sasarja sakalam tasmāt sva aṅgāt eva carācaram tatas brahmāṇam asṛjat brahmā rudram pitāmahaḥ mune kalpa antare rudraḥ harim tatas brahmānam aṃsṛjat mune kalpa antare hariḥ nārāyaṇam punar brahmā brahmāṇam ca punarbhavaḥ tadā vicārya vai brahmā duḥkham saṃsāraḥ iti ajaḥ saṃhṛtya prāṇa sañcāram pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ pūritam pūrakeṇa eva prabuddham ca abhavat tadā mṛṇāla tantu bhāga ekaśata bhāge yamī yama viśuddha ātmā niyamya evam hṛdi īśvaram lalāṭam asya nirbhidya prādurāsīt pitāmahāt lohitaḥ abhūt svayam nīlaḥ śivasya hṛdaya udbhavaḥ bahneḥ ca eva tu saṃyogāt prakṛtya puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ nīlaḥ ca lohitaḥ ca eva yatas kāla ākṛtiḥ pumān brahmaṇā bhagavān kālaḥ prīta ātmā ca abhavat vibhuḥ su prīta manasam devam tuṣṭāva ca pitāmahaḥ nāma aṣṭakena viśvātmā viśvātmānam mahā mune uvāca śarvāya kṣiti rūpāya sadā surabhine namaḥ īśāya vāyave tubhyam saṃsparśāya namaḥ namaḥ paśūnām pataye ca eva pāvakāya ati tejase bhīmāya vyoma rūpāya śabda mātrāya te namaḥ mahādevāya somāya amṛtāya namaḥ astu te yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api paitāḥ maham imam stavam rudrāya kathitam viprān śrāvayet vā samāhitaḥ aṣṭamūrteḥ tu sāyujyam varṣāt ekāt avāpnuyāt evam stutvā mahādevam mavaikṣata pitāmahaḥ tadā aṣṭadhā mahādevaḥ samātiṣṭhat samantataḥ tadā prakāśate bhānuḥ kṛṣṇavartmā niśākaraḥ kṣitiḥ vāyuḥ pumān ambhaḥ suṣiram sarvagam tathā tadā prabhṛti tam prāhṛ raṣṭamūrtiḥ iti īśvaram aṣṭamūrteḥ prasādena virañciḥ ca asṛjat punar brahmā punar kalpa antare prabhuḥ prajāḥ sraṣṭu manāḥ tepe tatas ugram tapaḥ mahat tatas dīrghena kālena duḥkhāt krodhaḥ vyajāyata krodha āviṣṭasya netrābhyām prāpatan aśru bindavaḥ sarvān tān agrajān dṛṣṭvā bhūta preta niśācarān jahau prāṇān ca bhagavān krodha āviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ tatas prāṇa mayaḥ rudraḥ prādurāsīt prabhoḥ mukhāt bhūtvā bāla arka sadṛśa dyutiḥ ardhena aṃśena sarvātmā sasarja asau śivām umām sā ca asṛjat tadā lakṣmīm durgām śreṣṭhām sarasvatīm vāmām raudrīm mahāmāyām vaiṣṇavīm vārija īkṣaṇām malām vikariṇīm ca eva kālīm kamala vāsinīm devīm balapramathinīm tathā tathā anyāḥ bahavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ stayā nāryaḥ sahasraśas sarvātmanaḥ ca tasya agre hi atiṣṭhat parameśvaraḥ ghṛṇī dadau punar prāṇān brahma putraḥ maheśvaraḥ brahmaṇaḥ pradadau prāṇān ātma sthān tu tadā prabhuḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ bhūt tatas rudraḥ kiñcid pratyāgata āsavam abhyabhāṣata deveśaḥ brahmānam paramam vacaḥ mā bhaiḥ deva mahābhāga viriñca jagantām guro mayā iha sthāpitāḥ prāmāḥ tasmāt uttiṣṭha vai prabhā pitāmahaḥ prasanna ātmā netraiḥ phulla ambuja prabhaiḥ tatas pratyāgata prāṇaḥ samudaikṣat maheśvaram saḥ udvīkṣya ciram kālam snigdha gambhīrayā girā uvāca bhagavān brahmā samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ kaḥ bhavān aṣṭamūrdiḥ vai sthitaḥ ekādaśa ātmakaḥ uvāca tasya tat vacanam śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ spṛśan karābhyām brahmāṇam sukhābhyām sa surāri hā uvāca mām viddhi paramātmāna mā enām māyām ajām iti ete vai saṃsthitāḥ rudrāḥ tvām rakṣitum iha āgatāḥ kṛtām jali puṭaḥ bhūtvā harṣa gadgadayā girā saṃsārān moktum īśāna mām iha arhasi śaṃkara mṛtyu hīnaḥ pumān viddhi sa mṛtyuḥ padamjaḥ pi saḥ kintu deveśvaraḥ rudraḥ prasīdati yadi īśvaraḥ mayā ca viṣṇunā ca eva brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā uvāca evam vyāhṛtya vipra indram anugṛhya ca tam ghṛṇī iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge indra vākyam nāmaka catvāraśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca gate puṇye ca vara de sahasrākṣe śilā aśanaḥ mahādevam tapasā atoṣayat bhavam divyam varṣa sahasram tu gatam kṣaṇam iva adbhutam valmīkena āvṛta aṅgaḥ ca lakṣyaḥ kīṭa gaṇaiḥ muniḥ vajrasūcī mukhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ rakta kīṭaiḥ ca sarvatas ca asthi śeṣaḥ abhavat paścāt tam amanyata śaṃkaraḥ yadā spṛṣṭaḥ muniḥ tena kareṇa ca smarāriṇā tapataḥ tasya tapasā prabhuḥ tuṣṭā atha śaṅkaraḥ tuṣṭaḥ tava iti atha uvāca sa gaṇaḥ ca umayā saha dadāmi putram sarvajñam sarva śāstra artha pāragam tatas praṇamya deveśam stutvā uvāca śilāśanaḥ harṣa gadgadayā vācā somam soma vibhūṣaṇam uvāca uvāca pūrvam ārādhitaḥ prāha tapasā parameśvaraḥ śilādam brahmaṇā rudraḥ prītya paramayā punar uvāca pūrvam ārādhitaḥ vipra brahmaṇā aham tapodhana tapasā ca avatāra artham munibhiḥ ca sura uttamaiḥ evam uktvā munim prekṣya praṇipatya sthitam ghṛṇī yajña aṅgaṇam mahat prāpya yajña artham yajña vittamaḥ tad aṅgaṇāt aham śaṃbhoḥ tanujaḥ tasya ca ājñayā saṃjātaḥ pūrvam eva aham yuga anta agni sama prabhaḥ vavarṣuḥ tadā puṣkarāvartaka ādyāḥ jaguḥ khecarāḥ kinnarāḥ siddhasādhyāḥ mayi upendraḥ sasarja atha vṛṣṭim supuṣpa ogha miśrām mām dṛṣṭvā kālasūrya ābham jaṭā mukuṭa dhāriṇam tryakṣam catur bhujam bālam śūla ṭaṅka gadā dharam vajriṇam vajradaṃṣṭram ca vajriṇā ārādhitam śiśum brahma ādyāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve sura indraḥ ca muni īśvarāḥ neduḥ samantataḥ sarve nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ muni śārdūla ṛc yajuḥ sāma saṃbhavaiḥ mantraiḥ māheśvaraiḥ stutvā saṃpraṇemuḥ mudā anvitāḥ brahmā hariḥ ca rudraḥ ca śakraḥ sākṣāt śivā ambikā jīvaḥ ca induḥ mahā tejāḥ bhāskaraḥ pavana unalaḥ īśānaḥ nirṛtiḥ yakṣaḥ yamaḥ varuṇaḥ eva ca viśvedevāḥ tathā rudrāḥ vasavaḥ ca mahā balāḥ lakṣmī sākṣāt śajī jyeṣṭhā devī ca eva sarasvatī aditiḥ ca ditiḥ ca eva śraddhā lajjā dhṛtiḥ tathā nandā bhadrā ca surabhī suśīlā sumanāḥ tathā vṛṣa indraḥ ca mahā tejāḥ dharmaḥ dharma ātmajaḥ tathā āvṛtya mām tathā āliṅgya tuṣṭuvuḥ muni sattama śilādaḥ api muniḥ dṛṣṭvā pitā mama tādṛśam tadā prītyā praṇamya puṇya ātmā tuṣṭāva iṣṭa pradam sutam uvāca putraḥ asi jagatām yasmāt trātā duḥkhāt hi kim punar tvayā aham nanditaḥ yasmāt nandī nāmnā sureśvara tasmāt nandaya mām nandin namāmi jagat īśvaram pitāmahāḥ ca bho nandin avatīrṇe maheśvare avatīrṇe sute nandīn rakṣā artham mahyam īśvara te namaḥ sureśāna nandīśvara namaḥ astu te putra tvam eva nandīśa matvā yat kīrtitam mayā yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api mama putra prabhāṣitam śrāvayet vā dvijān bhaktyā mayā sārdham sa modate evam stutvā sutam bālam praṇamya bahu mānāt muni īśvarān ca saṃprekṣya śilādā uvāca suvrataḥ paśyadhvam munayaḥ sarve mahābhāgyam mama avyayaḥ nandī yajña aṅgaṇe devaḥ ca avatīrṇaḥ yatas prabhuḥ mad samaḥ kaḥ pumān loke devaḥ vā dānavaḥ api vā eṣa nandī yatas jātaḥ yajña bhūmau hitāya mama iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge nandikeraśvarotpattiḥ nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca mayā saha pitā hṛṣṭaḥ praṇamya ca maheśvaram uṭajam svam jagāma āśu nidhim labdhvā iva nirdhanaḥ yadā āgatā ūham uṭajam śilādasya mahā mune tadā vai daivikam rūpam tyaktvā mānuṣya mā āsthitaḥ naṣṭā ca eva smṛtiḥ divyā yena kena api kāraṇāt mānuṣyam āsthitam dṛṣṭvā pitā me loka pūjitaḥ vilalāpa ati duḥkha ārtaḥ sva janaiḥ ca samāvṛtaḥ śālaṅkāyana putraḥ vai śilādaḥ putra vatsalaḥ upadiṣṭāḥ hi tena eva ṛk śākhāḥ yajuṣaḥ tathā samā śākhā sahasram ca sa aṅga upāṅgam mahā mune āyurvedam dhanurvedam gāndharvam ca aśva lakṣaṇam hastinām caritam ca eva narāṇām ca eva lakṣaṇam tasya āśramam gatau divyau draṣṭu mām ca ājñayā vibhoḥ ūcatuḥ ca mahātmanau mām nirīkṣya muhur muhur tāta nandī ayam alpa āyūḥ sarva śāstra artha pāragaḥ na dṛṣṭam evam āścaryam āyuḥ varṣāt atas param samāliṅgya ca duḥkha ārtaḥ ruroda atīva visvaram tasya ca ārta svaram śrutvā tad āśrama nivāsinaḥ nipetuḥ vihvala atyartham rakṣāḥ cakruḥ ca maṅgalam tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mahādeva tryambakam umāpatim dūrvām ayuta saṃkhyātām dravya samanvitām pitā vigata saṃjñaḥ ca tathā ca eva pitāmahaḥ viceṣṭaḥ ca lalāpa asau mṛta vat nipapāta ca mṛta vat patitam sākṣāt pitaram ca pitāmaham pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca tam rudra jāpya rataḥ abhavam hṛd puṇḍarīke suṣire dhyātvā devam tryambakam tryakṣam daśa bhujam śāntam pañcavaktram sadāśivam saritaḥ ca antare puṇye sthitam mām parameśvaraḥ tuṣṭaḥ bravīt mahādevaḥ sa umaḥ soma ardha bhūṣaṇaḥ vatsa nandīt mahā bāho mṛtyoḥ bhītiḥ kutas te na asti eva daivikam dṛṣṭam śilādena purā tava saṃsārasya śvabhāvaḥ iyam sukham duḥkham punar punar nṛṇām yoni parityāgaḥ sarvathā eva vivekinaḥ evam uktvā tu mām sākṣāt sarva deva mahā īśvaraḥ yad karābhyām su śubhābhyām ca ubhābhyām parameśvaraḥ uvāca ca mahādevaḥ tuṣṭa ātmā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ nirīkṣya gaṇapān ca eva devīm himavantaḥ sutām samālokya ca tuṣṭa ātmā mahādevaḥ sureśvaraḥ akṣayaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca eva sa pitā sa suhṛd janaḥ mama iṣṭaḥ gaṇapaḥ ca eva mad vīryaḥ mad parākramaḥ mama sadā ca eva mama pārśva gataḥ sadā evam uktvā ca mām devaḥ bhagavant sa gaṇaḥ tadā kuśeśaya mayīm mālām samunmucya ātmanaḥ tadā mahā tejāḥ mama devaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ tayā aham mālayā jātaḥ śubhayā kaṇṭha saktayā tryakṣaḥ daśa bhujaḥ ca eva dvitīyam iva śaṃkaraḥ tatas jaṭā āśritam vāri gṛhītvā ca ati nirmalam tatas sā divya toyā ca pūrṇa asita jalā śubhā tām āha ca mahādevaḥ nadīm parama śobhanām yasmāt jaṭā udakāt eva pravṛttā tvam mahā nadī tasmāt jaṭodakā puṇyā bhaviṣyasi sarit varā tatas devyāḥ mahādevaḥ śilāda tanayam prabhuḥ sā mām āghrāya śirasi pāṇibhyām parimārjatī payasā śaṅkha gaureṇa devadevam nirīkṣya sā tāni srotāṃsi trīṇi asyāḥ srotasvinyaḥ bhavan tadā trisrotasam nadīm dṛṣṭvā vṛṣaḥ parama harṣitaḥ vṛṣadhvaniḥ iti khyātā devadevena sā nadī jāmbūnada mayam citram sarva ratna mayam śubham svam devaḥ ca adbhutam divyam nirmitam viśvakarmaṇā mukuṭam ca ābabandha īśaḥ mama mūrdhani vṛṣadhvajaḥ kuṇḍale ca śubhe divye vajra vaiḍūrya bhūṣite mām tathā abhyarcitam vyomnaḥ dṛṣṭvā mavaiḥ prabhākaraḥ megha aṃbhasā ca abhyaṣiñcat śilādana mayaḥ mune tasya abhiṣiktasya tadā pravṛtta srotasā bhṛśam yasmāt suvarṇāt naḥ sṛtya nadī eṣā saṃpravartate jāmbūnada mayāt yasmāt dvitīyā mukuṭāt śubhā prāvartata nadī puṇyā ūvuḥ jaṃbūnadī iti tām yaḥ pañcanadam āsādya snātvā japya īśvara īśvaram pūjayet śiva sāyujyam nayāti eva na saṃśayaḥ devīm uvāca śarvāṇīm umām girisutām ajām devī nandīśvaram devam abhiṣiñcāmi bhūtapam gaṇa indram vyāhariṣyāmi kim vā tvam manyase avyaye tasya tat vacanam śrutvā bhavānī harṣita ānanā tatas sa bhagavant śarvaḥ sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ sasmāra gaṇapān divyān devadevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge nandikeśvaraprādurbhāvanandikeśvarābhiṣekamantraḥ nāma tricatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca smaraṇāt eva rudrasya saṃprāptāḥ ca gaṇeśvarāḥ sarve sahasra hastāḥ ca sahasra āyudha pāṇayaḥ tri netrāḥ ca mahātmānaḥ tridaśaiḥ api vanditāḥ koṭi kālāgni saṃkāśāḥ jaṭā mukuṭa dhāriṇaḥ daṃṣṭra karāla vadanāḥ nityāḥ buddhāḥ ca nirmalāḥ gaṇaiḥ tulyaiḥ ātmanā ca gaṇeśvarāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ mahātmānaḥ tatra ājagmuḥ mudā yutāḥ gāyantaḥ ca dravantaḥ ca nṛtyantaḥ ca mahā balāḥ mukha āḍambara vādyāni vādayantaḥ tathā eva ca rathaiḥ nāgaiḥ hayaiḥ ca eva siṃha markaṭa vāhanāḥ vimāneṣu tathā ārūḍhāḥ hema citreṣu vai gaṇāḥ bherī mṛdaṅgaka ādyaiḥ ca paṇava ānaka gomukhaiḥ vāditraiḥ vividhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ paṭahaiḥ eka puṣkaraiḥ bherī muraja saṃnādaiḥ āḍambaraka ḍiṇḍimaiḥ mardalaiḥ veṇu vīṇābhiḥ vividhaiḥ tāla niḥsvanaiḥ mahā yogāḥ ājagmuḥ deva saṃsadam te gaṇeśāḥ mahāsattvāḥ sarva deva īśvara īśvarāḥ ca smṛtāḥ devaḥ ājñāpaya mahā dyute kim sāgarān śoṣayāmaḥ yamam vā saha kiṅkaraiḥ saha devaiḥ ca saha viṣṇum ca vāyunā ānayāmaḥ su saṃkruddhāḥ daityān vā saha dānavaiḥ kasya adya vyasanam ghoram kariṣyāmaḥ te ājñayā tān tathāvādinaḥ sarvān gaṇeśān sarva saṃmatān uvāca devaḥ saṃpūjya koṭi koṭi śatān prabhuḥ śṛṇudhvam yatkṛte yūyam iha āhūtāḥ jagat hitāḥ śrutvā ca prayata ātmānaḥ kurudhvam tat aśaṅkitāḥ nandī īśvaraḥ ayam putraḥ naḥ sarveṣām īśvara īśvaraḥ vipraḥ yam nāyakaḥ ca eva senānīḥ vaḥ samṛddhimān tam imam mama saṃdeśāt yūyam sarve api saṃmatāḥ senānyam abhiṣiñcadhvam mahā yoga patim patim evam astu iti saṃmantrya saṃbhārān āharan tatas tasya sarva āśrayam divyam jāmbūnada mayam śubham meru saṃkāśam manoharam upāharan muktā dāma avalambam ca maṇi ratna avabhāsitam staṃbhaiḥ ca vaiḍurya mayaiḥ kiṅkiṇī jāla saṃvṛtam cāru ratnaka saṃyuktam maṇḍapam viśvatomukham tasya agratas pāda pīṭham nīla vajra ava bhāsitam cakruḥ pāda pratiṣṭhā artham kalaśau ca asya pārśva gau saṃpūrṇau parama ambhobhiḥ aravinda āvṛta ānanau kalaśānām sahasram tu sauvarṇam rājatam tathā tāmra jam mṛd mayam ca eva sarva tīrtha abu pūritam keyūre kuṇḍale ca eva mukuṭam hāram eva ca chatram śata śalākam ca vāla vyajanam eva ca hattam mahātmanā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā śaṅkha hāra aṅga gaureṇa pṛṣṭhena api virājitam vyajanam candra śubhram ca hema daṇḍam su cāmaram mukuṭam kāñcanam ca eva nirmitam viśvakarmaṇā jāmbūnada mayam sūtram keyūra dvayam eva ca saṃbhārāṇi tathā anyāni vividhāni bahūni api samantāt ninyuḥ avyagrāḥ gaṇapāḥ deva saṃmatāḥ tatas devāḥ ca sa indrāḥ ca nārāyaṇa mukhāḥ tathā devaiḥ ca lokāḥ sarve te tatas jagmuḥ mudā yutāḥ teṣu āgateṣu sarveṣu bhagavant parameśvaraḥ cakāra sarvam bhagavān abhiṣekam samāhitaḥ tatas viṣṇuḥ tatas śakraḥ lokapālāḥ tathā eva ca abhyaṣiñcanta vidhivat gaṇendram śiva śāsanāt ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca eva pitā maha purogamāḥ śirasi añjalim ādāya tuṣṭāva ca samāhitaḥ prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā jaya śabdam cakāra ca tatas gaṇādhipāḥ sarve tatas devāḥ tatas asurāḥ udvāhaḥ ca kṛtaḥ tatra niyogāt parameṣṭhinaḥ marutām ca sutā devī suyaśā ākhyā babhūva yā labdham śaśi prabham chatram tayā tatra vibhūṣitam cāmare cāmara āsakta hasta agraiḥ strī gaṇaiḥ yutā siṃhāsanam ca paramam tayā ca adhiṣṭhitam mayā alaṅkṛtā mahā lakṣmyā mukuṭa ādyaiḥ subhūṣaṇaiḥ labdhaḥ hāraḥ ca paramaḥ devyāḥ kaṇṭha gataḥ tathā vṛṣa indraḥ ca sitaḥ nāgaḥ siṃhaḥ siṃha dhvajaḥ tathā adya api sadṛśaḥ kaścid mayā na asti vibhuḥ kvacid sa anvayam ca gṛhītvā īśaḥ tathā saṃbandhi bāndhavaiḥ mayā devyā gataḥ śivaḥ tadā devīm bhavam dṛṣṭvā mayā ca prārthayan gaṇaiḥ muni devarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ ājñām pāśupatām dvijāḥ atha ājñām pradadau teṣām arhāṇām ajñayā vibhoḥ nandikaḥ nagajā bhartuḥ teṣām pāśupatām śubhām tasmāt hi munayaḥ labdhvā tad ājñām muni puṃgavāt bhādau kuryāt namaskāram tad ante śiva tām vrajet iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge nandikeśvarābhiṣekaḥ nāma catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ uvāca bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar mahaḥ ca eva janaḥ sākṣāt tapaḥ tathā satya lokaḥ ca pātālam naraka arṇava koṭayaḥ tārakā graha soma arkāḥ dhruvaḥ saptarṣayaḥ tathā vaimānikāḥ tathā anye ca tiṣṭhanti asya prasādāt anena nirmitāḥ tu evam tad ātmānaḥ dvijarṣabhāḥ sama aṣṭi rūpaḥ sarvātmā saṃsthitaḥ sarvadā śivaḥ sarvātmānam mahātmānam mahādevam maheśvaram na vijānanti saṃmūḍhāḥ māyayā tasya mohitāḥ tasmāt praṇamya tam vakṣye jagatām nirṇayam śubham purā vaḥ kathitam sarvam mayā aṇḍasya yathā kṛtiḥ bhuvanānām svarūpam ca brahmāṇḍe kathayāmi aham tapaḥ satyam ca saptā ete lokāḥ tu aṇḍa udbhavāḥ śubhāḥ adhastāt atra ca eteṣām dvijāḥ sapta talāni tu mahātala ādayaḥ teṣām adhastāt narakāḥ kramāt nṛpeṇa balinā ca eva pātāla svarga vāsinā śailam rasātalam viprāḥ śārkaram hi talātalam kṣmāyāḥ tu yāvat vistāraḥ hi adhas teṣām ca suvratāḥ talānām ca eva sarveṣām tāvat saṃkhyā samāhitā lakṣam sapta sahasram hi talānām sa ghanasya tu vyomnaḥ pramāṇam mūlam tu triṃśat sāhasrakeṇa tu suvarṇena muni śreṣṭhāḥ tathā vāsukinā śubham rasātalam ati khyātam tathā anyaiḥ ca pūrvadevaiḥ samākīrṇam sutalam ca tathā aparaiḥ vitalam dānava ādyaiḥ ca tārakā agni mukhaiḥ tathā mahānta ka ādyaiḥ nāgaiḥ ca grahlādena asureṇa ca vitalam ca atra vikhyātam kambala aśva niṣevitam mahākumbhena vīreṇa hayagrīveṇa dhīmatā saṃkukarṇena saṃbhinnam tathā namuci pūrvakaiḥ taleṣu teṣu sarveṣu ca aṃbayā parameśvaraḥ skandena sārdham gaṇapaiḥ sarvatas vṛtaḥ talānām ca eva sarveṣām ūrdhvatas sapta saptamāḥ talāni dharā ca api saptadhā kathayāmi vaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge pātālavarṇanam nāma pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sapta dvīpā tathā pṛthvī nadī parvata saṃkulā jambuḥ plakṣaḥ śālmaliḥ ca kuśaḥ krauñcaḥ tathā eva ca śākaḥ puṣkara nāmā ca dvīpāḥ tu abyantare kramāt sapta dvīpeṣu sarveṣu sa ambaḥ sarva gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ nānā veṣa dharaḥ bhūtvā sāṃnidhyam kurute haraḥ kṣāroda ikṣurasodaḥ ca surodaḥ ca ghṛta udadhiḥ dadhi arṇavaḥ ca kṣīrodaḥ svādūdaḥ ca api anukramāt samudreṣu iha sarveṣu sarvadā sa gaṇaḥ śivaḥ jala rūpī bhavaḥ śrīmān krīḍate ca ūrmi bāhubhiḥ kṣīrārṇava amṛtam iva sadā kṣīrārṇave hariḥ śete śiva jñāna adhiyā sākṣāt vai yoganidrayā tena eva sṛṣṭam akhilam dhṛtam rakṣitam eva ca saṃhṛtam devadevasya prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ suṣeṇāḥ iti vikhyātāḥ yajante puruṣa ṛṣabham aniruddham muni śreṣṭhāḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam ye ca aniruddham puruṣam dhyāyanti ātma vidām varāḥ nārāyaṇa samāḥ sarve sarva sampad samanvitāḥ vālakhilyāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca mitrāvaruṇakau tathā sapta dvīpeṣu tiṣṭhanti nānā śṛṅgāḥ mahā udayāḥ dharāyāḥ patayaḥ ca āsan bahavaḥ kāla gauravāt sāmarthyāt parama īśānāḥ krauñcāreḥ janakāt prabhoḥ manvantareṣu sarveṣu atīta anāgateṣu iha pravakṣyāmi dharā īśān vaḥ vakṣye svāyaṃbhuventare manvantareṣu sarveṣu atīta anāgateṣu ca svāyaṃbhuvasya ca manoḥ pautrāḥ tu āsan mahā balāḥ priyavrata ātmajāḥ vīrāḥ te daśā iha prakīrtitāḥ medhāḥ medhātithiḥ vasuḥ jambūdvīpa īśvaram cakre āgnīdhram su mahā balam plakṣadvīpa īśvaraḥ ca api tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ śālmaleḥ ca vapuṣmantam rājānam abhiṣiktavān jyotiṣmantam kuśadvīpe rājānam kṛtavan nṛpaḥ dyutimantam ca rājānam kraiñcadvīpe samādiśat śākadvīpa īśvaram ca api havyam cakre priyavrataḥ puṣkara adhipatim cakre savanam ca api suvratāḥ mahāvītam smṛtam varṣam tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ nāmnā tu dhātakeḥ ca eva dhātakīkhaṇḍam ucyate havyaḥ api ajanayat putrān śākadvīpa īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ jaladam ca kumāram ca sukumāram maṇīcakam kumārasya tu kaumāram dvitīyam parikīrtitam sukumāram tṛtīyam tu sukumārasya kīrtyate modakam ca api modākeḥ varṣam ṣaṣṭham prakīrtitam teṣām tu nāmabhiḥ stāni sapta varṣāṇi tatra vai kuśalaḥ manugaḥ ca uṣṇaḥ pīvaraḥ ca andhakārakaḥ teṣām sva nāmabhiḥ deśāḥ kraiñcadvīpa āśrayāḥ śubhāḥ uṣṇasya uṣṇaḥ smṛtaḥ deśaḥ paviraḥ ca andhakārasya kathitaḥ deśaḥ nāmnā andha kārakaḥ ete janapadāḥ sapta krauca dvīpeṣu bhāsvarāḥ udbhidaḥ veṇumant ca eva dvairathaḥ lavaṇaḥ dhṛtiḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākaraḥ ca api saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ udbhidam prathamam varṣam dvitīyam veṇumaṇḍalam tṛtīyam dvairatham ca eva caturtham lavaṇam smṛtam pañcamam dhṛtimat ṣaṣṭham prabhākaram anuttamam śālmalasya īśvarāḥ sapta sutāḥ te vai vapuṣmantaḥ śvetaḥ ca haritaḥ ca eva jīmūtaḥ rohitaḥ tathā śvetasya deśaḥ śvetaḥ tu haritasya ca hāritaḥ suprabhaḥ suprabhasya api sapta vai deśalān śakāḥ plakṣadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi jambūdvīpāt anantaram sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpa īśvarāḥ nṛpāḥ jyeṣṭha śāntabhayaḥ teṣām sapta varṣāṇi tāni vai mahā ānandaḥ ca śivaḥ ca eva kṣemakaḥ ca dhruvaḥ tathā tāni teṣām tu nāmāni sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśas niveśitāni taiḥ tāni pūrvam varṇa āśrama ācāra yutāḥ prajāḥ tatra niveśitāḥ plakṣadvīpa ādi varṣeṣu śākadvīpa antikeṣu vai jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmaḥ vai varṇa āśrama vibhāgaśaḥ sukham āyuḥ svarūpam ca balam dharmaḥ dvijottamāḥ pañcasu eteṣu dvīpeṣu sarva sādhāraṇam smṛtam rudra arcana ratāḥ nityam maheśvara parāyaṇāḥ anye ca puṣkaradvīpe prajātāḥ ca prajeśvarāḥ prajāpateḥ ca rudrasya bhāva amṛta sukha utkaṭāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bhuvanakośe dvīpadvīpeśvarakathanam nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ āgnīdhram jyeṣṭha dāya aham kāmya putram mahā balam priyavrataḥ abhyaṣiñcat vai jambūdvīpa īśvaram nṛpaḥ sa utīva bhava bhaktaḥ ca tapasvī taruṇaḥ sadā bhava arcana rataḥ śrīmān gomān dhīmān dvijarṣabhāḥ sarve māheśvarāḥ ca eva mahādeva parāyaṇāḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ nābhiḥ iti khyātaḥ tasya kiṃpuruṣaḥ anujaḥ harivarṣaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu caturthaḥ vai tu ilāvṛtaḥ kuruḥ tu saptamaḥ teṣām bhadrāśvaḥ tu aṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ navamaḥ ketumālaḥ tu teṣām deśān nibodhata nābheḥ tu dakṣiṇam varṣam hema ākhyam tu pitā dadau hemakūṭam tu yat varṣam dadau kiṃpuruṣāya saḥ naiṣayam yat smṛtam varṣam haraye tat pitā dadau nīla acala āśritam varṣam ramyāya pradadau pitā śvetam yat uttaram tasmāt pitrā dattam hiraṇmate yat uttaram śṛṅga varṣam pitā tat kurave dadau varṣam mālyavatam ca api bhadrāśvasya nyavedayat gandhamādana varṣam tu ketumālāya dattavan iti etāni mahānti iha nava varṣāṇi bhāgaśas āgnīdhraḥ teṣu varṣeṣu putrān tān abhiṣicya vai svādhyāya nirataḥ paścāt śiva dhyāna rataḥ tu abhūt yāni kiṃpuruṣa ādyāni varṣāṇi aṣṭau śubhāni ca teṣām svabhāvataḥ siddhiḥ sukha prāyā hi ayatnatas dharma adharmau na teṣu āstām na uttama adhama madhyamāḥ na teṣu asti yuga avasthā kṣetreṣu aṣṭasu sarvatas rudra kṣetre mṛtāḥ ca eva jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarāḥ tathā bhaktāḥ prāsaṅgikāḥ ca api teṣu kṣetreṣu yānti te teṣām hitāya rudreṇa ca aṣṭakṣetram vinirmitam tatra teṣām mahādevaḥ sāṃnidhyam kurute sadā dṛṣṭvā hṛdi mahādevam aṣṭakṣetra nivāsinaḥ sukhinaḥ sarvadā teṣām saḥ eva iha parā gatiḥ mahā pārthiva śreṣṭham sarva kṣatrasya pūjitam ṛṣabhāt bharataḥ jajñe vīraḥ putra śata agrajaḥ saḥ abhiṣicya atha ṛṣabhaḥ bharatam putra vatsalaḥ sarva ātmanā ātmani sthāpya paramātmānam īśvaram nagnaḥ jaṭī cīrī dhvānta gataḥ hi saḥ nirāśaḥ tyakta saṃdehaḥ śaivam āpa param padam himādreḥ dakṣiṇam varṣam bharatāya nyavedayat tasmāt tu bhāratam varṣam tasya nāmnā viduḥ budhāḥ babhūba tasmin tat rājyam bharataḥ saṃnyaveśayat mita śrīkaḥ vanam rājā viveśa saḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bharatavarṣakathanam nāma saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ nānā ratna mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sthitaḥ sthitimatām varaḥ catura aśīti sāhasram utsedhena prakīrtitaḥ praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt viṃstṛtaḥ ṣoḍaśa eva tu śarava vat saṃsthita tvāt dvātriṃśat mūrdhni vistṛtaḥ triguṇaḥ ca asya pariṇāhaḥ nu maṇḍalaḥ haimīkṛtaḥ maheśasya śubha aṅga sparśanena ca dhattūra puṣpa saṃkāśaḥ sarva deva niketanaḥ krīḍā bhūmiḥ ca devānām anekāḥ carya saṃyutaḥ lakṣa yojanaḥ āyāmaḥ tasya evam tu mahā gireḥ tatas ṣoḍaśa sāhasram yojanāni kṣiteḥ adhas śeṣam ca u apari vipra indrāḥ dharāyāḥ tasya śṛṅgiṇaḥ mūla āyāma pramāṇam tu vistārāt mūlataḥ gireḥ ūcuḥ vistāram asya eva dviguṇam mūlatas gireḥ pūrvatas padmarāga ābhaḥ dakṣiṇe hema sannibhaḥ amarāvatī pūrva bhāge nānā prāsāda saṃkulā nānā deva gaṇaiḥ kīrṇā maṇi jāla samāvṛtā saṃlāpa ālāpa kuśalaiḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaiḥ strī sahasraiḥ samākīrṇā ca apsarobhiḥ samantataḥ dīrghikābhiḥ vicitrābhiḥ phulla ambhoruha saṃkulaiḥ evaṃvidhaiḥ taṭākaiḥ ca nadībhiḥ ca nadaiḥ yutā mahī virājate purī śubhrā tayā asau parvataḥ śubhaḥ tejasvinī nāma purī āgneyyām pāvakasya tu vaivasvatī dakṣiṇe tu yamasya yaminām varāḥ bhavanaiḥ āvṛtā divyaiḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ śubhaiḥ nairṛte kṛṣṇa varṇā ca tathā suddhavatī śubhā tādṛśā gandhavantī ca vāyavyām diśi śobhanā mahodayā ca uttare ca eśānyām tu yaśovatī brahma viṣṇu maheśānām niketanam sahasra bhaumam vistīrṇam vimānam vāmanaḥ sthitam tasmin mahā bhujaḥ śarvaḥ soma sūrya agni locanaḥ siṃhāsane maṇi maye devyā āste ṣaṇmukhena ca teṣām teṣām vimāneṣu divyeṣu vividheṣu ca īśānyām īśvara kṣetre nitya arcā ca vyavasthitā siddha īśvaraiḥ ca bhagavān śailādiḥ śiṣya saṃmataḥ sanatkumāraḥ siddhaiḥ tu sukha āsīnaḥ sureśvaraḥ sanakaḥ ca sanandaḥ ca sadṛśāḥ ca sahasraśas bāla sūrya pratīkāśam vimānam tatra śobhanam śailādeḥ śubham ca asti tasmin āste gaṇeśvaraḥ ṣaṇmukhasya gaṇeśasya gaṇānām tu sahasraśas suyaśāyāḥ sunetrāyāḥ mātṝṇām madanasya ca tasya jaṃbūnadī nāma mūlam āveṣṭya saṃsthitā tasya dakṣiṇa pārśve tu jaṃbu vṛkṣaḥ su śobhanaḥ meroḥ samantāt vistīrṇam śubham varṣam ilāvṛtam tatra jambu phala āhārāḥ kecid ca amṛta bhojanāḥ jāṃbūnada sama prakhyāḥ nānā varṇāḥ ca bhoginaḥ meru pāda āśritaḥ viprāḥ dvīpaḥ yam madhyamaḥ śubhaḥ nava varṣa anvitaḥ ca eva nadīnada gīriśvaraiḥ nava varṣam tu vakṣyāmi jambūdvīpam yata atatham hi saṃvidam maṇḍalāt ca eva yojanaiḥ ca nibodhata iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge aṣṭacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śatam ekam sahasrāṇām yojanānām sa tu smṛtaḥ anudvīpam sahasrāṇām dviguṇam dviguṇa uttaram pañcāśat koṭi vistīrṇā sa samudrā dharā smṛtā dvīpaiḥ ca saptabhiḥ yuktā loka aloka āvṛtā śubhā śṛṅgī tasya uttare viprāḥ trayaḥ te varṣaparvatāḥ jaṭharaḥ devakūṭaḥ ca pūrvasyām diśi parvatau niṣadhaḥ dakṣiṇe meroḥ tasya dakṣiṇatas giriḥ hemakūṭaḥ iti khyātaḥ himavant tasya dakṣiṇe mālyavant gandhamādaḥ ca dvau etau uda gāyatau ete parvata rājānaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ teṣām antara viṣkaṃbhaḥ nava sāhasram ekaśas idam haimavatam varṣam bhāratam nāma viśrutam hemakūṭam param tasmāt nāmnā kiṃpuruṣam smṛtam naiṣadham hemakūṭāt tu harivarṣam tat ucyate harivarṣāt param ca eva meroḥ śubham ilāvṛtam ilāvṛtāt param nīlam ramyakam nāma viśrutam ramyāt parataram śvetam vikhyātam tat hiraṇmayam hiraṇmayāt param ca api śṛṅgī ca eva kuruḥ smṛtaḥ dīrghāṇi tatra catvārī madhyatas tat ilāvṛtam meroḥ paścima pūrveṇa dve tu dīrghe tare smṛte vedyardhe dakṣiṇe trīṇi varṣāṇi trīṇi ca uttare udak āyataḥ mahā śailaḥ mālyavān nāma parvataḥ yojanānām sahasre dve upariṣṭāt tu vistṛtaḥ prakīrtitaḥ tasya pratīcyām vijñeyaḥ parvataḥ gandhamādanaḥ āyāmataḥ sa vijñeyaḥ mālyavān iva vistṛtaḥ prāc āyatāḥ su parvāṇaḥ ṣaṭ ete varṣaparvatāḥ avagāḍhāḥ ca ubhayatas samudrau pūrva paścimau taruṇa āditya saṃkāśaḥ hauraṇyaḥ niṣadhaḥ smṛtaḥ catur varṇaḥ sa sauvarṇaḥ meruḥ ca ūrdhva āyataḥ smṛtaḥ vṛtta ākṛti parīṇāhaḥ cāturasraḥ samutthitaḥ nīlaḥ ca vaiḍūrya mayaḥ śvetaḥ śuklaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ mayūra barha varṇaḥ tu śātakumbhaḥ triśṛṅgavant evam saṃkṣepāt proktāḥ punar śṛṇu giri īśvarān mandaraḥ devakūṭaḥ ca pūrvasyām diśi parvatau pūrvatas ca āyatau etau arṇava antar vyavasthitau niṣadhaḥ pāriyātraḥ ca dvau etau vara parvatau yathā pūrvau tathā yāmyau etau paścimatas śritau pūrvatas ca āyatau etau arṇava antar vyavasthitau maryādāparvatān etān aṣṭau āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ yaḥ asau meruḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prāṃśuḥ kanakaparvataḥ tasya pādāḥ tu catvāraḥ catur dikṣu naga uttamāḥ yaiḥ viṣṭabdhā na calati sapta dvīpavatī mahī daśa yojana sāhasram āyāmaḥ teṣu paṭhyate pūrve tu mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaḥ ca uttare smṛtaḥ mahā vṛkṣāḥ samutpannāḥ catvāraḥ dvīpa ketavaḥ mandarasya gireḥ śṛṅge mahā vṛkṣaḥ sa ketu rāj pralamba śākhā śikharaḥ kadambaḥ caitya pādapaḥ dakṣiṇasya api śailasya śikhare deva sevitā jaṃbūḥ sadā puṇya phalā sadā mālya upa śobhitā sa ketuḥ dakṣime dvīpe jambuḥ lokeṣu viśrutā saṃjātaḥ śikhare aśvatthaḥ sa mahān caitya pādapaḥ supārśvasya uttarasya api śṛṅge jātaḥ mahā drumaḥ teṣām caturṇām vakṣyāmi śailendrāṇām yata ākramam amānuṣyāṇi ramyāṇi sarva kāla ṛtukāni ca manoharāṇi catvāri deva krīḍanakāni ca mitreśvaram tu pūrve tu ṣaṣṭheśvaram atas param mahā sarāṃsi ca tathā catvāri muni puṃgavāḥ aruṇodam saraḥ pūrvam dakṣiṇam mānasam smṛtam śākhasya dakṣiṇe kṣetram viśākhasya ca paścime aruṇodasya pūrveṇa śailendrāḥ nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ tān tu saṃkṣepataḥ vakṣye na śakyam vistareṇa tu sitāntaḥ ca kuraṇḍaḥ ca kuraraḥ ca acala uttamaḥ vikaraḥ maṇiśailaḥ ca vṛkṣavant ca acala uttamaḥ veṇumant ca sameghaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ deva parvataḥ mandarasya ete siddha āvāsāḥ udāhṛtāḥ rudra kṣetrāṇi divyāni viṣṇoḥ nārāyaṇasya ca sarasaḥ mānasasya iha dakṣiṇena mahā acalāḥ ye kīrtyamānāḥ tān sarvān saṃkṣipya pravadāmi aham śailaḥ ca viśirāḥ ca eva śikharaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ ekaśṛṅgaḥ mahāśūlaḥ gajaśailaḥ piśācakaḥ pañcaśailā utha kailāsaḥ himavant ca acala uttamaḥ iti ete deva caritāḥ utkaṭāḥ parvata uttamāḥ rudra kṣetrāṇi divyāni sthāpitāni sura uttamaiḥ digbhāge dakṣiṇe proktāḥ paścime ca vadāmi vaḥ kumudaḥ madhumant ca eva hi añjanaḥ mukuṭaḥ tathā pāṇḍuraḥ ca eva sahasraśikharaḥ ca yaḥ pārijātaḥ ca śaila indraḥ śrīśṛṅgaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ iti ete deva caritāḥ utkaṭāḥ parvata uttamāḥ ye sthitāḥ kīrtyamānān tān saṃkṣipya iha nibodhata mahā śailaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaparvataḥ nāgaḥ ca kapilaḥ ca eva indra śailaḥ ca sānumant nīlaḥ kaṇṭakaśṛṅgaḥ ca śataśṛṅgaḥ ca parvataḥ puṣpakośaḥ praśailaḥ ca virajaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ mayūraḥ ca acala uttamaḥ teṣu śaileṣu divyeṣu devadevasya śūlinaḥ asaṃkhyātāni divyāni vimānāni sahasraśas eteṣām śaila mukhyānām antareṣu yathākramam santi ca eva antara droṇyaḥ sarāṃsi upavanāni ca vasaṃti devāḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ ca śiva
