bhāvitāḥ kṛta vāsāḥ sa patnīkāḥ prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ lakṣmī ādyānām bilva vane kakubhe kaśyapa ādayaḥ udumbare kardamasya tathā anyeṣām mahātmanām vidyādharāṇām siddhānām puṇye tu āmra vane śubhe nāgānām siddha saṃghānām tathā nimba vane sthitiḥ kaumude tu vane viṣṇu pramukhānām mahātmanām śeṣaḥ tu aśeṣa jagantām patiḥ āste ati garvitaḥ saḥ eva jagatām kālaḥ pātāle ca vyāvasthitaḥ viṣṇoḥ viśva guroḥ mūrtiḥ divyaḥ sākṣāt halāyudhaḥ mayanam devadevasya sa hareḥ kaṅkamam vibhoḥ vane panasa vṛkṣāṇām sa śukraāḥ dānava ādayaḥ kinnaraiḥ uragāḥ ca eva viśākhaka vane sthitāḥ manohara vane vṛkṣāḥ sarva koṭi samanvitāḥ nandīśvaraḥ gaṇa varaiḥ stūyamānaḥ vyavasthitaḥ saṃtānaka sthalī madhye sākṣāt devī sarasvatī evam saṃkṣepataḥ proktāḥ vaneṣu vana vāsinaḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ mayā api atra vaktum no vistareṇa tu iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ekonapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śita anta śikhare śakraḥ pārijāta vane śubhe tasya prācyām kumudādri kūṭaḥ asau bahu vistaraḥ aṣṭau purāṇi udīrṇāni dānavānām dvijottamāḥ suvarṇa koṭare puṇye rākṣasāṇām mahātmanām nīlakānām purāṇi āhuḥ aṣṭaṣaṣṭiḥ dvijottamāḥ mahānīle ipi śaila indre purāṇi daśa pañca ca haya ānanānām mukhyānām kinnarāṇām ca suvratāḥ vaikuṇṭhe garuḍaḥ śrīmān karañje nīlalohitaḥ vasudhāre vasūnām tu nivāsaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ratnadhāre giri vare saptarṣiṇām mahātmanām sapta sthānāni puṇyāni siddhāvāsu yutāni ca mahat prajāpateḥ sthānam ekaśṛṅge naga uttame ādityāḥ ca tathā rudrāḥ kṛtāvāsāḥ tathā aśvinau sunīle rakṣasām vāsāḥ pañca koṭi śatāni ca pañcakūṭe purāṇyā san pañca koṭi pramāṇāt śakaśṛṅge pura śatam yakṣāṇām amita ojasām tāmra ābhe kādravāyāṇām viśākhe tu guhasya vai śveta udare muni śreṣṭhāḥ suparṇasya mahātmanaḥ piśācake kuberāsya harikūṭe hareḥ gṛham kumude kiṃnara āvāsaḥ tu añjane cāraṇa ālayaḥ kṛṣṇe gandharva nilayaḥ pāṇḍure pura saptakam vidyādharāṇām vipra indrāḥ sahasra śikhare śaile daityānām ugra karmaṇām purāṇām tu sahasrāṇi sapta śakra ariṇām dvijāḥ mukuṭe pannaga āvāsaḥ puṣpaketau muni īśvarāḥ brahma indra viṣṇu rudrāṇām guhasya ca mahātmanaḥ kuberasya ca somasya tathā anyeṣām mahātmanām saṃti āyatana mukhyāni maryādāparvateṣu api śrīkaṇṭha adri guhā vāsī sarva āvāsaḥ saha umayā śrīkaṇṭhasya ādhipatyam vai sarva deva īśvarasya ca aṇḍasya asya pravṛttiḥ tu śrīkaṇṭhena na saṃśayaḥ ananta īśa ādayaḥ tu evam pratyekam cāṇḍa pālakāḥ śrīkaṇṭha adhiṣṭhitāni atra sthānāni ca samā sataḥ maryādā parvateṣu adya śṛṇvantu pravadāmi aham śrīkaṇṭha adhiṣṭhitam viśvam carācaram idam jagat iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bhuvanavinyāsoddeśasthānavarṇanam nāma pañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca devakūṭe girau madhye mahā kūṭe su śobhane hema vaiḍūrya māṇikya nīla gomeda kāntibhiḥ sarva druma vibhūṣite campaka aśoka puṃnāga bakula āsana maṇḍite pārijātaka saṃpūrṇe nānā pakṣi gaṇa anvite nitamba puṣpa sa ālambe na eka sattva gaṇa anvite nirjharaiḥ kusuma ākīrṇaiḥ anekaiḥ ca vibhūṣite puṣpa uḍupa vahābhiḥ ca sravantībhiḥ alaṅkṛte ramyam hi avirala chāyam daśa yojana maṇḍalam tatra bhūtavanam nāma nānā bhūta gaṇa ālayam dīptam āyatanam tatra mahā maṇi vibhūṣitam hema prākāra saṃyuktam maṇi toraṇa maṇḍitam siṃhāsanaiḥ maṇi mayaiḥ śubha āstaraṇa saṃyutaiḥ tatas samyak śarveṇa adhiṣṭhitaiḥ śubhaiḥ amlāna mālā nicitaiḥ nānā varṇaiḥ gṛha uttamaiḥ maṇḍapaiḥ su vicitraiḥ tu sphaāṭika stambha saṃyutaiḥ varāha gaja siṃha ṛkṣa śārdūla karabha ānanaiḥ gṛdhra ulūka mukhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ mṛga uṣṭra aja mukhaiḥ api karālaiḥ hari keśaiḥ ca romaśaiḥ ca mahā bhujaiḥ nānā varṇa ākṛti dharaiḥ nānā saṃsthāna saṃsthitaiḥ brahma indra viṣṇu saṃkāśa araṇima ādi guṇa anvitaiḥ a śūnyam amaraiḥ nityam mahā pariṣadaiḥ tathā tatra bhūtapateḥ devāḥ pūjām nityam prayuñjate paṭahaiḥ bherī ḍiṇḍima gaumukhaiḥ nivālaḥ koṭi yakṣāṇām tathā anyeṣām mahātmanām savarṇa maṇi sopānā kubera śikhare śubhe jāmbūnada mayaiḥ padmaiḥ gandha sparśa guṇa anvitaiḥ tathā kumuda ṣaṇḍaiḥ ca mahā padmaiḥ alaṅkṛtā upaspṛṣṭa jalā puṇyā nadī mandākinī śubhā tasyāḥ ca uttara pārśve tu bhavasya āyatanam śubham dvijāḥ kanakanandāyāḥ tīre vai prāci dakṣiṇe vanam dvija sahasra āḍhyam mṛga pakṣi samākulam tatra api sa gaṇaḥ sa ambaḥ krīḍataḥ udri same gṛhe nandāyāḥ paścime tīre kiṃcid vai dakṣiṇa āśrite puram rudrapurī nāma nānā prāsāda saṃkulam tatra api śatadhā kṛtvā hi ātmānam ca ambayā saha krīḍate sa gamaḥ sa ambaḥ tat śiva ālayam ucyate evam śata sahasrāṇi śarvasya āyatanāni tu prati dvīpe muni śreṣṭhaḥ parvateṣu vaneṣu ca nadīnada taṭākānām tīreṣu arṇava sāṃdhiṣu iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ekapañcaśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca nadyaḥ ca bahavaḥ proktā sadā bahu jalāḥ śubhāḥ sarovarebhyaḥ saṃbhūtāḥ tu asaṃkhyātāḥ dvijottamāḥ prāc mukhāḥ dakṣiṇa āsyāḥ tu ca uttara prabhavāḥ śubhāḥ paścima agrāḥ pavitrāḥ ca prativarṣam prakīrtitāḥ ākāśa ambhaḥ nidhiḥ yaḥ asau somaḥ iti abhidhīyate mahā ādhāraḥ sarva bhūtānām devānām amṛta ākaraḥ asmāt pravṛttā puṇya udā nadī tu ākāśa gāminī saptamena anila pathinā pravṛttā ca amṛta udakā sā jyotiṃṣi anuvartantī jyotiḥ gaṇa niṣovitā tārā koṭi sahasrāṇām nabhasaḥ ca samā yutā catvāri aśītiḥ ca tathā sahasrāṇām samucchritaḥ yojanānām mahā meruḥ śrīkaṇṭha ākrīḍa komalaḥ tatra āsīnaḥ yataḥ śarvaḥ sa ambaḥ saha gaṇeśvaraiḥ su ciram kālam tasmāt puṇya jalā śivā girim merum nadī puṇyā sā prayāti pradakṣiṇam niyogāt devadevasya praviṣṭā sā mahā arṇavam asyāḥ vinirgatāḥ nadyaḥ śataśas tha sahasraśas sarva dvīpa adri varṣeṣu bahavaḥ varikīrtitāḥ kṣudra nadyaḥ tu asaṃkhyātāḥ gaṅgā yat gām gatā ambarāt ketumāle narāḥ kālāḥ sarve panasa bhojanāḥ striyaḥ ca utpala varṇa ābhāḥ jīvitam ca ayutam smṛtam bhadrāśve śukla varṇāḥ ca striyaḥ candra aṃśu saṃnibhāḥ kāla āmra bhojanāḥ sarve nirātaṅkāḥ rati priyāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi jīvanti śiva bhāvitāḥ hiraṇmayāḥ iva atyartham mīśvara arpita cetasaḥ tathā ramaṇake jīvāḥ nyagrodha phala bhojanāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti śuklāḥ te sarve śiva dhyāna parāyaṇāḥ hairaṇmayāḥ mahābhāgāḥ hiraṇmaya vana āśrayāḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca varṣāṇām tatra jīvanti aśvattha aśana jīvanāḥ hairaṇmayāḥ iva atyartham īśvara arpita mānasāḥ kuru varṣe tu kuravaḥ svarga lokāt parīcyutāḥ sarve maithuna jātāḥ ca kṣīriṇaḥ kṣīra bhojanāḥ anāmayāḥ hi aśokāḥ ca nityam sukha niṣeviṇaḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti te mahā vīryāḥ na ca anya strī niṣeviṇaḥ saha eva maraṇam teṣām kurūṇām svarga vāsinām hṛṣṭānām su pravṛddhānām sarva anna amṛta bhojinām sadā tu candra kāntānām sadā yovana śālinām śyāma aṅgānām sadā sarva bhūṣaṇa āspada dehinām jambūdvīpe tu tatra api kuru varṣam su śobhanam martyāḥ puṇyāḥ karma vaśa āyuṣaḥ śata āyuṣaḥ samākhyātāḥ nānā varṇa alpa dehinaḥ nānā deva ṛcane yuktāḥ nānā karma phala āśinaḥ nānā jñāna artha saṃpannāḥ durbalāḥ ca alpa bhoginaḥ tāmradvīpam gatāḥ kecid kaścid deśam gabhastimant nāgadvīpam saumyam gāndharvam vāruṇam gatāḥ kecid mlecchāḥ pulindāḥ ca nānā jāti samudbhavāḥ pūrve kirātāḥ tasya ante paścime yavanāḥ smṛtāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ madhye śudrāḥ ca sarvaśas teṣām saṃvyavahāraḥ iyam vartate atra parasparam dharma artha kāma saṃyuktaḥ varṇānām tu sva karmasu saṃkalpaḥ ca abhimānaḥ ca āśramāṇām yathāvidhi iha svarga apavarga artham pravṛttiḥ yatra mānuṣī teṣām ca yuga karmāṇi na anyatra muni puṃgavāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi sthitiḥ kiṃpuruṣe nṛṇām suvarṇa varṇāḥ ca nara astriyaḥ ca apsarasā upamāḥ anāmayāḥ hi aśokāḥ ca sarve te śiva bhāvitāḥ śuddha sattvāḥ ca hema ābhāḥ sa dārāḥ plakṣa bhojanāḥ mahārajata saṃkāśāḥ mānavāḥ deva lokāt cyutāḥ sarve deva ākārāḥ ca sarvaśas haram yajanti sarva īśam pibanti ikṣu rasam śubham na jarā bādhate tena na ca jīryānti te narāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvānti mānavāḥ madhyamam yat mayā proktam nāmnā varṣam ilāvṛtam candra sūryau na nakṣatram na prakāśam ilāvṛte padma prabhāḥ padma mukhāḥ padampattra nibha īkṣaṇāḥ jambu phala rasa āhārāḥ aniṣpandāḥ sugandhinaḥ deva loka āgatāḥ tatra jāyante hi ajara amarāḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām te nara uttamāḥ āyus pramāṇam jīvanti varṣe divye tu ilāvṛte jambu phala rasam pītvā na jarā bādhate tu imān na kṣudhā na klamaḥ ca api na janaḥ mṛtyu mān tathā tatra jāmbūnadam nāma kanakam deva bhūṣaṇam indragopa pratīkāśam jāyate bhāsvaram tu tat evam mayā samākhyātāḥ nava varṣa anuvartinaḥ varṇa āyus bhojana ādyāni saṃkṣipya na tu vistarāt hemakūṭe tu gandharvāḥ vijñeyāḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ sarve nāgāḥ ca niṣaghe śeṣa vāsuki takṣakāḥ mahā balāḥ trayāḥ triṃśat ramante yājñikāḥ surāḥ nīle tu vaiḍūrya maye siddhāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ amalāḥ daityānām dānavānām ca śvetaḥ parvataḥ ucyate śṛṅgavant parvataḥ ca eva pitṝṇām nilayaḥ sadā himavant yakṣa mukhyānām bhūtānām iśvarasya ca sarva adriṣu mahādevaḥ hariṇā brahmanā ambayā nandinā ca gaṇaiḥ ca eva varṣeṣu ca vaneṣu ca nīla śveta triśṛṅge ca bhagavant nīlalohitaḥ siddhaiḥ devaiḥ ca pitṛbhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ nityam viśeṣataḥ nīlaḥ ca vaiḍūrya mayaḥ śvetaḥ śuklaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ mayūra barha varṇaḥ tu śātakumbhaḥ triśṛṅgavān ete parvata rājānaḥ jambūdvīpe vyavasthitāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bhuvanakośasvabhāvavarṇanam nāma dvipañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca plakṣadvīpa ādi dvīpeṣu sapta saptasu parvatāḥ mṛjhu āyatāḥ pratidiśam varṣaparvatāḥ plakṣadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi sapta divyān mahā acalān tṛtīyaḥ nāradaḥ nāma caturthaḥ dundubhiḥ smṛtaḥ pañcamaḥ somakaḥ nāma sumanāḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ ucyate saptā ete girayaḥ proktāḥ plakṣadvīpe viśeṣataḥ sapta vai śālmali dvīpe tān tu vakṣyāmi anukramāt droṇaḥ kaṅkaḥ ca mahiṣaḥ kakudmant saptamaḥ smṛtaḥ kuśadvīpe tu sapta eva dvīpāḥ ca kulaparvatāḥ tān tu saṃkṣepataḥ vakṣye nāma mātreṇa vai kramāt tṛtīyaḥ dyutimant nāma caturthaḥ puṣpitaḥ smṛtaḥ kuśeśayaḥ pañcamaḥ tu ṣaṣṭhaḥ harigiriḥ smṛtaḥ mandāḥ iti hi apām nāma mandaraḥ dhāraṇāt apām tatra sākṣāt vṛṣāṅkaḥ tu viśveśaḥ vimalaḥ śivaḥ tapasā toṣitaḥ pūrvam mandareṇa maheśvaraḥ prārthitaḥ ca mahādevaḥ nivāsa artham saha ambayā krauñcadvīpe tu sapta iha kraiñca ādyāḥ kulaparvatāḥ kraiñcaḥ vāmanakaḥ paścāt tṛtīyaḥ ca andhakārakaḥ andhakārāt paraḥ ca api divāvṛt nāma parvataḥ vivindāt paratas ca api puṇḍarīkaḥ mahā giriḥ puṇḍarīkāt paraḥ ca api procyate dundubhisvanaḥ śākadvīpe ca girayaḥ sapta tān tu nibodhata udayaḥ raivataḥ ca api śtāmakaḥ muni sattamāḥ āmbikeyaḥ āmbikeyāt paraḥ ramyaḥ sarva oṣadhi samanvitaḥ puṣkare parvataḥ śrīmān ekaḥ eva mahā śilaḥ citraiḥ maṇi mayaiḥ kūṭaiḥ śilā jālaiḥ samucchritaiḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi ūrdhvam pañcāśat ucchritaḥ adhas ca eva cutaḥ triṃśat sahasrāṇi mahā acalaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi ūrdhvam pañcāśat ucchritaḥ tāvat eva tu vistīrṇaḥ pārśvatas parimaṇḍalaḥ saḥ eva dvīpa paśca ardhe mānasaḥ pṛthivīdharaḥ ekaḥ eva mahā sānuḥ saṃniveśāt dvidhā kṛtaḥ rājatau mānasaḥ tā atha parvatasya anu maṇḍalau mahāvītam tu yat varṣam bāhyatas mānasasya tu svādu udakena udadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva puṣkarasya samena tu evam dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta sapta āvṛtāḥ evam dvīpa samudrāṇām vṛddhiḥ jñeyā parasparam pareṇa tasya mahatī dṛśyate loka saṃsthitiḥ kāñcanī dviguṇā bhūmiḥ sarvā ca eka śilā u pamā tasyāḥ pareṇa śailaḥ tu maryādā pāra maṇḍalaḥ prakāśaḥ ca aprakāśaḥ ca lokālokaḥ saḥ ucyate dṛśya adṛśya giriḥ yāvat tāḥ vat eṣā dharā dvijāḥ yojanānām sarasrāṇi daśa tasya ucchrayaḥ smṛtaḥ tāvān ca vistaraḥ tasya lokāloka mahā gireḥ para ardhe tu tamaḥ nityam lokālokaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ ābhānoḥ vai bhuvaḥ svar tu ādhruvāt muni sattamāḥ āvaha adya niviṣṭāḥ tu vāyoḥ vai sapta nemayaḥ pravahaḥ ca eva tatas ca anuvahaḥ tathā saṃvahaḥ vivahaḥ ca atha tatas ca ūrdhvam parāvahaḥ balāhakāḥ tathā bhānuḥ candraḥ nakṣatra rāśayaḥ grahaṇi ṛṣayaḥ sapta dhruvaḥ viprāḥ kramāt iha yojanānām mahī pṛṣṭhāt ūrdhvam pañcadaśa adhruvāt niyutāni eka niyutam bhū pṛṣṭhāt bhānu maṇḍalam rathaḥ ṣoḍaśa sāhasraḥ bhāskarasya tathā upariḥ meruḥ ca upari bhū talāt mahar lokāt tathā koṭi dvayam dvijāḥ prājā patyāt brahma lokaḥ koṭi ṣaṭkam visṛjya tu puṇya lokāḥ tu sapta ete hi aṇḍaḥ asmin kathitāḥ dvijāḥ adhas sapta talānām tu narakāṇām hi koṭayaḥ māyā antāḥ ca eva ghora ādyāḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ eva tu avīci antāni sarvāṇi raurava ādyāni teṣu ca pratyekam pañcakāni āhuḥ narakāṇi viśeṣataḥ aṇḍam ādau mayā proktam aṇḍasya āvaraṇāni ca aṇḍānām īdṛśāṇām tu koṭayaḥ jñeyāḥ sahasraśas aṇḍeṣu eteṣu sarveṣu bhuvanāni caturdaśa prati aṇḍam dvija śārdūlāḥ teṣām hetuḥ maheścaraḥ aṇḍeṣu ca aṇḍa bāhyeṣu tathā aṇḍa āvaraṇeṣu ca tamaḥ ante ca tamaḥ pāre ca aṣṭamūrtiḥ vyavasthitaḥ asya aṣṭamūrteḥ śarvasya śivasya gṛha madhinaḥ gṛhiṇī prakṛtiḥ divyā prajāḥ ca mahat ādayaḥ paśavaḥ kiṅkaraḥ tasya sarve deha abhimāninaḥ pradhāna mūrtiḥ tu atha ṣoḍaśa aṅgaḥ maheśvaraḥ ca aṣṭa tanuḥ saḥ eva ājñā balāt tasya dharā sthitā iha dharādharāḥ vāridharāḥ samudrāḥ jyotiḥ gaṇaḥ śakra mukhāḥ surāḥ ca vaimānikāḥ sthāvara jaṅgamāḥ ca dṛṣṭvā yakṣam lakṣaṇaiḥ hinamīsam dṛṣṭvā sa indrāḥ te kim etat tu iha iti yakṣam gatvā niścayāt pāvaka ādyāḥ śakti kṣīṇāḥ ca abhavan yat tatas api dagdhum tṛṇam vā api samakṣam asya yakṣasya vahniḥ na śaśāka viprāḥ vāyuḥ tṛṇam cālayitum tathā anye svān svān prabhāvān sakala amara indrāḥ tadā svayam vṛtraripuḥ sura indraiḥ sureśvaraḥ sarva samṛddhi hetuḥ sureśvaram yakṣam uvāca kaḥ vā bhavān iti ittham sa kutūhala ātmā tadā hi adṛśyam gataḥ eva yakṣaḥ tadā aṃbikā haimavatī śubha āsyā umā śubhaiḥ ābharaṇaiḥ anekaiḥ su śobhamānā tu anu ca āvirāsīt tām śakra mukhyāḥ bahu śobhamānām umām ajām haimavatīm apṛcchan kim etat īśe bahu śobhamāne vā ambīke yakṣa vapuḥ cakāsti niśamya tat yakṣam umā ambikā āha tu agocaraḥ ca iti surāḥ sa śakraāḥ praṇemuḥ enām mṛgarāja gāminīm umām ajām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām saṃbhāvitā sā sakala amara indraiḥ sarva pravṛttiḥ tu sura asurāṇām aham purā āsam prakṛtiḥ ca puṃsaḥ yakṣasya ca ājñā vaśa gā iti atha āha tasmāt dvijāḥ sarvam ajasya tasya niyogataḥ ca aṇḍam abhūt ajāt vai ajaḥ ca aṇḍāt akhilam ca tasmāt jyotiḥ gaṇaiḥ lokam aja ātmakam tat iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bhuvanakośavinyāsanirṇayaḥ nāma tripañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ jyotiḥ gaṇa pracāram vai saṃkṣipya aṇḍe bravīmi aham mānasa upari māhendrī prācyām meroḥ purī sthitā dakṣiṇe bhānu putrasya varuṇasya ca vāruṇī saumye somasya vipulā tāsu digdevatāḥ sthitāḥ amarāvatī saṃyamanī sukhā ca eva vibhā kramāt lokapāla upariṣṭāt tu sarvatas dakṣiṇāyane kāṣṭhām gatasya sūryasya gatīḥ yā tām nibodhata dakṣiṇa prakrame bhānuḥ kṣipta iṣuḥ iva dhāvati jyotiṣām cakram ādāya satatam parigacchati sarvaiḥ sa āyamanaiḥ sauraḥ hi udayaḥ dṛśyate dvijāḥ saḥ eva sukhavatyām tu niśāta sthaḥ pradṛśyate astam eti punar sūryaḥ vibhāyām viśva dṛś vibhuḥ mayā proktā umarāvatyām yathā asau vāritaskaraḥ tathā saṃyamanīm prāpya sukhām ca eva vibhām khagaḥ yadā aparāhṇaḥ tu āgnoyyām pūrvāhṇaḥ naiṛte dvijāḥ tadā tu apararātraḥ ca vāyu bhāge su dāruṇaḥ īśānyām pūrvarātraḥ tu gatiḥ eṣā ca sarvatas triṃśa aṃśakam tu medinyām muhūrtena eva gacchati yojanānām muhūrtasya imām saṃkhyām nibodhata pūrṇā śata sahasrāṇām ekatriṃśatī tu sā smṛtā pañcāśat ca tathā anyāni sahasrāṇi adhikāni tu mauhūrtikī gatiḥ hi eṣā bhāskarasya mahātmanaḥ etena gati yogena yadā kāṣṭhām tu dakṣiṇām mānasottara śaile tu mahā tejāḥ vibhāvasuḥ maṇḍalānām śatam pūrṇam tat aśīti adhikam vibhuḥ bāhyam ca abhyantaram proktam uttarāyaṇa dakṣiṇe pratyaham carate tāni sūryaḥ vai maṇḍalāni tu tasmāt prakṛṣṭām bhūmim tu kālena alpena gacchati sūryaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ śīghram muhūrtaiḥ dakṣiṇāyane trayodaśa ardham ṛkṣāṇām ahnā tu carate raviḥ muhūrtaiḥ tāvat ṛkṣāṇi naktam aṣṭādaśaiḥ caran tasmāt dīrgheṇa kālena bhūmim alpām tu gaccati gandharvaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca sarpa rākṣasaiḥ pradīpayan sahasrāṃśuḥ agratas pṛṣṭhatas api adhas ūrdhvatas ca karam tyaktvā sabhām brāhmīm anuttamām ambhobhiḥ munibhiḥ tyaktaiḥ saṃdhyāyām tu niśācarān hatvā hatvā tu saṃprāptān brahmaṇaiḥ carate raviḥ aṣṭādaśa muhūrtam tu uttarāyaṇa paścimam traya uśa ardham ṛkṣāṇi naktam dvādaśabhiḥ raviḥ muhūrtaiḥ tāvat ṛkṣāmi divā aṣṭādaśabhiḥ caran triṃśat muhūrtaiḥ eva āhuḥ ahyerātram purāvidaḥ ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ madhye bhramataḥ maṇḍalāni tu auttānapādaḥ bhramati grahaiḥ sārdham grahāgraṇīḥ adhiṣṭhitaḥ punar tena bhānuḥ tu ādāya tiṣṭhati kiraṇaiḥ sarvatas toyam devaḥ vai sa samīraṇaḥ viṣṇoḥ auttānapādena ca āptam tātasya hetunā apaḥ pītāḥ tu sūryeṇa kramante śaśinaḥ kramāt niśākarāt nisnavante jīmūtān prati apaḥ kramāt vṛndam jalamucām ca eva śvasanena abhitāḍitam māyām sṛṣṭim visṛjate abhāsayat tena bhāskaraḥ hitāya sarva jantūnām gatiḥ sarva ima nirmitā bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar tathā hi apaḥ hi annam ca amṛtam eva ca prāṇāḥ vai jagatām apaḥ bhūtāni bhuvanāni ca apām śivasya bhagavān ādhipatye vyavasthitaḥ nārāyaṇa tvam devasya hareḥ ca adbhiḥ kṛtam vibhoḥ jagantām ālayaḥ viṣṇuḥ tu apaḥ tasya ālayāni tu yāḥ yāḥ ūrdhvam mārutena īritāḥ vai tāḥ tāḥ tu abhrāṇi agninā vāyunā ca atas dhūma agni vātānām saṃyogaḥ tu abhram ucyate vārīṇi varṣati iti abhram abhrasya īśaḥ yajña dhūma udbhavam ca api dvijānām hita kṛt sadā dāva agni dhūma saṃbhūtam abhram vana hitam smṛtam bhicāra agni dhūma uttham bhūtanāsāya vai dvijāḥ evam dhūma viśeṣeṇa jāgatām vai hita ahitam tasmāt ācchādayet dhūmam abhicāra kṛtam naraḥ an ācchādya dvijaḥ kuryāt dhūmam yaḥ ca ābhicārikam apām nidhānam jīmūtāḥ ṣaṭ māsān iha suvratāḥ varṣayanti eva jagatām hitāya pavana ājñayā tridhā teṣām iha utpattiḥ abhrāṇām muni puṃgavāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ vā ahnāḥ ca vairiñcyāḥ pakṣāḥ śca eva pṛthagvidhāḥ mājyānām kāṣṭha saṃyogāt agneḥ dhūmaḥ pravartitaḥ dvitīyānām ca saṃbhūtiḥ viriñca ucchvāsa vāyunā vāhneyāḥ tu atha jīmūtāḥ tu āvaha sthāna gāḥ śubhāḥ pakṣajāḥ puṣkara ādyāḥ ca varṣanti ca yadā jalam mūkāḥ sa śabda duṣṭa āśāḥ tu etaiḥ kṛtyam yathākramam kṣāma vṛṣṭi pradāḥ dīrgha kālam śīta samīriṇaḥ jīvakāḥ ca tathā kṣīṇāḥ vidyut dhvani vivarjitāḥ tiṣṭhanti ākrośa mātre tu dharā pṛṣṭhāt itas tatas ardha krośe tu sarve vai jīmūtāḥ giri vāsinaḥ meghāḥ yojana mātram tu sādhya tvāt brahu toya dāḥ dharā pṛṣṭhāt dvijāḥ kṣmāyām vidyut guṇa samanvitāḥ teṣām teṣām vṛṣṭi sargam tredhā kathitam atra tu pakṣajāḥ kalpa jāḥ sarve parvatānām mahattamāḥ te ca varṣanti rātrau nāśāya śāradāḥ pakṣajāḥ puṣkara ādyāḥ ca varṣanti ca yadā jalam tadā arṇavam abhūt sarvam tatra śete niśi īśvaraḥ āgneyānām śvāsa jānām pakṣajānām dvijarṣabhāḥ jaladānām sadā dhūmaḥ hi āpyāḥ yanaḥ iti smṛtaḥ pauṇḍrāḥ tu vṛṣṭayaḥ sarvāḥ vaidyutāḥ śīta śasya dāḥ puṇḍra deśeṣu patitāḥ nāgānām śīkarāḥ himāḥ mā aṅgā gaṅgā ambu saṃbhūtā parjanyena parāvahaiḥ nagānām ca nadīnām ca diggajānām samākulam meghānām ca pṛthak bhūtam jalam prāyāt agāt agam parāvahaḥ ūyaḥ śvayanaḥ ca ānayati ambikā gurum menā patim atikramya vṛṣṭi śeṣam dvijāḥ param vṛṣṭayaḥ kathitāḥ hi adya dvidhā vaḥ tu vivṛddhaye sraṣṭā bhānuḥ mahā tejāḥ vṛṣṭīnām viśva dṛś vibhuḥ saḥ api sākṣāt dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ ca īśānaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ cakṣuḥ śrotram manaḥ mṛtyuḥ ātmā manyuḥ vidiś diśaḥ satyam ṛtam tathā vāyuḥ ambaram khacaraḥ ca saḥ lokapālaḥ hariḥ brahmā rudraḥ sākṣāt maheśvaraḥ sahasrakiraṇaḥ śrīmān aṣṭa hastaḥ su maṅgalaḥ ardha nārī vapūḥ sākṣāt tra netraḥ tridaśādhipaḥ asya eva iha prasādāt tu vṛṣṭiḥ nānā bhavat dvijāḥ jalasya nāśaḥ vṛddhiḥ vā na asti eva asya vicārāt dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitaḥ vāyuḥ vṛṣṭim saṃharate punar grahāt niḥsṛtya sūryāt tu kṛtsne nakṣatra maṇḍale cārasya ante viśati arke dhruveṇa samadhiṣṭhitā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge jyotiścakre sūryagatyādikathanam nāma catuḥpañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sauram saṃkṣepāt vakṣye ratham śaśinaḥ eva ca yathā gacchati ca ambupaḥ sauraḥ tu brahmaṇā sṛṣṭaḥ rathaḥ tu artha vaśena saḥ saṃvatsarasya avayavaiḥ kalpitaḥ ca dvijarṣabhāḥ triṇā tu cakreṇa pañca āreṇa samanvitaḥ sauvarṇaḥ sarva devānām āvāsaḥ bhāskarasya tu nava yojana sāhasraḥ vistāra āyāmāt smṛtaḥ dviguṇaḥ api rathopasthāt īṣā daṇḍaḥ pramāṇāt prerakaḥ jyotiṣām dhīmān dhruvaḥ vai vāta raśmibhiḥ yuga akṣa koṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya hi bhrāmyataḥ tasya raśmī tu maṇḍaleṣu uttarāyaṇe vardhete dakṣiṇe ca eva bhramatā maṇḍalāni tu ākṛṣyete yadā te vai dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhite tadā aśīti maṇḍala śatam kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram dvayoḥ dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyām raśmibhyām punar eva tu tathā eva bāhyatas sūryaḥ bhramate maṇḍalāni tu devāḥ ca eva tathā nityam munayaḥ ca divāniśam gandharvaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca grāmaṇī sarpa rākṣasaiḥ māpyāyayanti ca ādityam tejobhiḥ bhāskaram śivam kurvate abhīṣu saṃgraham sarpāḥ vahanti vai sūryam yātudhāna anuyānti ca madhuḥ ca mādhavaḥ ca eva śukraḥ ca śuciḥ eva ca ete dvādaśa māsāḥ tu varṣam vai mānuṣam dvijāḥ vāsaṃtikaḥ tathā graiṣmaḥ śubhaḥ vai vārṣikaḥ tathā śāradaḥ ca himaḥ ca eva śaiśiraḥ ṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca indraḥ eva ca vivasvant ca eva pūṣā ca parjanya uṃśuḥ bhagaḥ tathā tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ pulastyaḥ ca pulahaḥ ca atriḥ eva ca vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṅgigaḥ ca eva bhṛguḥ buddhimatām varaḥ jamadagniḥ kauśikaḥ ca vāsukiḥ kaṅkaṇī karaḥ takṣakaḥ ca tathā nāgaḥ elāpattraḥ tathā dvijāḥ maṅkhapālaḥ tathā ca anyaḥ tu airāvataḥ iti smṛtaḥ dhanañjayaḥ mahāpadmaḥ tathā karkoṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ kambalaḥ aśvataraḥ ca eva tuṃburuḥ nāradaḥ tathā hūhūḥ muni śreṣṭhāḥ viśvāvasuḥ anuttamaḥ citrasenaḥ mahā tejāḥ ca ūrṇāyuḥ ca eva suvratāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sūryavarcāḥ devī sākṣātkṛtasthalā śubha ānanā śubha śroṇiḥ divyā vai puñjikasthalā anumlocā ghṛtācī ca viśvācī ca urvaśī tathā pūrvacittiḥ iti khyātā devī sākṣāt tilottamā rambhā ca ambhoja vadanā rathakṛt grāmaṇīḥ śubhaḥ varuṇaḥ ca tathā eva anyaḥ suṣeṇaḥ senajit śubhaḥ tārkṣyaḥ ca ariṣṭanemiḥ ca kṣatajit satyajit tathā sarpaḥ vyāghraḥ punar ca apaḥ vātaḥ vidyut divākaraḥ sthāna abhimāninaḥ hi ete gaṇāḥ dvādaśa saptakāḥ dhātṛ ādi viṣṇu paryantāḥ devāḥ dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ ādityam paramam bhānum bhābhiḥ āpyāyayanti te pulastya ādyāḥ kauśika antāḥ munayaḥ muni sattamāḥ nāgāḥ ca aśvatara antāḥ tu vāsuki pramukhāḥ śubhāḥ dvādaśa eva mahādevam vahanti evam yata ākramam krameṇa sūrya varcā antāḥ tumburu pramukha ambupam gītaiḥ enam upāsaṃte gandharvāḥ dvādaśa uttamāḥ kṛtasthalā ādyāḥ rambhā antāḥ divyāḥ ca apsarasaḥ ravim tāṇḍavaiḥ sarasaiḥ sarvāḥ ca upāsaṃte yathākramam divyāḥ satyajit antāḥ ca grāmaṇyaḥ rathakṛt mukhāḥ dvādaśā asya krameṇa eva kurvate bhīṣu saṃgraham prayānti yajñopeta antāḥ rakṣoheti mukhāḥ saha sa āyudhāḥ dvādaśa eva ete rākṣasāḥ ca yathākramam dhātā aryamā pulastyaḥ ca pulahaḥ ca prajāpatiḥ uragaḥ vāsukiḥ ca eva kaṅkaṇīkaḥ ca tau ubhau kṛtasthalā apsarāḥ ca eva tathā vai puñjikasthalā rathakṛt ca eva rathaujāḥ ca eva tau ubhau rakṣaḥ hetiḥ prahetiḥ ca yātudhānau udāhṛtau vasaṃti grāṣmikau māsau mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca ha ṛṣiḥ atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca takṣakaḥ nāgaḥ eva ca subāhu nāmā rathacitraḥ ca tau ubhau pauruṣeyaḥ vadhaḥ ca eva yātudhānau udāhṛtau ete vasaṃti vai sūrye māsayoḥ śuci śukrayoḥ tatas sūrye punar ca anyāḥ nivasanti iha devatāḥ indraḥ ca eva vivasvant ca āṅgirāḥ bhṛguḥ eva ca elāpattraḥ tathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ ca tau ubhau viśvāvasu ugrasenau ca varuṇaḥ ca rathasvanaḥ yātudhānāḥ tathā sarpaḥ vyāghraḥ ca eva tu tau ubhau dhanañjayaḥ irāvant ca suruciḥ sa parāvasuḥ ghṛtācī ca apsaraḥ śreṣṭhā viśvācī ca ati śobhanā senajit ca suṣeṇaḥ ca senānīḥ grāmaṇīḥ ca tau apaḥ vātaḥ ca tau ecau yātudhānau ubhau smṛtau aṃśuḥ bhagaḥ ca dvau etau kaśyapaḥ ca kratuḥ saha bhujaṃgaḥ ca mahāpadmaḥ sarpaḥ karkoṭakaḥ tathā urvaśī pūrvacittiḥ ca tathā eva apsarasau ubhe tārkṣyaḥ ca ariṣṭanemiḥ ca senānīḥ grāmaṇīḥ ca tau vidyut divākaraḥ ca ubhau yātudhānau udāhṛtau tatas śauśīrayoḥ ca api māsayoḥ nivasanti vai tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ jamadagniḥ viśvāmitraḥ tathā eva ca kādraveyau tathā nāgau kambala aśvatarau ubhau dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sa gandharvaḥ sūryavarcāḥ tathā eva ca tilottamā apsarāḥ ca eva devī rambhā manoharā brahmopetaḥ tathā rakṣaḥ yajñopetaḥ ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ sthāna abhimāninaḥ hi ete gaṇāḥ dvādaśa saptakāḥ kurvate ibhīṣu saṃgraham sarpāḥ vahanti vai sūryam yātu dhānā anuyānti vai eteṣām eva devānām yathā tejaḥ yathā tapaḥ yatā yogam yathā mantram yathā dharmam yathā balam ṛṣayaḥ deva gandharva pannaga apsarasām gaṇāḥ ca tathā yakṣāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca mukhyatas bhūtānām aśubham karma vyapohanti iha kīrtitāḥ mānavānām śubham hi ete haranti ca durātmanām varṣantaḥ ca tapantaḥ ca hlādayantaḥ ca vai dvijāḥ gopāyanti iha bhūtāni sarvāṇi hi āmanu kṣayāt sthāna abimāninām etat sthānam manvantareṣu vai atīta anāgatānām vai vartante sāṃpratam ca ye saṃkṣepāt vistarāt ca eva yatāvṛttam yathāśrutam kathitam muni śārdūlāḥ devadevasya dhīmataḥ sthāna abhimāninaḥ hi ete gaṇāḥ dvādaśa saptakāḥ iti eṣaḥ eka cakreṇa sūryaḥ tūrṇam rathena tu iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sūryarathanirṇayaḥ nāma pañcapañcāśattamaḥ dhyāyaḥ uvāca vīthi āśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi niśākaraḥ kramate śukla pakṣa ādau bhāskarāt param āsthitaḥ parasya antar satatam divasa kramāt devaiḥ pītam kṣaye somam āpyāyayati nityaśas pītam pañcadaśa aham tu raśmiṇā ekena bhāskaraḥ āpūrayan suṣumnena bhāgaṃbhāgam anukramāt iti eṣā sūrya vīryeṇa candrasya āpyāyitā tanuḥ sa paurmamāsyām dṛśyeta śuklaḥ saṃpūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ evam āpyāyitam somam śuklapakṣe dina kramāt saṃbhṛtam tu ardha māsena hi amṛtam sūrya tejasā pāna artham amṛtam somam paurṇamāsyām upāsate eka rātrim surāḥ sarve pitṛbhiḥ tu ṛṣibhiḥ saha somasya kṛṣṇa pakṣa ādau bhāskara abhimukhasya ca prakṣīyante parasya antar pīyamānāḥ kalāḥ kramāt trayastriṃśat sahasrāṇi devāḥ somam pibanti vai pītvā ardha māsam gacchanti amāvāsyām sura uttamāḥ pitaraḥ ca upatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyām niśākaram tatas pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcid ciṣṭe kalā ātmake aparāhṇe pitṛ gaṇāḥ jaghanyam paryupāsate pibanti dvi kalam kālam śiṣṭā tasya kalā tu yā nissṛtam tat amāvāsyām gabhastibhyaḥ svadhā amṛtam māsa tṛptim avāpya agryām pītvā gacchanti te amṛtam pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyām kalā tu yā yāvat tu kṣīyate tasya bhāgaḥ pañcadaśaḥ tu saḥ amāvāsyām tatas tasyāḥ antarā pūryate punar vṛddhi kṣayau vai pakṣa ādau ṣoḍaśyām śaśinaḥ smṛtau evam sūrya nimittā eṣā pakṣa vṛddhiḥ niśākare iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge somavarṇanam nāma ṣaṭpañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca mayaḥ ca atha piśaṅgaiḥ ca eva śobhanaiḥ daśabhiḥ ca akṛśaiḥ aśvaiḥ nānā varṇaiḥ rathaḥ smṛtaḥ śukrasya kṣmā mayaiḥ yuktaḥ daitya ācāryasya dhīmataḥ aṣṭa aśvaḥ ca atha bhaumasya rathaḥ haimaḥ su śobhanaḥ jīvasya haimaḥ ca aṣṭa aśvomandasya āyasa nirmitaḥ svarbhānoḥ bhāskara areḥ ca tathā ca aṣṭa hayaḥ smṛtaḥ etena bhrāmyamāṇāḥ ca yathāyogam vrajanti vai yāvantyaḥ ca eva tārāḥ ca tāvantaḥ ca eva raśmayaḥ yasmāt vahati jyotīṃṣi pravahaḥ tena saḥ smṛtaḥ nakṣatra sūryāḥ ca tathā graha tārā gaṇaiḥ saha unmuka abhimukhāḥ sarve cakra bhūtāḥ śritāḥ divi dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ ca eva dhruvam eva pradakṣiṇam prayānti ca īśvaram draṣṭum meḍhī bhūtam dhruvam divi nava yojana sāhasraḥ viṣkaṃbhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ triguṇaḥ tasya vistāraḥ maṇḍalasya pramām atas dviguṇaḥ sūrya avistārāt vistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ uddhṛtya pṛthivī chāyām nirmitām maṇḍala ākṛtim svarbhānoḥ tu bṛhat sthānam tṛtīyam yat tamaḥ mayam candrasya ṣoḍaśaḥ bhāgaḥ bhārgavasya vidhīyate viṣkambhāt maṇḍalāt ca eva yojanāt ca pramāṇāt bhārgavāt pāda hīnaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ vai bṛhaspatiḥ pāda hīnau vakra saurī tathā āyāma pramām atas vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva pāda hīnaḥ tayoḥ budhaḥ tārāḥ nakṣatra rūpāṇi vapuṣmanti iha yāni vai budhena tāni tulyāni vistārāt maṇḍalāt api prāyaśas candra yogīni vidyāt ṛkṣāṇi tattva vid tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve ca eva yojane sarva upari nikṛṣṭāni tārakā maṇḍalāni tu upariṣṭāt trayaḥ teṣām grahāḥ ye dūra sarpiṇaḥ saura uṅgirāḥ ca vakraḥ ca jñeyāḥ manda vicāriṇaḥ sūryaḥ somaḥ budhaḥ ca eva bhārgavaḥ ca eva śīghragāḥ tāvantyaḥ tārakāḥ koṭyaḥ yāvanti ukṣāṇi sarvaśas niyamāt ca eṣām ṛkṣa mārge uttarāyaṇa mārga sthaḥ yadā parvasu candramāḥ ucca tvāt dṛśyate śīghram na ati vyaktaiḥ gabhastibhiḥ tadā dakṣiṇa mārga sthaḥ nīcām vīthim upāśritaḥ bhumī rekhā vṛtaḥ sūryaḥ paurṇimā vāsyayoḥ tadā dadṛśe ca yathākālam śīghram astam upaiti ca tasmāt uttara mārga sthaḥ hi amāvāsyām nisākaraḥ dadṛśe dakṣiṇe mārge niyamāt dṛśyate na ca jyotiṣām gati yogena sūryasya tamasā vṛtaḥ dakṣiṇāyana mārga sthau yadā carati raśmivān ca eva sarveṣām sūryaḥ udhastāt prasarpati vistīrṇam maṇḍalam kṛtvā tasya ūrdhvam carate śaśī nakṣatra maṇḍalam kṛtsram somāt ūrdhvam prasarpati nakṣatrebhyaḥ budhaḥ ca ūrdhvam budhāt ūrdhvam tu bhārgavaḥ vakraḥ tu bhārgavāt ūrdhvam vakraāt ūrdhvam bṛhaspatiḥ tasmāt śanaiścaraḥ ca ūrdhvam tasmāt saptarṣi maṇḍalam ṛṣīṇām ca eva saptānām dhruvasya ūrdhvam vyavasthitiḥ tam viṣṇu lokam paramam jñātvā mucyeta kilbiṣāt dviguṇeṣu sahasreṣu yojanānām śateṣu ca graha nakṣatra tārāsu upariṣṭāt yathākramam graha nakṣatra sūryāḥ te nīca ucca ṛju saṃsthitāḥ mṛtāḥ ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ smṛtāḥ sarve samāgacchanti pañcadhā aṃsa kareṇa vijñeyaḥ teṣām yogaḥ tu vai budhaiḥ evam saṃkṣipya kathitam gamanam dvijāḥ bhāskara pramukhānām ca yata adṛṣṭam yathāśrutam abhiṣiktaḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ rudreṇa tu yathā guhaḥ tasmāt graha arcanā kāryā agnau codyam yata avidhi pīḍāyām sadbhiḥ kārya artha siddhaye iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge jyotiścakre grahacārakathanam nāma saptapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ abhyaṣiñcat katham brahmā ca ādhipatye prajāpatiḥ uvāca ṛkṣāṇām oṣadhīnām ca somam brahmā prajāpatiḥ apām ca varuṇam deva dhanānām yakṣa puṅgavam ādityānām tathā viṣṇum vasūnām pāvakam tathā prajāpatīnām dakṣam ca marutām śakam eva ca daityānām dānavānām ca prahlāda daitya puṃgavam dharmam pitṝṇām adhipam nirṛtim piśitāsinām rudram paśūnām bhūtānām nandīnām gaṇanāyakam mahānām varibhadram ca piśācānām bhayaṅkaram mātṝṇām ca eva cāmuṇḍām sarva deva namaskṛtām rudrāṇām devadevaśam nīlalohitam īśvaram vighnānām vyoma jam devam gajasyam tu vināyakam strīṇām devīm umā devīm vacasām ca sarasvatīm viṣṇum māyāvinām ca eva svatmānam jagatām tathā himavantam girīṇām tu nadīnām ca eva jāhnavīm samudrāṇām ca sarveṣām adhipam payasām nidhim vṛkṣāṇām ca eva ca aśvattham plakṣam ca prapitāmahaḥ maṅgharva vidyādhara kinnarāṇām īśam punāḥ citraratham cakāra nāga adhipam vāsukim ugra vīryam sarpa adhipam takṣakam ugra vīryam digvāraṇānām adhipam cakāra gaja indram airāvatam ugra vīryam suparṇa mīsam patatām atha aśva rājānam uccaiḥśravasam cakāra siṃham mṛgāṇām vṛṣabham gāvām ca mṛga adhipānām śarabham cakāra senā adhipānām guham aprameyam śrutī smṛtīnām lakulīśam īśam abhyaṣiñcat sudharmāṇam tathā śaṅkhāpadam diśām pṛthivyām pṛthum īśānam sarveṣām tu maheśvaram catur mūrtiṣu sarvajñam śaṃkaram vṛṣabhadhvajam prasādāt bhagavant śambhoḥ ca abhyaṣiñcat yathākramam purā abhiṣicya puṇya ātmā rarāja bhuvaneśvaraḥ abhiṣiktāḥ tatas tu ete viśiṣṭāḥ viśvayoninā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe sūryādyabhiṣekakathanam nāma aṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca etat śrutvā tu munayaḥ punar tam saṃśaya anvitāḥ ūcuḥ śrutvā tu vacanam teṣām tadā sūtaḥ samāhitaḥ uvāca paramam vākyam teṣām saṃśaya nirṇaye asmin arthe mahā prājñaiḥ yat uktam śānta buddhibhiḥ yathā deva gṛhāni iha sūrya candra ādayaḥ grahāḥ vyuṣṭāyām tu rajanyām ca brahmanaḥ avyakta janmanaḥ avyākṛtam idam tu āsīt naisena tamasā vṛtam catur bhāga avaśiṣṭe asmin loke naṣṭe viśeṣataḥ svayaṃbhūḥ bhagavān tatra loka sarva atha sādhakaḥ saḥ agnim sṛṣṭvā atha loka ādau pṛthivī jala saṃśritaḥ saṃhṛtya tad prakāśa artham tridhā vyabhajat īśvaraḥ yaḥ ca asau loka ādau sūrye śuciḥ agniḥ tu saḥ smṛtaḥ vaidyuta ubjaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ teṣām vakṣye tu lakṣaṇam jale ca abjaḥ samāviṣṭaḥ na adbhiḥ praśāmyati mānavānām ca kukṣi sthaḥ na agniḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ arciṣmān pavanaḥ sa ugniḥ niṣprabhaḥ jāṭharaḥ smṛtaḥ yaḥ ca ayam maṇḍalī suklī nirūṣmā saṃprajāyate prabhā saurā tu pādena hi astam yāte divākare agnim āviśate rātrau tasmāt dūrāt prakāśate udyantam ca punar sūryam auṣyam agneḥ samāviśet prakāśa uṣṇa svarūpe ca saura āgneye tu tejasī uttiṣṭhati punar sūryaḥ punar vai praviśati apaḥ tasmāt tāmrāḥ bhavanti apaḥ divā rātri praveśanāt astam yāti punar sūryaḥ uhar vai praviśati apaḥ tasmāt naktam punar śuklāḥ āpaḥ dṛśyanti bhāsvarāḥ pārthiva agni vimiśraḥ asau divyaḥ śuciḥ iti smṛtaḥ ādatte sa tu nāḍīnām sahasreṇa samantataḥ nādeyīḥ ca eva sāmudrīḥ kūpāḥ ca eva tathā ghanāḥ sthāvarāḥ jaṅgamāḥ ca eva vāpī kulyā ādikāḥ apaḥ tāsām catuḥśatāḥ nāḍyaḥ varṣante citra mūrtayaḥ mālyāḥ ca eva mālyāḥ ca ketanāḥ patanāḥ tathā amṛtāḥ nāmataḥ sarvāḥ raśmayaḥ vṛṣṭi sarjanāḥ hima udvahāḥ ca tāḥ nāḍyaḥ raśmayaḥ tri śatāḥ punar reśāḥ meghāḥ ca vātsyāḥ ca hlādinyaḥ hima sarjanāḥ candrabhā nāmataḥ sarvā pīta ābhāḥ ca gabhastayaḥ śuklāḥ ca kakubhāḥ ca eva gāvaḥ viśva bhṛtaḥ tathā śuklāḥ tāḥ nāmataḥ sarvāḥ triśatīḥ gharma sarjanāḥ indraḥ dhātā bhagaḥ pūṣā mitraḥ utha varumā uryamā naṃśuḥ vivasvant tvaṣṭā ca parjanyaḥ viṣṇuḥ eva ca caitre māsī bhavet aṃśuḥ dhātā vaiśākha tāpanaḥ jyeṣṭhe māsi bhavet indraḥ āṣāḍhe ca aryamā raviḥ vivasvāt śravaṇe māsi proṣṭhapāde bhagaḥ smṛtaḥ parjanya āśvayuje māsi tvaṣṭā vai kārttike raviḥ mārgaśīrṣe bhavet mitraḥ pauṣe viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ pañca raśmi sahasrāṇi varuṇasya arka karmaṇi ṣaḍbhiḥ sahasraiḥ pūṣā tu deva oṃśuḥ saptabhiḥ tathā dhātā aṣṭabhiḥ sahasraiḥ tu navabhiḥ tu śatakratuḥ vivasvān daśabhiḥ yāti yāti ekādaśabhiḥ bhagaḥ saptabhiḥ tapate mitraḥ tvaṣṭā smṛtaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ raśmi mahasraiḥ tu viṣṇuḥ tapati medinīm vasaṃte kapilaḥ sūryaḥ grīṣme kāñcana saprabhaḥ śvetaḥ varṣāsu varṇena pāṇḍuḥ śaradi bhāskaraḥ iti varṇāḥ samākhyātāḥ mayā sūrya samudbhavāḥ oṣadhīṣu balam dhatte svadhayā ca pitṛṣu api bhidyate lokam āsādya jala śīta uṣṇa nissravam iti etat maṇḍalam śuklam bhāsvaram sūrya saṃjñitam nakṣatra graha somānām pratiṣṭhā yoniḥ eva ca candra ṛkṣa grahāḥ sarve vijñeyāḥ sūrya saṃbhavāḥ nakṣatra adhipatiḥ somaḥ nayanam vāmam īśituḥ nayanam ca eva mīśasya dakṣiṇam bhāskaraḥ svayam teṣām janānām loke asmin nayanam nayate yatas iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sūryaraśmisvarūpakathanam nāma okonaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śeṣāḥ pañca grahāḥ jñeyāḥ īśvarāḥ kāma cāriṇaḥ paṭhyate ca agniḥ ādityaḥ udakam candramāḥ smṛtaḥ śeṣāṇām prakṛtim samyak vakṣyamāṇām nibodhata sura senāpatiḥ skandaḥ paṭhyate aṅgārakaḥ grahaḥ nārāyaṇam budham prāhuḥ devam jñāna vidaḥ janāḥ mahāgrahaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ manda gāmī śanaiścaraḥ prajāpati sutau uktau tatas śukra bṛhaspatī mūlam akhilam trailokyam na atra saṃśayaḥ sarva ātmā sarva loka īśaḥ mahādevaḥ prajāpatiḥ bhāva abhāvau hi lokānām ādityāt nissṛtau purā kṣaṇāḥ muhūrtāḥ divasāḥ niśāḥ pakṣāḥ ca kṛtsnaśas māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ ca eva ṛtavaḥ atha yugāni ca tadā ādityāḥ dṛte hi eṣā kāla saṃkhyā na vidyate yālāt ṛte na niyamaḥ na dīkṣā na āhnika kramaḥ ṛtūnām ca vibhāgaḥ ca puṣpam mūlam phalam kutas kutas sasya viniṣpattiḥ tṛṇa oṣadhi gaṇaḥ api ca abhāvaḥ vyavahārāṇām jantūnām divi ca iha ca jagat pratāpanam ṛte bhāskaram rudra rūpiṇam saḥ eṣa kālaḥ ca agniḥ ca dvādaśa ātmā prajāpatiḥ tapati eṣa dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ trailokyam sacarācaram saḥ eṣa tejasām rāśiḥ samastaḥ sārvalaukikaḥ pārśvatas ūrdhvam adhas ca eva tāpayati eṣa sarvaśas yathā prabhākaraḥ dīpaḥ gṛha madhye avalaṃbitaḥ raveḥ raśmi sahasram yat prāk mayā samudāhṛtam teṣām śreṣṭhā punar sapta raśmayaḥ graha yonayaḥ viśvavyacāḥ punar ca ādyaḥ saṃnaddhaḥ ca tatas paraḥ sarvāvasuḥ punar ca anyaḥ svarāj anyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ suṣumnaḥ sūrya raśmiḥ tu dakṣiṇām rāśim aidhayat pracāraḥ asya suṣumnaḥ parikīrtitaḥ harikeśaḥ purastāt yaḥ ṛkṣa yoniḥ prakīrtyate viśvavyacāḥ tu yaḥ paścāt śukra yoniḥ smṛtaḥ budhaiḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sarvāvasuḥ raśmiḥ sa yoniḥ tu bṛhaspateḥ manaiścaram punar ca api raśmiḥ āpyāyate svarāj evam sūrya prabhāvena nakṣatra graha tārakāḥ dṛśyante divi tāḥ sarvāḥ viśvam ca idam punar jagat na kṣīyante yatas tāni tasmāt nakṣatra tā smṛtā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca kṣetrāṇi etāni sarvāṇi ātapanti gabhastibhiḥ teṣām kṣetrāṇi atha ādatte sūryaḥ nakṣatra tārakāḥ cīrṇena sukṛtena iha sukṛta ante graha āśrayāḥ tāraṇāt tārakāḥ hi etāḥ śukla tvāt ca eva tārakāḥ divyānām pārthivānām ca naiśānām ca eva sarvaśas mādānāt nityam ādityaḥ tejasām tamasām api savanāt tejasaḥ apām ca tena asau savitā mataḥ śukla tve ca amṛta tve ca śīta tve ca vibhāvyate ghana toya ātmakam tatra maṇḍalam śaśinaḥ smṛtam ghana tejaḥ mayam śuklam maṇḍalam bhāskarasya tu vasaṃti sarva devāḥ ca sthānāni etāni sarvaśas manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛkṣa sūrya graha āśrayāḥ tena te bhavanti ca śaukram śukraḥ aviśat sthānam ṣoḍaśārcīḥ pratāpavān śanaiścaram tathā sthānam devaḥ ca api śanaiścaraḥ baudham budhaḥ tu svarbhānuḥ svarbhānu sthānam āśritaḥ nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi viśanti ca gṛhāni etāni sarvāṇi jyotiṣi sukṛta ātmanām kalpa ādau saṃpravṛttāni nirmitāni svayaṃbhuvā sthānāni etāni tiṣṭhanti yāva dābhūtasaṃplavam abhimāninaḥ avatiṣṭhante devāḥ sthānam punar punar asmin manvantare ca eva grahāḥ vaimānikāḥ smṛtāḥ dyutimān ṛṣi putraḥ tu somaḥ devaḥ vasuḥ smṛtaḥ bṛhattejāḥ smṛtaḥ devaḥ deva ācāryaḥ uṅgiras sutaḥ śanaiścaraḥ virūpaḥ tu saṃjñā putraḥ vivasvataḥ agniḥ vikeśyām jajñe tu yuvā asau lohitārciṣaḥ nakṣatra ṛkṣa nāminyaḥ dākṣāyaṇyaḥ tu tāḥ smṛtāḥ svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputraḥ bhūtasam tāpanaḥ asuraḥ soma ṛkṣa graha sūryeṣu kīrtitāḥ tu abhimāninaḥ sthānāni etāni atha uktāni sthāninyaḥ ca eva devatāḥ sauram agni mayam sthānam sahasrāṃśoḥ vivasvataḥ himāṃśoḥ tu smṛtam sthānam ammayam śuklam eva ca āpyam śyāmam manojñam ca budharaśmigṛham smṛtam śuklasya api ap mayam śuklam padam ṣoḍaśa raśmi vat haridrabham bṛhat ca api ṣoḍaśārciḥ bṛhaspateḥ aṣṭa raśmi gṛham ca api proktam kṛṣṇam śanaiścare svarbhānoḥ tāmasam sthānam bhūtasaṃtāpana ālayam vijñeyaḥ tārakāḥ sarvāḥ tu ṛṣayaḥ tu eka raśmayaḥ mad api sva varṇāt ghana toya ātmakāḥ jñeyāḥ klapa ādau eva nirmitāḥ bhū āditya raśmi saṃyogāt samprakāśa ātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ nava yojana sāhasraḥ viṣkaṃbhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ triguṇaḥ tasya vistāraḥ maṇḍalasya pramāṇāt dviguṇaḥ sūrya vistārāt vistāraḥ śāśinaḥ smṛtaḥ uddhṛtya pṛthivī chāyām nirmitam maṇḍala ākṛtim svarbhānoḥ tu bṛhat sthānam tṛtīyam yat tamaḥ mayam candrasya ṣoḍaśaḥ bhāgaḥ bhārgavasya vidhīyate viṣkambhāt maṇḍalāt ca eva yojana agrāt pramāṇataḥ bhārgavāt pāda hīnaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ vai bṛhaspatiḥ bṛhaspateḥ pāda hīnau vakra saurī ubhau smṛtau vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva pāda hīnaḥ tayoḥ budhaḥ tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi vapuṣmanti iha yāni vai budhena tāni tulyāni vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca vai prāyaśas candra yogīni vidyāt ṛkṣāṇi tattva vid tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve ca eva yojane sarva upari nikṛṣṭāni tārakā maṇḍalāni tu upariṣṭāt trayaḥ teṣām grahāḥ te dūra sarpiṇaḥ saura uṅgirāḥ ca vakraḥ ca jñeyāḥ manda vicāriṇaḥ pūrvam eva samākhyātā gatiḥ teṣām yathākramam eteṣu eva grahaḥ sarve nakṣatreṣu samutthitāḥ vivasvān adityāḥ putraḥ sūryaḥ vai muni sattamāḥ viśākhāsu samutpannaḥ grahāṇām prathamaḥ grahaḥ śītaraśmiḥ samutpannaḥ kṛttikāsu niśākaraḥ bhṛgoḥ putraḥ śukraḥ sūryāt anantaram tārāgrahāṇām pravaraḥ tiṣye kṣetre samutthitaḥ grahaḥ ca aṅgirasaḥ putraḥ dvādaśārcīḥ bṛhaspatiḥ phaālgunīṣu samutpannaḥ pūrva ākhyāsu jagadguruḥ āṣāḍhāsu iha pūrvāsu samutpannaḥ iti smṛtaḥ revatīṣu eva saptārciḥ sthāne sauriḥ śanaiścaraḥ tamaḥ mayaḥ mṛtyu sutaḥ prajā kṣaya karaḥ śikhī āśleṣāsu samutpannaḥ sarva hārī mahā grahaḥ tathā sva nāmadheyeṣu dākṣāyaṇyaḥ samutthitāḥ tamaḥ vīrya mayaḥ rāhuḥ prakṛtyā kṛṣṇa maṇḍalaḥ ete tārāḥ grahāḥ ca api boddhavyāḥ bhārgava ādayaḥ janma nakṣatra pīḍāsu yānti vaiguṇya tām yatas sarva grahānām eteṣām ādiḥ ādityaḥ ucyate tārā grahāṇām śukraḥ tu ketūnām ca api dhūmavān dhruvaḥ kila grahānām tu vibhaktānām caturdiśam nakṣatrāṇām śrapiṣṭhā syāt ayanānām tathā uttaram eva ṛtūnām śiśiraḥ ca api māsānām māghaḥ ucyate pakṣāṇām suklapakṣaḥ tu tithīnām pratipad tathā ahar rātra vibhāgānām ahar ca ādiḥ prakīrtitaḥ muhūrtānām tathā eva ādiḥ muhūrtaḥ rudra daivataḥ kṣaṇaḥ ca api nimeṣa ādiḥ kālaḥ kāla vidām varāḥ śravaṇa antam dhaniṣṭhā ādi yugam syāt pañca vārṣikam divākaraḥ smṛtaḥ tasmāt kāla kṛt vibhuḥ īśvaraḥ caturvidhānām bhūtānām pravartaka nivartakaḥ tasya api bhagavant rudraḥ sākṣāt devaḥ pravartakaḥ iti eṣa jyotiṣām evam saṃniveśaḥ artha niścayaḥ loka saṃvyavahāra artham mahādevena nirmitaḥ na eṣa śakyaḥ prasaṃkhyātum yāthātathyena kena cit manuṣyeṇa jyotiṣām māṃsa cakṣuṣā māgamāt anumānāt ca pratyakṣāt upapattyāḥ parīkṣya nipuṇam buddhyā śraddhātavyam vipaścitā cakṣuḥ śāstram jalam lekhyam gaṇitam muni sattamāḥ pañca ete hetavaḥ jñeyāḥ jyotis māna avinirṇaye iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge grahasaṃkhyāvarṇanam nāma ekaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham viṣṇoḥ prasādāt vai dhruvaḥ buddhimatām varaḥ meḍhī bhūtaḥ grāhānām vai vaktum arhasi sāṃpratam uvāca etam artham mayā pṛṣṭaḥ nānā śāstra viśāradaḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ purā prāha mahyam śuśrūṣave dvijāḥ uvāca sarvābhaumaḥ mahā tejāḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ uttānapādaḥ rājā vai pālayāmāsa medinīm agra jāyām abhūt putraḥ sunītau tu mahā yaśāḥ dhruvaḥ nāma mahā prājñaḥ kula dīpaḥ mahāmatiḥ suruciḥ tam vinirdhūya sva putram prīti mānasā nyaveśayat tam vipra indrāḥ hi aṅkam mānitā a labdhvā sa pituḥ dhīmān aṅkam duḥkhita mānasaḥ mātuḥ samīpam āgamya ruroda sa punar punar rudantam putram āha idam mātā śoka pariplutā suruciḥ dayitā bhartuḥ tasyāḥ putraḥ api tādṛśaḥ mama tvam mandabhāgyāyāḥ jātaḥ putraḥ upi abhāgyavān kim śocasi kimartham tvam rodamānaḥ punar punar santapta hṛdayaḥ bhūtvā mama śokam kariṣyasi svastha sthānam dhruvam putra sva saktyā tvam samāpnuyāḥ viśvāmitram tatas dṛṣṭvā praṇipatya yathāvidhi sarveṣām upari sthānam kena prāpsyāmi sattama pituḥ aṅke samāsīnam mātā mām suruciḥ mune vyadhūnayat sa tam rājā pitā na uvāca kiñcana etasmāt kāraṇāt brahyan trastaḥ ūham mātaram gataḥ sunītiḥ āha mama mātā mā akṛthāḥ śokam uttamam tasyāḥ hi vacanam śrutvā sthānam tava mahā mune prāptaḥ vanam idam brahman adya tvām dṛṣṭavan prabho rāja putra śṛṇuṣva idam sthānam uttamam āpsyasi ārādhya jagatām īśam keśavam kleśa nāśanam dakṣiṇa aṅga bhavam śambhoḥ mahādevasya dhīmataḥ japa nityam mahā prājña sarva pāpa vināśanam iṣṭa dam paramam śuddham pavitram amalam param dhyāyan sanātanam viṣṇum japa homa parāyaṇaḥ iti uktaḥ praṇipatya enam viśvāmitram mahā yaśāḥ prāc mukhaḥ niyataḥ bhūtvā jajāpa prīta mānasaḥ śāka mūla phala āhāraḥ saṃvatsaram atandritaḥ vetālāḥ rākṣasāḥ ghorāḥ siṃha ādyāḥ ca mahā mṛgāḥ tam abhyayus mahātmānam buddhi mohāya bhīṣaṇāḥ yā mātā tasyāḥ rūpeṇa saṃvṛtā piśāci samanuprāptā ruroda bhṛśa duḥkha tā mām anāthām apahāya tapaḥ āsthitavān asi evamādīni vākyāni bhāṣamāṇām mahā tapāḥ a nirīkṣya eva hṛṣṭa ātmā hareḥ nāma jajāpa saḥ sarva devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ stūyamānaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ bhagavant viṣṇuḥ dhruvantikam arāti hā piban iva hṛṣīkeśam naya nābhau jagatpatim śaṅkha prāntena govindaḥ pasparśa āsyam hi tasya vai tatas sa paramam jñānam avāpya kuruṣottamam tuṣṭāva prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā sarva loka īśvaram harim na viduḥ tvām mahātmānam sanaka ādyāḥ naha ṛṣayaḥ sthānam dhruvam samāsādya dyotiṣām agra bhuj bhava mātrā tvam sahitaḥ tatra jyotiṣām sthānam āpnuhi tapasā ārādhya deveśam purā labdham hi śaṃkarāt tatas devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ viṣṇoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya jyotiṣām sthānam āptavān evam dhruvaḥ mahā tejāḥ dvādaśa akṣara vidyayā uvāca tasmāt yaḥ vāsudevāya praṇāmam kurute naraḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge bhuvanakośe dhruvasaṃsthānavarṇanam nāma dviṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ devānām dānavānām ca gandharva uraga rakṣasām uvāca saṃkalpāt darśanāt sparśāt pūrveṣām sṛṣṭiḥ ucyate dakṣāt prācetasāt ūrdhvam sṛṣṭiḥ maithuna saṃbhavā dakṣaḥ putra sahasrāṇi pañca sūtyām ajījanat tān tu dṛṣṭvā mahābhāgān sisṛkṣuḥ vividhāḥ prajāḥ nāradaḥ prāha haryaśvān dakṣa putrān samāgatān bhuvaḥ pramāṇam sarvam tu jñātvā ūrdhvam adhas eva ca tatas sṛṣṭim viśeṣeṇa kurudhvam muni sattamāḥ te tu tad vacanam śrutvā prayātāḥ sarvatodiśam haryaśveṣu ca naṣṭeṣu punar dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ sūtyām eva ca putrāṇām sahasram asṛjat prabhuḥ śabalāḥ nāma te viprāḥ sametāḥ sṛṣṭi hetavaḥ nāradaḥ nugatān prāha punar tān sūrya varcasaḥ bhuvaḥ pramāṇam sarvam tu jñātvā bhrātṝn punar punar āgatya vā atha sṛṣṭim vai kariṣyatha viśeṣataḥ te api tena eva mārgeṇa jagmuḥ bhrātṛ gatim tathā tatas teṣu api naṣṭeṣu ṣaṣṭi kanyāḥ prajāpatiḥ hairiṇyām janayāmāsa dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ tadā prādāt sa daśakam dharme kaśyapāya trayodaśa dve ca eva bhṛguputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate dve ca eva aṅgirase tadvat tāsām nāmāni vistarāt śṛṇudhvam devamātṝṇām prajā vistāram āditas marutvatī vasūḥ yāmiḥ labā bhānuḥ arundhatī saṃkalpā ca muhūrtā ca sādhyā viśvā ca bhāmini dharmapatnyaḥ samākhyātāḥ tāsām putrān vadāmi vaḥ viśvedevāḥ tu viśvāyāḥ sādhyā sādhyān ajījanat bhānoḥ tu bhānavaḥ proktāḥ muhūrtāyāḥ muhūrtakāḥ lambāyāḥ ghoṣa nāmānaḥ nāgavīthī tu yāmi jaḥ saṃkalpāyāḥ tu saṃkalpaḥ vasu sargam vadāmi vaḥ jyotiṣmantaḥ tu ye devāḥ vyāpakāḥ sarvatodiśam vasavaḥ te samākhyātāḥ sarva bhūta hita eṣiṇaḥ mahā apaḥ dhruvaḥ ca somaḥ ca dharaḥ ca eva anila unalaḥ pratyūṣaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ oṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ haraḥ ca bahurūpaḥ ca tryaṃbakaḥ ca sureśvaraḥ sāvitraḥ ca jayantaḥ ca pinākī ca aparājitaḥ ete rudrāḥ samā khyātāḥ ekādaśa gaṇa īśvarāḥ aditiḥ ca ditiḥ ca eva ariṣṭā surasā muniḥ surabhiḥ vinatā tāmrā tadvat krodhavaśā ilā kadruḥ tviṣā danuḥ tadvat tāsām putrān vadāmi vaḥ tuṣitāḥ nāma ye devāḥ cākṣuṣa idam antare manoḥ te vai ādityāḥ dvādaśa smṛtāḥ vivasvān savitā pūṣā aṃśumant viṣṇuḥ eva ca ete sahasrakiraṇāḥ ādītyāḥ dvādaśa smṛtāḥ hiraṇyakaśipum ca eva hiraṇyākṣam tathā eva ca vipracittiḥ pradhānaḥ bhūt teṣām madhye dvijottamāḥ tāmrā ca janayāmāsa ṣaḍ kanyāḥ dvija puṃgavāḥ śukīm śyenīm ca bhāsīm ca sugrīvīm gṛdhrikām śucim śukī śukān ulūkān ca janayāmāsa dharmataḥ śyenī śyenān tathā bhāsī kuraṅgān ca vyajījanat gṛdhrī gṛdhrān kapotān ca pārāvatī vihaṃgamān haṃsa sārasa kāraṇḍa plavān śuciḥ ajījanat aja aśva meṣa uṣṭra kharān sugrīvī ca api ajījanat vinatā janayā māsa garuḍam ca aruṇam śubhā saudāminīm tathā kanyām sarva loka bhayaṅkarīm surasāyāḥ sahasram tu sarpāṇām abhavat purā kadrūḥ sahasra śirasām sahasram prāpa su vratā pradhānāḥ teṣu vikhyātāḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ anuttamāḥ śeṣa vāsuki karkoca śaṅkha airāvata kambalāḥ dhanañjaya mahānīla padma aśvatara takṣakāḥ elāpattra mahāpadma dhṛtarāṣṭra balāhakāḥ śaṅkhapāla mahāśaṅkha paṣpadaṃṣṭra śubha ānanāḥ śaṅkha lomā ca nahuṣaḥ vāmanaḥ phamitaḥ tathā rakṣaḥ gaṇam krodhavaśā mahā māyam vyajījanat rudrāṇām ca gaṇam tadvat go mahiṣyau vara aṅganā surabhiḥ janayāmāsa kaśyapāt iti naḥ śrutam muniḥ munīnām ca gaṇam gaṇam apsarasām tathā kiṃnara gandharvān ariṣṭā janayat bahūn tṛṇa vṛkṣa latā gulmam ilā sarvam ajījanat tviṣā tu yakṣa rakṣāṃsi janayāmāsa koṭiśas ete tu kāśyapeyāḥ ca saṃkṣepāt parikīrtitāḥ eteṣām putra pautra ādi vaṃśāḥ ca bahavaḥ smṛtāḥ evam prajāsu sṛṣṭāsu kaśyapena mahātmanā pratiṣṭhitāsu sarvāsu carāsu sthāvarāsu ca abhiṣicya ādhipatyeṣu teṣām mukhyān prajāpatiḥ svāyaṃbhuventare pūrvam brahmaṇā ye abhiṣecitāḥ taiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sa parvatā svāyaṃbhuventare pūrve brahmaṇā ye abhiṣecitāḥ manvantareṣu atīteṣu gatāḥ hi eteṣu pārthivāḥ atīta anāgatāḥ sarve nṛpāḥ manvantare smṛtāḥ etān utpādya putrān tu prajā saṃtāna kāraṇāt ha vatsarāt naidhruvaḥ jajñe raibhyaḥ ca su mahā yaśāḥ naidhruvasya tu sā patnī mātā vai kuṇḍapāyinām asitasya ekaparṇāyām brahmiṣṭhaḥ samapadyata śāṇḍilyānām varaḥ śrīmān devalaḥ su mahā tapāḥ śāṇḍilyāḥ naidhruvāḥ raibhyāḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ tu kāśyapāḥ ardha avaśiṣṭe tasmin tu dvāpare saṃpravartite mānavasya nariṣyantaḥ putraḥ āsīt damaḥ kila damasya tasya dāyādaḥ tṛṇabinduḥ iti smṛtaḥ tretā yuga mukhe rājā tṛtīye saṃbabhūva ha tasya kanyā tu ilavilā rūpeṇa apratimā abhavat purastyāya sa rājarṣiḥ tām kanyām pratyapādayat ṛṣiḥ airavilaḥ yasyām viśravāḥ samapadyata bṛhaspateḥ śubhā kanyā nāmnā vai devavarṇinī puṣpotkaṭā balākā ca sute mālyavantaḥ smṛtyāḥ kaikasī mālinaḥ kanyā tāsām vai śṛṇuta prajāḥ jyeṣṭham vaiśravaṇam tasmāt suṣuve deva varṇinī ca api ajanayat rāvaṇam rākṣasa adhipam kumbhakarṇam śūrpa nakhām dhīmantam ca vibhiṣaṇam puṣpotkaṭā hi ajanayat putrān tasmāt dvijottamāḥ mahodaram prahastam ca mahāpārśvam kharam tathā kumbhīnasīm tathā kanyām balāyāḥ śṛṇuta prajāḥ triśirāḥ dūṣamaḥ ca eva vidyujjihvaḥ ca rākṣasaḥ kanyā vai mālikā ca api balāyāḥ prasavaḥ smṛtaḥ iti ete krūra karmāṇaḥ paulastyāḥ rākṣasāḥ nava pulastyasya mṛgāḥ putrāḥ sarve vyāghraḥ ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ sarpāḥ ca sūkarāḥ hastinaḥ tathā vānarāḥ kiṃnarāḥ ca eva ye ca kimpuruṣāḥ tathā treḥ patnyaḥ daśa eva āsan sundaryaḥ ca pativratāḥ bhadrāśvasya ghṛtācyām vai daśa apsarasi sūnavaḥ balābalā ca vipra indrāḥ yā ca gopābalā smṛtā tathā tāmarasā ca eva varakrīḍā ca vai daśa ātreya vaṃśa prabhavāḥ stāsām bhartā prabhākaraḥ bhadrāyām janayāmāsa somam putram yaśasvinam sa tāsu janayāmāsa punar putrān tapodhanaḥ svastyātreyāḥ iti khyātāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vedapāragāḥ teṣām dvau khyāta yaśasau brahmiṣṭhau ca mahā ojasau yavīyāḥ svasā teṣām amalā brahma vādinī śyāvaḥ ca pratvasaḥ ca eva vavalguḥ ca atha gahvaraḥ ātreyāṇām ca catvāraḥ smṛtāḥ pakṣāḥ mahātmanām kāśyapaḥ nāradaḥ ca eva parvata anuddhataḥ tathā nāradaḥ tu vasiṣṭhāya arundhatīm pratyapādayat ūrdhvaretāḥ mahā tejāḥ dakṣa śāpāt tu nāradaḥ anāvṛṣṭyā hate loke hi ugre lokeśvaraiḥ saha vasiṣṭhaḥ tapasā dhīmān dhārayāmāsa vai prajāḥ tān etān jīvayāmāsa kāruṇyāt auṣadhena ca jyāyasaḥ janayat śakteḥ adṛśyantī parāśaram rakṣasā bhakṣite śaktau rudhireṇa tu vai tadā parāśarāt jajñe kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam prabhum upamanyum ca pīvaryām viddhi ime suka sūnavaḥ bhūriśravāḥ prabhuḥ śaṃbhuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ gauraḥ tu pañcamaḥ kanyā kīrti matī ca eva yogamātrī dhṛta vratā śvetaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca gauraḥ ca śyāmaḥ dhūmraḥ tathā aruṇaḥ nīlaḥ bādarikaḥ ca eva sarve ca ete parāśarāḥ parāśarāṇām aṣṭa te pakṣāḥ proktāḥ mahātmanām vasiṣṭhasya kapiñjalyaḥ ghṛtācyām udapadyata pṛthoḥ sutāyām saṃbhūtaḥ bhadraḥ tasyāḥ bhavadvasuḥ mitrāvaruṇayoḥ ca eva kauṇḍinyāḥ ye pariśrutāḥ eka ārṣeyāḥ tathā ca anye vāsiṣṭhāḥ nāma viśrutāḥ ete pakṣāḥ vasiṣṭhānām smṛtāḥ daśa mahātmanām iti ete brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ mānasāḥ viśrutāḥ bhuvi bhartāraḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ eṣām vaṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ triloka dhāraṇe śaktāḥ deva ṛṣi kula saṃbhavāḥ teṣām putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ ca sahasraśas iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge devādisṛṣṭikathanam nāma triṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ ha vāsiṣṭhaḥ vadatām śreṣṭha sūta vaktum iha arhasi uvāca rākṣasaḥ rudhiraḥ nāma vasiṣṭhasya sutam purā śaktim sa bhakṣayāmāsa śakteḥ śāpāt saha anujaiḥ vasiṣṭha yājyam vipra indrāḥ tadā diśya eva bhūpatim kalmāṣapādam rudhiraḥ viśvāmitreṇa coditaḥ bhakṣitaḥ saḥ iti śrutvā vasiṣṭhaḥ tena rakṣasā śaktiḥ śaktimatām śreṣṭhaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha dharma vid naṣṭam kulam iti śrutvā martum cakre matim tadā smaran putra śatam ca eva śakti jyeṣṭham ca śaktimān na tam vinā aham jīviṣye iti niścitya duḥkhitaḥ dharādharasya eva tadā dharāyām papāta patnyā sahasā aśru dṛṣṭiḥ dharādharāt tam patitam dharā tadā dadhāra tatra api vicitra kaṇṭhī kara ambujābhyām kari khela gāminī rudantam ādāya ruroda sā ca tadā tasya snuṣā prāha patnī śakteḥ mahā munim vasiṣṭham vadatām śreṣṭham rudantī bhaya vihvalā bhagavan brāhmaṇa śreṣṭha tava devam idam śubham evam uktvā atha dharma jñā karābhyām kamala īkṣaṇā utthāpya śvaśuram natvā netre saṃmṛjya vāriṇā duḥkhitā api paritrātum śvaśuram duḥkhitam tadā arundhatīm ca kalyāṇām prārthayāmāsa duḥkhitām snuṣā vākyam tatas śrutvā vasiṣṭha utthāya bhū talāt saṃjñām avāpya ca āliṅgya sā papāta su duḥkhitā aṃrudhatī kārabyām tām saṃspṛśya asra ākula īkṣaṇām ruroda muni śārdūlaḥ suta vatsalaḥ atha nābhi aṃbuje viṣṇoḥ yathā tasyāḥ caturmukhaḥ bhāsīnaḥ garbhaśayyāyām kumāraḥ ṛcam āha saḥ tatas niśamya bhagavān vasiṣṭhaḥ ṛcam ādarāt kena uktam iti saṃcintya tat ātiṣṭhat samāhitaḥ vyoma aṅgaṇa stha utha hariḥ puṇḍarīka nibha īkṣaṇaḥ vasiṣṭham āha viśvātmā ghṛṇayā sa ghṛṇā nidhiḥ tava pautra mukha aṃbhoja ādṛś eṣā adya viniḥsṛtā evam uktvā ghṛṇī vipram bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ vasiṣṭham muni śārdūlam tatra eva antaradhīyata tatas praṇamya śirasā vasiṣṭhaḥ vārija īkṣaṇam adṛśyantyā mahā tejāḥ pasparśa udaram ādarāt lalāpa arundhatī prekṣya tadā asau rudatīm dvijāḥ tava putram imam dṛṣṭvā bho śakte kula dhāraṇam tava antikam gamiṣyāmi tava mātrā na saṃśayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā rudan vipraḥ āliṅgya arundhatīm tadā papāta tāḍayantī iva svasya kukṣī karema vai adṛsyantī jaghāna atha śakti jasya ālayam śubhā sva udaram duḥkhitā bhūmau lalāpa ca papāta ca arundhati tadā bhītā vasiṣṭhaḥ ca mahāmatiḥ samutthāpya snuṣām bālām ūcatuḥ bhaya vihvalau tava ātmajam śakti sutam ca dṛṣṭvā ca āsvādya vaktra amṛtam ārya sūnoḥ trātum yatas deham imam muni indraḥ su niścitaḥ pāhi tatas śarīram uvāca evam snuṣām upālabhya munim ca arundhatī sthitā arandhatī vasiṣṭhasya prāha ca ārtā iti vihvalā jīvitam rakṣa dehasya dhātrī ca kuru yāt hitam uvāca mayā yadi muni śreṣṭhaḥ trātum vai niścitam svakam mama aśubham śubham deham kathaṃcid pālayāmi aham priya duḥkha maham hi asatī na atra saṃśayaḥ mune duḥkhāt aham dagdhā yatas putrī mune tava aho udbhutam mayā dṛṣṭam duḥkha pātrī hi aham vibho tathā api bhartṛ rahitā dīnā nāri bhavet iha pāhi mām tatas ārya indra paribhūtā bhaviṣyati pitā mātā ca putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ śvaśuraḥ eva ca ete na bāndhavāḥ strīṇām bhartā bandhuḥ parā gatiḥ tat api atra mṛṣā hi āsīt gataḥ śaktiḥ aham sthitā patim prāṇa samam tyaktvā sthitā yatra kṣaṇam yatas vasiṣṭha aśvattham āśritya hi amṛtā tu yathā latā nirmūlā api amṛtā bhartrā atyaktā dīnā sthitā api aham snuṣā vākyam niśamya eva vasiṣṭhaḥ bhāryayā saha tadā cakre matim dhīmān yātum sva āśramam āśramī kṛcchrāt sa bhāryaḥ bhagavān vāsiṣṭhaḥ sva āśramam kṣaṇāt adṛśyantyā ca puṇya ātmā saṃviveśa sa cintayan sā garbham pālayāmāsa kathacid muni puṃgavāḥ kula saṃdhāraṇa arthāya patnī pativratā tatas sā asūta tanayam daśame māsi su prabham śakti patnī yathā śaktim śaktimantam arundhatī asūta sā ditiḥ viṣṇum yatā svāhā guham sutam agnim yathā araṇiḥ patnī śakteḥ sākṣāt parāśaram yadā tadā śaktisūjuḥ avatīrṇaḥ mahī tale śaktiḥ tyaktvā tadā duḥkham pitṝṇām sama tām yayau bhrātṛbhiḥ saha puṇya ātmā ādityaiḥ iva bhāskaraḥ rarāja pitṛ loka sthaḥ vāsiṣṭhaḥ muni puṃgavāḥ jaguḥ tadā ca pitaraḥ nanṛtuḥ ca pitāmahāḥ prapitāmahāḥ ca vipra indrāḥ hi avatīrṇe parāśare puṣkara ādyāḥ ca sasṛjuḥ puṣpa varṣam ca khecarāḥ pureṣu rākṣasānām ca praṇādam viṣamam dvijāḥ munayaḥ samūhuḥ harṣa saṃtatim avatīrṇaḥ yathā hi aṇḍāt bhānuḥ saḥ api parāśaraḥ adṛśyantyāḥ catur vaktraḥ megha jālāt divākaraḥ sukham ca duḥkham abhavat adṛśyantyāḥ tathā dvijāḥ dṛṣṭvā putram patim smṛtvā muneḥ tathā dṛṣṭvā ca tanayam bālā parāśaram ati dyutim lalāpa vihvalā bālā sannakaṇṭhā papāta ca sā parāśaram aho mahāmatim deva dānava gaṇaiḥ ca pūjitam mātram anagham śuci smitā budhya sa aśru nayanā lalāpa ca tyajya dīna vadanām vana antare putra darśana parām imām prabho śakte svam ca sutam paśya bhrātṛbhiḥ saha ṣaṣ mukham yathā maheśvara upaśyat sa gaṇaḥ hṛṣita ānanaḥ atha tasyāḥ tad ālāpam vasiṣṭhaḥ muni sattamaḥ śrutvā snuṣām uvāca idam mā arodīḥ iti duḥkhitaḥ ājñayā tasya sā śokam visiṣṭhasya kula aṅganā tyaktvā hi apālayat bālam bālā bāla mṛga īkṣaṇā dṛṣṭvā tām abalām prāha maṅgala ābharaṇaiḥ vinā māsīnām ākulām sādhum bāṣpa paryākule kṣaṇām uvāca amba maṅgala vibhūṣaṇaiḥ vinā deha yaṣṭiḥ anaghe na śobhate mātar mātar katham tyaktvā maṅgala ābharaṇāni vai māsīnā bhartṛ hīnā iva vaktum arhasi śobhane adṛśyantī tadā vākyam śrutvā tasya sutasya sā na kiṃcid abravīt putram śubham vā yadi vā itarat adṛśyantīm punar prāha śākteyaḥ bhagavān mama mātar kutra mahā tejāḥ pitā vada vada iti tām śrutvā ruroda sā vākyam putrasya atīva vihvalā śrutvā vasiṣṭhaḥ api papāta bhūmau pautrasya vākyam sa rudan dayāluḥ arundhatī ca āśrama vāsinaḥ tadā muneḥ vasiṣṭhasya muni īśvarāḥ ca śrutvā vasiṣṭhaḥ api papāta bhūmau pautrasya vākyam sa rudan dayāluḥ arundhatī ca āśrama vāsinaḥ tadā muneḥ vasiṣṭhasya muni īśvarāḥ ca bhakṣitaḥ rakṣasā mātuḥ pitā tava mukāt iti śrutvā parāśaraḥ dhīmān prāha ca asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ uvāca mātar pitaram darśayāmi iti mama matiḥ sā niśamya vacanam tadā śubham sa smitā tanayam āha vismitā jñātvā śakti sutasya asya saṃkalpam muni puṃgavaḥ mahān prāha pautram dhīmān ghṛṇā nidhiḥ tathā api śṛṇu lokasya kṣayam kartum na ca arhasi rākṣasānām abhāvāya kuru sarvesvara arcanam trailokyam śṛṇu śākteya aparādhyati kim tava rākṣasānām abhāvāya matim cakre mahāmatiḥ adṛśyantīm vasiṣṭham ca praṇamya arundhatīm tatas kṛtvā eka liṅgam kṣaṇikam pāṃsunā muni sāṃnidhau saṃpūjya śivasūktena tryaṃbakena śubhena ca nīla rudram ca śākteyaḥ tathā rudram ca śobhanam mānīyam pavamānam ca pañca brahma tathā eva ca hotāram liṅga sūktam ca atharvaśiraḥ eva ca aṣṭāṅgam arghyam rudrāya da tvā abhyarcya yathāvidhi uvāca pitā mama mahā tejāḥ bhratṛbhiḥ saha śaṃkara evam vijñāpayān liṅgam praṇipatya muhur muhur tam dṛṣṭvā bhagavant nudraḥ devīm āha ca śaṃkaraḥ paśya bālam mahābhāge bāṣpa paryakula īkṣaṇam sā ca dṛṣṭvā mahādevī parāśaram aninditā prāha bhartāram īśānam śaṃkaram jagantām umā īṣsitam yaccha sakalam prasīda parameśvara niśamya vacanam tasyāḥ śaṃkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ bhāryām āryām umām prāha tatas hālāhala aśanaḥ rakṣāmi enam dvijam bālam phulla indīvara locanam dadāmi dṛṣṭim mad rūpa darśana kṣamaḥ eṣa vai brahma indra viṣṇu rudra ādyaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ saḥ api dṛṣṭvā mahādevam ānanda asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ nipapāta ca hṛṣṭa ātmā pādayoḥ tasya sa ādaram punar bhavānyāḥ pādau ca nandinaḥ ca mahātmanaḥ saphalam jīvitam medyaiḥ brahma ādyān tān tat āha saḥ rakṣā artham āgataḥ tu adya mama vāla indu bhūṣaṇaḥ pitaram bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdha śāktoyaḥ tu parāśaraḥ sūrya maṇḍala saṃkāśe vimāne viśvatas mukhe bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitam dṛṣṭvā nanāma ca jaharṣa ca tadā vṛṣadhvajaḥ devaḥ sa bhāryaḥ sa gaṇeśvaraḥ uvāca śakte paśya sutam bālam ānanda asra āvila īkṣaṇam adṛśyantīm ca vipra indra vasiṣṭham pitaram te arundhatīm mahābhāgām kalyāṇīm devatā upamām tadā haram praṇamya āśu devadevam umām tathā vasiṣṭham ca tadā śreṣṭham śaktiḥ vai śaṃkara ājñayā mātaram ca mahābhāgām kalyāṇīm pati devatām arundhatīm jagannātha niyogāt prāha śaktimān uvāca rakṣitaḥ aham tvayā tāta garbha sthena mahātmanā aṇima ādi guṇa aiśvaryam mayā vatsa parāśara labdham adya ānanam dṛṣṭam te bāla mama ājñayā adṛśyantīm mahābhāgām rakṣa vatsa mahāmate arundhatīm ca pitaram vasiṣṭham mama sarvadā īpsitam varaya īśānam jagantām prabhavam prabhum gamiṣyāmi abhivandya īśam bhrātṛbhiḥ saha śakaram nirīkṣya bhāryām sadasi jagāma pitaram vaśī gatam dṛṣṭvā atha pitaram tadā abhyarcya eva śaṃkaram tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ śākteyaḥ śaśibhūṣaṇam anugṛhya atha śākteyam tatra eva antaradhīyata dadāha rākṣasāṇām tu kulam mantreṇa mantra vid tadā āha pautram dharma jñaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ munibhiḥ vṛtaḥ rākṣasāḥ na aparādhyanti pituḥ te vihitam tathā mūḍhānām eva bhavati krodhaḥ buddhimatām na hi saṃcitasya ati mahatā vatsa kleśena mānavaiḥ yaśasaḥ tapasaḥ ca eva krodhaḥ nāśa karaḥ smṛtaḥ satram te viramatu etat kṣamā sārāḥ hi sādhavaḥ evam vasiṣṭha vākyena śākteyaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ tatas prītaḥ ca bhagavān vasiṣṭhaḥ muni sattamaḥ saṃprāptaḥ ca tadā satram pulastyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ vasiṣṭhena tu datta arghyaḥ kṛta āsana parigrahaḥ parāśaram uvāca idam praṇipatya sthitam muniḥ vaire mahati yad vākyāt guroḥ adya āśritā akṣamā tvayā tasmāt samastāni bhavān śāstrāṇi vetsyati tvayā tasmāt mahābhāga dadami anyam mahā varam purāṇa saṃhitā kartā bhavān vatsaiḥ bhaviṣyati pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā karmaṇaḥ te amalā matiḥ tatas ca prāha bhagavān vasiṣṭhaḥ vadatām varaḥ prasādāt vaiṣṇavam cakre purāṇam vai parāśaraḥ ṣaṣ prakāram samasta artha sādhakam jñāna saṃcayam ṣaṣ sāhasra mitam sarvam veda arthena ca saṃyutam caturtham hi purāṇānām saṃhitāsu su śobhanam eṣa vaḥ kathitaḥ sarve vāsiṣṭhānām samāsatas prabhavaḥ śakti sūnoḥ ca prabhāvaḥ muni puṃgavāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vāsiṣṭhakathanam nāma catuḥṣaṣṭimaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ āditya vaṃśam somasya vaṃśam vaṃśa vidām vara vaktum arhasi ca naḥ saṃkṣepāt romaharṣaṇam uvāca aditiḥ suṣuve putram ādityam kaśyapāt dvijāḥ saṃjñā rājñī prabhā chāyā putrān tāsām vadāmi vaḥ saṃjñā tvāṣṭrī ca suṣuve sūryāt manum anuttamam yamam ca yamunām ca eva rājñī revatam eva ca prabhā prabātam ādityāt chāyām saṃjñāpyakalpayat chāyā ca tasmāt suṣuve sāvarṇi bhāskarāt dvijāḥ tatas śanim ca tapatīm viṣṭim ca eva yata ākramam saṃtāḍayāmāsa ruṣā pādam udyamya dakṣiṇam yam eva tāḍitā sā tu chāyā vai duḥkhitā abhavat pūya śoṇita saṃpūrṇam kṛmīṇām nicaya anvitam saḥ api gokarṇam āśritya phalakena anila aśanaḥ mahādevam yāvat varṣa ayuta ayutam pitṝṇām ādhipatyam tu śāpa mokṣam tathā eva ca labdhavān devadevasya prabhāvāt śūlapāṇinaḥ rūpam tvāṣṭrī sva dehāt tu chāyā ākhyām sā tu akalpayat haḍabā rūpam āsthāya tapaḥ tepe tu suvratā kālāt prayatnāt jñātvā chāyām chāyāpatiḥ prabhuḥ vaḍabām agamat saṃjñām aśva rūpeṇa bhāskaraḥ vaḍabā ca tadā tvāṣṭrī saṃjñā tasmāt divākarāt suṣuve ca aśvinau devau devānām tu bhiṣaj prasādāt muni puṃgavāḥ punar śaravaṇam prāpya strī tvam prāptaḥ bhava ājñayā sudyumnaḥ mānavaḥ śrīmān soma vaṃśa pravṛddhaye tasya ilā kiṃpuruṣaḥ abhavat māsam ekam pumān vīraḥ strī tvam māsam abhūt punar somaputrāt budhāt ca api ailaḥ jajñe purūravāḥ soma vaṃśa agrajaḥ dhīmān bhava bhaktaḥ pratāpavān yad ikṣvākoḥ vaṃśa vistāram paścāt vakṣye tapodhanāḥ utkalasya utkalam rāṣṭram vinatāśvasya paścimam gayā gayasya ca ākhyātā purī parama śobhanā surāṇām saṃsthitiḥ yasyām pitṝṇām ca sadā sthitiḥ avāptavan vasiṣṭha vacanāt tu āsīt pratīṣṭhāne mahā dyutiḥ tat purūravase prādāt rājyam prāpyaḥ mahā yaśāḥ mānaveyaḥ mahābhāgaḥ strī lakṣaṇa anvitaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ putra śatasya āsīt daśa pañca ca tad sutāḥ tatas pṛthuḥ muni śreṣṭhāḥ viśvakaḥ pārthivaḥ tathā viśvakasya ārdrakaḥ dhīmān yuvanāśvaḥ tu tad sutaḥ śābastiḥ ca mahā tejāḥ vaṃśakaḥ tu tatas bhavat nirmitā yena śābastī gauḍa deśe dvijottamāḥ vaṃśāt ca bṛhadaśvaḥ bhūt kuvalāśvaḥ tu tad sutaḥ dṛḍhāśvaḥ ca eva caṇḍāśvaḥ kapilāśvaḥ ca te smṛtāḥ ca saṃhatāśva ātmajā pubhau yuvanāśvaḥ raṇāśvasya māndhātā tasya vai sutaḥ māndhātuḥ ca vīryavān mucukundaḥ ca puṇya ātmā trayaḥ trailokya viśrutāḥ ambarīṣasya dāyādaḥ yuvān āśva uparaḥ smṛtaḥ haritaḥ yuvanāśvasya haritāḥ tu yatas smṛtāḥ ete hi aṅgirasaḥ pakṣe kṣatra upetāḥ dvijātayaḥ purukutsasya dāyādaḥ trasaddasyuḥ mahā yaśāḥ narmadāyām samutpannaḥ saṃbhūtiḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ viṣṇuvṛddhaḥ sutaḥ tasya viṣṇuvṛddhāḥ yatas smṛtāḥ ete hi aṅgirasaḥ pakṣe kṣatra upetāḥ samāśritāḥ haryaśvāt tu dṛṣadvatyām jajñe vasumanāḥ nṛpaḥ prasādāt brahya sūnoḥ vai taṇḍinaḥ prāpya siṣyatām aśvamedha sahasrasya phalam prāpya tad ājñayā dhana hīnaḥ ca dharma ātmā dṛṣṭavān brahmaṇaḥ sutam taṇḍi saṃjñam dvijam tasmāt labdhavan dvijasattamāḥ nāmnām sahasram rudrasya brahmaṇā kathitam purā tena nāmnām sahasreṇa stutvā taṇḍiḥ maheśvaram tatas tasmāt nṛpaḥ labdhvā taṇḍinā kathitam purā nāmnām sahasram japtvā vai gāṇapatyam avāptavān ūcuḥ nāmnām sahasram rudrasya tāṇḍinā brahma yoninā nāmnām sahasram viprāṇām vaktam arhasi śobhanam uvāca aṣṭostara sahasram tu nāmnām śṛṇuta suvratāḥ yat japtvā tu muni śreṣṭhāḥ gāṇapatyam avāptavān sthiraḥ sthāṇuḥ prabhuḥ bhānuḥ pravare vara daḥ varaḥ jaṭī daṇḍī śikhaṇḍī ca sarvagaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ hariḥ ca hariṇākṣaḥ ca sarva bhūta haraḥ smṛtaḥ pravṛttiḥ ca nivṛttiḥ ca śānta ātmā śāśvataḥ dhruvaḥ śmaśāna vāsī bhagavān khacaraḥ gocara irdanaḥ abhivādyaḥ mahā karmā tapasvī bhūta dhārāmaḥ mahā rūpaḥ mahā kāyaḥ sarva rūpaḥ mahā yaśāḥ mahātmā sarva bhūtaḥ ca virupaḥ vāmanaḥ naraḥ pavitraḥ ca mahān ca eva niyataḥ niyata āśrayaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ sarva karmā ca ādiḥ ādi karaḥ nidhiḥ sahasrākṣaḥ viśālākṣaḥ somaḥ nakṣatrasādhakaḥ candraḥ sūryaḥ śāniḥ ketuḥ grahaḥ grahapatiḥ mataḥ rājā rājya udayaḥ kartā mṛga bāṇa arpaṇaḥ ghanaḥ mahā tapāḥ darghita pāḥ adṛśyaḥ dhana sādhakaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ kṛtaḥ mantra prāṇāyāmaḥ parantapaḥ yogī yogaḥ mahābījaḥ mahārataḥ mahābalaḥ suvarṇaretāḥ sarvajñaḥ subījaḥ vṛṣavāhanaḥ daśabāhuḥ tu animiṣaḥ nīlakaṇṭhaḥ umāpatiḥ bala vīraḥ bala agraṇī ca kamaṇḍalu dharaḥ dhanvī bāṇa hastaḥ kapālavān śarī śataghnī khaṅgī ca paṭṭiśī ca āyudhī mahān uṣṇīṣī ca suvaktraḥ ca udagraḥ vinataḥ tathā dīrghaḥ ca harikeśaḥ ca sutīrthaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva ca śṛgāla rūpaḥ sarva arthaḥ muṇḍaḥ sarva śubhaṅkaraḥ siṃha śārdula rūpaḥ ca gandhakārī kapardī api ūrdhvaretāḥ ūrdhvaliṅgī ca ūrdhvaśāyī nabhastalaḥ trijaṭī cīra vāsāḥ ca rudraḥ senā patiḥ vibhuḥ gaja hā daitya hā kālaḥ loka dhātā guṇa ākaraḥ siṃha śārdula rūpāṇām ārdra carma aṃbaraṃdharaḥ tad yogī mahā nādaḥ sarva āvāsaḥ catuṣpathaḥ niśācaraḥ pretacārī sarvadarśī maheśvaraḥ bahu bhūtaḥ bahu dhanaḥ sarva sāraḥ amṛta īśvaraḥ sa kārmukaḥ mahā bāhuḥ mahā ghoraḥ mahā tapāḥ mahā śaraḥ mahā pāśaḥ nityaḥ giri caraḥ mataḥ amarṣaṇaḥ marṣaṇa ātmā yajña hā kāma nāśanaḥ gambhīra ghoṣaḥ yoga ātmā yajña hā kāma nāśanaḥ gambhīra roṣaḥ gambhīraḥ gambhīra bala vāhanaḥ tīkṣṇa upāyaḥ ca haryaśvaḥ sahāyaḥ karma kāla vid viṣṇuḥ prasāditaḥ yajñaḥ samudraḥ vaḍavāmukhaḥ hutāśana sahāyaḥ ca praśānta ātmā hutāśanaḥ khaṅgī śaṅkhī jaṭī jvālī kha caraḥ dyucaraḥ balī vaiṇavī paṇavī kālaḥ kālakaṇṭhaḥ kaṭam kaṭaḥ mekhalā ākṛti rūpaḥ ca jala ācāraḥ stutaḥ tathā vīṇī ca paṇavī tālī nālī kalikaṭuḥ tathā vimocanaḥ bandhanaḥ tu sura indrāṇām yudhi śatru vināśanaḥ sakhiḥ pravāsaḥ durvāpaḥ sarva sādhu niṣevitaḥ sarva vāsaḥ sarva cārī durvāsāḥ vāsavaḥ mataḥ ākāśaḥ nirvirūpaḥ ca vivāsāḥ uragaḥ khagaḥ bhukṣuḥ ca bhikṣu rūpī ca raudra rūpaḥ su rūpavān manaḥ vegaḥ niśā ācāraḥ sarva loka śubha pradaḥ sarva āvāsī trayī vāsī upadeśa karaḥ dharaḥ pakṣī ca pakṣa rūpaḥ ca ati dīptaḥ niśākaraḥ vāsudevaḥ ca devaḥ ca vāmadevaḥ ca vāmanaḥ siddhi yoga apahārī ca siddhaḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ akṣuṇṇaḥ kṣuṇṇa rūpaḥ ca vṛṣaṇaḥ mṛduḥ avyayaḥ mahāsenaḥ viśākhaḥ ca ṣaṣṭi bhāgaḥ gavām patiḥ vānaspatyaḥ vāja sanaḥ nityam āśrama pūjitaḥ īśānaḥ īśvaraḥ kālaḥ niśācārī hi anekadṛś nandīśvaraḥ sunandī ca nandanaḥ viṣamardanaḥ bhaga hārī niyantā ca kālaḥ loka pitāmahaḥ liṅga adhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣaḥ kāla adhyakṣaḥ yugāvahaḥ bīja adhyakṣaḥ bīja kartā adya ātma anugataḥ balaḥ itihāsaḥ ca kalpaḥ ca damanaḥ jagat īśvaraḥ dambhaḥ dambha karaḥ dātā vaṃśaḥ vaṃśa karaḥ kaliḥ lokakartā paśupatiḥ mahākartā hi adhokṣajaḥ nityaḥ hi anīśaḥ śuddha ātmā śuddhaḥ mānaḥ gatiḥ haviḥ sūtrakāraḥ vidvān ca para mardanaḥ mahā megha nivāsī ca mahā ghoraḥ vaśī karaḥ agni jvālaḥ mahā jvālaḥ paridhūmra āvṛtaḥ raviḥ dhiṣaṇaḥ śaṅkaraḥ nityaḥ varcasvī dhūmra locanaḥ nīlaḥ tathā aṅga luptaḥ ca śobhanaḥ nara vigrahaḥ utsaṃgaḥ ca mahāṅgaḥ ca mahāgarbhaḥ pratāpavān kṛṣṇa varṇaḥ suvarṇaḥ ca indriyaḥ sarvavārṇikaḥ mahā pādaḥ mahā hastaḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā yaśāḥ mahāmūrdhā mahāmātraḥ mahāmitraḥ naga ālayaḥ mahā skandhaḥ mahā karṇaḥ mahā uṣṭhaḥ ca mahā hanuḥ mahā nāsaḥ mahā kaṇṭhaḥ mahā grīvaḥ śmaśānavān mahā balaḥ mahā tejāḥ hi antarātmā mṛga ālayaḥ laṃbita uṣṭhaḥ ca niṣṭhaḥ ca mahāmāyaḥ payonidhiḥ mahā dantaḥ mahā daṃṣṭraḥ mahā jihvaḥ mahā mukhaḥ mahā nakhaḥ mahā romā mahā keśaḥ mahā jaṭaḥ asapatnaḥ prasādaḥ ca pratyayaḥ gītasādhakaḥ vṛṣakaḥ vṛṣaketuḥ ca analaḥ vāyuvāhanaḥ maṇḍalī meruvāsaḥ ca devavāhanaḥ eva ca arthava śīrṣaḥ sāma āsyaḥ ṛc sahasra ūrjita īkṣaṇaḥ amogha artha prasādaḥ ca antarbhāvyaḥ sudarśanaḥ upahāraḥ priyaḥ sarvaḥ kanakaḥ kāñcana sthitaḥ sarva śāstraḥ dhanaḥ ca ādyaḥ yajñaḥ yajvā samāhitaḥ nagaḥ nīlaḥ kaviḥ kālaḥ makaraḥ kāla pūjitaḥ sa gaṇaḥ gaṇakāraḥ ca bhūtabhāvana sārathiḥ āgamaḥ ca vilopaḥ ca mahātmā sarva pūjitaḥ śuklaḥ strī rūpa saṃpannaḥ śuciḥ bhūta niṣevitaḥ āśrama sthaḥ kapota sthaḥ viśvakarmā patiḥ virāj viśāla śākhaḥ tāmra uṣṭhaḥ hi ambujālaḥ su niścitaḥ kapilaḥ kalaśaḥ sthūlaḥ āyudhaḥ ca eva romaśaḥ gandharvaḥ hi aditiḥ tārkṣyaḥ hi avijñeyaḥ su śāradaḥ mahākopaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ jaleśayaḥ ugraḥ vaṃśa karaḥ vaṃśaḥ vaṃśa vādī hi aninditaḥ sarva aṅga rūpī māyāvī suhṛdaḥ hi anilaḥ balaḥ rākṣasaghnaḥ atha kāmāriḥ mahādaṃṣṭraḥ mahā āyudhaḥ laṃbitaḥ laṃbita uṣṭhaḥ ca laṃba hastaḥ vara pradaḥ bāhuḥ tu aninditaḥ sarvaḥ śaṅkaraḥ utha api akopanaḥ amara īśaḥ mahā ghoraḥ viśvadevaḥ surāri hā mahā kāpālī śam kumāraḥ mahā giriḥ dhātā viṣṇuḥ ca śakraḥ ca mitraḥ tvaṣṭā dharaḥ dhruvaḥ prabhāsaḥ parvataḥ vāyuḥ aryamā savitā raviḥ dhṛtiḥ ca eva vidhātā ca māndhātā bhūtabhāvanaḥ nīraḥ tīrthaḥ ca bhīmaḥ ca sarva karmā guṇa udvahaḥ balavān ca upaśāntaḥ ca purāmaḥ puṇya kṛttamaḥ krūrakartā krūravāsī tanuḥ ātmā mahauṣadhaḥ sarva āśayaḥ sarva cārī prāṇa īśaḥ prāṇinām patiḥ kailāsa sthaḥ guhā vāsī himavat giri saṃśrayaḥ prāṇeśaḥ bandhakī vṛkṣaḥ nakulaḥ ca adrikaḥ tathā hrasvagrīvaḥ mahājānuḥ alolaḥ ca mahauṣadhī siddhāntakārī siddhārthaḥ chandaḥ vyākaraṇodbhavaḥ siṃha nādaḥ siṃha daṃṣṭraḥ siṃha āsyaḥ siṃha vāhanaḥ prabhāva ātmā jagatkālaḥ kālaḥ kaṃpī taruḥ tanuḥ sāraṅgaḥ bhūtacakra āṅkaḥ ketumālī suvedhakaḥ vasubhṛt sarva bhūta ātmā niścalaḥ su viduḥ budhaḥ asuhṛd sarva bhūtānām niścalaḥ cala vid budhaḥ amoghaḥ saṃyamaḥ hṛṣṭaḥ bhojanaḥ prāṇa dhāraṇaḥ dhṛtimān matimān tryakṣaḥ sukṛtaḥ tu yudhāṃpatiḥ hiraṇyabāhuḥ ca tathā guhāvāsaḥ praveśanaḥ mahāmanāḥ cittakāmaḥ jita indriyaḥ gāndhāraḥ ca surāpaḥ ca tāpa karma rataḥ hitaḥ mahā bhūtaḥ bhūta vṛtaḥ hi apsaraḥ gaṇa sevitaḥ mahāketuḥ dharādhātā na ekatāna rataḥ svaraḥ a vedanīyaḥ āvedyaḥ sarva gaḥ ca sukha āvahaḥ tāraṇaḥ caraṇaḥ dhātā paridhā paripūjitaḥ saṃyogī vardhanaḥ vṛddhaḥ gaṇīkaḥ atha gaṇādhipaḥ nityaḥ dhātā sahāyaḥ ca deva asura patiḥ patiḥ āṣāḍhaḥ ca suṣāḍhaḥ ca skadhandaḥ haritaḥ haraḥ śiraḥ vimarśanaḥ sarva lakṣya lakṣaṇa bhūṣitaḥ akṣayaḥ ratha gītaḥ ca sarva bhogī mahā balaḥ sāmnāyaḥ utha mahāmnāyaḥ tīrthadevaḥ mahā yaśāḥ ratna bhūtaḥ atha ratnāṅgaḥ mahā arṇava nipāta vid mūlam viśālaḥ hi amṛtam vyakta avyaktaḥ taponidhiḥ ca śīla dhārī mahā tapāḥ mahākaṇṭhaḥ mahāyogī yugaḥ yuga karaḥ hariḥ nyāyaḥ nirvāpaṇaḥ apādaḥ paṇḍitaḥ hi acala upamaḥ bahu mālaḥ mahā mālaḥ śipiviṣṭaḥ su locanaḥ vistāraḥ lavaṇaḥ kūpaḥ kusumāṅgaḥ phalodayaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ bhaṅgaḥ induḥ visargaḥ sumukhaḥ śūraḥ sarva āyudhaḥ sahaḥ nivada enaḥ sudhā jātaḥ svargadvāraḥ mahā dhanūḥ mirāvāsaḥ visargaḥ ca sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣa vid gandhamālī ca bhagavān anantaḥ sava lakṣaṇaḥ saṃtānaḥ bahulaḥ bāhuḥ sakalaḥ sarva pāvanaḥ karasthālī kapālī ca ūrdhva saṃhananaḥ yuvā muṇḍaḥ virūpaḥ vikṛtaḥ daṇḍī kuṇḍī vikurvaṇaḥ mahā akṣaḥ kakubhaḥ vajrī dīpta tejāḥ sahasrapād sahasra bāhuḥ sarva aṅgaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarva loka kṛt pavitram trimadhuḥ mantraḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇa piṅgalaḥ brahmadaṇḍa vinirmātā śataghnaḥ kalā kāṣṭhā lavaḥ mātrā muhūrta ūhaḥ kṣapā kṣaṇaḥ viśva kṣetra pradaḥ bījam liṅgam ādyaḥ tu nirmukhaḥ sat asat vyaktam avyaktam pitā mātā pitā mahaḥ svargadvāram mokṣadvāram prajādvāram triviṣṭapaḥ nirvāṇam hṛdayaḥ ca eva brahma lokaḥ parā gatiḥ deva asura vinirmātā deva asura parāyaṇaḥ deva asura mahāmātraḥ deva asura gaṇa āśrayaḥ deva asura gaṇa adhyakṣaḥ deva asura gaṇa agraṇī deva asura īśvaraḥ viṣṇuḥ deva asura mahā īśvaraḥ vibudha agryaḥ suraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ svargadevaḥ tathā uttamaḥ saṃyuktaḥ śobhanaḥ vaktā āśānām prabhavaḥ vyayaḥ guruḥ kāntaḥ nijaḥ sargaḥ pavitraḥ sarva āvāhanaḥ śṛṅgī śṛṅgapriyaḥ baśruḥ rājarājaḥ nirāmayaḥ abhirāmaḥ su śaraṇaḥ nirāmaḥ sarva sādhanaḥ lalāṭa akṣaḥ viśva dehaḥ hariṇaḥ brahmavarcasaḥ sthāvarāṇām patiḥ ca eva niyata indriya vartanaḥ siddhārthaḥ sarva bhūta arthaḥ acintyaḥ satyaḥ śuci vrataḥ vrata adhipaḥ param brahma muktānām paramā gātiḥ muktaḥ mukta keśaḥ ca śrīmān śrī vardhanaḥ jagant tatas hi anujñām prāpya evam stutaḥ bhaktimatām gatiḥ tasmāt labdhvā stavam śambhoḥ nṛpaḥ trailokya viśrutaḥ aśvamedha sahasrasya phalam prāpya mahā yaśāḥ gaṇa ādhipatyam saṃprāptaḥ taṇḍinaḥ tejasā prabhoḥ yaḥ paṭhet caṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet brāhmaṇān api śaraṇa āgata dhātī ca mitra viśvāsa ghātakaḥ mātṛ hā pitṛ hā ca eva virahāḥ bhrūṇa hā tathā param saṃvatsaram kramāt japtvā trisaṃdhyam śaṃkara āśrame trisaṃdhyam ca sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge rudrasahasranāmakathanam nāma pañcaṣaṣṭittamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca gām apatyam dṛḍham prāptaḥ sarva deva namaskṛtaḥ āsīt tridhanvanaḥ ca api vidvāḥ trayyāruṇaḥ nṛpaḥ pāṇigrahaṇa mantreṣu niṣṭhām a prāpiteṣu iha tena adharmeṇa saṃyuktam rājā trayyāruṇā atyajat pitaram saḥ bravīt tyaktaḥ kva gacchāmi iti vai dvijāḥ sa tu satya vrataḥ dhīmān śbapāka āvasatha antike pitrā tyaktaḥ avasat vīraḥ pitā ca asya vanam yayau sarva lokeṣu vikhyātaḥ triśaṅkuḥ iti vīryavān vasiṣṭha kopāt puṇya ātmā rājā satyavrataḥ purā viśvāmitraḥ mahā tejāḥ varam dattvā triśaṅkave rājye abhiṣicya tam pitrye yājayāmāsa tam muniḥ miṣatām devatānām ca vasiṣṭhasya ca kauśikaḥ sa śarīram tadā tam vai divam āropayat vibhuḥ tasya satya vratā nāma bhāryā kaikaya vaṃśa jā kumāram janayāmāsa hariścandram akalmaṣam rucakasya vṛkaḥ putraḥ tasmāt bāhuḥ ca jajñivān dve bhārye sagarasya api prabhā bhānumatī tathā tābhyām ārādhitaḥ pūrvam aurvaḥ agniḥ putra kāmyayā aurvaḥ tuṣṭaḥ tayoḥ prādāt yatheṣṭam varam uttamam ekā ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi sutam ekam parā tathā āgṛhṇāt vaṃśa kartāram prabhā agṛhṇāt sutān bahūn ekam bhānumatiḥ putra magṛhṇāt asamañjasam tatas ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi suṣuve sā tu vai prabhā khanantaḥ pṛthivīm dagdhāḥ viṣṇu huṅkāra mārgaṇaiḥ asamañjasya tanayaḥ saḥ uṃśumant nāma viśrutaḥ yena bhāgīrathī gaṅgā tapaḥ kṛtvā avatāritā bhagīratha sutaḥ ca api śrutaḥ nāma babhūva ha nābhāgaḥ tasya dāyādaḥ bhava bhaktaḥ pratāpavān nābhāgena ambarīṣeṇa bhujābhyām paripālitā putraḥ ayuta āyuṣaḥ dhīmān ṛtuparṇaḥ mahā yaśāḥ divya akṣa hṛdaya jñaḥ vai rājā nala sakhaḥ balī nalau dvau eva vikhyātau purāṇeṣu dṛḍha vratau vīrasena sutaḥ ca anyaḥ yaḥ ca ikṣvāku kula udbhavaḥ īśvaraḥ sudāsasya sutaḥ proktaḥ saudāsaḥ nāma pārthivaḥ khyātaḥ kalmāṣapādaḥ vai nāmnā mitrasahaḥ ca saḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ tu mahā tejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake aśmakam janayāmāsa ikṣvāku kula vardhanam sa hi rāma bhayāt rājā strībhiḥ parivṛtaḥ vane mūlakasya api dharma ātmā rājā satarathaḥ sutaḥ tasmāt śatarathāt jajñe rājā tu ilavilaḥ balī āsīt tu ailaviliḥ śrīmān vṛddhaśarmā pratāpavān yena svargāt iha āgatya muhūrtam prāpya jīvitam ajaḥ putraḥ raghoḥ ca api tasmāt jajñe ca vīryavān rājā daśarathaḥ tasmāt śrīmān ikṣvāku vaṃśa kṛt rāmaḥ daśarathāt vīraḥ dharma jñaḥ loka viśrutaḥ bharataḥ lakṣmaṇaḥ ca eva śatrughnaḥ ca mahā balaḥ teṣām śreṣṭhaḥ mahā tejāḥ rāmaḥ parama vīryavān rāvaṇam samare hatvā yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā ca dharma vid daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi rāmaḥ rājyam cakāra saḥ lavaḥ ca su mahābhāgaḥ satyavant abhavat sudhīḥ nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīka ākhyaḥ kṣemadhanvā tatas smṛtaḥ tasya putraḥ bhavat vīraḥ devānīkaḥ pratāpavān ahīnaraḥ sutaḥ stasya sahasrāśvaḥ tatas paraḥ śubhaḥ candrāvalokaḥ ca tārāpīḍaḥ tatas bhavat śrutāyuḥ abhavat tasmāt bṛhadbalaḥ iti smṛtaḥ bhārate yaḥ mahā tejāḥ saubhadreṇa nipātitaḥ ete ikṣvāku dāyādāḥ rājānaḥ prāyaśas smṛtāḥ vaṃśe pradhānāḥ etasmin prādānyena prakīrtitāḥ sarve pāśupate jñānam adhītya parameśvaram samabhyarcya yathājñānam iṣṭvā yajñaiḥ yathāvidhi divam gatāḥ mahātmānaḥ kecid mukta ātma yoginaḥ nṛgaḥ brāhmaṇa śāpena kṛkalāsa tvam āgataḥ dhṛṣṭaḥ ca dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca yamabālaḥ ca vīryavān ca te putrāḥ trayaḥ parama dhārmikāḥ ānartaḥ nāma śaryāteḥ sukanyā nāma dārikā mānartasya abhavat putraḥ rocamānaḥ pratāpavān kakudmī ca aparaḥ jyeṣṭha putraḥ putra śatasya tu revatī yasya sā kanyā patnī rāmasya viśrutā nariṣyantasya putraḥ bhūt jitātmā tu mahā balī nābhāgāt ambarīṣaḥ tu viṣṇu bhaktaḥ pratāpavān ṛtaḥ tasya sutaḥ śrīmān sarva dharma vidām varaḥ kṛtaḥ tasya sudharmā abhūt pṛṣitaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ karūṣasya tu kārūṣāḥ sarve prakhyāta kīrtayaḥ pṛṣitaḥ hiṃsayitvā gām guroḥ prāpa su kalmaṣam śāpāt śūdra tvam āpannaḥ cyavanasya iti viśrutaḥ diṣṭa putrāḥ tu nābhāgaḥ tasmāt api bhalandanaḥ bhalandanasya rājā āsīt ajavāhanaḥ ete samāsatas proktāḥ manu putrāḥ mahā bhujāḥ ikṣvākoḥ putra pautra ādyaḥ elasya atha vadāmi vaḥ uvāca ailaḥ purūravāḥ nāma rudra bhaktaḥ pratāpavān cakre tu akaṇṭakam rājyam deśe puṇyatame dvijāḥ pratiṣṭhāna adhipaḥ śrīmān pratiṣṭhāne pratiṣṭhitaḥ ca viśvāyuḥ ca eva vīryavān śrutāyūḥ ca śatāyūḥ ca divyāḥ ca eva urvaśī sutāḥ āyuṣaḥ tanayāḥ vīrāḥ pañca eva āsan mahā ojasaḥ svarbhānu tanayāyām te prabhāyām jajñire nṛpāḥ nahuṣaḥ prathamaḥ teṣām dharma jñaḥ loka viśrutaḥ nahupasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaṭ indra upama tejasaḥ utpannāḥ pitṛ kanyāyam virajāyām mahā ojasaḥ yatiḥ yayātiḥ saṃyātiḥ āyātiḥ pañcamaḥ andhakaḥ vijātiḥ ca iti ṣaṭ ime sarve prakhyāta kīrtayaḥ yatiḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ ca teṣām vai yayātiḥ tu tatas avaraḥ teṣām yayātiḥ pañcānām mahā bala parākramaḥ devayānīm uśanasaḥ sutām bhāryām avāpa saḥ śarmiṣṭhām āsurīm ca eva tanayām vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ tau ubhau śubha karmaṇau stutau vidyā viśāradau druhyam ca anum ca pūrum ca śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī su saṃgam kāñcanam divyam akṣaye ca mahā iṣudhī yathā atiḥ yudhi durdharṣaḥ deva dānava mānuṣaiḥ bhava bhaktaḥ tu puṇya ātmā dharma niṣṭhaḥ samañjasaḥ yajña yājī jita krodhaḥ sarva bhūta anukampanaḥ kauravāṇām ca sarveṣām sa bhavat rathaḥ uttamaḥ pūroḥ vaṃśasya rājñaḥ tu rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya tu jagāma sa rathaḥ nāśam śāpāt gargasya dhīmataḥ gargasya hi sutam bālam sa rājā janamejayaḥ akrūram hiṃsayāmāsa brahma hatyām avāpa saḥ sa lohagandhī rājarṣiḥ paridhāvan itas tatas jagāma śaunakam ṛṣim śaraṇyam vyathitaḥ tadā yājayāmāsa ca indretiḥ tam nṛpam janamejayam aśvamedhena rājānam pāvana artham dvijottamāḥ sa loha gandha annar muktaḥ enasā ca mahā yaśāḥ yajñasya avabhṛthe madhye yātaḥ divyaḥ rathaḥ śubhaḥ tasmāt vaṃśāt paribhraṣṭaḥ vasoḥ cedi pateḥ punar dattaḥ śakreṇa tuṣṭena lebhe tasmāt bṛhadrathaḥ uvāca abhyaṣiñcat purum putram yayātiḥ nāhuṣaḥ prabhuḥ kṛta upakāraḥ tena eva puruṇā dvijasattamāḥ abhiṣektu kāmam ca nṛpam purum putram kanīyasam brāhmaṇa pramukhāḥ varṇāḥ idam vacanam abruvan katham śukrasya naptāram devayānyāḥ sutam prabho ete saṃbodhayāmaḥ tvām dharmam ca anupālaya iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca brāhmaṇa pramukhāḥ varṇāḥ sarve śṛṇvantu me vacaḥ jyeṣṭham prati yathā rājyam na deyam me kathaṃcana mama jyeṣṭhena yadunā niyogaḥ na anupālitaḥ pratikūla matiḥ ca eva na sa putraḥ satām mataḥ druhyena ca anunā ca eva mayi avajñā kṛtā bhṛśam puruṇā ca kṛtam vākyam mānitaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ kanīyān mama dāyādaḥ jarā yena dhṛtā mama śukreṇa me samādiṣṭā devayānyāḥ kṛte jarā prārthitena punar tena jarā saṃcāriṇī kṛtā śukreṇa ca varaḥ dattaḥ kāvyena uśanasā kvayam ūcuḥ yaḥ putraḥ guṇa saṃpannaḥ mātā pitroḥ hitaḥ sadā sarvam arhati kalyāṇam kanīyāḥ sa prabhuḥ arhaḥ pūruḥ idam rājyam yaḥ sutaḥ vākya kṛt tava uvāca evam jāna padaiḥ tuṣṭaiḥ iti uktaḥ nāhuṣaḥ tadā abhiṣicya tatas rājyam pūrum sa sutam ātmanaḥ diśi turvasum putram ādiśat dakṣiṇāyām atho rājā yadum jyeṣṭham nyayojayet pratyañci uttarasyām tu druhyum ca anum ca tau ubhau saptadvīpām yayātiḥ tu jitvā pṛthvīm sa sāgarām harṣa nirbhara mānasaḥ prītimān abhavat rājā bhāraiḥ mā āveśya bandhuṣu atra gāthāḥ mahā rājñā purā gītāḥ yayātinā yābhiḥ pratyāharet kāmān sarvatas uṅgāni kūrma vat tābhiḥ eva naraḥ śrīmān na anyathā karma koṭi kṛt na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā iva bhūyas eva abhivardhate yat pṛthivyām vrīhi yavam hiraṇyam paśavaḥ striyaḥ yadā na kurute bhāvam sarva bhūteṣu pāpakam karmaṇā manasā vācā brahma saṃpadyate tadā yā dustyajā durmatibhiḥ yā asau prāṇāntikaḥ rogaḥ tām tṛṣṇām tyajataḥ sukham jīryanti jīryataḥ keśāḥ dantāḥ jīryānti jīryataḥ cukṣuḥ śrotre ca jīryete tṛṣṇā ekā nirupadravā hi jīryanti dehinaḥ sarve svabhāvāt eva na anyathā jīvita āśā dhana āśā ca jīyataḥ api na jīryate tṛṣṇā kṣaya sukhasya etat kalām na arhati ṣoḍaśīm evam uktvā saḥ rājarṣiḥ sa dāraḥ prāviśat vanam bhṛgutuṅge vā tatra eva ca mahā yaśāḥ sādhayitvā tu anaśanam sa dāraḥ svargam āptavan tasya vaṃśāḥ tu pañca ete puṇyāḥ deva ṛṣi satkṛtāḥ yaiḥ vyāptā pṛthivī kṛtsnā sūryasya iva marīcibhiḥ dhanī prajāvān āyuṣmān kīrtimān ca bhavet naraḥ yayāti caritam puṇyam paṭhan śṛṇvan ca buddhimān iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge soma vaṃśe yayāticaritam nāma saptaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca yadoḥ vaṃśam pravakṣyāmi jyeṣṭhasya uttama tejasaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa ānupūrvyāt ca gadataḥ mama nibodhata yadoḥ putrāḥ babhūbuḥ hi pañca deva suta upamāḥ sahasrajit sutaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ kroṣṭuḥ nīlojakaḥ laghuḥ sutāḥ śatajitaḥ khyātāḥ trāyaḥ parama kīrtayaḥ haihayaḥ ca hayaḥ ca eva rājā veṇuhayaḥ ca yaḥ sañjayasya tu dāyādaḥ mahiṣmān nāma dhārmikaḥ māhiṣmantaḥ putraḥ bhadraśreṇyaḥ pratāpavān bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādaḥ durdamaḥ nāma pārthivaḥ dhanakasya tu dāyādāḥ catvāraḥ loka saṃmatāḥ kṛtavīryaḥ kṛtāgniḥ ca kṛtavarmā tathā eva ca kṛtaujāḥ ca caturthaḥ bhūt kārtavīryaḥ tatas ūrjunaḥ jajñe bāhu sahasreṇa saptadvīpā īśvara uttamaḥ tasya tu āsīt mṛtyuḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ tasya putra śatāni āsan pañca tatra mahā rathāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ balīnaḥ śūrāḥ dharma ātmānaḥ manasvinaḥ śūraḥ ca śūrasenaḥ ca dhṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā eva ca bayadhvajaḥ ca rājā āsīt āvantīnām viśām patiḥ śatam putrāḥ tu tasya iha tālajaṅghāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām jyeṣṭhaḥ mahā vīryaḥ vītihotraḥ abhavat nṛpaḥ vṛṣa prabhṛtayaḥ ca anye tad sutāḥ puṇya karmaṇaḥ madhoḥ putra śatam ca āsīt vṛṣṇiḥ tasya tu vaṃśa bhāj vṛṣṇeḥ tu vṛṣṇayaḥ sarve mādhoḥ vai mādhavāḥ smṛtāḥ yādavāḥ yadu vaṃśena nirucyante tu hauhayāḥ teṣām pañca gaṇāḥ hi ete haihayānām mahātmanām haryātāḥ ca haryātāḥ bhojāḥ ca avantayaḥ tathā śūrasonāḥ tu vikhyātāḥ tālajaṅghāḥ tathā evam ca śūraḥ ca śūrasenaḥ ca vṛṣaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā eva ca śūraḥ ca śūravīraḥ ca śūrasenasya ca anaghāḥ śūrasenāḥ iti khyātāḥ deśāḥ teṣām mahātmanām durjayaḥ kṛṣṇa putraḥ tu babhūva amitra karśanaḥ kroṣṭuḥ ca śṛṇu rājarṣe vaṃśam uttama pauruṣam yasya anvaye tu saṃbhūtaḥ viṣṇuḥ vaṣṇi kula udvahaḥ kroṣṭoḥ ekaḥ abhavat putraḥ vṛjinīvant mahā yaśāḥ atha prasūtim icchan vai kuśaṅkuḥ su mahā balaḥ śaśarbaduḥ tu vai rājā anvayāt bratam uttamam cakravartī mahā sattvaḥ mahā vīryaḥ bahu prajāḥ śaśabindoḥ tu putrāṇām sahasrāṇām abhūt śatam tasya putrāṇām anantakam anuttamam uśanāḥ tasya tanayaḥ saṃprāpya tu mahīm imām ājahāra aśvamedhānām śatam uttama dhārmikaḥ smṛtaḥ ca uśanasaḥ putraḥ siteṣuḥ nāma pārthivaḥ vīraḥ
