kaṃbalabarhīḥ tu maruḥ tasya ātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ dhanvinaḥ viśitaiḥ vāṇaiḥ avāpa śriyam uttamām aśvamedhe tu dharma ātmā ṛtvigbhyaḥ pṛthivīm dadau jajñe tu rukmakavacāt parāvṛt para vīra hā pañca putrāḥ tu mahā sattvāḥ parāvṛtaḥ rukmeṣuḥ pṛthurukmaḥ ca jyāmaghaḥ parigham hariḥ rukmeṣuḥ abhavat rājā pṛthurukmaḥ tad āśrayāt taiḥ tu pravrājitaḥ rājā jyāḥ maghaḥ avasat āśrame jagāma dhanuḥ ādāya deśam anyam dhvajī rathī narmadā tīram ekākī kevalam bhāryayā yutaḥ giram gatvā tyaktam anyaiḥ uvāsa saḥ hasya abhavat bhāryā śaibyā śīlavatī satī sā ca eva tapasaḥ greṇa śaibyā vai saṃprasūyata sutam vidarbha subhagā vayaḥ pariṇatā satī tu vidvasau kratha kaiśikau putrau vidarbha rājasya śūrau raṇa viśāradau romapādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ ca babhruḥ tasya ātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ kauśikaḥ tanayaḥ tasmāt tasmāt caidya anvayaḥ smṛtaḥ kunteḥ vataḥ tatas jajñe raṇadhṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān raṇadhṛṣṭasya ca sutaḥ nidhṛtiḥ para vīra hā daśārhe naidhṛtaḥ nāmnā mahā ari gaṇa sūdanaḥ darśārhasya sutaḥ vyāptaḥ jīmūtaḥ iti tad sutaḥ jīmūta putraḥ vikṛtiḥ tasya bhīmarathaḥ sutaḥ dāna dharma rataḥ nityam satya śīla parāyaṇaḥ tasya ca āsīt dṛḍharathaḥ śakuniḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ tasmāt karaṃbhaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ devarātaḥ abhavat tatas devarātāt abhūt rājā devarātiḥ mahā yaśāḥ devakṣatra sutaḥ śrīmān madhuḥ nāma mahā yaśāḥ madhūnām vaṃśa kṛt rājā madhoḥ tu kuruvaṃśakaḥ kuruvaṃśāt anuḥ tasmāt purutvant puruṣa uttamaḥ aṃśuḥ jajñe ca vaidarbhyām bhadravatyām purutvantaḥ pra ikṣvākīm avahat ca aṃśuḥ sattvaḥ tasmāt ajāyata mayā proktā sṛṣṭiḥ vai vistareṇa vaḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api tu iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vaṃśānuvarṇanam nāma aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sāttvataḥ satya saṃpannaḥ prajajñe caturaḥ sutān bhajanam bhrābhamānam ca divyam devāvṛdham nṛpam andhakam ca mahābhāgam vṛṣṇim ca yadu nandanam teṣām nisargān caturaḥ śṛṇudhvam vistareṇa vai sṛṃjayyām bhajanāt ca eva bhrājamānāt vijajñire ayutāyūḥ śātayuḥ ca balavān harṣa kṛt smṛtaḥ teṣām devāvṛdhaḥ rājā cacāra paramam tapaḥ anuvaṃśa purāṇa jñāḥ gāyanti iti pariśrutam guṇān devāvṛdhasya atha kīrtayantaḥ mahātmanaḥ yathā eva śṛṇumaḥ dūrāt saṃpaśyāmaḥ tathā antikāt babhruḥ śreṣṭhaḥ manuṣyāṇām devaiḥ devāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ puruṣāḥ pañca ṣaṣṭiḥ tu ṣaḍ sahasrāṇi ca aṣṭa ca ye amṛta tvam anuprāptāḥ babhroḥ devāvṛdhāt api yajvā dāna matiḥ vīraḥ brahmaṇyaḥ tu dṛḍha vrataḥ kīrtimān ca mahā tejāḥ sātvatānām mahā rathaḥ tasya anvavāye saṃbhūtāḥ bhojāḥ vai daivata upamāḥ gāndhārī ca eva mādrī ca vṛṣṇi bhāryaḥ babhūvatuḥ mādrī lebhe ca tam putram tatas sā devamīḍhuṣam prasenaḥ ca mahābhāgaḥ satrājit ca sutau ubhau tasya satrājitaḥ sūryaḥ sakhā prāṇa samaḥ abhavat pṛthivyām sarva ratnānām asau rājā abhavat maṇiḥ kadācid mṛgayām yātaḥ prasenena saha eva saḥ vadham sahāyaḥ ca siṃhādeva su dāruṇāt atha putraḥ śineḥ jajñe kaniṣṭhāt vṛṣṇi nandānāt sātyakiḥ yuyudhānaḥ tu śineḥ naptā pratāpavān kuṇeḥ yugaṃdharaḥ putraḥ śaineyāḥ iti kīrtitāḥ sutasya saṃjajñe sutaḥ vārṣṇiḥ yudhājitaḥ na asti vyādhi bhayam tatra na avṛṣṭi bhayam api uta śvaphalkaḥ kāsi rājasya sutām bhāryām avāpa saḥ gāndinīm nāma kāśyaḥ hi dadau tasmai sva kanyakām sā mātuḥ udara sthā vai bahūn varṣa gaṇān kila vasantī na ca saṃjajñe garbha sthā tām pitā bravīt māyasva śīghram bhadram te kimartham ca abhitiṣṭhasi provāca ca enam garbha sthā sā kanyā gāndīnī tadā varṣa trayam pratidinam gām ekām brāhmaṇāya tu yadi dadyāḥ tatas kukṣeḥ nirgamiṣyāmi aham pitar dātā śūraḥ ca yajvā ca śrutavān atithi priyaḥ tasyāḥ putraḥ smṛtaḥ akrūraḥ śvaphalkāt bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ ratnā kanyā ca śaivasya hi akrūraḥ tām avāptavan asyām utpādayāmāsa tanayān tān nibodhata āvāha prativāhau ca sudhārā ca vara aṅganā sumitrasya sutaḥ jajñe citrakaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ aśvagrīvaḥ subāhuḥ ca sudhāsūka gavekṣaṇau subhūmiḥ bahubhūmiḥ ca śraviṣṭhā śravaṇe striyau andhakāt kāśya duhitā lebhe ca caturaḥ sutān kukuram bhajamānam ca śucim kaṃbalabarhiṣam kukurasya sutaḥ vṛṣmiḥ vaṣṇeḥ śūraḥ tatas abhavat aśvamedham sa putra artham ājahāra nara uttamaḥ tatas tu vidvān sarvajñaḥ dātā yajvā punarvasuḥ ca ca eva khyātau māhukāt kāśya duhituḥ dvai putrau saṃbabhūvatuḥ devakasya sutāḥ rājñaḥ jajñire tridaśa upamāḥ teṣām svasāraḥ sapta āsan vasudevāya tāḥ dadau vṛṣadevā upadevā ca tathā anyā devarakṣitā śrīdevā śāntidevā ca sahadevā tathā aparā devakī ca api tāsām ca variṣṭhā abhūt sumadhyamā navā ugrasenasya sutāḥ teṣām kaṃsaḥ tu pūrvajaḥ teṣām putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ ca śataśas utha sahasraśas rohiṇī ca mahābhāgā patnī ca ānakadundubheḥ pauravī bāhlika sutā saṃpūjyā āsīt suraiḥ api asūta rohiṇī rāmam bala śreṣṭham halāyudham māśritam kaṃsa bhītyā ca sva ātmānam śānta tejasam jāte rāme atha nihate ṣaṅgarbhe ca ati dakṣiṇe bhṛgu śāpa chalena eva mānayan mānuṣīm tanum babhūva tasyām devakyām vāsudevaḥ janārdana umā deha samudbhūtā yoga nidrā ca kauśikī sā ca eva prakṛtiḥ sākṣāt sarva deva namaskṛtā puruṣaḥ bhagavant kṛṣṇaḥ dharma mokṣa phala pradaḥ tām kanyām jagṛhe rakṣan kaṃsāt svasya ātmajam tadā catur bhujam viśāla akṣam śrīvatsa kṛta lāñchanam śaṅkha cakra gadā padmam dhārayantam janārdanam rakṣakam jagantām viṣṇum sva icchayā dhṛta vigraham rāmeṇa sārdham tam dattvā vara dam parameśvaram bhū bhāra nigraha artham ca hi avatīrṇam jagadgurum atas vai sarva kalyāṇam yādāvānām bhaviṣyati ayam sa garbhaḥ devakyāḥ yaḥ naḥ kleśyān hariṣyati ugrasena ātmajāya atha kaṃsāya ānakadundubhiḥ nivedayāmāsa tadā jātām kanyām su lakṣaṇām asyāḥ ta vā aṣṭamaḥ garbhaḥ devakyāḥ kaṃsa suvrata mṛtyuḥ eva na saṃdehaḥ iti vāṇī purātanī tatas tām hantum ārebhe kaṃsaḥ sa ullaṅghya ca ambaram uvāca aṣṭa bhujā devī megha gaṃbhīrayā girā rakṣamāṇasya dehasya māyāvī kaṃsa rūpiṇaḥ kim kṛtam duṣkṛtam mūrkha jātaḥ khalu te antakṛt devakyāḥ sa bhayāt kaṃsaḥ jaghāna eva aṣṭabham tu iti prabhāvāt muni sārdūlāḥ tayā ca eva jaḍīkṛtaḥ kaṃsaḥ api nihataḥ tena kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā nihatāḥ bahavaḥ ca anye deva brāhmaṇa ghātinaḥ tasya kṛṣṇasya tanayāḥ pradyumna pramukhāḥ tathā bahavaḥ parisaṃkhyātāḥ sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ kṛṣṇa putrāḥ samākhyātāḥ kṛṣṇena sadṛśāḥ sutāḥ putreṣu eteṣu sarveṣu cārudeṣṇa ādayaḥ hareḥ viśiṣṭāḥ balavantaḥ ca raukmiṇeya ari sūdanāḥ adhikam kṛṣṇasya tāsu sarvāsu priyā jyeṣṭhā ca rukmiṇī tayā dvādaśa varṣāṇi kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā uṣyatā vāyubhakṣeṇa putra artham pūjitaḥ haraḥ cārudeṣṇaḥ sucāruḥ ca cāruveṣaḥ yaśodharaḥ cāruśravāḥ cāruyaśāḥ pradyumnaḥ sa ambaḥ eva ca ete labdhāḥ tu kṛṣṇena śūlapāṇi prasādāt tān dṛṣṭvā tanayān vīrān raukmiṇeyān ca rukmiṇīm jāmbavatī abravīt kṛṣṇam bhāryā kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ mama tvam puṇḍarīkākṣa viśiṣṭam guṇavattaram jāmbavatyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā jagannāthaḥ tatas hariḥ saḥ atha nārāyaṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ ṛṣim dṛṣṭvā tu aṅgirasam praṇipatya janārdanaḥ divyam pāśupatam yogam labdhavan tasya ca ājñayā pralupta śmaśru keśaḥ ca ghṛta aktaḥ muñja mekhalī dīkṣitaḥ bhagavant kṛṣṇaḥ tatāpa ca paraṃtapaḥ bāhuḥ nirālambaḥ pādāṅguṣṭha agra dhiṣṭhitaḥ tapasā tasya saṃtuṣṭaḥ dadau rudraḥ bahūn varān sa ambam jāmbavatī putram kṛṣṇāya ca mahātmane tathā jāṃbavatī ca eva sāṃbam bhāryā hareḥ sutam bāṇasya ca tadā tena cheditam muni puṃgavāḥ bhujānām ca eva sāhasram śāpāt rudrasya dhīmataḥ tathā duṣṭa kṣitīśānām līlayā eva raṇa ajire sva upabogyāni kanyānām ṣoḍaśa atula vikramaḥ śata adhikāni jagrāha sahasrāṇi mahā balaḥ śāpa vyājena viprāṇām upasaṃhṛtavān kulam saṃhṛtya tad kulam ca eva prabhāse atiṣṭhat acyutaḥ tadā tasya eva tu ganta varṣāṇām adhikam śatam kṛṣṇasya dvārakāyām vai śāpa hāriṇaḥ viśvāmitrasya kaṇvasya nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ śāpam piṇḍārake arakṣat vacaḥ durvāsasaḥ tadā tyaktvā ca mānuṣam rūpam jaraka astra chalena tu aṣṭāvakrasya śāpena bhāryāḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ cauraiḥ ca apahṛtāḥ sarvāḥ tasya māyā balena ca mahiṣyaḥ tasya kṛṣṇasya rukmiṇī pramukhāḥ śubhāḥ saha agnim viviśuḥ sarvāḥ kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā revatī ca tathā devī balabhadreṇa dhīmatā praviṣṭā pāvakam viprāḥ sā ca bhartṛ patham gatā pretakāryam hareḥ kṛtvā pārthaḥ parama vīryavān rāmasya ca tathā anyeṣām vṛṣṇīnām api suvrataḥ dravya abhāvāt svaṃyam pārthaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ ca divam gataḥ evam saṃkṣepāt proktaḥ kṛṣṇasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ iti etat soma vaṃśānām nṛpāṇām caritam dvijāḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api brāhmaṇān śrāvayet api sa yāti vaiṣṇavam lokam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge somavaṃśānukīrtanam nāma ekonasaptatitamaḥ adhyacāyaḥ ūcuḥ ādi sargaḥ tvayā sūta sūcitaḥ na prakāśitaḥ uvāca maheśvaraḥ mahādevaḥ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca paratve saṃsthitaḥ devaḥ paramātmā muni īśvarāḥ avyaktam ca īśvarāt tasmāt abhavat kāraṇam param pradhānam prakṛtiḥ ca iti yat āhuḥ tattva cintakāḥ jagat yonim mahābhūtam param brahma sanātanam vigrahaḥ sarva bhūtānām īśvara ājñā pracoditam anādi antam ajam sūkṣmam triguṇam prabhava avyayam asya ātmanā sarvam idam vyāptam tu āsīt śiva icchayā sarga kāle pradhānasya kṣetrajña dhiṣṭhitasya vai guṇa bhāvāt vyajyamānaḥ mahant prādurbabhūva ha sūkṣmeṇa mahatā ca atha avyaktena samāvṛtam manaḥ mahant tu vijñeyam ekam tat kāraṇam smṛtam samutpannam liṅgamātram kṣetrajña adhiṣṭhitam hi tat dharma ādīni ca rūpāṇi loka tattva artha hetavaḥ mahant sṛṣṭim vikurute codyamānaḥ sisṛkṣayā manaḥ mahant matiḥ brahma pūḥ buddhiḥ khyātiḥ īśvaraḥ prajñā citiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃvid viśveśaḥ ca iti saḥ smṛtaḥ manute sarva bhūtānām yasmāt ceṣṭā phalam tatas tattvānām agrajaḥ yasmāt mahant ca parimāṇataḥ viśeṣebhyaḥ guṇebhyaḥ api mahant iti tatas smṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ bhoga saṃbandhāt tena ca asau matiḥ smṛtaḥ bṛhat tvāt bṛṃhaṇa tvāt ca bhāvānām sakala śrayāt yaḥ pūrayati yasmāt ca kṛtsnān devān anugrahaiḥ budhyate puruṣaḥ ca atra sarvān bhāvān hitam tathā bhogasya jñāna niṣṭha tvāt tena khyātiḥ iti smṛtaḥ tad guṇaiḥ vā api jñāna ādibhiḥ anekaśas tasmāt ca mahantaḥ saṃjñā khyātiḥ iti abhidhīyate sākṣāt sarvam vijānāti mahātmā tena ca īśvaraḥ yasmāt jñāna anugaḥ ca eva prajñā tena saḥ ucyate jñāna ādini ca rūpāṇi bahu karma phalāni ca tathā eva anāgatāni api kṛtsnam ca vindate jñānam yasmāt māhātmyam uttamam mānāteḥ jñānam iti āhuḥ bhagavān jñāna saṃnidhiḥ bandhana ādi parībhāvāt īśvaraḥ procyate budhaiḥ vyākhyātam tattva bhāva jñaiḥ deva sadbhāva cetakaiḥ mahant sṛṣṭim vikurute codyamānaḥ sisṛkṣayā mahantā ca vṛtaḥ sargaḥ bhūtādiḥ bāhmataḥ tu saḥ tasmāt eva tama udriktāt ahaṅkārāt ajāyata bhūtādiḥ tu vikurvāṇaḥ śabda mātram sasarja ha mākāśam suṣiram tasmāt utpannam śabda lakṣaṇam ākāśam śabda mātram tu sparśa mātram samāvṛṇot vāyuḥ ca api vikurvāṇaḥ rūpa mātram sasarja ha sparśa mātraḥ tu vai vāyuḥ rūpa mātram samāvṛṇot jyotiḥ ca api vikurvāṇam rasa mātram sasarja ha rasa mātrāḥ tu tāḥ hi apaḥ rūpa mātrā ugniḥ āvṛṇot saṃghātaḥ jāyate tasmāt tasya gandhaḥ guṇaḥ mataḥ tasmin tasmin ca tanmātram tena tanmātra tā smṛtā aviśeṣa vācaka tvāt aviśeṣāḥ tatas tu te praśānta ghora mūḍha tvāt aviśeṣāḥ tatas punar vaikārikāt ahaṃkārāt sattva udriktāt tu sāttvikāt sādhakāni indriyāṇi syuḥ devāḥ vaikārikāḥ daśa śrotram tvac cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā ca eva pañcamī śabda ādīnām avāpti artham buddhi yuktāni tāni vai ākāśam śabda mātram ca sparśa mātram samāviśat rūpam tathā eva viśataḥ sabda sparśa guṇau ubhau sa śabda sparśa rūpam ca rasa mātram samāviśat tasmāt catur gumāḥ apaḥ vijñeyāḥ tu rasa ātmakāḥ śabda sparśam ca rūpam ca rasaḥ vai gandham āviśat saṃgatāḥ gandha mātreṇa āviśantaḥ mahīm imām tasmāt pañcaguṇā bhūmiḥ sthūlā bhūteṣu śasyate śāntāḥ ghorāḥ ca mūḍhāḥ ca viśeṣāḥ tena te smṛtāḥ bhūmyāḥ antar tu idam sarvam lokāloka acala āvṛtam viśeṣāḥ ca indriya grāhyāḥ niyata tvāt ca te smṛtāḥ teṣām yāvat ca tat yat ca yat ca tāvat guṇam smṛtam pṛthivyām eva tam vidyāt apām vāyoḥ ca saṃśrayāt puruṣa dhiṣṭhita tvāt ca avyakta anugraheṇa ca mahā dayaḥ viśeṣa antāḥ hi aṇḍam utpādayanti te adbhiḥ daśaguṇābhiḥ tu bāhya toṇḍam samāvṛtam apaḥ daśaguṇena etāḥ tejasā bāhyatas vṛtāḥ tejaḥ daśaguṇena eva vāyunā bāhyatas vṛtam vāyuḥ daśaguṇena eva bāhyatas nabhasā vṛtaḥ ākāśa ūna āvṛtaḥ vāyuḥ kham tu bhūtādinā āvṛtam bhūtādiḥ mahatā ca api avyaktena āvṛtaḥ mahant śarvaḥ ca aṇḍa kapāla sthaḥ bhavaḥ ca ambhasi suvratāḥ bhīmaḥ ca avani madhya sthaḥ hi ahaṅkāre maheśvaraḥ buddhau ca bhagavant īśaḥ sarvatas parameśvaraḥ etaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ aṇḍam saptabhiḥ prākataiḥ vṛtam etāḥ āvṛtya ca anyonyam aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ bhāvena vikārāḥ te vikāriṣu aṇḍāt jajñe saḥ eva īśaḥ puruṣa ūrka sama prabhaḥ tasya vāma aṅga jaḥ viṣṇuḥ sarva deva namaskṛtaḥ lakṣmyā devyā hi abhūt devaḥ icchayā parameṣṭhinaḥ dakṣiṇa aṅga bhavaḥ brahmā sarasvatyā jagadguruḥ yat tu sṛṣṭau prasaṃkhyātam mayā kāla antaram dvijāḥ etat kāla antaram jñeyam ahar vai pārameśvaram rātriḥ ca etāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśas ahar tasya tu yā sṛṣṭiḥ rātriḥ ca pralayaḥ smṛtaḥ upacāraḥ tu kriyate lokānām hita kāmyayā indriyāṇi indriya arthāḥ ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni buddhiḥ ca saha daivataiḥ ahar tiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi parameśasya dhīmataḥ sādharmyeṇa avatiṣṭhete pradhāna puruṣau ubhau guṇa sāmye layaḥ jñeyaḥ vaiṣamye sṛṣṭiḥ ucyate upāsya rajanīm kṛtsnām parām māheśvarīm tathā kṣobhayāmāsa yogena pareṇa parameśvaraḥ pradhānam puruṣam ca eva praviśya sa maheśvaraḥ maheśvarāt trayaḥ devāḥ jajñire jagat īśvarāt śāśvatāḥ paramāḥ guhyaḥ sarva ātmānaḥ śarīreṇa yad kṣaṇam viyogaḥ na hi eṣām na tyajanti parasparam īśvaraḥ tu paraḥ devaḥ viṣṇuḥ ca mahataḥ paraḥ paraḥ saḥ puruṣaḥ jñeyaḥ prakṛtiḥ sā parā smṛtā anupravṛttaḥ tu mahān tat enām ciras tiratvāt viṣayam śriyaḥ svayam īśvara dhiṣṭhitāt pūrvam tasmāt sat asat ātmakāt tejasā apratimaḥ dhīmān avyaktaḥ saṃprakāśakaḥ brahmā ca bhagavān tasmāt caturvaktraḥ prajāpatiḥ saṃsiddhaḥ kārya kāraṇe tathā vai samavartata apratīpena jñānena aiśvaryeṇa samanvitaḥ dharmeṇa ca apratīṣeṇa vairāgyeṇa ca te anvitāḥ avyaktāt jāyate teṣām manasā yat yat īhitam vaśīkṛta tvāt traiguṇyam sāpekṣa tvāt svabhāvāt sahasramūrdhā puruṣaḥ tisraḥ avasthāḥ svayambhoḥ puruṣa tve hi udāsīnaḥ tisraḥ avesthāḥ prajāpateḥ puruṣaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ rūpam tat paramātmanaḥ maheśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca nānā ākṛti kriyā rūpa nāmavanti sva līlayā maheśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca yat ca asya satatam bhāvaḥ tasmāt ātmā nirucyate ṛṣiḥ sarva gata tvāt ca śarīrī saḥ usya yat prabhuḥ svāmi tvam asya yat sarvam viṣṇuḥ sarva praveśanāt bhagavān bhagavat bhāvāt nirmala tvāt śivaḥ smṛtaḥ paramaḥ saṃprakṛṣṭa tvāt avanādaḥ om iti smṛtaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vijñānāt sarvaḥ sarva mayaḥ yatas ādi tvāt ādideva usau ajāta tvāt ajaḥ smṛtaḥ pāti yasmāt prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpatiḥ iti smṛtaḥ deveṣu ca mahān devaḥ mahādevaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ sarvaga tvāt ca devānām avaśya tvāt ca īśvaraḥ bṛhat tvāt ca smṛtaḥ brahmā bhūta tvāt bhūtaḥ ucyate kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetra vijñānāt eka tvāt kevalaḥ smṛtaḥ yasmāt puryām sa śete ca tasmāt pūruṣaḥ ucyate anādi tvāt ca pūrva tvāt svayaṃbhūḥ iti saṃsmṛtaḥ yājya tvāt ucyate yajñaḥ kaviḥ vikra anta darśanāt kramaṇaḥ kramaṇīya tvāt pālakaḥ ca api pālanāt āditya saṃjñaḥ kapilaḥ hi agrahaḥ ugniḥ iti smṛtaḥ na śakyaḥ parisaṃkhyātum api varṣa śataiḥ api kāla saṃkhyā vivṛttasya parārdhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ koṭi koṭi sahasrāṇi ahar bhūtāni yāni vai samatītāni kalpānām tāvat śeṣāḥ pare tu ye prathamaḥ sāṃprataḥ teṣām kalpaḥ yam vartate dvijāḥ atītāḥ vartamānāḥ ca bhaviṣyāḥ ye ca vai punar taiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sa parvatā pūrṇam yuga sahasram vai paripālyāḥ maheśvaraiḥ prajābhiḥ tapasā ca eva teṣām śṛṇuta vistaram manvantareṇa ca ekena sarvāṇi eva antarāṇi ca atītāni ca kalpāni sa udarkāṇi saha anvayaiḥ anāgateṣu tadvat ca tarkaḥ kāryaḥ vijānatā mānta tārā eka nīre ismin na prājñāyata kiñcana ekārṇave tadā tasmin naṣṭe stāvara jaṅgame sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ rukma varṇaḥ tu atīndriyaḥ brahmā nārāyaṇa ākhyaḥ tu suṣvāpa salile tadā imam ca udāharanti atra ślokam nārāyaṇam prati āpaḥ nārāḥ ca sūnavaḥ iti apām nāma śuśrumaḥ āpūrya tābhiḥ ayanam kṛtavan ātmanaḥ yatas apsu śete yatas tasmāt tatas nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ niśāyām iva khadyotaḥ prāvṛṣ kāle tatas tu saḥ tatas tu salile tasmin vijñāya antargatām mahīm anumānāt asam mūḍhaḥ bhūmeḥ uddharaṇam punar akarot sa tanūm anyām kalpa ādiṣu yathā purā salilena āplutām bhūmim dṛṣṭvā sa tu samantataḥ kim nu rūpam aham kṛtvā uddhareyam mahīm imām jala krīḍā anu sadṛśam vārāham rūpam āviśat adhṛṣyam sarva bhūtānām vāc mayam brahma saṃjñitam pṛthivī uddharaṇa arthāya praviveśa rasātalam adbhiḥ saṃchāditām bhūmim sa tām āśu prajāpatiḥ upagamya ujjahāra enām apaḥ ca api samāviśat sāmudrāḥ vai samudreṣu nādeyāḥ ca nadīṣu ca rasātala tale magnām rasātala puṭe gatām prabhuḥ loka hita arthāya daṃṣṭrayā abhyujjahāra gām tatas sva sthānam ānīya pṛthivīm pṛtivīdharaḥ mumoca pūrva vādasau dhārayitvā dharādharaḥ tatas tām devaḥ jagantaḥ sthāpana icchayā pṛthivyāḥ pravibhāgāya manaḥ cakra imbuja īkṣaṇaḥ pṛthivīm ca samām kṛtvā pṛthivyām saḥ cinot girīn prāñc sarge dahyamāne tu tadā saṃvartaka agninā tena agninā viśīrṇāḥ te parvatāḥ bhūri vistarāḥ śaityāt ekārṇave tasmin vāyunā tena saṃhatāḥ tadā acala tvāt acalāḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ tatas teṣu vikīrṇeṣu koṭiśas hi giriṣu atha viśvakarmā vibhajate kalpa ādiṣu punar punar sa samudrām imām pṛthvīm saptadvīpām sa parvatām bhūḥ ādyān ca turaḥ lokān punar sā utha vyakalpayat brahmā svayambhuḥ bhagavān sisṛkṣuḥ vividhāḥ prajāḥ sasarja sṛṣṭim tad rūpām kalpa ādiṣu yathā purā tamas mohaḥ mahā mohaḥ tāmisraḥ ca andha saṃjñitaḥ avidyā pañca parvā eṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ pañcadhā avasthitaḥ sargaḥ dhyāyataḥ saḥ abhimāninaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ tamasā ca eva bīja aṅkura vat āvṛtaḥ bahis antar ca aprakāśa stabdhaḥ niḥsaṃjñaḥ eva ca yasmāt teṣām vṛtā buddhiḥ duḥkhāni karaṇāni ca tasmāt te saṃvṛta ātmānaḥ nagāḥ mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ mukhya sargam tathābhūtam dṛṣṭvā brahmā hi asādhakam tasmāt tiryañc pravṛttaḥ sa tiryaksrotāḥ tatas smṛtaḥ paśu ādayaḥ te vikhyātāḥ utpatha grāhinaḥ dvijāḥ te sukha prīti bahulāḥ bahis antar ca saṃvṛtāḥ ca ūrdhva srotaḥ bhavāḥ smṛtāḥ te sattvasya ca yogena sṛṣṭāḥ sattva udbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ prakāśāt brahis antar ca ūrdhva srota udbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ te ūrdhvasrotasaḥ jñeyāḥ tuṣṭa ātmānaḥ budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ ūrdhvasrotaḥ su sṛṣṭeṣu deveṣu vara daḥ prabhuḥ prādurāsīt tadā vyaktāt arvāksrotāḥ tu sādhakaḥ te ca prakāśa bahulāḥ tamaḥ pṛktāḥ rajaḥ adhikāḥ tasmāt te duḥkha bahulāḥ bhūyas bhūyas ca kāriṇaḥ saṃvṛtāḥ bahis antar ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāḥ ca te lakṣaṇaiḥ tārakā ādyaiḥ te hi aṣṭadhā tu vyavastitāḥ viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca siddhyā tuṣṭyā tathā eva ca sthāvareṣu viparyāsaḥ s tiryagyoniṣu śaktitaḥ siddha ātmānaḥ manuṣyāḥ tu ṛṣi deveṣu kṛtsnaśas iti eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ vaikṛtaḥ anavamaḥ smṛtaḥ bhūta ādikānām bhūtānām ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ saḥ ucyate nivṛttam vartamānam ca teṣām jānanti vai punar bhūta ādikānām bhūtānām saptamaḥ sargaḥ eva ca te a parigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāga ratāḥ punar svādanāḥ ca api aśīlāḥ ca jñeyāḥ bhūta ādikāḥ ca te viparyayeṇa bhūta ādiḥ aśaktyā ca vyavasthitaḥ tanmātrāṇām dvitīyaḥ tu bhūta sargaḥ saḥ ucyate iti eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ mukhya sargaḥ caturthaḥ ca mukhyāḥ vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ tatas urvāksrotasām sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ aṣṭamaḥ anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikaḥ tāmasaḥ ca saḥ pañca ete vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāḥ tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ prākṛtaḥ vaikṛtaḥ ca eva kaumāraḥ navamaḥ smṛtaḥ abuddhi pūrvakāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāḥ tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ caturdhā avasthitaḥ saḥ utha sarva bhūteṣu kṛtsraśas iti ete prākṛtāḥ ca eva vaikṛtāḥ ca nava smṛtāḥ paraspara anuraktāḥ ca kāraṇaiḥ ca budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ agre sasarja vai brahmā mānasān ātmanaḥ samān ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraḥ ca dvau etau ūrdhvaretasau vyatīte tu aṣṭame kalpe purāṇau loka sākṣiṇaḥ tau vārāhe tu bhūrloke tejaḥ saṃkṣipya dhiṣṭhitau tau ubhau mokṣa karmaṇau āropya ātmānam ātmani prajām dharmam ca kāmam ca tyaktvā vairāgyam āsthitau sanandam sanakam ca eva vidvāṃsam ca sanātanam saṃbuddhāḥ ca eva nānātve apravṛttāḥ ca yoginaḥ a sṛṣṭvā eva prajā sargam pratisargam gatāḥ punar tatas teṣu vyatīteṣu tatonyān sādhakān sutān mānasān asṛjat brahma punar sthāna abhimāninaḥ mahī apaḥ ugnim pṛthivīm vāyum antarikṣam divam tathā samudrān ca nadīḥ ca eva tathā śaila vanaspatīn oṣadhīnām tathā ātmānaḥ vallīnām vṛkṣa vīrudhām latāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kalāḥ ca eva muhūrtāḥ saṃdhi rātri ahān ardha māsān ca māsān ca ayana abda yugāni ca sthāna abhimāninaḥ sarve sthāna ākhyāḥ ca eva te smṛtāḥ devān ṛṣīn ca mahataḥ gadataḥ tān na abodhata dakṣam atrim vasiṣṭham ca nava brahmānaḥ iti ete purāṇe niścayam gatāḥ teṣām brahma ātmakānām vai sarveṣām brahma vādinām sthānāni kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat padmasaṃbhavaḥ saḥ sṛjat vyavasāyāt tu dharmam devaḥ maheśvaraḥ mānasaḥ ca ruciḥ nāma vijajñe brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ prāṇāt brahmā asṛjat dakṣam cakṣurbhyām ca marīcinam bhṛguḥ tu hṛdayāt jajñe ṛṣiḥ salila janmanaḥ śirasā uṅgirasaḥ ca eva śrotrāt atrim tata sṛjat pulastyam ca tathā udānāt vyānāt ca pulaham punar samāna jaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca apānāt nirmame kratum iti ete brahmanaḥ putrāḥ divyāḥ ekādaśā smṛtāḥ dharma ādayaḥ prathama jāḥ sarve te brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ bhṛgu ādayaḥ tu te sṛṣṭāḥ navā ete brahma vādinaḥ gṛhamedhinaḥ purāṇāḥ te dharmaḥ taiḥ saṃpravartitaḥ teṣām dvādaśa te vaṃśāḥ divyāḥ deva guṇa anvitāḥ kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ alaṅkṛtāḥ ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraḥ ca dvau etau ūrdhvaretasau mahā iti aṣṭame kalpe purāṇau loka sākṣiṇaḥ virājetām ubhau loke tejaḥ saṃkṣipya dhiṣṭhitau tau ubhau yoga karma amau āropya ātmānam ātmani prajām dharmam ca kāmam ca tyaktvā vairāgyam āsthitau tasmāt sanatkumāra ūti nāma asya iha pratiṣṭhitam tatas abhidhyāyataḥ tasya jajñire mānasāḥ prajāḥ tad śarīra samutpannaiḥ kāryaiḥ taiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebhyaḥ tasya dhīmataḥ tatas deva asura pitṝn mānuṣān ca catuṣṭayam sisṛkṣuḥ ambhā asi etāni svam ātmānam ayūyujat tatas asya jaghanāt pūrvam asurāḥ jajñire sutāḥ asuḥ prāṇaḥ smṛtaḥ vipraḥ tad janmānaḥ tatas usurāḥ yayā sṛṣṭa asurāḥ sarve tām tanum sa vyapohata sā tamaḥ bahulā yasmāt tatas rātriḥ niyāmakā māvṛtāḥ tamasā rātrau prajāḥ tasmāt svapanti uta sṛṣṭvā surān tatas saḥ vai tanum anyām agṛhṇata avyaktām sattva bahulām tatas tām saḥ abhyapūjayat tatas tām yuñjataḥ tasya priyam āsīt prajāpateḥ yatas asya dīvyataḥ jātāḥ tena devāḥ prakīrtitāḥ dhātuḥ dyauḥ iti yaḥ proktaḥ krīḍāyām saḥ vibhāvyate devān sṛṣṭvā atha deveśaḥ tanum anyām apadyata utsṛṣṭā sā tanuḥ tena sadyas ūhaḥ samajāyata pitṛ vat manyamānasya putrān tān dhyāyataḥ prabhoḥ tasmāt te pitaraḥ devāḥ pitṛ tvam tena teṣu tat yayā sṛṣṭāḥ tu pitaraḥ tanum tām sa vyapohata yasmāt ahar devatānām rātriḥ yā sā āsurī smṛtā tayoḥ madhye tu paitrā yā tanuḥ sā tu garīyāḥ tasmāt devā surāḥ sarve ṛṣayaḥ mānavāḥ tathā upāsaṃte mudā yuktāḥ rātri ahnoḥ madhyamām tanum rajas mātra ātmakāyām tu mānasā saḥ sṛjat prabhuḥ rajaḥ priyān tatas saḥ utha mānasān asṛjat sutān sṛṣṭvā punar prajāḥ ca api svām tanum tām apohata yasmāt bhavanti saṃhṛṣṭā jyotsnāyāḥ udbhave prajāḥ jyotsnā saṃdhyā ahar ca eva sattva mātra ātmakam trayam tamaḥ mātra ātmakā rātriḥ sā vai tasmāt niśā ātmakā tasmāt devāḥ divā tanvā tuṣṭyā sṛṣṭāḥ mukhāt tu vai yasmāt teṣām divā janma balinaḥ tena vai divā tanvā yayā asurān rātrau jaghanāt asṛjat prabhuḥ etāni eva bhaviṣyāṇām daṃvānām asuraiḥ saha pitṝṇām mānavānām ca atīta anāgateṣu vai jyotsnā rātri ahanī saṃdhyā catvāri aṃbhāṃsi tāni vai bhānti yasmāt tatas umbhāṃsi śabdaḥ yam su manīṣibhiḥ bhātiḥ dīptau nigaditaḥ punar ca atha prajāpatiḥ saḥ ambhāṃsi etāni sṛṣṭvā tu deva mānuṣa dānavān pitṝn ca eva sṛjat tanvaḥ ātmanā vividhān punar tām utsṛjya tanum jyotsnām tatas nyām prāpya sa prabhuḥ mūrtim tamaḥ rajaḥ prāyām punar eva abhyapūjayat andhakāre kṣudhā āviṣṭān tatonyasaḥ sṛjat prabhuḥ tena sṛṣṭāḥ kṣudhā ātmānaḥ ambhāṃsi ādātum udyatāḥ rakṣāma uktavantaḥ tu teṣu ye rākṣasāḥ nāma te yasmāt kṣudhā āviṣṭāḥ niśācarāḥ ye bruvan yakṣamā umbhāṃsi teṣām hṛṣṭāḥ parasparam tena te karmaṇā yakṣāḥ guhyakāḥ gūḍha karmaṇā rakṣā iti pālane ca api dhātuḥ eṣa vibhāṣyate tam dṛṣṭvā hi apriyeṇa asya keśāḥ śīrṇāḥ tu dhīmataḥ te śīrṇāḥ ca utthitāḥ hi ūrdhvam te ca eva ārurudhuḥ prabhum hīnāḥ tad śirasaḥ bālāḥ yasmāt ca eva avasarpiṇaḥ vyāla ātmānaḥ smṛtāḥ bālāḥ hīna tvāt ahayaḥ smṛtāḥ pata tvāt pannagāḥ ca eva sarpāḥ ca eva avasarpaṇāt sa tu sarpān saha utpannān āviveśa viṣa ātmakaḥ sarpān sṛṣṭvā tatas kruddhaḥ krodha ātmānaḥ vinirmame varṇena kapiśena ugrāḥ te bhūtāḥ piśita aśanāḥ bhūta tvāt te smṛtāḥ bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ piśita aśanāt dhayati iti eṣa vai dhātuḥ pāna tve paripaṭhyate hayantaḥ jajñire vācam gandharvāḥ tena te smṛtāḥ aṣṭasu etāsu sṛṣṭāsu deva yoniṣu sa prabhuḥ tatas sva chandāt anyāni vayāṃsi vayasā sṛjat paśūn sṛṣṭvā sa deveśaḥ asṛjat pakṣi gaṇān api mukha tojāḥ sasarja atha vakṣasaḥ ca āvayoḥ sṛjat gāḥ ca eva atha udarāt brahmā pārśvābhyām ca vinirmame padbhyām ca aśvān sa mātaṅgān rāsabhān āvayāt mṛgān uṣṭrān aśvatarān ca eva tathā anyāḥ ca eva jātayaḥ evam paśu oṣadhīḥ sṛṣṭvā ayūyujat sa udhvare prabhuḥ gauḥ ajaḥ pūruṣaḥ meṣaḥ hi aśva uśvatara gardabhau etān grāmyān paśūn āhuḥ āraṇyān vai nibodhata śvāpadaḥ dvi khuraḥ hastī vānarāḥ pakṣi pañcamāḥ ādakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāḥ tu sarīsṛpāḥ mahiṣāḥ gavaya akṣāḥ ca plavaṅgāḥ śarabhāḥ vṛkāḥ siṃhaḥ tu saptamaḥ teṣām āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ smṛtāḥ gāyatram ca ṛcam ca eva trivṛt sāma rathantaram agniṣṭomam ca yajñānām nirmame prathamāt mukhāt yajuṃṣi traiṣṭubham chanda stomam pañcadaśam tathā vṛhatsāma tathā ukthyam ca dakṣiṇāt asṛjat mukhāt sāmāni jagatī chanda stomam saptadaśam tathā vairūpam atirātram ca paścimāt asṛjat mukhāt ekaviṃśam atharvāṇam āptoryā māṇam eva ca anuṣṭubham sa vairājam uttarāt asṛjat mukhāt vidyutā uśani meghān ca rohita indradhanūṃṣi ca uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyaḥ tasya jajñire sṛṣṭvā catuṣṭayam pūrvam deva asura narān pitṝn tatas asṛjat sa bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca yakṣān piśācān gandharvan tu atha eva apsarasām gaṇān nara kinnara rakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśu mṛga uragān avyayam ca vyayam ca api yat idam sthāṇu jaṅgamam teṣām vai yāni karmāṇi prāk sṛṣṭyām pratipedire tāni eva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punar punar hiṃsra ahiṃsre mṛdu krūre dharma adharme nṛta anṛte mahābhūteṣu sṛṣṭeṣu indrīya artheṣu mūrtiṣu viniyogam ca bhūtānām dhātā eva vyādadhāt svayam kecid puruṣakāram tu prāhuḥ karma su mānavāḥ daivam iti apare viprāḥ svabhāvam bhūta cintakāḥ karma sthāḥ viṣamam brūyuḥ sattva sthāḥ sama darśanāḥ nāma rūpam ca bhūtānām kṛtānām ca prapañcanam ṛṣīṇām nāmadheyāni yāḥ ca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ śarvarī ante prasūtānām tāni eva ebhyaḥ dadāti ajaḥ evaṃvidhāḥ sṛṣṭayaḥ tu brahmanaḥ vyakta janmanaḥ śarvarī ante pradṛśyante siddhim āśritya mānasīm evaṃbhūtāni sṛṣṭāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca yadā asya tāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ na vyavardhanta sattamāḥ tamaḥ mātrā vṛtaḥ brahmā tadā śokena duḥkhitaḥ atha ātmani samadrākṣīt tamaḥ mātrām niyāmakām tamaḥ ca vyanudat paścāt rajaḥ sattvam tam āvṛṇot adharmaḥ tamasaḥ jajñe hiṃsā śokāt ajāyata āsīt ca enam aśiśriyat svām tanum sa tatas brahmā tām apohata bhāsvarām ardhena nārī sā tasya śatarūpā vyajāyata prakṛtim bhūtadhātrim tām kāmāt vai sṛṣṭavan prabhuḥ sā divam pṛthivīm ca eva mahimnā vyāpya adhiṣṭhitā brahmaṇaḥ sā tanuḥ pūrvā divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati yā tu ardhāt sṛjataḥ nārī śatarūpā vyajāyata sā devī niyutam taptvā tapaḥ parama duścaram bhartāram dīpta yaśasam puruṣam pratyapadyata sa vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvam puruṣaḥ manuḥ ucyate lebhe sa puruṣaḥ patnīm śatarūpāḥ ma yoni jām virājam asṛjat brāhmā saḥ bhavat puruṣaḥ virāj samrāj ca śatarūpāḥ vai verājaḥ sa manuḥ smṛtaḥ sa vairājaḥ prajā sargam sasarja puruṣaḥ manuḥ vairājāt puruṣā dvīrāt śatarūpā vyajāyata kanye dve ca mahābhāge yābhyām jātāḥ imāḥ prajāḥ devī nāma tathā ākūtiḥ prasūtiḥ ca eva te ubhe svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prasūtim tu dakṣāya pradadau prabhuḥ prāṇaḥ dakṣaḥ iti jñeyaḥ saṃkalpaḥ manuḥ ucyate ruceḥ prajāpateḥ sa ūthaḥ ākūtim pratyapādayat ākūtau mithunam jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham yajñaḥ ca dakṣiṇā ca eva yamalau saṃbabhūvatuḥ yajñasya dakṣiṇāyām tu putrāḥ dvādaśa jajñire yāmāḥ iti samākhyātāḥ devāḥ svāyaṃbhuventare etasya putrāḥ yajñasya tasmāt yāmāḥ ca te smṛtāḥ ajitaḥ ca eva śukraḥ ca gaṇau dvau brahmaṇā kṛtau yāmāḥ pūrvam prajātāḥ ye te abhavan tu divaukasaḥ svāyaṃbhuva sutāyām tu prasūtyām loka mātaraḥ tasyām kanyāḥ caturviśatīḥ dakṣaḥ tu ajanayat prabhuḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ sarvāḥ kamala locanāḥ bhogavatyaḥ ca tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ yoga mātaraḥ sarvāḥ ca brahma vādinyaḥ sarvāḥ viśvasya mātaraḥ śraddhā lakṣmīḥ dhṛtiḥ tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ medhā kriyā tathā buddhiḥ lajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtiḥ trayodaśa patnī artham pratijagrāha dharmaḥ dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ dārāṇi etāni vai tasya vihitāni svayaṃbhuvā tābhyaḥ śiṣṭa yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ satī khyāti atha saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā saṃnatiḥ ca anasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā rudraḥ bhṛguḥ mariciḥ ca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ satīm bhavāya prāyacchat khyātim ca bhṛgave tatas prītim ca eva pulastyāya kṣamām vai pulahāya ca kratuḥ iva saṃnatim nāma anasūyām tathā atraye ūrjām dadau vasiṣṭhāya svāhām api agnaye dadau etāḥ sarvāḥ mahābhāgāḥ prajāsu anusṛtāḥ sthitāḥ manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam śraddhā kāmam vijajñe vai darpaḥ lakṣmī sutaḥ smṛtaḥ dhṛtyāḥ tu niyamaḥ putraḥ tuṣṭyāḥ saṃtoṣaḥ eva ca puṣṭyāḥ lobhaḥ sutaḥ ca api medhā putraḥ śrutaḥ tathā lajjāyām vinayaḥ putraḥ vyavasāyaḥ vasoḥ sutaḥ kṣemaḥ śānti sutaḥ ca api sukham siddhyāḥ vyajāyata yaśaḥ kīrti sutaḥ ca api iti ete dharma sūnavaḥ kāmasya harṣaḥ putraḥ vai devyām prītau vyajāyata jajñe hiṃsā tu adharmāt vai nikṛtim ca anṛtam sutam nikṛtau tu dvayam jajñe bhayam narakaḥ eva ca bhūyas vai māyā mṛtyum bhūta apahāriṇam vedanāyāḥ sutaḥ ca api duḥkham jajñe ca rauravaḥ mṛtyoḥ vyādhi jarā śoka krodha asūyāḥ ca jajñire duḥkha uttarāḥ sutāḥ hi ete sarve ca adharma lakṣaṇāḥ na eṣām bhāryāḥ tu putrāḥ ca sarve hi ete parigrahāḥ iti eṣa tāmasaḥ sargaḥ jajñe dharma niyāmakaḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti vyādiṣṭaḥ brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ sā ubhidhyāya satīm bhāryām nirmame hi atma saṃbhavān na adhikān na ca hīnān tān mānasān ātmanaḥ samān sahasram hi sahasrāṇām saḥ sṛjat kṛttivāsasaḥ tulyān eva ātmanaḥ sarvān rūpa tejaḥ balu śrutaiḥ piṅgalān sa niṣaṅgān ca sa kapardān sa lohitān viśiṣṭān hari keśān ca dṛṣṭi ghnān ca kapālinaḥ mahā rūpān virūpān ca viśva rūpān svarūpiṇaḥ rathinaḥ carmiṇaḥ ca eva varmiṇaḥ ca varūthinaḥ sahasra śata bāhūn ca divyān bhau mā antarikṣa gān sthūla śīrṣān aṣṭa daṃṣṭrān dvi jihvān tān tri locanān ca ājyapān somapān api mīḍhuṣoti kapālān ca śiti kaṇṭha ūrdhvaretasaḥ havya ādān śruta dharman ca dharmiṇaḥ hi atha barhinaḥ āsīnān dhāvataḥ ca eva pañca bhūtān sahasraśas vṛddhān buddhimataḥ ca eva brahmiṣṭhān śubha darśanān nīlagrīvān sahasra akṣān sarvān ca atha kṣamā karān adṛśyān sarva bhūtānām mahā yogān mahā ojasaḥ ayātayāmān asṛjat rudrān etān sura uttamān brahmā dṛṣṭvā abravīt enam mā asrākṣīḥ īdṛśīḥ prajāḥ sraṣṭavyāḥ na ātmanaḥ tulyāḥ prajāḥ deva namaḥ astu te anyāḥ sṛja tvam bhadram te prajāḥ vai mṛtyu saṃyutāḥ na ārapsyante hi karmāṇi prajā avagata mṛtyavaḥ evam uktaḥ abravīt enam na aham mṛtyu jarā anvitāḥ prajāḥ sakṣyāmi bhadram te sthitā uha tvam sṛja prajāḥ ete ye vai mayā sṛṣṭāḥ virūpāḥ nīla lohitāḥ sahasrāṇām sahasram tu ātmanaḥ nissṛtāḥ prajāḥ ete devāḥ bhaviṣyanti rudrāḥ nāma mahā balāḥ pṛthivyām antarikṣe ca dikṣu ca eva pariśritāḥ śata rudrāḥ sama ātmanaḥ yājñikāḥ sārdham taiḥ ījyamānāḥ te sthāsyanti iha ā yuga kṣayāt pratyuvāca namaskṛtya hṛṣyamāṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ evam bhavatu bhadram te yathā te vyāhṛtam vibho brahmaṇā samanu jñāte tathā sarvam abhūt kila tatas prabhṛti deveśaḥ na ca asūyata vai prajāḥ yasmāt uktaḥ sthitaḥ asmi iti tasmāt sthāṇuḥ iti smṛtaḥ sva icchayā asau dvidhā bhūtaḥ pṛthak strī puruṣaḥ pṛthak tatra yā sā mahābhāgā śaṃkarasya ardha kāyinī prāk uktā tu mahā devī strī sā eva iha satī hi abhūt hitāya jagantām devī dakṣeṇa ārādhitā purā kārya artham dakṣiṇam tasyāḥ śuklam vāmam tathā asitam ātmānam vibhajasva iti proktā devena śaṃbhunā sā tathā uktā dvidhā bhūtā śuklā kṛṣṇā ca vai dvijāḥ tasyāḥ nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇvantu ca samāhitāḥ svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā medhā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā icchā śaktiḥ kriyā ātmakā aparṇā ca ekaparṇā ca tathā ca eva ekapāṭalā umā haimavatī ca eva kalyāṇī ca ekamātṛkā khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurī iti viśrutā gaṇāṃbikā mahā devī nandinī jātavedasī eka rūpam atha etasyāḥ pṛthak deha vibhāvatān sāvitrī vara dā puṇyā pāvanā loka viśrutā ājñā āveśanī kṛṣṇā tāmasī sāttvikī śivā prakṛtiḥ vikṛtā raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī kālarātriḥ mahāmāyā revatī bhūtanāyikā dvāpara anta vibhāge ca nāmāni imā imāni suvratāḥ gautamī kauśikī ca āryā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī kumārī yādavī devī varadā kṛṣṇapiṅgalā barhīdhvajā śūla dharā paramā brahmacāriṇī aparājitā bahubhujā pragalbhā siṃhavāhinī śumbha ādi daitya hantrī ca mahā mahiṣamardinī amoghā vindhyanilayā vikraāntā gaṇanāyikā devyāḥ nāma vikārāṇi iti etāni yathākramam ye paṭhanti narāḥ teṣām vidyate na ca pātakam rakṣām etām prayuñjīta jale vā atha sthale api vā bhaya sthāne viśeṣataḥ mad api ca sarvāsu devyāḥ nāmāni kīrtayet āryaka graha bhūtaiḥ ca pūtanā mātṛbhiḥ tathā abhyarditānām bālānām rakṣām etām prayojayet mahādevī kale dve tu prajñā śrīḥ ca prakīrtite mābhyām devī sahasrāṇī yebhiḥ vyāptam akhilam jagant ātiṣṭhat sarva lokānām hitāya parameśvaraḥ rudraḥ paśupatiḥ ca āsīt purā dagdham puratrayam devāḥ ca paśavaḥ sarve babhūvuḥ tasya tejasā yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api ādi sarga kramam śubham sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ lokam śrāvayet vā dvijottamān iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sṛṣṭivistāraḥ nāma saptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ samāsāt vistarāt ca eva sargaḥ proktaḥ tvayā śubhaḥ katham paśupatiḥ ca āsīt puram dagdhum maheśvaraḥ katham ca paśavaḥ ca āsan devāḥ sa brahmakāḥ prabhoḥ purasya saṃbhavaḥ sarvaḥ vara lābhaḥ purā śrutaḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā sūtāḥ paurāṇika uttamaḥ yathā śrutam tathā prāha vyāsāt viśva artha sūcakāt uvāca trailokyasya asya śāpāt hi manaḥ vāc kāya sambhavāt vidyunmālī tārakākṣaḥ kamalākṣaḥ ca vīryavān tapaḥ tepuḥ mahātmānaḥ mahā bala parākramāḥ tapasā karśayāmāsuḥ dehān svān dānava uttamāḥ teṣām pitāmahaḥ prītaḥ vara daḥ pradadau varam ūcuḥ avadhya tvam ca sarveṣām sarva bhūteṣu sarvadā tān abravīt tadā devaḥ lokānām prabhuḥ avyayaḥ anyam varam vṛṇīdhvam vai yādṛśam saṃprarocate vayam purāṇi trīṇi eva samāsthāya mahīm imām tathā varṣa sahasreṣu sameṣyāmaḥ parasparam ekībhāvam gamiṣyanti purāṇi etāni ca anaghaiḥ ca etāni yaḥ hanyāt bhagavant tadā ekena eva iṣuṇā devaḥ sa naḥ mṛtyuḥ bhaviṣyati tatas mayaḥ sva tapasā cakre vīraḥ purāṇi atha kāñcanam divi tatra āsīt antarikṣe ca rājatam bhavat bhumau puram teṣām mahātmanām ekaikam yojana śatam vistāra āyāmāt samam kāñcanam tārakākṣasya kamalākṣasya rājatam mayaḥ ca balavān tatra daitya dānava pūjitaḥ hairaṇye rājate ca eva kṛṣṇāyasa maye tathā manaḥ ca ātmanaḥ kṛtvā te āste balavān tadā evam babhūvuḥ daityānām ati durgāṇi suvratāḥ purāṇi vipra indrāḥ trailokyam iva ca aparam nānā prasāda saṃkīrṇam maṇi jālaiḥ samāvṛtam sūrya maṇḍala saṃkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ viśvatomukhaiḥ śobhitam tripuram teṣām pṛthak pṛthak anuttamaiḥ divya strībhiḥ su saṃpūrṇam gandharvaiḥ siddha cāraṇaiḥ rudra ālayaiḥ pratigṛham sa agnihotraiḥ dvijottamāḥ ca dīrghikābhiḥ tu sarvatas matta mātaṃga yūthaiḥ ca turaṃgaiḥ ca su śobhanaiḥ sabhā prapādibhiḥ ca eva krīḍā sthanaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak veda adhyayana śālābhiḥ vividhābhiḥ samantataḥ adhṛṣyam manasā api anyaiḥ mayasya eva ca māyayā pativratābhiḥ sarvatra sevitam muni puṃgavāḥ kṛtvā api su mahat pāpām apāpaiḥ śaṃkara arcanāt daitya īśvaraiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ sa dāraiḥ sa sutaiḥ dvijāḥ mahādeva itaram tyaktvā devam tasya arcanam sthitaiḥ vyūḍha uraskaiḥ vṛṣa skandhaiḥ sarva āyudha dharaiḥ sadā sarvadā kṣudhitaiḥ ca eva dāva agni sadṛśa īkṣaṇaiḥ nīla adri meru saṃkāśaiḥ nīrada upama niḥsvanaiḥ mayena rakṣitaiḥ sarvaiḥ śikṣitaiḥ yuddha lālasaiḥ sa indrāḥ devāḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ drumāḥ dāva agninā yathā atha evam te tadā dagdhāḥ devāḥ deveśvaram harim saḥ upi nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān cintayāmāsa cetasā kim kāryam deva kāryeṣu bhagavant iti sa prabhuḥ tadā sasmāra vai yajñam yajñamūrtiḥ janārdanaḥ yajvā yajñabhuj īśānaḥ yajvanām phala daḥ prabhuḥ devam te puruṣam ca eva praṇemuḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ tadā bhagavān api tam dṛṣṭvā yajñam prāha sanātanam sanātanaḥ tadā sa indrān devām na ālokya ca acyutaḥ śrī viṣṇuḥ uvāca uvāca siṃha nādam mahat kṛtvā yajñeśam tuṣṭuvuḥ surāḥ punar prāha sa sarvān tān tridaśān tridaśeśvaraḥ hatvā dagdhvā ca bhūtāni bhuktvā ca anyāyataḥ api vā yajet yadi mahādevaiḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ apāpāḥ na eva hantavyāḥ pāpāḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ hantavyāḥ sarva yatnena katham vadhyāḥ sura uttamāḥ asurāḥ durmadāḥ pāpāḥ api devaiḥ mahā balaiḥ brahmā athavā devāḥ daityāḥ deva ari sūdanāḥ munayaḥ ca mahātmānaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ yaḥ saptaviṃśakaḥ nityaḥ parātparataraḥ prabhuḥ viśva amara īśvaraḥ vandyaḥ viśvādhāraḥ maheśvaraḥ saḥ eva sarva deva īśaḥ sarveṣām api śaṅkaraḥ tasya aṃśame kam sampūjya devāḥ deva tvam āgatāḥ dharma niṣṭhāḥ ca te sarve śrauta smārta vidhau sthitāḥ rudram iṣṭvā yathānyāyam jeṣyāmaḥ daitya sattamān sa tārakākṣeṇa mayena guptam svastham ca guptam sphaṭika ābham ekam uvāca evam uktvā hariḥ ca iṣṭvā yajñena upasadā prabhum upaviṣṭaḥ dadarśa atha bhūta saṃghān sahasraśas śūla śakti gadā hastān ṭaṅka upala śilā āyudhān nānā praharaṇa upetān nānā veṣa dharān tadā kālāgni rudra saṃkāśān kālarudra upamān tadā prāha devaḥ hariḥ sākṣāt praṇipatya sthitān prabhuḥ uvāca tatas praṇamya deveśam bhūta saṃghāḥ puratrayam praviśya naṣṭāḥ te sarve śalabhāḥ iva pāvakam tatas tu naṣṭāḥ te sarve bhūtāḥ deveśvara ājñayā tuṣṭuvuḥ devadeveśam paramātmānam īśvaram tatas parājitāḥ devāḥ dhvasta vīryāḥ kṣaṇena tu sa indrāḥ saṃgamya deveśam upendram dhiṣṭhitāḥ bhayāt tān dṛṣṭvā cintayāmāsa bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ kim kṛtyam iti saṃtaptaḥ saṃtaptān sa indrakān kṣaṇam katham tu teṣām daityānām balam hatvā prayatnāt deva kāryam kariṣyāmi prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ pāpam vicārāt na asti dharmiṣṭhānām na saṃśayaḥ pāpam nudati dharmeṇa dharmeṃ sarvam pratiṣṭhitam dharmāt aiśvaryam iti eṣā śrutiḥ eṣā sanātanī daityāḥ ca ete hi dharmiṣṭhāḥ sarve tripura vāsinaḥ tasmāt avadhya tām prāptāḥ na anyathā dvija puṅgavāḥ pūjasā bhoga saṃpattiḥ avaśyam jāyate dvijāḥ tasmāt te bhoginaḥ daityāḥ liṅga arcana parāyaṇāḥ tasmāt kṛtvā dharma vighnam aham devāḥ sva māyayā daityānām deva akārya artham jeṣya iham tripuram kṣaṇāt uvāca vicārya enam tatas teṣām bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ kartum vyavasitaḥ ca abhūt dharma vighnam sura arīṇām asṛjat ca mahā tejāḥ puruṣam ca ātma saṃbhavam māyī māyā mayam teṣām dharma vighna artham acyutaḥ śāstram ca śāstā sarveṣām akarot kāma rūpadhṛk sarva saṃmohanam māyī dṛṣṭa pratyaya saṃyutam etat sva aṅgabhavāya eva puruṣāya upadiśya tu māyī māyā mayam śāstram grantha ṣoḍaśa lakṣakam puratraya vināśāya prāha onam puruṣam hariḥ gantum arhasi nāśāya bho tūrṇam puravā sinām dharmāḥ tathā pramaśyantu śrauta smārtāḥ na saṃśayaḥ tatas praṇamya tam māyī māyā śāstra viśāradaḥ praviśya tat puram tūrṇam muniḥ māyām tadā akarot māyayā tasya te daityāḥ puratraya nivāsinaḥ śraitam smārtam ca saṃtyajya tasya śiṣyāḥ tadā abhavan tatyajuḥ ca mahādevam śaṅkaram parameśvaram nāradaḥ upi tadā māyī niyogāt māyinaḥ prabhoḥ praviśya tat puram tena māyinā saha dīkṣitaḥ muniḥ śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyaiḥ ca saṃvṛtaḥ sarvatas svayam strī dharmam ca akarot strīṇām duścāra phala siddhi dam jana āsaktāḥ babhūvuḥ tāḥ vinindya pati devatāḥ nāryaḥ caranti saṃtyajya bhartṝn svairam vṛthak adhamāḥ strīṇām mātā pitā bandhuḥ sakhiḥ mitram ca bāndhavaḥ bhartā eva na saṃdehaḥ tathā api asaha māyayā kṛtvā api su mahat pāpam yā bhartuḥ prema saṃyutā purā ekāmuni śārdūlāḥ sarva dharmān sadā patim saṃtyajya apūjayan sādhvyaḥ devān anyān jagadgurūn tāḥ svarga lokam āsādya modante vigata jvarāḥ narakam ca jagāma anyā tasmāt bhartā parā gatiḥ tathā api bhartṝn svān tyaktvā babhūvuḥ svaira vṛttayaḥ māyayā devadevasya viṣṇoḥ tasya ājñayā prabhoḥ alakṣmīḥ ca svayam tasya niyogāt tripuram gatā yā lakṣmīḥ tapasā labdhā deveśvarāt ajāt moham viṣṇu māyā vinirmitam teṣām dattvā kṣaṇam devaḥ tāsām māyī ca nāradaḥ evam naṣṭe tadā dharme śrauta smārte su śobhane pāṣaṇḍe khyāpite tena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā tārthaḥ iva deveśaḥ devaiḥ sārdham umāpatim tapasā prāpya sarva jñam tuṣṭāva puruṣottamaḥ śrī bhagavant uvāca nārāyaṇāya śarvāya brahmaṇe brahma rūpiṇe śāśvatāya hi anantāya avyaktāya ca te namaḥ uvāca evam stutvā mahādevam daṇḍa vat praṇipatya ca jajāpa rudram bhagavant koṭi vāram jale sthitaḥ devāḥ ca sarve te devam tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram sa indrāḥ sa sādhyāḥ sa yamāḥ sa rudrāḥ sa marut gaṇāḥ ūcuḥ namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyam śaṃkarāya ārti hāriṇe tvam ādiḥ tvam anantaḥ ca anantaḥ ca akṣayaḥ prabhuḥ prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ sākṣāt sraṣṭā hartā jagadguro trātā netā jagati asmin dvijānām dvija vatsala vara daḥ vāc mayaḥ vācyaḥ vācya vācaka varjitaḥ hṛd puṇḍarīka suṣire yoginām saṃsthitaḥ sadā vadanti sūrayaḥ santam param brahma svarūpiṇam dṛṣṭam śrutam sthitam sarvam jāyamānam jagadguro sarvatas pāṇi pādam tvām sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhasi mahādevam anirdeśyam sarvajñam tvām anāmayam viśvarūpam virupākṣam sadāśivam anāmayam koṭi bhāskara saṃkāśam koṭi śītāṃśu sannibham koṭi kālāgni saṃkāśam ṣaḍviṃśakam anīśvaram ha vadānti vara dam devam sarva āvāsam svayambhum śrutayaḥ śruti sāram tvām śruti sāra vidojanāḥ adṛṣṭam asmābhiḥ aneka mūrte vinā kṛtam yat bhavatā atha loke tvam eva daitya asura bhūta saṃghān devān nān sthāvara jaṅgamān ca pāhi nā anyā gatiḥ śaṃbho vinihatya asura uttamān māyayā mohitāḥ sarve bhavataḥ parameśvara yathā taraṅgāḥ lahari samūhāḥ yudhyanti ca anyonyam apāṃnidhau ca yalāśrayāt eva jaḍīkṛtāḥ ca sura asurāḥ tadvat ajasya sarvam uvāca yaḥ idam prātar utthāya suciḥ bhūtvā japet naraḥ śṛṇuyāt vā stavam puṇyam sarva kāmam avāpnuyāt śṛṇuyāt vā stavam puṇyam sarva kāmam avāpnuyāt prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā devān ālokya śaṃkaraḥ jñātam mayā idam adhunā deva kāryam sura īśvarāḥ viṣmoḥ māyā balam ca eva nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ teṣām adharma niṣṭhānām daityānām deva sattamāḥ puratraya vināśam ca kariṣye iham sura uttamāḥ uvāca atha sa brahmakāḥ devāḥ sa iṃdra pendrāḥ samāgatāḥ śrutvā prabhoḥ tadā vākyam praṇemuḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca te līlā ambujena ca āhatya kalam āha vṛṣadhvajam krīḍamānam vibho paśya ṣaṇmukham ravi sānnibham putram putravatām śreṣṭham bhūpitam bhūṣaṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ kaṭakaiḥ ca eva kuṇḍalaiḥ valayaiḥ śubhaiḥ kalpakadruma jaiḥ puṣpaiḥ śobhitaiḥ alakaiḥ śubhaiḥ hāraiḥ vārīja rāga ādi maṇi citraiḥ tathā aṅgadaiḥ tilakaiḥ ca mahādevaiḥ paśya putram su śībhanam aṅkitam kuṅkuma ādyaiḥ ca vṛttam bhasita nirmitam vakra vṛndam ca paśya īśaiḥ vṛndam kāmalakam yathā netrāṇi ca vibho paśya śubhāni tvam śubhāni ca añjanāni vicitrāṇi maṅgala artham ca mātṛbhiḥ kṛttikā ādyaiḥ svāhayā ca viśeṣataḥ iti evam lokamātryāḥ ca vāgbhiḥ saṃbodhitaḥ śivaḥ na yayau tṛptim īśānaḥ piban skanda ānana amṛtam na sasmāra ca tān devān daitya śastra nipīḍitān saḥ api līlā alasaḥ bālaḥ nanarta ārti haraḥ prabhuḥ saha eva nanṛtuḥ ca anve saha tena gaṇeśvarāḥ trailokyam akhilam tatra nanarta īśa ājñayā kṣaṇam nāgāḥ ca nanṛtuḥ sarve devāḥ sa indra purogamāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ gaṇapāḥ skandam mumoda ambā ca mātaraḥ sasṛjuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi jaguḥ gandharva kinnarāḥ nṛtya amṛtam tadā pītvā pārvatī parameśvarau ava patuḥ tadā tṛptim nandinā ca gaṇeśvarāḥ tatas sa nandī saha ṣaṇmukhena tathā ca sārdham girirājaputryā viveśa divyam bhavanam bhavaḥ api yathām budaḥ anya ambudam ambuda ābhaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mahādevam kiṃcid udvigna cetasaḥ pāpāḥ hi anye abhāgyāḥ ca iti ca apare bhāgyavantaḥ ca daitya indrāḥ iti ca anye sura īśvarāḥ pūjā phalam imam teṣām iti anye na iti ca apare etasmin antare teṣām śrutvā śabdān anekaśas kumbhodaraḥ mahā tejāḥ daṇḍena atāḍayat surān dudruvuḥ te bhaya āviṣṭāḥ devāḥ hāhā iti vādinaḥ patan munayaḥ ca anye devāḥ ca dharaṇī tale dṛṣṭvā api devadeveśam devānām ca asura dviṣām abhāgyāt na samāptam tu kāryam iti apare dvijāḥ procuḥ namaḥ śivāya iti pūjya ca alpataram hṛdi tatas kapardi nandīśaḥ mahādeva apriyaḥ muniḥ śūlī mālī tathā hālī kuṇḍalī valayī gadī vṛṣam āruhya su śvetam yayau tasya ājñayā tadā tatas vai nandinam dṛṣṭvā gaṇaḥ kumbhodaraḥ api saḥ nandī bhāti mahā tejāḥ vṛṣa pṛṣṭe vṛṣadhvajaḥ sa gaṇaḥ gaṇa senā nīḥ megha pṛṣṭhe yathā bhavaḥ daśa yojana vistīrṇam muktā jālaiḥ alaṅkṛtam sita ātapatram śailādeḥ ākāśam iva bhāti tat tatra antar baddha mālā sā muktāphala mayā śubhā gaṅgā ākāśāt nipatitā bhāti mūrdhani vibhoḥ yathā atha dṛṣṭvā gaṇādhyakṣam deva dundubhayaḥ śubhāḥ niyogāt vajriṇaḥ sarve vineduḥ muni puṃgavāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca gaṇeśānam vāgbhiḥ iṣṭa pradam śubham yathā devāḥ bhavam dṛṣṭvā prīti kaṇṭa kita tvacaḥ niyogāt vajriṇaḥ mūrdhani puṣpa varṣam ca khecarāḥ vṛṣṭyā tuṣṭaḥ tadā reje tuṣṭyā puṣṭyā yathārthayā nandī bhavaḥ cāndrayā tu snātayā gandha vāriṇā puṣpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ tatra bhāti pṛṣṭham vṛṣasya tat saṃkīrṇam tu divaḥ pṛṣṭham nakṣatraiḥ iva suvratāḥ kusumaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ nandī vṛṣa pṛṣṭhe rarāja saḥ divaḥ pṛṣṭhe yathā candraḥ nakṣatraiḥ iva suvratāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā nandinam devāḥ sa indra upendrāḥ tathāvidham tu stuvuḥ gaṇapa īśānam devadevam iva aparam ūcuḥ kūṣmāṇḍa gaṇa nāthāya yoginām pataye namaḥ sarva dāya śaraṇyāya sarvajñāya ārti hāriṇe vajriṇe vajradaṃṣṭrāya vajri vajra nivāriṇe vajra alaṅkṛta dehāya vajriṇā ārādhitāya te raktānām bhava pāda abje rudra loka pradāyine namaḥ senā adhipataye rudrāṇām pateya namaḥ bhūtānām bhuvane śānām pataye pāpa hāriṇe namaḥ śivāya saumyāya rudra bhaktāya te namaḥ uvacā tatas prītaḥ gaṇādhyakṣaḥ prāha ratham ca sārathim śambhoḥ kārmukam śaram uttamam atha te brahmaṇā sārdham tathā vai viśvakarmaṇā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge pura dāhe nandikeśvaravākyam nāma ekasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca rathāṅgam dakṣiṇam sūryaḥ vāma aṅgam somaḥ eva ca dakṣiṇam dvādaśa aram hi ṣoḍaśa aram tathā uttaram teṣu vipra indrāḥ ca ādityāḥ dvādaśa eva tu śaśinaḥ ṣoḍaśa areṣu kalāḥ vāmasya suvratāḥ ṛkṣāṇi ca tadā tasya vamasya eva tu bhūṣaṇam nemyaḥ ṣaṣ ṛtavaḥ ca eva tayoḥ vai vipra puṃgavāḥ puṣkaram ca antarikṣam vai rathanīḍaḥ ca mandaraḥ adhiṣṭhānam mahā meruḥ āśrayāḥ kesara acalāḥ muhūrtāḥ bandhurāḥ tasya śamyāḥ ca eva kalāḥ smṛtāḥ tasya kāṣṭhāḥ smṛtāḥ ghoṇā ca akṣadaṇḍā kṣaṇāḥ ca vai nimeṣāḥ ca anukarṣāḥ ca īṣā ca asya lavāḥ smṛtāḥ dharmaḥ virāgaḥ daṇḍaḥ usya daṇḍa āśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ dakṣiṇāḥ saṃdhayaḥ tasya lohāḥ pañcāśat agnayaḥ īṣā daṇḍaḥ tathā avyaktam buddhiḥ tasya eva naḍvalaḥ koṇaḥ tathā hi ahaṅkāraḥ bhūtāni ca balam smṛtam indriyāṇi ca tasya eva bhūṣaṇāni samantataḥ ca gatiḥ asya eva vedāḥ tasya hayāḥ smṛtāḥ padāni bhūṣaṇāni eva ṣaḍaṅgāni upabhūṣaṇam purāṇa nyāya mīmāṃsā dharma śāstrāṇi suvratāḥ bāla āśrayāḥ paṭāḥ ca eva sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutāḥ mantrāḥ ghaṇṭāḥ smṛtāḥ teṣām varṇāḥ pādāḥ tathā āśramāḥ diśaḥ pādāḥ rathasya asya tathā ca upadiśaḥ ca ha puṣkara ādyāḥ patākāḥ ca sauvarṇāḥ ratna bhūṣitāḥ samudrāḥ tasya catvāraḥ ratha kaṃbalikāḥ smṛtāḥ gaṅgā ādyāḥ saritaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ cāmara āsakta hasta agrāḥ sarvāḥ strī rūpa śobhitāḥ tatra tatra kṛta sthānāḥ śobhayāñcakrire ratham māvaha ādyāḥ tathā sapta sopānam haimam uttamam sārathiḥ bhagavān brahmā deva abhīṣu dharāḥ smṛtāḥ viṣamaḥ ca tadā abāhyaḥ mānasa adriḥ su śobhanaḥ nāsāḥ samantataḥ tasya sarve eva acalāḥ smṛtāḥ talāḥ kapotāḥ kāpotāḥ sarve tala nivāsinaḥ meruḥ eva mahā chatram mandaraḥ pārśva ḍiṇḍimaḥ śaila indraḥ kārmukam ca eva jyāḥ bhuñjaga adhipaḥ svayam kaṇṭā sarasvatī devī dhanuṣaḥ śruti rūpiṇī iṣuḥ viṣṇuḥ mahā tejāḥ śalyam somaḥ śarasya ca kālāgniḥ tad śarasya eva sākṣāt tīkṣṇaḥ su dāruṇaḥ anīkam viṣa saṃbhūtam vāyavaḥ vājakāḥ smṛtāḥ evam kṛtvā ratham divyam kārmukam ca śaram tathā sārathim jagantām ca eva brahmānam prabhum īśvaram āruroha ratham divyam raṇa maṇḍana dhṛk bhavaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamānaḥ ca vandyamānaḥ ca vandibhiḥ upanṛtyaḥ ca apsarasām gaṇaiḥ nṛtya viśāradaiḥ śirobhiḥ patitāḥ bhūmīm turagāḥ veda saṃbhavāḥ atha adhastāt rathasya asya bhagavān dharaṇīdharaḥ vṛṣa indra rūpī ca utthāpya sthāpayāmāsa vai kṣaṇam kṣaṇa antare vṛṣa indraḥ api jānubhyām agamat dharām tatas uśvān codayāmāsa manaḥ māruta raṃhasaḥ purāṇi uddiśya kha sthāni dānavānām tarasviṇām atha āha bhagavān rudraḥ devān ālokya śaṅkaraḥ paśūnām ādhipatyam me dattam hanmi tatas asurān pṛthak paśu tvam devānām tathā anyeṣām sura uttamāḥ iti śrutvā vacaḥ sarvam devadevasya dhīmataḥ agaman sarve paśu tvam prati śaṅkitāḥ teṣām bhāvam tatas jñātvā devaḥ tān idam abravīt śrūyatām paśu bhāvasya vimokṣaḥ kriyatām ca saḥ paśu tvāt iti satyam ca pratijñātam samāhitāḥ ye ca api anye cariṣyanti vratam pāśupatam mama mokṣyanti te na saṃdehaḥ puśu tvāt sura sattamāḥ naiṣṭhikam dvādaśa abdam vā tad ardham varṣaka trayam śuśrūṣām kārayet yaḥ tu sa paśu tvāt vimucyate tasmāt vai paśavaḥ sarve deva asura narāḥ prabhoḥ rudraḥ paśupatiḥ ca eva paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ tat kṛtvā na ca pāpīyān iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ tatas vināyakaḥ sākṣāt bālaḥ abāla parākramaḥ apūjitaḥ tadā devaiḥ prāha devān nivārayan śrī vināyakaḥ uvāca mām apūjya jagati asmin bhakṣya bhojya ādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ kaḥ pumān siddhim āpnoti devaḥ vā dānavaḥ api vā tatas tasmin kṣaṇāt eva deva kārye sura īśvarāḥ vighnam kariṣye deveśa katham karttum samudyatāḥ tatas sa indrāḥ surāḥ sarve bhītāḥ saṃpūjya tam prabhum bruvan te gaṇeśānam nirvighnam ca astu naḥ sadā āliṅgya ca āghrāya sutam tadānīm apūjayat sarva sura indra mukhyaḥ saṃpūjya pūjyam saha deva saṃghaiḥ vināyakam nāyakam īśvarāṇām tam devadevam sura siddha saṃghāḥ maheśvaram bhūta gaṇāḥ ca sarve gaṇeśvarāḥ nandi mukhāḥ tadānīm sva vāhanaiḥ anvayuḥ īśam īśāḥ agre surāṇām ca gaṇa īśvarāṇām tadā atha nandī girirāja kalpam mānam āruhya puram prahartum jagāma mṛtyum bhagavān iva īśaḥ yāntam tadānīm tu śilāda putram āruhya nāga indra vṛṣa aśva varyān devāḥ tadānīm gaṇapāḥ ca sarve gaṇāḥ yayuḥ sva āyudha cihna hastāḥ sura asura īśam sahasraraśmiḥ bhagavān su tīkṣṇaḥ rarāja madhye bhagavān surāṇām vivāhanaḥ vārija pattra varṇaḥ yathā sumeroḥ sikhara adhirūḍhaḥ sahasraraśmiḥ bhagavān su tīkṣṇaḥ sahasranetraḥ prathamaḥ surāṇām gaja indram āruhya ca dakṣiṇe asya samantataḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ iṣṭa dam te jaya iti śakram vara puṣpa vṛṣṭyā tadā hi ahalyā upapatim sureśam jagatpatim diviṣṭhāḥ apām patiḥ tathā īśānaḥ bhavam ca anusamāgatāḥ mahā indram samāruhya roma jaiḥ ca samāvṛtaḥ mahākālaḥ mahā tejāḥ mahādevaḥ iva aparaḥ vāyavyām sa gaṇaiḥ sa arvam sevāñcakre rathasya tu ṣaṇmukhaḥ api saha siddha cāraṇaiḥ senayā ca girirāja saṃnibhaḥ deva nātha gaṇa vṛnda saṃvṛtaḥ vāraṇena ca tathā agni sambhavaḥ vighnam gaṇeśaḥ upi asura īśvarāṇām kṛtvā surāṇām bhagavant avighnam vighna īśvaraḥ vighna gaṇaiḥ ca sārdham tam deśam īśāna padam jagāma kālī tadā kālaniśā prakāśam śūlam kapāla ābharaṇā kareṇa prakaṃpayantī ca tadā suredrān mahā asura asṛj madhu pāna mattā matta ibha gāmī mada lola netrā mattaiḥ piśācaiḥ ca gaṇaiḥ ca mattaiḥ matta ibha carma ambara voṣṭita aṅgā yayau purastāt ca gaṇeśvarasya tām siddha gandharva piśāca yakṣa vidyādhara ahi indra sura indra mukhyāḥ mātaraḥ sura vari sūdanāḥ sādaram sura gaṇaiḥ surūjitāḥ durga ārūḍha mṛga adhipā duratigā dos daṇḍa vṛndaiḥ śivā bibhrāṇā aṅkuśa śula pāśa paraśum cakra asi śaṅkha āyudham tam devam īśam tripuram nihantum tadā tu deva indra ravi prakāśāḥ gajaiḥ hayaiḥ siṃha varaiḥ rathaiḥ ca vṛṣaiḥ yayuḥ te gaṇa rāja mukhyāḥ ca phaālaiḥ musalaiḥ bhuśuṃbhuśuṇḍaiḥ girīndra kūṭaiḥ giri sannibhāḥ te yayuḥ purastāt hi maheśvarasya sura īśvarāḥ bhūta gaṇa īśvarāḥ ca tathā indra padmodbhava viṣṇu mukhyāḥ surāḥ gaṇa īśāḥ ca gaṇeśam īśam jaya iti vāgbhiḥ bhagavantam ūcuḥ kirīṭa datta añjalayaḥ samantāt nanṛtuḥ munayaḥ sarve daṇḍa hastāḥ jaṭā dharāḥ vavṛṣuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ gaṇa īśvaraiḥ deva gaṇaiḥ ca bhṛṅgī saha āvṛtaḥ sarva gaṇa indra varyaḥ jagāma yogī tripuram nihantum vimānam āruhya yathā mahā indraḥ mahākeśaḥ vigata vāsāḥ ca mahākeśaḥ mahājvaraḥ sūryavācaḥ ca sūryapeṣaṇakaḥ tathā sūryākṣaḥ sūri nāmā ca suraḥ suṃdaraḥ eva ca prakṛdaḥ kakudantaḥ ca kaṃpanaḥ ca prakaṃpanaḥ śatākṣaḥ ca eva pañcākṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ mahodaraḥ yamajihvaḥ śatāśvaḥ ca kaṇṭhanaḥ kaṇṭhapūjanaḥ dviśikhaḥ triśikhaḥ ca eva tathā pañcaśikhaḥ dvijāḥ muṇḍa ūrdhva muṇḍaḥ dīrghaḥ ca piśācāsyaḥ pinākadhṛk pippalāyatanaḥ ca eva tathā hi aṅgārakāśanaḥ śithilaḥ śithilāsyaḥ ca akṣapādaḥ hi ajaḥ kujaḥ ityādyāḥ parivārya īśam lakṣya lakṣaṇa varjitāḥ vṛndaśas tam samāvṛtya jagmuḥ somam gaṇaiḥ vṛtāḥ sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi rudrāṇām ūrdhvaretasām samāvṛtya mahādevam devadevam maheśvaram dagdhum puratrayam jagmuḥ koṭi koṭi gaṇaiḥ vṛtāḥ trayastriṃśat surāḥ ca eva trayaḥ ca triśatāḥ tathā mātaraḥ sarva lokānām gaṇānām ca eva mātaraḥ bhūtānām mātaraḥ ca eva jagmuḥ devasya pṛṣṭhatas bhāti madhye gaṇānām ca ratha madhye gaṇeśvaraḥ nabhasi amala nakṣatre tārā madhye iva uḍurāj rarāja devī devasya girijā pārśva saṃsthitā śubhāvatī tadā devī pārśva saṃsthā vibhāti sā cāmara āsakta hasta agrā sā hema ambuja varṇakā bhāti indradhanuṣā ākāśam meruṇā ca yathā jagat hiraṇya dhanuṣā saumyam vapuḥ śambhoḥ śaśi dyuti sita ātapatram ratna aṃśu miśritam parameṣṭhinaḥ yathā udaye śaśāṅkasya bhāti akhaṇḍam hi maṇḍalam sa dukūlā śive raktā laṃbitā bhāti mālikā chattra antā ratna jā ākāśāt patantī iva saridvarā dagdhum samarthaḥ manasā kṣaṇena carācaram sarvam idam triśūlī kim atra dagdhum tripuram pinākī svayam gataḥ ca atra gaṇaiḥ ca sārdham rathena kim ca iṣu vareṇa tasya gaṇaiḥ ca kim deva gaṇaiḥ ca śaṃbhoḥ manvāma nūnam bhagavant pinākī līlā artham etat sakalam pravartum vyavasthitaḥ ca iti tathā anyathā ced āḍambareṇa asya phalam kim anyat gaṇaiḥ gaṇeśaḥ tu rarāja devyā jagat rathaḥ meruḥ iva aṣṭa śṛṅgaiḥ atha nirikṣya sureśvaram īśvaram sa gaṇam adrisutā sahitam tadā atha sajyam dhanuḥ kṛtvā śarvaḥ saṃdhāya tam śaram yuktvā pāśupata astreṇa tripuram samacintayat babhūva tumulaḥ harṣaḥ devatānām mahātmanām tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve siddhāḥ ca parama ṛpayaḥ jaya iti vācaḥ mumucuḥ saṃstuvantaḥ aṣṭamūrtinam puṣya yogaḥ upi saṃprāpte līlā vaśam umāpatim sthāne tava mahādeva ceṣṭeyam parameśvara pūrvadevāḥ ca devāḥ ca samāḥ te yatas prabho tathā api devāḥ dharmiṣṭhāḥ pūrvadevāḥ ca pāpinaḥ iṣuṇā bhūta saṃghaiḥ ca viṣṇunā ca mayā prabho dagdhum arhasi śīghram tvam trīṇi etāni purāṇi vai puratrayam virūpākṣaḥ tad kṣaṇāt bhasma vai kṛtam somaḥ ca bhagavant viṣṇuḥ kālāgniḥ vāyuḥ eva ca mad hita artham deveśa śaram moktum iha arhasi mumoca bāṇam vipra indrāḥ vyākṛṣya ākarṇam īśvaraḥ tad kṣaṇāt tripuram dagdhvā tripura anta karaḥ śaraḥ devadevam samāsādya namaskṛtvā vyavasthitaḥ ye pūjayanti tatra api daityāḥ rudram sa bāndhavāḥ gāṇapatyam tadā śaṃbhoḥ yayuḥ pūjā vidheḥ balāt na kiṃcid abruvan devāḥ sa indra upendrāḥ gaṇa īśvarāḥ bhayāt devam nirīkṣya eva devīm himavantaḥ sutām dṛṣṭvā bhītam tadā anīkam devānām deva puṃgavaḥ kim ca iti āha tadā devān praṇemuḥ tam samantataḥ tuṣṭāva hṛdaye brahmā devaiḥ saha samāhitaḥ viṣṇunā ca bhavam devam tripura arātim īśvaram śrī pitāmahaḥ uvāca prasīda jagantām nātha prasīda ānanda da avyaya pañca asya rudra rudrāya pañcāśat koṭi mūrtaye namaḥ śivāya śivatattvāya aghorāya namaḥ namaḥ aghora aṣṭaka tattvāya dvādaśa ātma svarūpiṇe vidyut koṭi pratīkāśam aṣṭa kāśam su śobhanam rūpam āsthāya loke asmin saṃsthitāya śiva ātmane agni varṇāya raudrāya ambikā ardha śarīriṇe dhavala śyāma raktānām mukti dāya amarāya ca jyeṣṭhāya rudra rūpāya somāya vara dāya ca tri lokāya tri devāya vaṣaṭkārāya vai namaḥ aṣṭa kṣetra aṣṭa rūpāya aṣṭa tattvāya te namaḥ pañcadhā pañcadhā ca eva pañca mantra śarīriṇe catuḥṣaṣṭi prakārāya akārāya namaḥ namaḥ dvātriṃśat tatva rūpāya ukārāya namaḥ namaḥ ṣoḍaśa ātma svarūpāya makārāya namaḥ namaḥ aṣṭadhā ātma svarūpāya ardha mātrā ātmane namaḥ oṃkārāya namaḥ tubhyam caturdhā saṃsthitāya ca gagana īśāya devāya svarga īśāya namaḥ namaḥ sapta lokāya pātāla naraka īśāya vai namaḥ aṣṭa kṣetra aṣṭa rūpāya parātparatarāya ca sahasra pāda yuktāya śarvāya parameṣṭhine nava ātma tattva rūpāya nava aṣṭa ātma ātma śaktaye punar aṣṭa prakāśāya tathā aṣṭa aṣṭaka mūrtaye catuḥṣaṣṭi ātma tattvāya punar aṣṭavidhāya te guṇa aṣṭaka vṛtāya eva guṇine nirguṇāya te namaḥ tubhyam śāsvata sthāna vāsine nābhi maṇḍala saṃsthāya hṛdi niḥsvana kāriṇe tasmai eva śivāya śiva rūpiṇe vahni soma arka rūpāya ṣaṭtriṃśat śakti rūpiṇe tri prakāram stitāya eva tretāgni maya rūpiṇe sadāśivāya śāntāya maheśāya pinākine sarvajñāya śaraṇyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ tatpuruṣāya namaḥ astu īśānāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ triṃśat prakāśāya śānta atītāya vai namaḥ ananta īśāya sūkṣmāya uttamāya namaḥ astu te namaḥ trimūrtaye tubhyam śrīkaṇṭhāya śikhaṇḍine ananta āsana saṃsthāya anantāya anta kāriṇe vimalāya viśālāya vimala aṅgāya te namaḥ vimala āsana saṃsthāya vimala artha artha rūpiṇe yoginām hṛdi saṃsthāya sadā nīvāra śūka vat pratyāhārāya te nityam pratyāhāra ratāya te pratyāhāra ratānām ca prati sthāna sthitāya ca dhāraṇāyai namaḥ te dhāraṇa abhiratāya te dhāraṇa abhyāsa yuktānām purastāt saṃsthitāya ca dhyānāya dhyāna rūpāya dhyāna gamyāya te namaḥ samādhāna abhigamyāya samādhānāya te namaḥ samādhāna ratānām tu nirvikalpa artha rūpiṇe kaḥ stotum icchet katham īdṛśam tvām steṣya iha tuṣṭāya śivāya tubhyam ete gaṇāḥ siddha gaṇaiḥ praṇāmam kurvāti deveśa gaṇeśa tubhyam līlā alasena ambikayā kṣaṇena dagdham kila iṣuḥ ca tadā atha muktaḥ kṛtaḥ rathaḥ ca eṣu varaḥ ca śubhram śarasanam te tripura kṣayāya aneka yatnaiḥ ca mayā atha tubhyam na dṛṣṭam phalam na dṛṣṭam sura siddha saṃghaiḥ ca ananta mūrtiḥ katham īdṛśaḥ tvam toṣyam katham īdṛśam tvām stūlāya sūkṣmāya su sūkṣma sūkṣma sūkṣmāya sūkṣma artha vide vidhātre sraṣṭre namaḥ sarva sura asurāṇām bhartre ca hartre jagatām vidhātre netre surāṇām asura īśvarāṇām dātre praśāstre mama sarva śāstre ādi anta śūnyāya ca saṃsthitāya tathā tva śūnyāya ca liṅgine ca aliṅgine liṅga mayāya tubhyam ligāya veda ādi mayāya sākṣāt rudrāya mūrdhāna nikṛntanāya mama ādi devasya ca yajñamūrteḥ mama kartum īśa dṛṣṭvā eva bhūmau karaja agra koṭyā dehi iva devaiḥ saha deva kāryam kariṣyase nirgumīśa dṛṣṭvā eva bhūmau karaja agra koṭyā ekam sthūlam sūkṣmam ekam su sūkṣmam sūrta amūrtam mūrtam ekam hi amūrtam ekam dṛṣṭam vāc mayam ca ekam īśam dhyeyam ca ekam tattvam atra adbhutam te svapne dṛṣṭam yat padārtham hi alakṣyam dṛṣṭam nūnam bhāti manye na ca api tathā api bhaktyā vilapantam īśa pitāmaham mām bhagavant kṣamasva uvāca yaḥ imam śṛṇuyāt dvijottamāḥ bhuvi devam praṇipatya paṭhet śrutvā ca bhaktyā caturānanena stutaḥ hasan śailasutām nirīkṣya stavam tadā prāha mahā anubhāvam mahā bhujaḥ mandara śṛṅga vāsī uvāca harān varaya bhadram te devānām ca yathā īpsitān uvāca tatas praṇamya deveśam bhagavān padmasaṃbhavaḥ kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā prāha idam prīta mānasaḥ śrī pitāmahaḥ uvāca devānām ca eva sarveṣām tvayī sarva artha da īśvara kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā prāha sa ambam tryambakam he vāhana tvam tava īśāna nityam īhe prasīda me sāmarthyam ca sadā mahyam bhavantam voḍhum īśvaram uvāca tayoḥ śrutvā mahādevaḥ vijñaptim parameśvaraḥ sārdham devyāḥ nandinā bhū saṃghaiḥ antardhānam kārayāmāsa śarvaḥ tatas tadā maheśvare gate raṇāt gaṇaiḥ saha sura īśvarāḥ su vismitāḥ bhavam praṇamya pārvatīm yayuḥ ca duḥkha varjitāḥ sva vāhanaiḥ divam tatas sura īśvarāḥ muni īśvarāḥ gaṇa īśvarāḥ ca bhāskarāḥ tripurāreḥ imam puṇyam nirmitam brahmaṇā purā yaḥ paṭhet śrāddha kāle vā daive karmaṇi ca dvijāḥ mānasaiḥ vācikaiḥ kāpaiḥ tathā vai kāyikaiḥ punar sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ su sūkṣmaiḥ ca mahāpātaka saṃbhavaiḥ pātakaiḥ ca dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ upapātaka saṃbhavaiḥ pāpaiḥ ca mucyate jantuḥ śrutvā adhyāyam imam śubham śatravaḥ nāśam āyānti saṃgrāme vijayībhavet iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge tripura dāhe brahmastavaḥ nāma dvisaptitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca gate maheśvare deve dagdhvā ca tripuram kṣaṇāt sadasi āha suredrāṇām bhagavān padmasaṃbhavaḥ uvāca saṃtyajya deva deveśam liṅga mūrti maheśvaram tārakākṣaḥ api ditijaḥ kamalākṣaḥ ca vīryavān vidyunmālī ca daitya īśaḥ anye ca api sa bāndhavāḥ tyaktvā devam mahādevam māyayā ca hareḥ prabhoḥ sarve vinaṣṭāḥ pradhvastāḥ sva puraiḥ pura sambhavaiḥ tasmāt sadā pūjanīyaḥ liṅga mūrtiḥ sadāśivaḥ yāvat pūjā sura īśānām tāvat eva sthitiḥ yatas pūjanīyaḥ śivaḥ nityam śraddhayā deva puṃgavaiḥ tasmāt saṃpūjayet liṅgam yaḥ icchet siddhim ātmanaḥ sarve liṅga arcanāt eva devāḥ daityāḥ ca dānavāḥ yakṣāḥ vidyādharāḥ siddhāḥ rākṣasāḥ piśita aśanāḥ pitaraḥ munayaḥ ca api piśācāḥ kinnara ādayaḥ arcayitvā liṅga mūrti saṃsiddhāḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ tasmāt liṅgam yajet nityam yena kena api vā surāḥ paśu tvam ca parityajya kṛtvā pāśupatam tatas pūjanīyaḥ mahādevaḥ liṅga mūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ viśodhya ca eva bhūtāni pañcabhiḥ praṇavaiḥ samam prāṇāyāmaiḥ samāyuktaiḥ pañcabhiḥ sura puṃgavāḥ caturbhiḥ praṇavaiḥ ca eva prāṇāyāma parāyaṇaiḥ tribhiḥ ca praṇavaiḥ devāḥ prāṇāyāmaiḥ tathāvidhaiḥ dvidhā nyasya tathā uṅkāram prāṇāyāma parāyaṇaḥ tatas coṅkāram uccārya prāṇa apānau niyamya ca jñāna amṛtena sarva aṅgāni āpūrya praṇavena ca guṇatrayam caturdhā ākhyam ahaṅkāram ca suvratāḥ tanmātrāṇi ca bhūtāni tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca karmendriyāṇi saṃśodhya puruṣam yugalam tathā cit ātmānam tanum kṛtvā ca agniḥ bhasma iti saṃspṛśet triyāyuṣam tri saṃdhyam ca dhūlayet bhasitena yaḥ bhavena pāśa mokṣa artham kathitam deva sattamāḥ evam pāśupatam kṛtvā saṃpūjya parameśvaram liṅge purā mayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā ca mahātmanā paśavaḥ na eva jāyante varṣa mātreṇa devatāḥ asmābhiḥ sarva kāryāṇām devam abhyarcya yatnatas pratijñā mama viṣṇoḥ ca divyā eṣā sura sattamāḥ munīnām ca na saṃdehaḥ tasmāt saṃpūjayet śivam sā hāniḥ tat mahat chidram saḥ mohaḥ sā ca mūka tā yat kṣaṇam vā muhūrtam vā śivam ekam na cintayet bhavanāni manojñāni divyam ābharaṇam striyaḥ dhanam vā tuṣṭi paryantam śiva pūjā vidheḥ phalam ye vāñchanti mahā bhogān rājyam ca tridaśālaye teḥ acayantu sadā kālam liṅga mūrtim maheśvaram yajet ekam virūpākṣam na pāpaiḥ sa pralipyate śailam liṅgam madīyam hi sarva deva namaskṛtam tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ devadevam tryambakam tadā prabhṛti śakra ādyāḥ pūjayāmāsuḥ īśvaram sākṣāt pāśupatam kṛtvā bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge brahmaproktaliṅgārcanavidhiḥ nāma trisaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca liṅgāni kalpayitvā evam sva adhikāra anurūpatas teṣām niyogāt brahmanaḥ prabhoḥ indranīla mayam liṅgam viṣṇunā pūjitam sadā padmarāga mayam śakraḥ haimam viśravasaḥ sutaḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā raupyam vasavaḥ kāntikam śubham ārakūṭa mayam vāyuḥ aśvinaḥ pārthivam sadā sphaāṭikam varuṇaḥ rājā ādityāḥ tāmra nirmitam mauktikam somarāj dhīmān tathā liṅgam anuttamam ananta ādyāḥ mahā nāgāḥ pravālaka mayam śubham daitya hyoya mayam ligam rākṣasāḥ ca mahātmanaḥ trailohikam guhyakāḥ ca sarva loha mayam gaṇāḥ cāmuṇḍā saikatam sākṣāt mātaraḥ ca dvijottamāḥ dāru jam nairṛtiḥ bhaktyā yamaḥ mārakatam śubham nīla ādyāḥ ca tathā rudrāḥ śuddham bhasma mayam śubham lakṣmīvṛkṣa mayam lakṣmīḥ guhaḥ vai gomaya ātmakam munayaḥ muni sārdūlāḥ kuśa agra mayam uttamam vāmā ādyāḥ puṣpa liṅgam tu gandha liṅgam manonmanī ugrā piṣṭa mayam sarve mantrāḥ hi ājya mayam śubham vedāḥ sarve dadhi mayam piśācāḥ sīsa nirmitam ṣaḍvidham liṅgam iti āhuḥ dravyāṇām ca prabhedataḥ teṣām bhedāḥ catur yukta catvāriṃśat iti smṛtāḥ tṛtīyam dhātu jam liṅgam aṣṭadhā parameṣṭhinaḥ turīyam dāru jam liṅgam tat tu ṣoḍaśadhā ucyate mṛd mayam pañcamam liṅgam dvidhā bhinnam dvijottamāḥ ṣaṣṭham tu kṣaṇikam liṅgam saptadhā parikīrtitam ratna jam liṅgam śaila jam sarva siddhi dam dhātujam dhana dam sākṣāt dārujam bhoga siddhi dam bahudhā liṅga bhejāḥ ca nava ca eva samāsatas mūle brahmā tathā madhye viṣṇuḥ tribhuvana īśvaraḥ rudra upari mahādevaḥ pramava ākhyaḥ sadāśivaḥ liṅga vediḥ mahādevī triguṇā tri mayā ambikā śaila jam ratna jam vā api dhātu jam vā api dāru jam mṛd mayam kṣaṇikam vā api bhaktyā sthāpya phalam śubham sura idra ambhojagarbha agni yama ambupa dhaneśvaraiḥ stūyamānaḥ su puṇya ātmā deva dundubhi niḥsvanaiḥ liṅga sthāpana sat mārga nihita su āyata asinā āśu brahmāṇḍam udbhidya nirgacchan nirviśaṅkayā śaila jam ratna jam vā api dhātu jam vā api dāru jam mṛd mayam kṣaṇikam tyaktvā sthāpayet sakalam vapuḥ vidhinā ca eva kṛtvā tu skanda umā sahitam śubham liṅgam yaḥ sthāpayet naraḥ nṝṇām tanum samāsthāya sthitaḥ rudraḥ na saṃśayaḥ darśanāt sparśanāt tasya labhante nirvṛtim narāḥ sarveṣām eva martyānām vibhoḥ divyam vapuḥ śubham sakalam bhāvanā yogyam yoginām eva niṣkalam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivaliṅgabhedasaṃsthāpanādivarṇanam nāma catuḥsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ vaktum arhasi ca naḥ yathā pūrvam yathā śrutam uvāca parama artha vidaḥ kecid ūcuḥ praṇava rūpiṇam vijñānam iti vipra indrāḥ śrutvā śrutiśirasi ajam śabda ādi viṣayam jñānam jñānam iti abhidhīyate yat jñānam nirmalam śuddham nirvikalpam nirāśrayam guru prakāśakam jñānam iti anye munayaḥ dvijāḥ dyauḥ mūrdhā tu vibhoḥ tasya kham nābhiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ soma sūrya agnayaḥ netre diśaḥ śrotram mahātmanaḥ caraṇau ca eva pātālam samudraḥ tasya ca ambaram devāḥ tasya bhujāḥ sarve nakṣatrāṇi ca bhūṣaṇam vattrāt vai brāhmaṇāḥ sarve brahmā ca bhagavān prabhuḥ indra upendrau bhujābhyām tu kṣatriyāḥ ca mahātmanaḥ vaiśyāḥ ca ūru pradeśāt tu śūdrāḥ pādāt pinākinaḥ puṣkarāvartaka ādyāḥ tu keśāḥ tasya prakīrtitāḥ vāyavaḥ ghrāṇa jāḥ tasya gatiḥ śrautam smṛtiḥ tathā puṃsām tu puruṣaḥ śrīmān jñāna gamyaḥ na ca anyathā dhyāna yajñāt paraḥ na asti dhyānam jñānasya sādhanam yadā samarase niṣṭhaḥ yogī dhyānena paśyati dhyāna yajña ratasya asya tadā saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ na asti vijñāninām śaucam prāyaścitta ādi codanā viśuddhāḥ vidyayā sarve brahma vidyā vidaḥ janāḥ na asti kriyā ca lokeṣu sukham duḥkham vicārataḥ dharma adharmau japaḥ homaḥ dhyāninām saṃnidhiḥ sadā parānanda ātmakam liṅgam viśuddham śivam akṣaram niṣkalam sarva gam jñeyam yoginām hṛdi saṃsthitam liṅgam tu dvividham prāhuḥ bāhyam ābhyantaram dvijāḥ bāhyam sthūlam muni śreṣṭhāḥ sūkṣmam ābhyantaram dvijāḥ karma yajña ratāḥ sthūlāḥ sthūla liṅga arcane ratāḥ asatām bhāvanā arthāya na anyathā sthūla vigrahaḥ ādhyātmikam ca yat liṅgam pratyakṣam yasya no bhavet jñāninām sūkṣmam amalam bhavet pratyakṣam avyayam yatā sthūlam ayuktānām mṛd kāṣṭhāt yauḥ prakalpitam niṣkalaḥ sakalaḥ ca iti sarvam śiva mayam tatas vyom ekam api dṛṣṭam hi śarāvam prati suvratāḥ pṛthaktvam ca apṛthaktvam ca śaṃkarasya iti ca apare ekaḥ api bahudhā dṛṣṭaḥ jalādhāreṣu suvratāḥ jantavaḥ divi bhūmā ca sarve vai pāñcabhautikāḥ tathā api bahulā dṛṣṭā jāti vyakti vibhedataḥ bhedaḥ janānām loke ismin pratibhāsaḥ vicārāt duḥkhī ca bhegam duḥkham ca na anubhūtam vicārāt hṛdi saṃsāriṇām sākṣāt sakalaḥ parameśvaraḥ yoginām niṣkalaḥ devaḥ jñāninām ca jagat mayaḥ tṛtīyam sakalam ca eva na anyathā iti dvijottamāḥ sakalam munayaḥ kecid sadā saṃsāra vartinaḥ evam abhyarcayanti eva sa dārāḥ sa suta narāḥ yathā śivaḥ tathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ daśa are dvādaśa are ca ṣoḍaśa are tris asrake sa sva icchayā śivaḥ sākṣāt devyā sārdham sthitaḥ prabhuḥ saṃtāraṇa artham ca śivaḥ sat asat vyakti varjitaḥ ūcuḥ tathā tam ca śivam tathā anye saṃsāriṇam veda vidaḥ vadanti bhaktyā ca yogena śubhena yuktāḥ viprāḥ sadā dharma ratāḥ viśiṣṭāḥ te yānti ca enam na ca yoginaḥ anye tayā ca devyā puruṣam purāṇam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivādvaitakathanam nāma pañcasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca pratiṣṭhāyāḥ phalam sarvam sarva loka hitāya vai skanda umā sahitam devam āsīnam parama āsane kṛtvā bhakyā pratiṣṭhāpya sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt skanda umā sahitam devam saṃpūjya vidhinā sakṛt sūrya koṭi pratikāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ rudra kanyā samākīrṇaiḥ gaya nāṭya samanvitaiḥ śiva vat krīḍate yogī yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ aumam kaumāram aiśānam vaiṣṇavam brāhmam eva ca prājāpatyam mahā tejāḥ janalokam mahar tathā caidra tva kṛ varṣa ayuta punar merum āsādya devānām bhavaneṣu pramodate eka pādam catur bāhum tri netram śūla saṃyutam sṛṣṭvā sthitam harīm vāme dakṣiṇe caturānanam koṭiḥ sarva aṅga su prabham pañcaviṃśatikam sākṣāt puruṣam hṛdayāt tathā prakṛtim vāmatas ca eva buddhim vai buddhi deśāt ahaṅkāram ahaṅkārāt tanmātrāṇi tu tatra vai indriyāṇi indriyāt eva līlayā parameśvaram pṛthivīm pāda mūlāt tu guhya deśāt jakam tathā nābi deśāt tathā vahnim hṛdayāt bhāskaram tathā kaṇṭhāt somam tathā ātmānam bhrū madhyāt mastakāt divam sṛṣṭa evam saṃsthitam sākṣāt jagant sarvam carācaram sarvajñam sarva gam devam kṛtvā vidyā vidhānāt pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyam śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt tri pādam sapta hastam ca catur śṛṅgam dvi śīrṣakam kṛtvā yajñeśam īśānam viṣṇu loke mahīyate tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān kalpa lakṣam sukhī naraḥ vṛṣa ārūḍham tu yaḥ kuryāt somam soma ardha bhūṣaṇam hayamedha ayutam kṛtvā yat puṇyam tat ā avāpya saḥ kāñcanena kiṅkiṇī jāla mālinā nandinā sahitam devam sābam sarva gaṇaiḥ vṛtam sūrya maṇḍala saṃkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ vṛṣa saṃyutaiḥ apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇaiḥ deva dānava durlabhaiḥ nṛtya adbhiḥ apsaraḥ saṃghaiḥ sarvatas sarva śaubhitaiḥ gatvā śiva puram divyam gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt nṛtyantam devadeveśam śailajā sahitam prabhum sahasra bāhum sarvajñam catur bāhum atha api vā bhṛgu ādyaiḥ bhūta saṃghaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam parameśvaram śailajā sahitam sākṣāt vṛṣabhadhvajam īśvaram kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yat phalam tat vadāmi aham tat phalam koṭi guṇitam labdhvā yāti śivam padam tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān yāvat ā bhūtasaṃplavam sṛṣṭi antare punar prāpte mānavam padam āpnuyāt kapāla hastam deveśam kṛṣṇa kuñcita mūrdhajam kṛtvā bhakyā pratiṣṭhāpya śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt ibha indra dārakam devam sa ambam siddhārtha dam prabhum su dhūmra varṇam rakta akṣam tri netram candra bhūṣaṇam kākapakṣa dharam mūrdhnā nāga ṭaṅka dharam haram siṃha ajina uttarīyam ca mṛga carma ambaram prabhum tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭram gadā hastam kapāla udyata pāṇim huṃ phaṭkāre mahā śabda śabdita akhila diṅmukham puṇḍarīka ajinam dorbhyām bibhrantam kambukam tathā hasantam ca nadantam ca pibantam kṛṣṇa sāgaram nṛtyantam bhūta saṃghaiḥ ca gaṇa saṃghaiḥ tu alaṅkṛtam kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yathā vibhava vistaram tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam strī puṃs bhāvena saṃsthānam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śiva loke mahīyate tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān aṇima ādi guṇaiḥ yutaḥ mucyate yaḥ kuryāt devadeveśam sarvajñam lakuli īśvaram hi śiṣya praśiṣyaiḥ ca vyākhyāna udyata pāṇim kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śiva lokam sa gacchati bhuktvā tu vipulān tatra bhogān yuga śatam naraḥ pūrvadeva amarāṇām ca yat sthānam sakala īpsitam tripuṇḍra dhāriṇaḥ teṣām śiraḥ mālā dharasya ca brahmaṇaḥ keśakena ekam upavītam ca bibhrataḥ viṣṇoḥ kalevaram ca eva bibhrataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya mucyate bhava sāgarāt om namaḥ nīlakaṇṭhāya iti puṇya akṣara aṣṭakam mantram āha sakṛt vā yaḥ pātakaiḥ sa vimucyate mantreṇa anenam gandha ādyaiḥ bhaktyā vitta anusāratas saṃpūjya devadeveśam śiva loke mahīyate kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya dvidhā bhūtam jalaṃdharam prayāti śiva sāyujyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā sudarśana pradam devam sākṣāt pūrva ukta lakṣaṇam kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śiva loke mahīyate tiṣṭhataḥ utha nikumbhasya pṛṣṭhatas caraṇa ambujam vāmetaram su vinyasya vāme ca āliṅgya ca adrijām śūla agre kūrparam sthāpya kiṅkiṇī kṛta pannagam saṃprekṣya ca andhakam pārśve kṛta añjali puṭam sthitam rūpam kṛtvā yathānyāyam śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt yaḥ kuryāt devadeveśam tripurāntakam īśvaram dhanus bāṇa samāyuktam sa umam soma ardha bhūṣaṇam tad ākāra tayā saḥ api gatvā śiva puram sukhī krīḍate na atra saṃdehaḥ dvitīyaḥ iva śaṅkaraḥ gaṅgā dharam sukha āsīnam candraśekharam eva ca gaṅgayā sahitam ca eva vāma utsaṅga iṃbikā anvitam vināyakam tathā skandam jyeṣṭham durgām su śobhanām bhāskaram ca tathā somam brahmāṇīm ca maheśvarīm kaumārīm vaiṣṇavaīm devaīm vārāhīm vāradām tathā indrāṇīm ca eva cāmuṇḍām vīrabhadra samanvitām āpnuyāt liṅga mūrtim mahā jvāla mālā saṃvṛtam avyayam vyomni kuryāt tathā liṅgam brahmāṇam haṃsa rūpiṇam viṣṇum varāha rūpeṇa liṅgasya adhas tu adhomukham brahmāṇam dakṣiṇe tasya kṛta añjali puṭam sthitam kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt kṣetra saṃrakṣam devam tathā pāśupatam prabhum kṛtvā bhaktyā yathānyāyam śiva loke mahīyate iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivamūrtipratiṣṭhāphalakathanam nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ liṅga pratiṣṭhā puṇyam ca liṅga sthāpanam eva ca liṅgānām ca eva bhedāḥ ca śrutam te mukhāt iha mṛd ādi ratna paryantaiḥ dravyaiḥ kṛtvā śiva ālayam uvāca tathā api bhaktāḥ parameśvarasya kṛtvā iṣṭa loṣṭaiḥ api rudra lokam bālyāt tu loṣṭena ca kṛtvā mṛdā api vā pāṃsubhiḥ ādidevam ca tādṛgvidham asya śaṃbhoḥ saṃpūjya rudra tvam avāpnuvanti kesaram nāgaram vā api drāvīḍam vā tathā aparam kṛtvā rudra ālayam bhaktyā śiva loke mahīyate kailāsa ākhyam ca yaḥ kuryāt prāsādam parameṣṭhinaḥ kailāsa śikhara ākāraiḥ vimānaiḥ modate sukhī mandaram vā prakurvīta śivāya vidhi pūrvakam mandara adri pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ viśvatomukhaiḥ apsaras gaṇa saṃkīrṇaiḥ deva dānava durlabhaiḥ gatvā śiva puram ramyam bhuktvā bhogān yathā īpsitān jñāna yogam samāsādya gāṇapatyam labhet naraḥ yaḥ kuryāt meru nāmānam prāsādam parameṣṭhinaḥ niṣadham nāma yaḥ kuryāt prāsādam bhaktitaḥ sudhīḥ kuryāt vā yaḥ śubham viprāḥ himaśailam anuttamam jñāna yogam samāsādya gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt nīla adri śikhara ākhyam vā prāsādam yaḥ su śobhanam kṛtvā vitta anusāreṇa bhaktyā rudrāya śaṃbhave mahendra śaila nāmānam prāsādam rudra saṃmatam mahendra parvata ākāraiḥ vimānaiḥ vṛṣa saṃyutaiḥ gatvā śiva puram divyam bhuktvā bhogān yathā īpsitān jñānam vicāritam rudraiḥ saṃprāpya muni puṃgavāḥ viṣayān viṣa pat tyaktvā śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt hemnā yaḥ tu prakṛrvīta prāsādam ratna śobhitam dravīḍam nāgaram vā api kesaram vā vidhānāt kūṭam vā maṇḍapam vā api samam vā dīrgham eva ca jīrṇam vā patitam vā api khaṇḍitam sphuṭitam tathā pūrvavat kārayet yaḥ tu dvāra ādyaiḥ su śubham dvijāḥ prasādam maṇḍapam vā api prākāram gopuram tu vā kartuḥ api adhikam puṇyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ vṛtti artham vā prakurvīta naraḥ karma śiva ālaye yaḥ sa yāti na saṃdehaḥ svarga lokam sa bāndhavaḥ tasmāt āyatanam bhaktyā yaḥ kuryāt muni sattamāḥ kāṣṭha iṣṭakā ādibhiḥ martyaḥ śiva loke mahīyate prasāda artha maheśasya prāsāde muni puṃgavāḥ aśaktaḥ ced muni śreṣṭhāḥ prāsādam kartum uttamam sammārjana ādibhiḥ vā api sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt saṃmārjanam tu yaḥ kuryāt mārjanyā mṛdu sūkṣmayā yaḥ kuryāt vastra pūtena gandha gomaya vāriṇā ālepanam yathānyāyam varṣa cāndrāyaṇam labhet ardha krośam śiva kṣetram śiva liṅgāt samantataḥ yaḥ tyajet dustyajān prāṇān śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt svāyaṃbhuvasya mānam hi tathā bāṇasya suvratāḥ svāyaṃbhuve tad ardham syāt syāt ārṣe ca tad ardhakam mānuṣe ca tad ardham syāt kṣetra mānam dvijottamāḥ evam yatīnām āvāse kṣetra mānam dvijottamāḥ rudra avatāre ca ādyam yat śiṣye ca eva praśiṣyake nara avatāre tad ciṣye cat śiṣye ca praśīṣyake śrīparvate mahā puṇye tasya prānte ca vā dvijāḥ tasmin vā yaḥ tyajet prāṇān śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt vārāṇasyām tathā api evam avimukte viśeṣataḥ kedāre ca mahā kṣetre prayāge ca viśeṣataḥ ca yaḥ prāṇān saṃtyajet yāti nirvṛtim prabhāse puṣkare avantyām tathā ca eva amareśvare ca eva mṛtaḥ yāti śiva ātma tām mṛtaḥ jantuḥ na jātu jantu tām vrajet mālake vā tyajet prāṇān tathā vai jambukeśvare śukreśvare vā gokarṇe bhāskareśe guheśvare hiraṇyagarbhe nandīśe sa yāti paramām gatim sa yāti śivatām yogī mānuṣe vā muni śreṣṭhāḥ tathā svāyambhuve api vā svayam bhūte tathā deve na atra kāryā vicāraṇā mahā agnim śiva kṣetre saṃpūjya parameśvaram piṇḍam juhuyāt yaḥ sa yāti parām gatim yāvat tāvat nirāhāraḥ bhūtvā prāmān parityajet śiva kṣetre muni śreṣṭhāḥ śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt chittvā pāda dvayam ca api śiva kṣetre vaset tu yaḥ sa yāti śivatām ca eva na atra kāryā vicāraṇā kṣetrasya darśanam puṇyam praveśaḥ tad śa tad adhikaḥ tasmāt śataguṇam puṇyam sparśanam ca pradakṣiṇam tasmāt śataguṇam puṇyam jala snānam atas param kṣīra snānam tatas viprāḥ śata adhikam anuttamam ghṛta snānena ca anantam śārkare tat śata adhikam śiva kṣetra samīpa sthām nadīm prāpya avagāhya ca tyajet deham vihāya annam śiva loke mahīyate śiva kṣetra samīpa sthāḥ nadyaḥ sarvāḥ su śobhanāḥ ca snātvā teṣu naraḥ bhaktyā tīrtheṣu dvijasattamāḥ brahmahatyā ādibhiḥ pāpaiḥ mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ prātar snātvā muni śreṣṭhāḥ śiva tīrtheṣu mānavaḥ madhyāhne śiva tīrtheṣu snātvā bhaktyā sakṛt naraḥ gaṅgā snāna samam puṇyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ pāpa kañcukam utsṛjya śiva tīrtheṣu mānavaḥ dvijāḥ triṣavaṇam snātvā śiva tīrthe sakṛt naraḥ bhagavat sāyujyam āpnoti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā purā atha sūkaraḥ kaścid śvānam dṛṣṭvā bhayāt pathini prasaṅgāt vāram ekam tu śiva tīrthe avagāhya ca mṛtaḥ svayam dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ gāṇapatyam avāptavān yaḥ prātar devadeveśam śivam liṅga svarūpiṇam madhyāhne ca mahādevam dṛṣṭvā yajña phalam labhet sāyāhne sarva yajñānām phalam prāpya vimucyate mānasaiḥ vācikaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiḥ ca mahattaraiḥ tathā upapātakaiḥ ca eva pāpaiḥ ca eva anupātakaiḥ saṃkrame devam īśānam dṛṣṭvā liṅga ākṛtim prabhum māsena yat kṛtam pāpam tyaktvā yāti śivam padam ayane ca ardha māsena dakṣiṇe ca uttarāyaṇe viṣuve ca eva saṃpūjya prayāti paramām gatim pradakṣiṇā trayam kuryāt yaḥ prāsādam samantataḥ savya apasavya nyāyena mṛdu gatyā śuciḥ naraḥ vācā yaḥ tu śivam nityam saṃrauti parameśvaram saḥ api yāti śivam sthānam prāpya kim punar eva ca kṛtvā maṇḍalakam kṣetram gandha gomaya vāriṇā padmarāga mayaiḥ ca eva sphaāṭikaiḥ ca su śobhanaiḥ bhadran daśa hasta pramāṇataḥ sa karṇikam mahābhāgāḥ mahādeva samīpatas pañcabhiḥ ca tathā ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ ca iṣṭa dam param punar aṣṭābhiḥ īśānam daśa are daśabhiḥ tathā punar bāhye ca daśabhiḥ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca śāli piṣṭa ādibhiḥ vā api padmam ālikhya nirdhanaḥ pūrva uktam akhilam puṇyam labhate na atra śaṃśayaḥ dvādaśa aram tathā ālikhya maṇḍalam ratna cūrṇa ādibhiḥ cūrṇaiḥ tathā dvādaśa mūrtibhiḥ grahaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam vā api sūrya sāyujyam uttamam evam prākṛtam api āryām ṣaṣ asram parikalpya ca madhyadeśe ca deveśīm prakṛtim brahma rūpiṇīm dakṣiṇe sattva mūrtim ca vāmatas ca rajaḥ guṇam agratas tu tamaḥ mūrtim madhye devīm tathā ambikām pañcabhūtāni tanmātra pañcakam ca eva dakṣiṇe ātmānam ca antarātmānam yugalam buddhim eva ca ahaṅkāram ca mahatā sarva yajña phalam labhet evam vaḥ kathitam sarvam prākṛtam maṇḍalam param atas vakṣyāmi vipra indrāḥ sarva kāma artha sādhanam alaṅkṛtya vitāna ādyaiḥ chatraiḥ vā api manoramaiḥ sita mṛd pātrakaiḥ ca eva su ślakṣṇaiḥ pūrṇa kumbhakaiḥ pañcāśat dīpa mālābhiḥ dhūpaiḥ pañcavidhaiḥ tathā tad tad varṇaiḥ tathā cūrṇaiḥ śveta cūrṇaiḥ atha api vā eka hasta pramāṇena kṛtvā padmam vidhānāt karṇikāyām nyeset devam devyāḥ deveśvaram bhavam praṇava ādi namaḥ ntāni sarva varṇāni suvratāḥ saṃpūjya evam muni śreṣṭhāḥ gandha puṣpa ādibhiḥ kramāt brāhmaṇān bhojayet tatra pañcāśat vidhi pūrvakam akṣamālā upavītam ca kuṇḍalam ca kamaṇḍalum māsanam ca tathā daṇḍam uṣṇīṣam vastram eva ca tat muni indrāṇām devadevāya śaṃbhave mahā carum nivedya evam kṛṣṇam go mithunam tathā ante ca devadevāya dāpayet cūrṇa maṇḍalam oṃkāra ādyam japet dhīmān prativarṇam anukramāt sa aṃgān vedān yathānyāyam adhītya vidhi pūrvakam iṣṭvā yajñaiḥ yathānyāyam jyotiṣṭoma ādibhiḥ kramāt tatas viśvajit antaiḥ ca putrān utpādya tādṛśān gatvā sa sa eva ca cāndrāyaṇa ādikāḥ sarvāḥ kṛtvā nyasya kriyāḥ dvijāḥ brahma vidyām adhītya eva jñānam āsādya yatnatas mālokya yogī yat kāmam āpnuyāt tat phalam labhate sarvam varṇa maṇḍala darśanāt yena kena api vā martyaḥ pralipya āyatana agratas uttare dakṣiṇe vā api pṛṣṭhatas vā dvijottamā catuṣkoṇam tu vā cūrṇaiḥ alaṅkṛtya samantataḥ puṣpa akṣata ādibhiḥ pūjya sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate prārthayet devam īśānam śiva lokam saḥ gacchati tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān kalpa koṭi śatam naraḥ kramāt gāndharvam āsādya gandharvaiḥ ca su pūjitaḥ kramāt āgatya loke asmin rājā bhavati vīryavān sargaḥ ca bhuvana adhīśaḥ śarva vyāpī sadāśivaḥ śiva brahma amṛtam grāhyam mokṣa sādhana muttamam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge upalepanādikathanam nāma saptasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca muni śreṣṭhāḥ na anyathā siddhiḥ iṣyate apaḥ pūtāḥ bhavanti etāḥ vastra pūtāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ aphenāḥ muni sārdūlāḥ nādeyāḥ ca viśeṣataḥ tasmāt vai sarva kāryāṇi daivikāni dvijottamāḥ adbhiḥ kāryāṇi pūtābhiḥ sarva kārya prasiddhaye jantubhiḥ miśritāḥ hi apaḥ sūkṣmābhiḥ tān nihatya tu yat pāpam sakalam ca adbhiḥ a pūtābhiḥ ciram labhet saṃmārjane tathā nṝṇām mārjane ca viśeṣataḥ hiṃsā sadā sṛhasthānām tasmāt hiṃsām vivarjayet ahiṃsā iyam paraḥ dharmaḥ sarveṣām prāṇinām dvijāḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvadā ahiṃsakam naram tad phalam koṭi guṇitam labhate ahiṃsakaḥ naraḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ kāryam abhyukṣaṇam nityam snapanam ca viśeṣataḥ śiva āryam sarvadā kāryā puṣpa hiṃsā dvijottamāḥ yajña artham paśu hiṃsā ca kṣatriyaiḥ duṣṭa śāsanam vihita avihitam na asti yoginām brahma vādinām yatas tasmāt na hantavyāḥ niṣiddhānām niṣevaṇāt na hantavyāḥ sadā pūjyāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ api pavitrāḥ tu striyaḥ sarvāḥ atreḥ ca kula saṃbhavāḥ brahmahatyā samam pāpam ātreyīm vinihatya ca striyaḥ sarvāḥ na hantavyāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ api na yajña artham striyaḥ grāhyāḥ sarvaiḥ sarvatra sarvadā sarva varṇeṣu vipra indrāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ api malināḥ rūpavatyaḥ ca virupāḥ malina ambarāḥ na hantavyāḥ sadā martyaiḥ śiva vat caṅkayā tathā veda bāhya vrata ācārāḥ śrauta smārta bahiṣkṛtāḥ pāṣaṇḍinaḥ iti khyātāḥ na saṃbhāṣyāḥ dvijātibhiḥ na spṛṣṭavyā na draṣṭavyā dṛṣṭvā bhānum samīkṣate prasaṅgāt vā api yaḥ martyaḥ satām sakṛt aho dvijāḥ bhavānti duḥkhitāḥ sarve nirdayāḥ muni sattamāḥ putreṣu dāreṣu gṛheṣu nṝṇām bhaktam yathā cittam atha ādideve sakṛt prasaṅgāt yati tāpasānām teṣām na dūraḥ parameśa lokaḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe
