pūrva bhāge bhaktimahimāvarṇanam nāma aṣṭasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ saṃvatsara sahasraiḥ ca tapasā pūjya śaṃkaram na paśyanti surāḥ ca api katham devam yajanti te uvāca kathitam tathya mā eva atra yuṣmābhiḥ muni puṃgavāḥ tathā api śraddhayā dṛśyaḥ pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣyaḥ eva ca prasaṃgāt ca eva saṃpūjya bhakti hīnaiḥ api dvijāḥ bhāva anurūpa phala daḥ bhagavant iti kīrtitaḥ ucchiṣṭaḥ pūjayan yāti paiśācam tu dvija adhamaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasam sthānam prāpnuyāt mūḍha dhīḥ dvijāḥ abhakṣya bhakṣī saṃpūjya yākṣam prāpnoti durjanaḥ gāna śīlaḥ ca gāndharvam nṛtya śīlaḥ tathā eva ca khyāti śīlaḥ tathā cāndram strīṣu saktaḥ nara adhamaḥ mada ārtaḥ pūjayan rudram soma sthānam avāpnuyāt brāhmam hi praṇavena eva vaiṣṇavam ca abhinandya ca saṃśodhya ca śubham liṅgam amara asura pūjitam pūtaiḥ pīṭhe devam āvāhya bhaktyāḥ dṛṣṭvā devam yathānyāyam praṇipatya ca śaṅkaram pādyam ācamanam ca arghyam dattvā rudrāya śambhave tatas śuddha ambunā snāpya candana ādyaiḥ ca pūjayet rocanā ādyaiḥ ca saṃpūjya divya puṣpaiḥ ca pūjayet nīlotpalaiḥ ca rājīvaiḥ nadyāvartaiḥ ca mallikaiḥ caṅkapaiḥ jātipuṣpaiḥ cava kulaiḥ karavīrakaiḥ apāmārga kadambaiḥ ca bhūṣaṇaiḥ api śobhanaiḥ dattvā pañcavidham dhūpam pāyasam ca nivedayet śuddha annam ca eva mudga annam ṣaḍvidham ca nivedayet kevalam ca api śuddha annam āḍhakam taṇḍulam pacet kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam ca ante namaskṛtya muhur muhur stutvā ca devam īśānam punar saṃpūjya śaṃkaram mahā īśānam puruṣam ca eva aghoram vāmam eva ca sadyojātam japan ca api pañcabhiḥ pūjayet śivam vṛkṣāḥ puṣpa ādi pattra ādyaiḥ upayuktāḥ śiva arcane gāvaḥ ca eva dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prayānti paramām gatim pūjayet yaḥ śivam rudram śarvam bhavam ajam sakṛt arcitam parameśānam bhavam śarvam umāpatim sakṛt prasaṅgāt vā dṛṣṭvā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate pūjitam vā mahādevam pūjyamānam atha api vā dṛṣṭvā prayāti vai martyaḥ brahma lokam na saṃśayaḥ śrutvā anumodayet ca api sa yāti paramām gatim yaḥ dadyāt hṛta dīpam ca sakṛt liṅgasya ca agratas sa tām gatim avāpnoti sva āśramaiḥ durlabhām sthirām dīpavṛkṣam pārthivam vā dāravam vā śiva ālaye dattvā kula śatam sāgram siva loke mahīyate āyasam tāmra jam vā api raupyam sauvarṇikam tathā śivāya dīpam yaḥ dadyāt vidhinā vā api bhaktitaḥ sūrya ayuta samaiḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ yānaiḥ śiva puram vrajet kārttike māsi yaḥ dadyat hṛta dīpam śiva agratas saṃpūjyamānam vā paśyet vidhinā parameśvaram sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ lokam śraddhayā muni sāttamāḥ bhāvāhanam su sāṃnidhyam sthāpanam pūjanam tathā saṃproktam rudra gāyatryā āsanam praṇavena vai pañcabhiḥ snapanam proktam rudra ādyaiḥ ca viśeṣataḥ brahmāṇam dakṣiṇe tasya praṇavena samarcayet uttare devadeveśam viṣṇum gāyatriyā yajet vahnau hutvā yathānyāyam pañcabhiḥ praṇavena ca sa yāti śiva sāyujyam evam saṃpūjya śaṅkaram vyāsena kathitaḥ pūrvam śrutvā rudra mukhāt svayam iti śrī laṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivārcanavidhiḥ nāma ekānāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham paśupatim dṛṣṭvā paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam uvāca mahitāya sarva devānām brahmaṇā ca janārdanaḥ sa indrāḥ sa sādhyāḥ sa yamāḥ praṇemuḥ girim uttamam bhagavant vāsudevaḥ asau garuḍāt garuḍadhvajaḥ sakala durita hītam sarva dam bhoga mukhyam mudita kurara vṛndam nāditam nāga vṛndaiḥ madhura raṇita gītam sa anukūla andhakāram pada racita vanāntam kānta vāta anta toyam gireḥ pṛṣṭhe param śārvam kalpitam viśvakarmaṇā krīḍā artham devadevasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ apaśyan tat puram devāḥ sa indra upendrāḥ samāhitāḥ praṇemuḥ dūratas ca eva prabhāvāt eva śūlinaḥ mahātmā meru prabhāge puram ādidevaḥ gaṇaiḥ gaṇeśaiḥ ca giri indra sannibham mahā pura dvāram ajaḥ hariḥ ca atha jāṃbūnada mayaiḥ bhavanaiḥ maṇi bhūṣitaiḥ mānaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ prākāraiḥ ca samāvṛtam dṛṣṭvā śaṃbhoḥ puram bāhyam devaiḥ sa brahmakaiḥ hariḥ prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ bhūtvā praviveśa tatas puram harmya prāsāda sambādham mahā aṭṭāla samanvitam vajra vaiḍūrya māṇikya maṇi jālaiḥ samāvṛtam dolā vikṣepa saṃyuktam ghaṇṭā cāmara bhūṣitam mṛdaṅga murajaiḥ juṣṭam vīṇā veṇu nināditam nṛtyadbhiḥ apsaraḥ saṃghaiḥ bhūta saṃghaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam prāsāda śṛṅgeṣu atha paura nāryaḥ sahasraśas puṣpa phala akṣata ādyaiḥ dṛṣṭvā nāryaḥ tadā viṣṇum mada āghūrṇita locanāḥ sadyas nanṛtuḥ mumuduḥ jaguḥ kāścid dṛṣṭvā harim nāryaḥ kiṃcid prahasita ānanāḥ ca srasta kāñcī guṇāḥ jaguḥ caturtham pañcamam ca eva ṣaṣṭham ca saptamam tathā aṣṭamam navamam ca eva daśamam ca pura uttamam atītya āsādya devasya puram śambhoḥ su śobhanam su vṛttam sutarām śubhram kailāsa śikhare śubhe sūrya maṇḍala saṃkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ ca vibhūṣitam sphaāṭikaiḥ maḍapaiḥ śubhraiḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ tathā nānā ratna mayaiḥ ca eva diś vidikṣu vibhūṣitam gopuraiḥ gopateḥ śaṃbhoḥ nānā bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitaiḥ prākāraiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ aṣṭāviṃśatibhiḥ vṛtam upadvāraiḥ mahādvāraiḥ vidikṣu vividhaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ grāmyaiḥ anyaiḥ mahābhāgāḥ mauktikaiḥ dṛṣṭi mohanaiḥ candanaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ puṣpa udyānaiḥ ca śaubhanaiḥ taḍāgaiḥ dirghikābhiḥ ca hema sopānapaṅktibhiḥ strīṇām aṅgati jitaiḥ haṃsaiḥ sevitābhiḥ samantataḥ mayūraiḥ ca eva kāraṇḍaiḥ kokilaiḥ cakravākakaiḥ śobhitābhiḥ ca vāpībhiḥ divya amṛta jalaiḥ tathā saṃlāpa ālāpa kuśalaiḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaiḥ stana bāra avanamraiḥ ca mada āghūrṇita locanaiḥ rudra strī gama saṃkīrṇaiḥ jala krīḍā rataiḥ tathā dṛṣṭvā vismayam āpannāḥ tasthuḥ devāḥ samantataḥ tatra eva dadṛśuḥ devāḥ vṛndam rudra gaṇasya ca gaṇa īśvarāṇām vīrāṇām api vṛndam sahasraśas suvarṇa kṛta sopānān vajra vaiḍūrya bhūṣitān sphaāṭikān devadevasya dadṛśuḥ te vimānakān teṣām śṛṅgeṣu hṛṣṭāḥ ca nāryaḥ kamala locanāḥ kinnaryaḥ kiṃnarāḥ ca eva bhujaṅgāḥ siddha kanyakāḥ nānā veṣa dharāḥ ca anyāḥ nānā bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitāḥ nānā prabhāva saṃyuktāḥ nānā bhoga rati priyāḥ nīlotpala dala prakhyāḥ padma pattra āyata īkṣaṇāḥ padma kiñjalka saṃkāśaiḥ aṃśukaiḥ ati śobhanāḥ valayaiḥ nūpuraiḥ hāraiḥ chattraiḥ citraiḥ tathā aṃśukaiḥ bhūṣitāḥ bhūṣitaiḥ ca anyaiḥ māṇḍitāḥ maṇḍana priyāḥ dṛṣṭvā atha vṛndam sura suṃdarīṇām gaṇeśvarāṇām sura suṃdarīṇām jagmuḥ gaṇeśasya puram sura īśāḥ puradviṣaḥ śakra purogamāḥ ca dṛṣṭvā ca tasthuḥ sura siddha saṃghāḥ purasya madhye puruhūta pūrve nandinam dadṛśuḥ sarve devāḥ sakra purogamāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā nandinam sarve pramamya āhuḥ gaṇeśvaram jaya iti devāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā saḥ api āha ca gaṇaiśvaraḥ bho bho devāḥ mahābhāgāḥ sarve nirdhūta kalmaṣāḥ saṃprāptāḥ sarva loke sāḥ vaktum arhatha suvratāḥ paśu pāśa vimokṣa artham darśaya asmān maheśvaram purā puratrayam dagdhum paśu tvam paribhāṣitam śaṅkitāḥ ca vayam tatra paśu tvam prati suvrata mad pāśupatam proktam bhavena parameṣṭhinā atha dvādaśa varṣam vā māsa dvādaśakam tu vā dina dvādaśakam vā api kṛtvā tat bratam uttamam darśayāmāsa tān devān nārāyaṇa purogamān mandī śilāda tanayaḥ sarva bhūta gaṇāgraṇī tam dṛṣṭvā devam īśānam sa ambam sa gaṇam avyayam praṇemuḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ vai eva prīti kaṇṭakita tvacaḥ vijñāpya śitikaṇṭhāya paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam tasthuḥ tadā agratas śaṃbhoḥ praṇipatya punar punar tatas saṃprekṣya tān sarvān devadevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ viśodhya teṣām devānām paśu tvam parameśvaraḥ vratam pāśupatam ca eva svayam devaḥ maheśvaraḥ upadiśya munīnām ca saha āste ca ambayā bhavaḥ tadā prabhṛti te devāḥ sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ paśūnām ca patiḥ yasmāt teṣām sākṣāt hi devatāḥ tasmāt pāśupatāḥ proktāḥ tapaḥ tepuḥ ca te punar tatas dvādaśa varṣa ante mukta pāśāḥ sura uttamāḥ yayuḥ yathāgatam sarve brahmaṇā saha viṣṇunā purā sanatkumāreṇa tasmāt vyāsena dhīmatā yaḥ śrāvayet śruciḥ viprān śṛṇuyāt vā śuciḥ naraḥ sa dehabhedam āsādya paśu pāśaiḥ pramucyate iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge pāśupatavratamāhātmyam nāma aśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ vratam etat tvayā proktam paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam bratam pāśupatam laiṅgam purā devaiḥ anuṣṭhitam vaktum arhasi ca asmākam yathāpūrvam tvayā śrutam uvāca purā sanatkumāreṇa pṛṣṭaḥ śailādiḥ ādarāt bratam dvādaśa liṅga ākhyam paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam aviyoga karam puṇyam bhaktānām bhaya nāśanam ṣaḍaṅga sahitān vedān mathitvā tena nirmitam sarva dāna uttamam puṇyam aśvamedha ayuta adhikam sarva maṅgala dam puṇyam sarva śatru vināśanam saṃsāra ṛṇava magnānām jantūnām api mokṣa dam devaiḥ anuṣṭhitam pūrvam brahmanā viṣṇunā tathā kṛtvā ākanīyasam liṅgam snāpya candana vāriṇā caitra māsa ādi vipra indrāḥ śiva liṅga vratam caret kṛtvā haimam śubham padmam karṇikā kesara anvitam karṇikāyām nyaset liṅgam sphaāṭikam pīṭha saṃyutam śveta arka karṇikāraiḥ ca karavīraiḥ bakaiḥ api etaiḥ anyaiḥ yathālābham gāyatryā tasya suvratāḥ saṃpūjya ca eva gandha ādyaiḥ dhūpaiḥ dīpaiḥ ca maṅgalaiḥ nīrājana ādyaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca liṅga mūrti maheśvaram agarum dakṣiṇe dadyāt aghoreṇa dvijottamāḥ paścime sadya mantreṇa divyām ca eva manaḥśilām puruṣeṇa muni śreṣṭhāḥ haritālam ca pūrvatas sita agaru udbhavam viprāḥ tathā kṛṣṇa agaru udbhavam sitāram nāma dhūpam ca dadyat īśāya bhaktyāḥ mahā caruḥ nivedyaḥ syāt āḍhaka annam atha api vā etat vāḥ kathitam puṇyam śiva liṅga mahā vratam sarva māseṣu sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ api ca kīrtyate vaiśākhe vajraliṅgam ca jyeṣṭhe mārakatam tathā āṣāḍham mauktikam liṅgam śrāvaṇe nīla nirmitam māsi bhādrapade liṅgam padmarāga mayam śubham mayam pravaleṇa eva kārttikyām tathā vai mārgaśīrṣake vaiḍūlya nirmitam liṅgam puṣparāgeṇa puṣyake alābhe rājatam vā api ke valam kamalam tu vā ratnānām paya lābhe tu hemnā vā rājatena vā śailam vā dāru jam vā api mṛd mayam vā sa vedikam sarva gandha mayam vā api kṣāṇikam parikalpayet haimantike mahādevam śrī patreṇa eva pūjayet tad ardha ardhena vā rudram aṣṭottaraśatena vā bilva pattre sthitā lakṣmīḥ devī lakṣaṇa saṃyutā nīlotpala iṃbikā sākṣāt utpale ṣaṇmukhaḥ svayam padma āśritāḥ mahādevaḥ sarva deva patiḥ śivaḥ nīlotpalam ca utpalam ca kamalam ca viśeṣataḥ sarva vaśyā karam padmam śilā sarva artha siddhi dā mahā agaru samudbhutam sarva pāpa nikṛntanam guggulu prabhṛtīnām ca eva dīpānām ca nivedanam saugandhikam tathā dhūpam sarva kāma artha sādhakam śvetagaru udbhavam ca eva tathā kṛṣṇa agaru udbhavam saumyam sītāri dhūpam ca sākṣāt nirvāṇa siddhi dam śveta arka kusume sākṣāt caturvattraḥ prajāpatiḥ karṇikārasya kusume medhā sākṣāt vyavasthitā karavīre gaṇādhyakṣaḥ bake nārāyaṇaḥ svayam tasmāt etaiḥ yathālābham puṣpa dhūpa ādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ pūjayet devadeveśam bhaktyā vitta anusārāt śuddha annam vā api mudga annam āḍhakam ca ardhakam tu vā upahārāṇi puṇyāni nyāyena eva arjitāni api nānāvidhāni ca arhāni prokṣitāni ambhasā punar kṣīrāt vai sarva devānām sthiti artham amṛtam dhruvam viṣṇunā jiṣṇunā sākṣāt anne sarvam pratiṣṭhitam bhūtānām anna dānena prītiḥ bavati śaṃkare tasmāt saṃpūjayet devam anne prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ upahāre tathā tuṣṭiḥ vyañjane pavanaḥ svayam pīṭhe vai prakṛtiḥ sākṣāt mahat ādyaiḥ vyavasthitā paurṇamāsyām vratam kāryam sarva kāma artha siddhaye satyam śaucam dayā śāntiḥ saṃtoṣaḥ dānam eva ca paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyām upavāsam ca kārayet saṃvatsara ante godānam vṛṣotsargam viśeṣataḥ bhojayet brāhmaṇān bhaktyā śrotriyān vedapāragān sthāpayet vā śiva kṣetre dāpayet brāhmaṇāya vā yaḥ evam sarva māseṣu śiva liṅga mahāvratam kuryāt bhaktyā muni śreṣṭhāḥ saḥ eva tapatām varaḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ ratna bhūṣitaiḥ gatvā śiva puram divyam na iha āyāti kadācana bhava lokam avāpnoti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā varṣam ekam caret evam tān tān prāpya śivam vrajet deva tvam vā pitṛ tvam vā deva rāja tvam eva ca vidyā arthī labhate vidyām bhoga arthi bhogam āpnuyāt dravya arthī ca nidhim paśyet āyus kāmaḥ cira āyuṣam yān yān cintayate kāmān tān tān prāpya iha modate idam pavitram paramam rahasyam vrata uttamam viśvasṛjā api sṛṣṭam hitāya deva asura siddha martya vidyādharāṇām paramam śivena saṃpūjya pūjyam vidhinā evam īśam praṇamya mūrdhnā saha bhṛtya putraiḥ vyapohanam nāma japet stavam ca pradakṣiṇam kṛtya śivam prayatnāt purā kṛtam viśvasṛjā stavam ca hitāya devena jagattrayasya iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge paśupāśavimocanaliṅgapūjādikathanam nāma ekāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca nandinaḥ ca mukhāt śrutvā kumāreṇa mahātmanā vyāsāya kathitam tasmāt bahu mānena vai mayā namaḥ śivāya śuddhāya nirmalāya yaśasvine duṣṭa antakāya sarvāya bhavāya paramātmane śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśaḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ sarvajña sarva gaḥ śāntaḥ sarva upari su saṃsthitaḥ padmāsana sthaḥ soma īśaḥ pāpam āśu vyapohatu īśānaḥ puruṣaḥ ca eva aghoraḥ sadyaḥ eva ca vāmadevaḥ ca bhagavān pāpam āśu vyapohatu anantaḥ sarva vidyā īśaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva daḥ prabhuḥ śiva dhyāna eka saṃpannaḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu sūkṣmaḥ sura asura īśānaḥ viśveśaḥ gaṇa pūjitaḥ śiva dhyāna eka saṃpannaḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu śiva uttamaḥ mahā pūjyaḥ śiva dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ sarvagaḥ sarva daḥ śāntaḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu ekāśraḥ bhagavant īśaḥ śiva arcana parāyaṇaḥ śiva dhyāna eka saṃpannaḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu trimūrtiḥ bhagavant īśaḥ śiva bhakti prabodhakaḥ śiva dhyāna eka saṃpannaḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śrīpatiḥ śrīmān śiva dhyāna rataḥ sadā śiva arcana rataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpam vyapohatu trailokya namitā devī sa ulkā ākārā purātanā śiva arcana rataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpam vyapohatu trailokya nam iti devī sa ulkā ākārā purātanā dākṣāyaṇī mahā devī bhaurī haimavatī śubhā ekaparṇā agrajā saumyā tathā vai ca ekapāṭalā aparṇā avaradā devī vara dāna eka tatparā umā sura harā sākṣāt kauśikī vā kapardinī khaṭvāṅga dhāriṇī divyā kara agra taru pallavā menāyāḥ nandinī devī vāri jā vārija īkṣaṇā ambāyāḥ vīta śokasya nandinaḥ ca mahātmanaḥ śubhāvatyāḥ sakhī śāntā pañcacūḍā vara pradā sṛṣṭi artham sarva bhūtānām prakṛti tvam gatā avyayā manonmanī mahādevī māyāvī maṇḍana priyā māyayā yā jagant sarvam brahma ādyam sacarācaram kṣobhiṇī mohinī nityam yoginām hṛdi saṃsthitā eka aneka sthitā loke indīvara nibha īkṣaṇā saṃstutā jananī teṣām sarva upadrava nāśinī bhaktānām ārti hā bhavyā bhava bhāva vināśanā sā me sākṣāt mahādevī pāpām āśu vyapohatu caṇḍaḥ sarva gaṇa īśānaḥ mukhāt śambhoḥ vinirgataḥ śiva arcana rataḥ śrīmān sa mama pāpam vyapohatu śālaṅkāyana putraḥ tu halamārga utthitaḥ prabhuḥ marutām devaḥ sarva bhūta mahā īśvaraḥ sarvagaḥ sarva dṛś śarvaḥ sarva īśa sadṛśaḥ prabhuḥ sa nārāyaṇakaiḥ devaiḥ sa indra candra divākaraiḥ uragaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ ca eva brahmanā ca mahātmanā sarvadā pūjitaḥ sarvaiḥ nandī pāpam vyapohatu mahā kāyaḥ mahā tejāḥ mahādevaḥ iva aparaḥ śiva arcana rataḥ śrīmān sa mama pāpam vyapohatu meru mandāra kailāsa taṭa kūṭa prabhedanaḥ sapta pātāla pādaḥ ca sapta dvīpa ūru jaṅghakaḥ sapta arṇava aṅkuśaḥ ca eva sarva tīrtha udaraḥ śivaḥ brahma vidyā mahā utkaṭaḥ baddhaḥ hṛd puṇḍarīka ākhye stambhe vṛttim nirudhya ca nāga indra vattraḥ yaḥ sākṣāt gaṇa koṭi śataiḥ vṛtaḥ vyapohatu bhṛṅgīśaḥ piṅgalākṣa usau bhasita āśaḥ tu dehu yuj śiva arcana rataḥ śrīmān sa mama pāpam vyapohatu skandaḥ śakti dharaḥ śāntaḥ senā nīḥ śikhivāhanaḥ deva senāpatiḥ śrīmān sa me pāpam vyapohatu bhavaḥ śarvaḥ tathā īśānaḥ rudraḥ paśupatiḥ tathā ugraḥ bhīmaḥ mahādevaḥ śiva arcana rataḥ sadā etāḥ pāpam vyapohantu mūrtayaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ mahādevaḥ śivaḥ rudraḥ śaṅkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ kapālī īśaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ rudrāḥ rudra aṃśa saṃbhavāḥ śiva praṇāma saṃpannāḥ vyapohantu malam mama vikartanaḥ vivasvant ca mārtaṇḍaḥ bhāskaraḥ raviḥ loka prakāśakaḥ ca eva loka sākṣī trivikramaḥ ādityaḥ ca tathā sūryaḥ ca aṃsumān ca divākaraḥ gaganam sparśanam tejaḥ rasaḥ ca pṛthivī tathā candraḥ sūryaḥ tathā ātmā ca tanavaḥ śiva bhāṣitāḥ varuṇaḥ vāyu somau ca īśānaḥ bhagavant hariḥ pitāmahaḥ ca bhagavant śiva dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ prāṇaḥ prāṇeśa jīveśau mārutaḥ śiva bhāṣitāḥ suṣeṇaḥ śāśvataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ supuṣṭaḥ ca mahābalaḥ ete vai cāraṇāḥ śaṃbhoḥ pūjayā atīva bhāvitāḥ vyapohantu malam sarvam pāpam ca eva mayā kṛtam mantra jñaḥ mantra vid prājñaḥ mantra rāj siddha pūjitaḥ vyapohantu malam sarve siddhāḥ śiva pada arcakāḥ yakṣaḥ yakṣeśaiḥ dhanadaḥ jṛṃbhakaḥ maṇibhadrakaḥ pūrṇabhadra īśvaraḥ mālī śitikuṇḍaliḥ eva ca balaḥ śiva praṇāma saṃpannāḥ śiva deha prabhūṣaṇāḥ mama pāpam vyapohantu viṣam sthāvara jaṅgamam vīṇā jñaḥ kinnaraḥ ca eva surasenaḥ pramardanaḥ atiśayaḥ sa prayogī gīta jñaḥ ca eva kinnarāḥ śiva praṇāma saṃpannāḥ vyopohantu malam mama ca vibuddhaḥ vibudhaḥ śrīmān kṛtajñaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ ete vidyādharāḥ sarve śiva dhyāna parāyaṇāḥ vāmadevī mahājaṃbhaḥ kālanemiḥ mahā balaḥ prahrādaḥ ca api anuhrādaḥ saṃhrādaḥ kila bāṣkalau jambhaḥ kumbhaḥ ca māyavī kārtavīryaḥ kṛtañjayaḥ ete asurāḥ mahātmānaḥ mahādeva parāyaṇāḥ garutmant kha gatiḥ ca eva pakṣirāj nāga mardanaḥ nāgaśatruḥ hiraṇyāṅgaḥ vainateyaḥ prabhañjanaḥ nāga āśīrviṣa nāśaḥ ca viṣṇuvāhanaḥ eva ca ete hiraṇya varṇa ābhāḥ garuḍāḥ viṣṇu vāhanāḥ nānā ābharaṇa saṃpannāḥ vyapohantu malam mama agastyaḥ ca vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ bhṛguḥ eva ca kāśyapaḥ nāradaḥ ca eva dadhīcaḥ cyavanaḥ tathā upamanyuḥ tathā anye ca ṛṣayaḥ śiva bhāvitāḥ pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ ca tathā eva prapitāmahāḥ agniṣvāttāḥ barhiṣadaḥ tathā mātāmaha ādayaḥ vyapohantu bhayam pāpam śiva dhyāna parāyaṇāḥ lakṣmīḥ ca dharaṇī ca eva gāyatrī ca sarasvatī durgāḥ uṣā śacī jyeṣṭhā mātaraḥ sura pūjitāḥ devānām mātaraḥ ca eva gaṇānām mātaraḥ tathā bhūtānām mātaraḥ sarvāḥ yatra yāḥ gaṇa mātaraḥ urvaśī menakā ca eva raṃbhā rati tilottamāḥ sumukhī durmukhī ca eva kāmukhī kāma vardhanā tathā anyāḥ sarva lokeṣu divyāḥ ca apsarasaḥ tathā śivāya tāṇḍavam nityam kurvatyā utīva bhāvitāḥ arkaḥ soma uṅgārakaḥ ca budhaḥ ca eva bṛhaspatiḥ śukraḥ śanaiścaraḥ ca eva rāhuḥ ketuḥ tathā eva ca vyapohantu bhayam ghoram grahapīḍām śiva arcakāḥ meṣaḥ vṛṣaḥ atha mithunaḥ tathā karkaṭakaḥ śubhaḥ siṃhaḥ ca kanyā vipulā tulā vai vṛścikaḥ tathā rāśayaḥ dvādaśa hi ete śiva pūjā parāyaṇāḥ vyapohantu bhayam pāpam prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ aśvinī bharaṇī ca eva kṛttikā rohiṇī tathā śrīmat mṛgaśiraḥ ca ārdrā punarvasu puṣya sārpakāḥ maghāḥ vai pūrva phaālgunyaḥ uttarā phaālgunī tathā hastaḥ citrā tathā svātiḥ viśākhā ca anurādhikā jyeṣṭhā mūlam mahābhāgā pūrvāṣāḍhā tathā eva ca uttara āṣāḍhikā ca eva śravaṇam ca śraviṣṭhikā śatabhiṣaj pūrvabhadrā tathā proṣṭhapadā tathā mahā jvaraḥ kumbhodaraḥ ca eva śaṅkukarṇaḥ mahā balaḥ mahākarṇaḥ prabhātaḥ ca mahā bhūta pramardanaḥ śyenajit śiva dūtaḥ ca pramathāḥ prīti vardhanāḥ koṭi koṭi śataiḥ ca eva bhūtānām mātaraḥ sadā vyapohantu bhayam pāpam mahādeva prasādāt śiva dhyāna eka saṃpannaḥ himarāj ambu sannibhaḥ kunda indu sadṛśa ākāraḥ kumbha kunda indu bhūṣaṇaḥ vaḍavānala śatruḥ yaḥ vaḍavāmukha bhedanaḥ catuṣpāda samāyuktaḥ kṣīrodaḥ iva pāṇḍuraḥ rudra loke sthitaḥ nityam rudraiḥ sārdham gaṇa īśvaraiḥ vṛṣā indraḥ viśvadhṛk devaḥ viśvasya jagantaḥ pitā gaṅgā mātā jaganmātrī rudra loke vyavasthitā śiva bhaktā tu yā nandā sā mama pāpam vyapohatu mātā gavām mahābhāgā sā me pāpam vyapohatu surabhiḥ sarvatobhadrā sarva pāpa praṇāśanī rudra pūjā ratā nityam sā mama pāpam vyapohatu mahā śīlā śīla saṃpannā śrī pradā śiva bhāvitā śiva loke sthitā nityam sā mama pāpam vyapohatu sarva kārya abhicintakaḥ samasta guṇa saṃpannaḥ sarva deva śvara ātmajaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ saumyaḥ mahā viṣṇu tanuḥ svayam āryaḥ senāpatiḥ sākṣāt gahanaḥ makha mardanaḥ airāvata gaja ārūḍhaḥ kṛṣṇa kuñcita mūrdhajaḥ kṛṣṇa aṅgaḥ rakta nayanaḥ śaśi pannaga bhūṣaṇaḥ bhūtaiḥ pretaiḥ piśācaiḥ ca kūṣmāṇḍaiḥ ca samāvṛtaḥ śiva arcana rataḥ sākṣāt sa mama pāpam vyapohatu brahmāṇī ca eva māheśī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā vārāhī ca eva māhendrī cāmuṇḍā agneyikā tathā etāḥ vai mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarva loka prapūjitāḥ yoginī bhīḥ mahā pāpam vyapohantu samāhitāḥ rudrasya tanayaḥ raudraḥ śūla āsakta mahā karaḥ mātṝṇām rakṣakaḥ nityam mahā vṛṣabha vāhanaḥ trailokya namitaḥ śrīmān śiva pāda arcane rataḥ yajñasya ca śiraḥ chettā pūṣṇaḥ danta vināśanaḥ pādāṅguṣṭhena soma aṅga peṣakaḥ prabhu saṃjñakaḥ upendra idra yama ādīnām devānām aṅga rakṣakaḥ nāsikā uṣṭha avakartanaḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā vara dā vara ābharaṇa bhūṣitā mahā lakṣmīḥ jaganmātrī sā me pāpam vyapohatu mahā mohā mahābhāgā mahā bhūta gaṇaiḥ vṛtā vyapohatu lakṣmīḥ sarva guṇa upetā sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutā sarvadā sarva gā devī sā me pāpam vyapohatu siṃha ārūḍhā mahādevī pārvatyāḥ tanayā avyayā viṣṇoḥ nidrā mahāmāyā vaiṣṇavā sura pūjitā śiva arcana ratā durgā sā me pāpam vyavohatu brahmāṇḍa dhārakāḥ rudrāḥ sarva loka prapūjitāḥ satyāḥ ca mānasāḥ sarve vyapohantu bhayam mama bhūtāḥ pretāḥ piśācāḥ ca kūṣmāṇḍa gaṇa nāyakāḥ kūṣmāṇḍakāḥ ca te pāpam vyapohantu samāhitāḥ praṇamya śirasā bhūmau pratimāse dvijottamāḥ vyapohana stavam divyam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt api vidyā arthī labhate vidyām bhoga arthī bhogam āpnuyāt yān yān prārthayate kāmān mānavaḥ śravaṇāt iha tān sarvān śīghram āpnoti devānām ca priyaḥ bhavet paṭhyamānam idam puṇyam yam uddiśya tu paṭhyate tasya rogāḥ na bādhante vāta pitta ādi saṃbhavāḥ yat puṇyam ca eva tīrthānām yajñānām ca eva yat phalam dānānām ca eva yat puṇyam vratānām ca viśeṣataḥ tat puṇyam koṭi guṇitam japtvā ca āpnoti mānavaḥ śaraṇa āgata ghātī ca mitra viśvāsa ghātakaḥ duṣṭaḥ pāpa samācāraḥ mātṛ hā pitṛ hā tathā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vyapohanastavanirūpaṇam nāma dvyaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ vyapohana stavam puṇyam śrutam asmābhiḥ ādarāt uvāca vratāni vaḥ pravakṣyāmi śubhāni muni sattamāḥ tāni vyāsāt upaśrutya vaḥ pravadāmi aham aṣṭamyām ca caturdaśyām pakṣayoḥ ubhayayoḥ api varṣam ekam tu bhuñjānaḥ naktam yaḥ pūjayet śivam sarva yajña phalam prāpya sa yāti paramām gatim pṛthivīm bhājanam kṛtvā bhuktvā parvasu mānavaḥ kṣīpadhārāvratam kuryāt sa uśvamedha phalam labhet kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām tu naktena yāvat kṛṣṇa caturdaśī brahmacārī jita krodhaḥ śiva dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ sa yāti śāṅkaram lokam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā upavāsāt param bhaikṣyam bhaikṣyāt parama yācitam devaiḥ bhuktam tu pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne ṛṣibhiḥ tathā aparāhṇe ca pitṛbhiḥ saṃdhyāyām guhyaka ādibhiḥ haviṣya bhojanam snāṃna satyam āhāra lāghavam agnikāryam adhaḥśayyām nakta bhojī samācaret dharma kāma artha mokṣa artham sarva pāpa viśuddhaye satya vādī jita krodhaḥ śāli godhūma gorasaiḥ pakṣayoḥ aṣṭamīm yatnāt upavāsena vartayet bhūmi śayyām ca māsa aṃte paurṇamāsyām ghṛta ādibhiḥ snāpya rudram mahādevam saṃpūjya vidhi pūrvakam yāvakam ca odanam dattvā sa kṣīram sa ghṛtam dvijāḥ bhījayet brāhmaṇān śiṣṭān japet śāntim viśeṣataḥ bhavāya devadevāya śivāya parameṣṭhine māgha māse tu saṃpūjya yaḥ kuryāt naktabhojam kṛsaram ghṛta saṃyuktam bhuñjānaḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ sa upavāsam caturdaśyām bhavet ubhaya pakṣayoḥ rudrāya paurṇamāsyām tu dadyāt vai ghṛtakaṃbalam kṛṣṇam go mithunam dadyāt pūjayet ca eva saṃkaram śyāmāka anna ghṛta kṣīraiḥ jita krodhaḥ jita indriyaḥ caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām upavāsam ca kārayet paurṇamāsyām mahādevam snāpya saṃpūjya śaṅkaram dadyāt go mithunam vā api tāmra ābham śūlapāṇaye sa yāti candra sāyujyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā śālyannam payasā yuktam ghṛtena ca yathāsukham goṣṭha śāyī muni śreṣṭhāḥ kṣitau niśi bhavam smaret paurṇamāsyām śivam snāpya dadyāt go mithunam sitam brāhmaṇān bhojayet ca eva nirṛtyāḥ sthānam āpnuyāt vaiśākhe ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam paurṇamāsyām bhavam snāpyam pañcagavya ghṛta ādibhiḥ jyeṣṭhe māse ca deveśam bhavam śarvam umāpatim saṃpūjya śraddhayā bhaktyā kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam ca ca pūtam ghṛta ādibhiḥ ca paurṇamāsyām tu saṃpūjya devadevam umāpatim snāpya śaktyā yathānyāyam carum dadyāt ca śūline dhūmram go mithunam dattvā vāyu loke mahīyate āṣāḍhe māsi ca api evam naktabhojana tatparaḥ bhūri khaṇḍa ājya sammiśram saktubhiḥ ca eva gorasam paurṇamāsyām ghṛta ādyaiḥ tu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān dadyāt go mithunam gauram vāruṇam lokam āpnuyāt śrāvaṇe ca dvijāḥ māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam kṣīra ṣaṣṭika bhaktena saṃpūjya vṛṣabhadhvajam paurṇamāsyām ghṛta ādyaiḥ tu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān śveta agra pādam pauḍram ca dadyāt go mithunam punar huta śeṣam ca viprandrān vṛkṣa mūla āśritaḥ divā paurṇamāsyām tu deveśam snāpya saṃpūjya śaṃkaram nīla skandham vṛṣam gām ca dattvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca veda vedāṅga pāragān tatas ca āśvayuje māsi kṛtvā evam naktabhojanam sa ghṛtam śaṅkaram pūjya paurṇamāsyām ca pūrvavat brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śiva bhaktān sadā śucīn vaṣabham nīla varṇa ābham uras deśa samunnatam maiśānam lokam āpnuyāt paurṇamāsyām ca vidhivat snāpya dattvā carum punar dattvā go mithunam ca eva kāpilam sūrya sāyujyam āpnoti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā mārgasīrṣe ca kṛtvā evam naktabhojanam yava annena yathānyāyam ājya kṣīra ādibhiḥ samam paurṇamāsyām ca pūrva uktam kṛtvā śarvāya śaṃbhave brāhmaṇān bhojayittvā ca daridrān vedapāragān dattvā go mithunam ca eva pāṇḍuram vidhi pūrvakam ahiṃsā satyam asteyam brahmacaryam kṣamā dayā tris snānam ca agnihotram ca bhū śayyā naktabhojanam pakṣayoḥ upavāsam ca caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca kuryāt varṣam krameṇa eva vyutkrameṇa api vā dvijāḥ sa yāti śiva sāyujyam jñāna yogam avāpnuyāt iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivavratakathanam nāma tryaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca umāmaheśvaram vakṣye vratam īśvara bhāṣitam nara nārī ādi jantūnām hitāya muni sattamāḥ paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyām caturdasi aṣṭamīṣu ca umā maheśa pratimām hemnā kṛtvā su śobhanām rājatām vā atha varṣa ante pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dattvā śaktyā ca dakṣiṇām ratha ādyaiḥ vā api devaśam nītvā rudra ālayam prati sarva atiśaya saṃyuktaiḥ chatra cāmara bhūṣaṇaiḥ sa yāti śivā sāyujyam nārī devyāḥ yadi prabho aṣṭamyām ca caturdaśyām niyatā brahmacāriṇī varṣam ekam na bhuñjati kanyā vā vidhavā api vā varṣa ante pratimām kṛtvā pūrva ukta vidhinā tatas pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyam dattvā rudra ālaye punar brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca bhavānyā saha modate yā nārī evam caret abdam kṛṣṇām ekām caturdaśīm varṣa ante pratimām kṛtvā yena kena api vā dvijāḥ pūrva uktam akhilam kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate amāvāsyām nirāhārā bhavet abdam su yantritā śūlam ca vidhinā kṛtvā varṣa ante vinivedayet snāpya īśānam yajet bhaktyā sahasraiḥ kamalaiḥ sitaiḥ rājatam kamalam ca eva jāmbūnada su karṇikam dattvā bhavāya viprebhyaḥ pradadyāt dakṣiṇām api kāmatas api kṛtam pāpam bhrūṇahatyā ādikam ca yat tat sarvam śūla dānena bhindyāt nārī na saṃśayaḥ sāyujyam ca evam āpnoti bhavānyāḥ dvijasattamāḥ kuryāt yat vā naraḥ saḥ api rudra sāyujyam āpnuyāt paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyām varṣam ekam atandritā upavāsa ratā nārī narāḥ api dvijasattamāḥ niyogāt eva tat kāryam bhartṝṇām dvijasattamāḥ japam dānam tapaḥ sarvam asvatantrāḥ yatas striyaḥ sā bhavānyāḥ ca sāyujyam sārūyam ca api suvratā kārttikyām vā tu yā nārī eka bhaktena vartate kṣamā hiṃsā ādi niyamaiḥ saṃyuktā brahmacāriṇī dadyāt kṛṣṇa tilānām ca bhāram ekam atandriyā sa ghṛtam sa guḍam ca eva odanam parameṣṭhine aṣṭamyām ca caturdaśyām upavāsa ratā ca sā bhavānyā modate sārdham sārūpyam prāpya suvratā kṣamā satyam dayā dānam śaucam indriya nigrahaḥ samāsāt vaḥ pravakṣyāmi pratimāsam anukramāt mārgaśīrṣakam āsādi kārttikya antam yata ākramam vratam su vipulam puṇyam nandinā paribhāṣitam mārgaśīrṣaka māsetha vṛṣam pūrṇa aṅgam uttamam alaṅkṛtya yathānyāyam śivāya vinivedayet sā ca sārdham bhavānyā vai modate na atra saṃśayaḥ puṣya māse tu vai śūlam pratiṣṭhāpya nivedayet pūrva uktam akhilam kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate māgha māse ratham kṛtvā sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitam dadyāt saṃpūjya deveśam brāhmaṇān ca eva bhojayet sā ca devyā mahābhāga modate na atra saṃśayaḥ phaālgune pratimām kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi sā ca sārdham mahādevyā modate na atra saṃśayaḥ caitre bhavam kumāram ca bhavānīm ca yathāvidhi tāmra ādyaiḥ vidhivat kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi bhavānyā modate sārdham dattvā rudrāya śambhave kṛtvā ālayam hi kauberam rājatam rajatena vai īśvara umā samāyuktam gaṇeśaiḥ ca samantataḥ jyeṣṭhe māsi mahādevam liṅga mūrtim umāpatim kṛtāñjali puṭena eva brahmanā viṣṇunā tathā haṃsena ca varāhena kṛtvā tāmra ādibhiḥ śubhām pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyam brāhmaṇān bhojayet tatas śivāya śivam āsādya śiva sthāne yathāvidhi brāhmaṇaiḥ sahitām sthāpya devyāḥ sāyujyam āpnuyāt māse ca śubhe māse gṛham kṛtvā su śobhanam sarva bīja rasaiḥ ca api saṃpūrṇam sarva śobhanaiḥ gṛha upakaraṇaiḥ ca eva musala ulūkhala ādibhiḥ dāsī dāsa ādibhiḥ ca eva śayanaiḥ asana ādibhiḥ saṃpūrṇaiḥ ca gṛham vastraiḥ ācchādya ca samantataḥ devam ghṛta ādibhiḥ snāpya mahādevam umāpatim brāhmaṇānām sahasram ca bhojayitvā yathāvidhi vidyā vinaya saṃpannam brāhmaṇam vedapāragam prathama āśramiṇam bhaktyā saṃpūjya ca yathāvidhi kanyām sumadhyamām yāvat kāla jīvana saṃyutām bhavānyā sadṛśībhūtvā sarva kalpeṣu sā avyayā bhavānyāḥ ca eva sāyujyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ nivedayīta śarvāya śrāvaṇe tila parvatam kṛtvā bhādrapade māsi śobhanam śāli parvatam brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dāpayet ca yathāvidhi sā ca sūrya aṃśu saṃkāśā bhavānyā saha modate kṛtvā ca āśvayuje māsi vipulam dhānya parvatam suvarṇa vastra yaṃyuktam dattvā saṃpūjya śaṃkaram sarva dhānya samāyuktam sarva bīja rasa ādibhiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ caturbhiḥ saṃyuktam vitāna chatra śobhitam gandha mālyaiḥ tathā dhūpaiḥ citraiḥ ca api su śobhitam vicitraiḥ nṛtya geyaiḥ ca śaṅkha vīṇā ādibhiḥ tathā brahmaghoṣaiḥ mahā puṇyam maṅgalaiḥ ca viśeṣataḥ dakṣiṇe ca yathānyāyam brahmāṇam ca catur mukham uttare devadeveśam nārāyaṇam anāmayam indra ādi lokapālān ca kṛtvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi devasya dakṣiṇe haste śūlam tridaśa pūjitam vāme pāśam bhavānyāḥ ca kamalam hema bhūṣitam viṣṇoḥ ca śaṅkham cakram ca gadām abjam prayatnāt brahmaṇaḥ ca akṣa sūtram ca kamaṇḍalum anuttamam yamasya daṇḍam nirṛteḥ khaḍgam niśicarasya tu varuṇasya mahā pāśam nāga ākhyam rudram adbhutam vāyoḥ yā aṣṭim kuberasya gadām loka prapūjitām ṭaṅkam ca īśāna devasya nivedya evam krameṇa ca śivasya mahatīm pūjām kṛtvā caru samānvitām brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūjām kṛtvā prayatnāt mahā meru vratam kṛtvā mahādevāya dāpayet ciram sāyucyam āpnoti mahādevyā na saṃśayaḥ kārttikyām api yā nārī kṛtvā devīm umām śubhām sarva ābharaṇa saṃpūrṇām sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitām hema tāmra ādibhiḥ ca eva pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ devam ca kṛtvā deveśam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutam nārāyaṇam ca dātāram sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam lokapālaiḥ tathā siddhaiḥ saṃvṛtam sthāpya yatnatas mārgaśīrṣaka māsa ādi kārttika antam pravartitam nara nārī ādi jantūnām hitāya muni sattamāḥ naraḥ kṛtvā vratam ca eva śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt nārī devyā na saṃdehaḥ śivena paribhāṣitam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge umāmaheśvaravratam nāma caturaśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca japet pañcākṣarām vidyām vidhinā eva dvijottamāḥ mapāt eva na saṃdehaḥ vratānām vai viśeṣataḥ samāptiḥ na anyathā tasmāt japet pañcākṣarīm śubhām ūcuḥ katham pañcākṣarī vidyā prabhāvaḥ vā katham vada krama upāyam mahābhāga śrotum kautūhalam hi naḥ uvāca pārvatyāḥ kathitam puṇyam pravadāmi samāsatas uvāca pañcākṣarasya mahātmyam śrotum icchāmi tattvāt śrī bhagavant uvāca pañcākṣarasya mahātmyam varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api na śakyam kathitum devi śṛṇu naṣṭe devāsure ca eva naṣṭe ca uraga rākṣase sarvam prakṛtim āpannam tvayā pralayam eṣyati tasmin vedāḥ ca śāstrāṇi mantre pañca akṣare sthitāḥ te nāśam na eva saṃprāptāḥ mad śaktyā hi anupālitāḥ sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ śete devaḥ māyā mayīm tanum tad nābhi paṅkajāt jātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ sisṛkṣamāṇaḥ lokān vai trīn aśaktaḥ asahāyavān daśa brahmā sasarja ādau mānasān amita ojasaḥ teṣām sṛṣṭi prasiddhi artham mām provāca pitāmahaḥ mad putrāṇām mahādeva śaktim dehi maheśvaraiḥ pañca akṣarān pañca mukhaiḥ proktavan padmayonaye tān pañca vadanaiḥ gṛhṇan brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvena jñātavan parameśvaram vācyaḥ pañca akṣaraiḥ devi śivaḥ trailokya pūjitaḥ paramaḥ jñātvā prayogam vidhinā ca siddhim labdhvā tathā pañcamukhaḥ mahātmā te labdhvā mantra ratnam tu sākṣāt lokapitāmahāt tam ārādhayitum devam parātparataram śivam tatas tutoṣa bhagavant trimūrtīnām paraḥ śivaḥ dattavan akhilam jñāna maṇima ādi guṇa aṣṭakam te api labdhvā varān viprāḥ tad ārādhana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ mad priyaḥ satatam śrīmān mad bhūtaiḥ parirakṣitaḥ tasya abhyāśe tapaḥ tīvram loka sṛṣṭi samutsukāḥ divya varṣa sahasram tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran tiṣṭhantaḥ anugraha arthāya devi te ṛṣayaḥ purā teṣām bhaktim aham dṛṣṭvā sadyas pratyakṣatām iyām pañcākṣaram ṛṣicchandau daivatam śakti bījavat nyāsam ṣaḍaṅgam digbandham viniyogam aśeṣatas proktavan aham āryāṇām lokānām hita kāmyayā tat śrutvā mantra māhātmyam ṛṣayaḥ te tapodhanāḥ mantrasya viniyogam ca kṛtvā sarvam anuṣṭhitāḥ tad māhātyāt tad ālokān sa deva asura mānuṣān varṇān varṇa vibhāgān ca sarva dharmān ca śobhanān pañcākṣara prabhāvāt ca lokāḥ vedāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ tiṣṭhanti śāśvatāḥ dharmāḥ devāḥ sarvam idam jagat tat itānīm pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu ca avahita akhilam alpa akṣaram mahārtham ca veda sāram vimukti dam mājñā siddham asaṃdigdham vākyam etat śiva ātmakam nānā siddhi yutam divyam loka citta anurañjakam su niścita artham gambhīram vākyam mama pārameśvaram tat bījam sarva vidyānām mantram ādyam su śojakam ati sūkṣmam mahā artham ca jñeyam tat vaṭa bīja vat vedaḥ sa triguṇa atītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva kṛt prabhuḥ om iti ekākṣaram mantram sthitaḥ sarva gataḥ śivaḥ mantre ṣaṣ akṣare sūkṣme pañca akṣara tanuḥ śivaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvena sthitaḥ sākṣāt svabhāvataḥ vācyaḥ śivaḥ prameya tvāt mantraḥ tad vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ yamana ādiḥ saṃsthitaḥ tayoḥ vede śiva āgame vā api yatra yatra ṣaāḍakṣaraḥ mantraḥ sthitaḥ sadā mukhyaḥ loke pañca akṣaraḥ mataḥ yasya evam hṛdi saṃsthaḥ iyam mantraḥ syāt pārameśvaraḥ tena adhītam śrutam tena tena sarvam anuṣṭhitam etāvat hi śiva jñānam etāvat paramam padam pañca akṣaraiḥ sa praṇavaḥ mantraḥ iyam hṛdayam mama guhyāt guhyataram sākṣāt mokṣa jñānam anuktamam bījam śaktim svaram varṇam sthānam ca eva akṣaram prati vāmadevaḥ nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiḥ chandaḥ udāhṛtaḥ devatā śivaḥ eva aham mantrasya asya varānane nakāra ādīni bījāni pañcabhūta ātmakāni ca tvadīyam praṇavam kiñcid madīyam praṇavam tathā tvadīyam devīm mantrāṇām śakti bhūtam na saṃśayaḥ akāra ukāra makārāḥ madīye praṇave sthitāḥ ukāram ca makāram ca akāram ca krameṇa vai oṃkārasya svara udāttaḥ ṛṣiḥ brahma sitam vapuḥ chandaḥ devī ca gāyatrī paramātma adhidevatā pañcamaḥ svaritaḥ ca eva madhyamaḥ niṣadhaḥ smṛtāḥ nakāraḥ pīta varṇaḥ ca sthānam pūrva mukham smṛtam indraḥ adhidaivatam chandaḥ gāyatrī gautamaḥ ṛṣiḥ makāraḥ kṛṣma varṇaḥ asya sthānam vai dākṣiṇāmukham chandaḥ anuṣṭubh ṛṣiḥ ca atrī rudraḥ daivatam ucyate śikāraḥ dhūmra varṇaḥ usya sthānam vai paścimam mukham viśvāmitraḥ ṛṣiḥ triṣṭubh chandaḥ viṣṇuḥ tu daivatam brahma adhidaivatam chandaḥ bṛhatī ca aṅgirāḥ ṛṣiḥ yakāraḥ rakta varṇaḥ ca sthānum ūrdhvam mukham virāj brahmacāri gṛhasthānām yatīnām kramaśas bhavet utpattiḥ brahmacārīṇām gṛhasthānām sthitiḥ sadā yatīnām saṃhṛtiḥ nyāsaḥ siddhiḥ bhavati na anyathā aṅga nyāsaḥ kara nyāsaḥ deha nyāsaḥ iti tridhā aṅganyāsam tatas paścāt akṣarāṇām vidhi kramāt pāda ādi mūrdha paryantam saṃhāraḥ bhavati priye hṛdaya āsya gala nyāsaḥ sthiti nyāsaḥ udāhṛtaḥ brahmacāri gṛhasthānām yatīnām ca eva śobhane sa śiraskam tatas deham sarvamantreṇa saṃspṛśet dakṣiṇa aṅguṣṭham ārabhya vāma aṅguṣṭha ante eva hi aṅguṣṭha ādi kaniṣṭhā antam nyasyate hastayoḥ dviyoḥ atīva bhoga daḥ devī sthiti nyāsaḥ kuṭumbinām kara nyāsam purā kṛttvā taram aṅganyāsam nyaset paścāt eṣa sādhāraṇaḥ vidhiḥ oṃkāram saṃpuṭīkṛtya sarva aṅgeṣu ca vinyaset karayoḥ ubhayayoḥ ca eva daśa agrām guliṣu kramāt prakṣālya pādau ācamya śuciḥ bhūtvā samāhitaḥ prāc mukha udak mukhaḥ vā api nyāsa karma samācaret smaret pūrvam ṛṣin chandaḥ daivatam bījam eva ca śaktim ca paramātmānam gurum ca eva varānane mantreṇa pāṇī saṃmṛjya talayoḥ praṇavam nyaset aṅgulīnām ca sarveṣām tathā ca ādi anta parvasu ubhābhyām eva pāṇibhyām āpādatalamastakam mantreṇa saṃspṛśet deham praṇavena eva saṃpuṭam kṛtvā aṅganyāsam evam hi mukhāni parikalpayet bhavat aṅgāni nyaset paścāt yathāsthānam ca śobhanam namaḥ svāhā vaṣaṭ hum ca vai ṣaṣ phaṭkārakaiḥ saha praṇavam hṛdayam vidyāt nakāraḥ śiraḥ ucyate śikhā makāraḥ ākhyātaḥ śikāraḥ kavacam tathā vākāraḥ netram astram tu yakāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ māgneya ādiṣu koṇeṣu caturṣu api yathākramam aṅguṣṭha tarjanī agrābhyām saṃsthāpya su mukham śubham gale madhye tathā aṅguṣṭhe tarjanī ādyā aṅgulīṣu ca aṅguṣṭhena kara nyāsam kuryāt eva vicakṣaṇaḥ evam nyāsam imam proktam sarva pāpa haram śubham sarva siddhi karam puṇyam sarva rakṣā karam śivam janma antara kṛtam pāpam api naśyati tad kṣaṇāt evam vinyasya medhāvī śuddha kāyaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ japet pañcākṣaram mantram labdhvā ācārya prasādāt atas param pravakṣyāmi mantra saṃgrahaṇam śubhe yam vinā niṣphalam nityam yena vā saphalam bhavet ājñā hīnam kriyā hīnam śraddhā hīnam amānasam ājñaptam dakṣiṇā hīnam sadā japtam ca niṣphalam mānasam evam ca dakṣiṇā siddham mantram siddham yatas tatas jñāninam sat guṇa upetam dhyāna yoga parāyaṇam pūjayet śiṣyaḥ sarvadā ati prayatnāt hasti aśva ratha ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāni ca bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni vividhāni ca vitta śāṭhyam na kurvīta yadi icchet siddhim ātmanaḥ mantram jñānam ca eva krameṇa tu evam tuṣṭaḥ guruḥ śiṣyam pūjitam vatsara uṣitam śuśrūṣum anahaṅkāram upavāsa kṛśam śucim snāpayitvā tu siṣyāya brāhmaṇān api pūjya ca samudra tīre nadyām ca goṣṭhe devālaye api vā śivam ca astu śubham ca astu śobhanau astu priyau astu iti evam labdhvā param mantram jñānam ca eva guroḥ tatas anaśran tad paraḥ bhūtvā sa yāti paramām gatim japet akṣara lakṣam vai catur guṇitam ādarāt nakta āsī saṃyamī yaḥ ca pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ puraścaraṇa jāpī vā api vā nitya jāpakaḥ yaḥ puraścaraṇam kṛtvā nitya jāpī bhavet naraḥ maunī ca ekāgra mānasaḥ mādya antayoḥ japasya api kuryāt vai prāṇasaṃyamān tathā ca ante japet bījam śatam aṣṭa uttaram śubham catvāriṃśat samāvṛtti prāṇān āyamya saṃsmaret pañca akṣarasya mantrasya prāṇāyāmaḥ udāhṛtaḥ prāṇāyāmāt bhavet kṣipram sarva pāpa parikṣayaḥ indriyāṇām vaśi tvam ca tasmāt prāṇān ca saṃyamet gṛhe japaḥ samam vidyāt goṣṭhe śataguṇam bhavet nadyām śata sahasram tu anantaḥ śiva saṃnidhau puṇya āśrameṣu sarveṣu japaḥ koṭi guṇaḥ bhavet aṅgulī japa saṃkhyānam ekam ekam śubha ānane śatam vai śaṅkha maṇibhiḥ pravalaiḥ ca sahasrakam padmākṣaiḥ daśa lakṣam tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭiḥ ucyate pañcaviṃśati mokṣa artham saptaviṃśati pauṣṭikam triṃśat ca dhana saṃpattyai pañcāśat ca ābhicārikam tad pūrva abhimukham vaśyam dakṣiṇam ca ābhicārikam paścimam dhanadam vidyāt uttaram śāntikam bhavet aṅguṣṭham mokṣa dam vidyāt tarjanī śatru nāśanā madhyamā dhanadā śāntim karoti eṣā hi anāmikā kaniṣṭhā rakṣaṇīyā sā japa karmaṇi śobhane aṅguṣṭhena vinā karma kṛtam tat aphalam yatas śṛṇuṣva sarva yajñebhyaḥ japa yajñaḥ viśiṣyate yāvantaḥ karma yajñāḥ syuḥ pradānāni tapāṃsi ca sarve te japa yajñasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm tasmāt śataguṇa upāṃśuḥ sahasraḥ mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ yat ucca nīca svaritaiḥ śabdaiḥ spaṣṭa pada akṣaraiḥ mantram uccārayet vācā japa yajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ śanais uccārayet mantram īṣat eṣṭhau tu cālayet kiñcid karṇa antaram vidyāt upāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ dhyā yat akṣara śreṇyā varṇāt varṇam padāt padam śabda artham cintayet bhūyas sa tu uktaḥ mānasaḥ japaḥ trayāṇām japa yajñānām śreyāḥ syāt uttara uttaraḥ bhavet yajña viśeṣeṇa vaiśiṣṭyam tad phalasya ca hi nityam stūyamānā prasīdati prasannā vipulān bhogān dadyāt muktim ca śāśvatām yakṣa rakṣaḥ piśācāḥ ca grahāḥ sarve ca bhīṣaṇāḥ jāpinam na upasarpanti bhaya bhītāḥ samantataḥ yat tat kṛtam janma paraṃparāsu evam labdhvā śivam jñānam jñātvā japa vidhi kramam sat ācārī japan nityam dhyāyan bhadram samaśnute yasmāt ācāra hīnasya sādhanam niṣphalam bhavet ācāraḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ ācāraḥ paramantapaḥ ācāraḥ paramā vidyā ācāraḥ paramā gatiḥ sat ācāravatām puṃsām sarvatra api abhayam bhavet tadvat ācāra hīnānām sarvatra eva bhayam bhavet sat ācāreṇa deva tvam ṛṣi tvam ca varānane ninditaḥ śuddhi bhūyiṣṭhaḥ pāpīyān jñāna dūṣakaḥ varṇa āśrama vidhāna uktam dharmam kurvīta yatnatas saṃdhyā upāsana śīlaḥ syāt sāyam prātar prasanna dhīḥ udaya astamayāt pūrvam āramya vidhinā śuciḥ kāmāt mohāt bhayāt lobhāt saṃdhyām na atikramet dvijaḥ saṃdhyā atikramaṇāt vipraḥ brāhmaṇyāt patate yatas anṛtam paruṣam śāṭhyam paiśunyam pāpa hetukam para dārān para dravyam para hiṃsām ca sarvadā kvacid ca api na kurvīta vācā ca manasā tathā śūdra annam yātayāma annam naivedyam śrāddham eva ca gaṇa annam samudāya annam rāja annam ca vivarjayet rāja pratigrahaiḥ dagdhān brāhmaṇān brahma vādinaḥ svinnānām api bījānām punarjanma na vidyate a snātvā na ca bhuñjīyāt a japa ugnim a pūjya ca parṇa pṛṣṭhe na bhuñjīyāt rātrau dīpam vinā tathā bhinna bhāṇḍe ca rathyāyām patitānām ca saṃnidhau śūdra śeṣam na bhuñjīyāt saha annam śisukaiḥ api śuddha annam snigdham aśrīyāt saṃskṛtam ca abhimantritam bhoktā śivaḥ iti smṛtvā maunī ca ekāgra mānasaḥ māsyena na pibet toyam tiṣṭhan añjalinā api vā vāma hastena śayyāyām tathā eva anyaṃkareṇa vā vibhītaka arka kārañja snuhī chāyām na ca āśrayet stambha dīpa manuṣyāṇām anyeṣām praṇinām tathā na avaroheta kūpa ādim na ārohet ucca pādapān sūrya agni jala devānām gurūṇām vimukhaḥ śubhe na kuryāt iha kāryāṇi japa karma śubhāni vā agnau na tāpayet pādau hastam padbhyām na saṃspṛśet na jalam tāḍayet padbhyām na ambhasi aṅga malam tyajet malam prakṣālayet tīre prakṣālya snānam ācaret aśrī karam manuṣyāṇām asuddham saṃspṛśet yadi aja aśvān akhara uṣṭrāṇām mārjanāt tupa reṇukān mūḍha ātmā śriyam hanti hareḥ api tat cāṇḍāla samam jñeyam na atra kāryā avicāraṇā sphic vātam śūrpa vātam ca vātam prāṇa mukha anilam sukṛtāni haranti ete saṃspṛṣṭāḥ puruṣasya tu uṣṇīṣī kañcukī nagnaḥ mukta keśaḥ mala āvṛtaḥ krodhaḥ madaḥ kṣudhā tandrā niṣṭhīvana vijṛṃbhaṇe śva nīca darśanam nidrā pralāpāḥ te japa dviṣaḥ eteṣām saṃbhave vā api kuryāt sūrya ādi darśanam ācamya vā japet śeṣam kṛtvā vā prāṇasaṃyamam sūrya ugniḥ candramāḥ ca eva graha nakṣatra tārakāḥ ete jyotīṃṣi proktāni vidvadbhiḥ bāhmaṇaiḥ tathā anāsanaḥ śayānaḥ vā rathyāyām śūdra sannidhau rakta bhūmau ca khaṭvāyām na japet jāpakaḥ tathā kauśeyam vyāghra carmam vā cailam taulam atha api vā dāravam tāla parṇam vā āsanam parikalpayet trisaṃdhyam tu guroḥ pūjā kartavyā hitam icchatā yaḥ guruḥ sa śivaḥ proktaḥ yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ yathā śivaḥ tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ sa guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ vā api tasya ājñām śirasā vahet śreyaḥ ūrthi yaḥ tu guru ājñām manasā api na laṅghayet guru ājñā pālakaḥ samyak jñāna saṃpattim aśnute guroḥ deva samakṣam vā na yathā iṣṭa āsanaḥ bhavet guruḥ devaḥ yatas sākṣāt tat gṛham deva mandiram pāpinā ca yata āsaṅgāt tad pāpaiḥ patanam bhavet tathā eva guru saṃparkāt pāpam tyajati mānavaḥ tathā pāpam vilīyeta ācāryasya samīpatas yathā prajvalitaḥ vahniḥ viṣṭhā kāṣṭham ca nirdahet guruḥ tuṣṭaḥ dahati evam pāpam tat mantra tejasā kurvanti anugraham tuṣṭāḥ gurau tuṣṭe na saṃśayaḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā guroḥ krodham na kārayet tasya krodhena dahyante tad krodham ye kariṣyanti teṣām yajñāḥ ca niṣphalāḥ mantrāṇi aniyamāḥ ca eva na atra kāryā vicāraṇā guroḥ hitam priyam kuryāt ādiṣṭaḥ vā na vā sadā asamakṣam samakṣam vā guroḥ kāryam samācaret evam ācāravān bhaktaḥ nityam japa parāyaṇaḥ yasya yena viyuñjīta kāryeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ rājya aiśvaryam ca vijñānam svargaḥ nirvāṇe eva ca prokṣaṇam ca abhiṣekam ca aghamarṣaṇam eva ca snāne ca saṃdhyayoḥ ca eva kuryāt ekādaśena vai mahānadyām dvi lakṣam tu dīrgham āyuḥ avāpnuyāt dūrvā aṅkurāḥ tilāḥ vāṇī guḍūcī guṭikā tathā teṣām tu daśa sāhasram homam āyuṣya vardhanam aśvattha vṛkṣam āśritya japet lakṣa dvayam sudhīḥ śanaiścara dine spṛṣṭvā dīrgha yuṣyam labhet naraḥ śanaiścara dine aśvattham pāṇibhyām saṃspṛśet sudhīḥ mukhaḥ bhūtvā japet lakṣam an anya dhīḥ samasta vyādhi śānti artham palāśa samidhaiḥ naraḥ bhuñjīyāt annam ca eva abhimantritam bhakṣyam ca anyat tathā peyam viṣam api amṛtam bhavet japet lakṣam tu pūrvāhṇe hutvā ca aṣṭaśatena vai nadī toyena saṃpūrṇam ghaṭam saṃspṛśya śobhanam japtvā ayutam ca tad snānāt rogāṇām bheṣajam bhavet aṣṭāviṃśat japitvā annam aśrīyāt anvaham śuciḥ hutvā ca tāvat pālaśaiḥ evam vā ārogyam aśnute candra sūrya grahe pūrvam upoṣya vidhinā śuciḥ yāvat grahaṇa mokṣam tu tāvat nadyām samāhitaḥ pibet brāhmī rasam dvijāḥ hikām labhate medhām sarva śāstra dharām śubhām sārasvatī bhavet devī tasya vāc ati mānuṣā graha nakṣatra pīḍāsu japet bhaktyā ayutam naraḥ hutvā ca aṣṭa sahasram tu grahapīḍām vyapohati duḥsvapna darśane snātvā japet vai ca ayutam naraḥ ghṛte na aṣṭaśatam hutvā sadyas śāntiḥ bhaviṣyati saṃnidhau devasya śuciḥ saṃyata mānasaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti puruṣaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ gajānām turagāṇām tu go jātīnām viśeṣataḥ vyādhi āgame śuciḥ bhūtvā juhuyāt samidh āhutim teṣām ṛddhiḥ ca śāntiḥ ca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ utpāte śatru bādhāyām juhuyāt ayutam śuciḥ pālāśa samidhaiḥ devi tasya śāntiḥ bhaviṣyati mābhicārika bādhāyām etat devi samācaret pratyak bhavati tad śaktiḥ śatroḥ pīḍā bhaviṣyati juhuyāt viṣeṇa rudhira abhyaktaḥ vidveṣāṇa karam nṝṇām prayās cittam pravakṣyāmi sarva pāpa a viśuddhaye pāpa śuddhiḥ na ced puṃsaḥ kriyāḥ sarvāḥ ca niṣphalāḥ tasmāt kartavyam pāpa śodhanam vidyā lakṣmī viśuddhi artham mām dhyātvā añjalinā śubhe śivena ekā daśena adbhiḥ abhiṣiñcet samantataḥ aṣṭottaraśatena eva snāyāt pāpa viśuddhaye saṃdhyā upāsana vicchede japet aṣṭaśatam naraḥ viḍvarāhaiḥ ca cāṇḍālaiḥ durjanaiḥ kukkuṭaiḥ api spṛṣṭam annam na bhuñjīta bhuktvā ca aṣṭaśatam japet brahmahatyā viśuddhi artham japet lakṣa ayutam naraḥ pātakānām tad ardham syāt na atra kāryā vicāraṇā upapātaka duṣṭānām tad ardham parikīrtitam śeṣāṇām api pāpānām japet pañca sahasrakam ātma bodha param guhyam śiva bodha prakāśakam japet japet ca pañca lakṣam tu vigṛhīta indriyaḥ śuciḥ pañca indriyāṇām vijayaḥ bhaviṣyati varānane viṣayāṇām ca pañcānām jayam prāpnoti mānavaḥ bhūtānām iha pañcānām vijayam manujaḥ labhet samyak vijayam āpnoti karaṇānām varānane pañcaviṃśati lakṣāṇām japena kamala ānane pañcaviṃśati tattvānām vijayam manujaḥ labhet madhyarātre ca śivayoḥ paśyati eva na saṃśayaḥ andhakāra vināśaḥ ca dīpasya iva prakāśanam hṛdaya antar bahis vā api bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ sa bīja sampuṭam mantram śata lakṣam japet śuciḥ iti te sarvam ākhyātam pañca akṣara vidhi kramam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api sa yāti paramām gatim śravayet ca dvijān śuddhān pañcākṣara vidhi kramam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge pañcākṣaramāhātmyam nāma pañcāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ prāhuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ viraktānām prabuddhānām dhyāna yajñam su śobhanam tasmāt vadasva sūtaiḥ adya dhyāna yajñam aśeṣatas vistārāt sarva yatnena viraktānām mahātmanām teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā munīnām dīrgha sattriṇām rudreṇa kathitam prāha guhām prāpya mahātmanām saṃhṛtya kālakūṭa ākhyam viṣam vai viśvakarmaṇā uvāca guhām prāpya sukha āsīnam bhavānyā saha śaṃkaram munayaḥ saṃśita ātmānaḥ preṇamuḥ tam guhā āśrayam astuvan ca tatas sarve nīlakaṇṭham umāpatim ati ugram kālakūṭa ākhyam saṃhṛtam bhagavan tvayā atas pratiṣṭhitam sarvam tvayā deva vṛṣadhvaja teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā bhagavān nīlalohitaḥ kim anena dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ viṣam vakṣye su dāruṇam na viṣam kālakūṭa ākhyam saṃsāraḥ viṣam ucyate saṃsāraḥ dvividhaḥ proktaḥ sva adhikāra anurūpataḥ puṃsām saṃmūḍha cittānām asaṃkṣīṇaḥ su dāruṇaḥ sargaḥ jñānena suvratāḥ tad vaśāt eva sarveṣām dharma adharmau na saṃśayaḥ asat nikṛṣṭe tu arthe api śāstram tad śravaṇāt satām buddhim utpādayati eva saṃsāre vidvasām dvijāḥ tasmāt dṛṣṭa ānuśravikam duṣṭam iti ubhaya ātmakam śāstram iti ucyate abhāgam śruteḥ karmasu tat dvijāḥ mūrdhānam brahmaṇaḥ sāram ṛṣīṇām karmaṇaḥ phalam nanu svabhāvaḥ sarveṣām kāmaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca anyathā śrutuḥ pravartakā teṣām iti karmaṇya tā dvidaḥ nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ samarthānām miha ucyate tasmāt ajñāna mūlaḥ hi saṃsāraḥ sarva dehinām kalā saṃśoṣam āyāti karmaṇā anya svabhāvataḥ nārakī pāpa kṛt svargī puṇya kṛt puṇya gairavāt vyatimiśreṇa vai jīvaḥ caturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ udbhijaḥ sveda jaḥ ca eva aṇḍa jaḥ vai jarāyu jaḥ evam vyavasthitaḥ dehī karmaṇā ajñaḥ hi anirvṛtaḥ evam ajñāna doṣeṇa nānā karma vaśena ca bhajati eṣa kalevaram vicārāt satām duḥkham strī saṃsarga ādi bhī dvijāḥ duḥkhena ekena vai duḥkham praśāmyanti iha duḥkhinaḥ na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānam upabhogena śāmyati haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā iva bhūyas eva abhivardhate tasmāt vicārataḥ na asti saṃyogāt api vai nṛṇām paiśāce rākṣase duḥkham yākṣe ca eva prājāpatye tathā brāhme prākṛte pauruṣe tathā kṣaya sātiśaya ādyaiḥ tu duḥkhaiḥ duḥkhāni suvratāḥ tāni bhāgyāni aśuddhāni saṃtyajet ca dhanāni ca tasmāt aṣṭaguṇam bhogam tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitam caturviśat prakāreṇa saṃsthitam ca api suvratāḥ dvātriṃśat bhedam anaghāḥ catvāriṃśadguṇam punar tathā aṣṭacatvāriṃśat ca ṣaṭpañcaṭāśat prakārāt catuḥṣaṣṭividham ca eva duḥkham eva vivekinaḥ pārthivam ca tathā āpyam ca taijasam ca vicārāt ābhimānikam api evam bauddham prākṛtam eva ca duḥkham eva na saṃdehaḥ yoginām brahma vādinām gauṇam gaṇa īśvarāṇām ca duḥkham eva vicārāt tamānāni duḥkhāni bhaviṣyāṇi yathātatham doṣa duṣṭeṣu deśeṣu duḥkhāni vividhāni ca na bhāvayanti atītāni hi ajñāne jñāna māninaḥ kṣudh vyādheḥ parihāra artham na sukhāya annam ucyate yathā itareṣām rogāṇām auṣadham na sukhāya tat śīta uṣṇa vāta varṣa ādyaiḥ tad tad kāleṣu dehinām duḥkham eva na saṃdehaḥ na jānānti hi apaṇḍitāḥ svarge api evam muni śreṣṭhāḥ hi aviśuddha kṣaya ādibhiḥ rogauḥ nānāvidhaiḥ grastāḥ rāga dveṣa bhaya ādibhiḥ puṇya vṛkṣa kṣayāt tadvat gām patanti divaukasaḥ duḥkha abhilāṣa niṣṭhānām duḥkha bhoga ādi saṃpadām asmāt tu patatām duḥkham kaṣṭam svargāt divaukasām narake duḥkham eva atra nākānām niṣevaṇāt vihita akaraṇāt ca eva varṇinām muni puṃgavāḥ evam yatiḥ dhyāna paraḥ mahātmā saṃsāra bhītaḥ na labheta nidrām kīṭa pakṣi mṛgāṇām ca paśūnām gaja vājinām dṛṣṭam eva asukham tasmāt tyajataḥ sukham uttamam vaimānikānām api evam duḥkham kalpa adhikāriṇām sthāna abhimāninām ca eva manu ādīnām ca suvratāḥ devānām ca eva daityānām anyonya vijigīṣayā duḥkham eva nṛpāṇām ca rākṣasāṇām jagattraye śrama artham āśramaḥ ca api varṇānām paramārthāt na ca devaiḥ ca yajñaḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ vrataiḥ tathā bhasma śāyī bhavet nityam vrate pāśupate budhaḥ pañcārtha jñāna saṃpannaḥ śivatattve samāhitaḥ pañcārtha yoga saṃpannaḥ duḥkha antam vrajate sudhīḥ śikṣā kalpaḥ vyākaraṇam niruktam chandaḥ eva ca jyotiṣam ca aparā vidyā para akṣaram iti sthitam tat adṛśyam tat agrāhyam agotram tat avarṇakam tat a cakṣuḥ tat a śrotram tat a pāṇi a pādakam tat ajātam abhūtam ca tat aśabdam dvijottamāḥ avyayam ca apratiṣṭham ca tat nityam sarvagam vibhum mahāntam tad gṛham tam ca tat ajam cit mayam dvijāḥ asaṃvṛtam tat ātmā ekam parā vidyā na ca anyathā mattaḥ na anyat iti īkṣeta manaḥ vāc pāṇibhiḥ tathā sarvam ātmani saṃpaśyet sat ca asat ca samāhitaḥ adhas dṛṣṭyā vitastyām tu nābhyām upari tiṣṭhati hṛdayam tat vijānīyāt viśvasya āyatanam mahat dharma kanda samudbhūtam jñāna nālam su śobhanam aiśvarya aṣṭadalam śvetam param vairāgya karṇikam chidrāṇi ca diśaḥ yasya prāṇa ādyāḥ ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ prāṇa ādyaiḥ ca eva saṃyuktaḥ paśyate bahudhā kramāt daśa prāṇa vahāḥ nāḍyaḥ pratyekam muni puṃgavāḥ saṃparikīrtitāḥ netra sthan jāgrantam vidyāt kaṇṭhe svapnam samādiśet suṣuptam hṛdaya stham tu turīyam mūrdhani sthitam jāgre brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca svapne ca eva yathākramāt īśvaraḥ tu suṣupte tu turīye ca maheśvaraḥ ma ṇa na u buddhiḥ ahaṃkāram cittam ca u ti catuṣṭayam karaṇāni vilīnāni yadā sva ātmani suvratāḥ paraḥ turīya atītaḥ asau śivaḥ parama kāraṇam buddhīndriyāṇi vipra indrāḥ tathā karmendriyāṇi ca manaḥ buddiḥ ahaṅkāraḥ cittam ca iti catuṣṭayam adhyātmam pṛthak eva idam caturdaśavidham smṛtam draṣṭavyam ca eva śrotavyam ghrātavyam ca yathākramam rasitavyam muni śreṣṭhāḥ sparśitavyam tathā eva ca tathā cetayitavyam ca vaktavyam muni puṃgavāḥ mādityaḥ api diśaḥ ca eva pṛthivī varuṇaḥ tathā vāyuḥ candraḥ tathā brahmā rudraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ eva ca rājñī sudarśanā ca eva jitā saumyā yathākramam moghā rudra amṛtā satyā madhyamā ca dvijottamāḥ nāḍī rāśi śukā ca eva asurā ca eva kṛttikā bhāsvatī nāḍayaḥ ca etāḥ caturdaśa nibandhanāḥ vāyavaḥ nāḍi madhya sthāḥ vāhakāḥ ca caturdaśa prāṇaḥ vyānaḥ tu apānaḥ ca udānaḥ ca samānakaḥ kūrmakaḥ ca tathā śyenaḥ śvetaḥ kṛṣmaḥ tathā anilaḥ yaḥ cakṣuṣu atha draṣṭavye tathā āditye ca suvratāḥ nāḍyām prāṇe ca vijñāne tu ānande ca yathākramam ca carati tam upāsīta mām prabhum eṣa sarva adhipaḥ devaḥ tu antaryāmī mahā dyutiḥ upāsyamānaḥ vedaiḥ ca śāstraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ api na vā eṣa veda śāstrāṇi sarvajñe yāsyati prabhuḥ sva ātmanā rakṣitam ca adyāt anna bhūtam na kutracid sarvatra prāṇinām annam prāṇinām granthiḥ asmi aham praśāstā nayanaḥ ca eva pañca ātmā sa vibhāgaśaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ ca indriya ātmā saṃkalpa ātmā manaḥ mayaḥ kāla ātmā somaḥ eva iha vijñāna mayaḥ ucyate sadānanda mayaḥ bhūtvā maheśaḥ parameśvaraḥ na prajñāna ghanaḥ tu evam na prājñaḥ jñāna pūrvakaḥ viditam na asti vedyam ca nirvāṇam paramārthāt nirvāṇam ca eva kaivalyam niḥśreyasam anāmayam amṛtam ca akṣaram brahma paramātmā parāparam nirvikalpam nirābhāsam jñānam paryāya vācakam prasannam ca yat ekāgram tadā jñānam iti smṛtam ajñānam itarat sarvam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā rāga dveṣa anṛta krodham kāma tṛṣṇā ādibhiḥ sadā aparāmṛṣṭam adya eva vijñeyam mukti dam tu idam ajñāna mala pūrva tvāt puruṣaḥ malinaḥ smṛtaḥ bhānam ekam vinā na asti puṇya pāpa parikṣayaḥ jñāna abhyāsāt hi vai puṃsām buddhiḥ bhavati nirmalā tasmāt sadā abhyaset jñānam tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ jñāna abhyāsa rataḥ nityam jñāna tattva artha vid svayam varṇa āśrama abhimānī yaḥ tyakta krodhaḥ dvijottamāḥ anyatra ramate mūḍhaḥ saḥ ajñānī na atra saṃśayaḥ saṃsāra hetuḥ ajñānam saṃsāraḥ tanu saṃgrahaḥ mokṣa hetuḥ tathā jñānam muktaḥ sva ātmani avasthitaḥ ajñāne sati vipra indrāḥ krodha ādyāḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ dharma adharmau hi teṣām ca tad vaśāt tanu saṃgrahaḥ śarīre sati vai kleśaḥ saḥ vidyām saṃtyajet budhaḥ krodha ādyāḥ nāśam āyānti dharma adharmau ca vai dvijāḥ tad kṣayāt ca śarīreṇa na punar saṃprayujyate saḥ eva muktaḥ saṃsārāt duḥkha traya vivarjitaḥ evam jñānam vinā na asti dhyānam dhyātuḥ dvijarṣabhāḥ jñānam guroḥ hi saṃparkāt na vācā paramārthāt catur vyūham iti jñātvā dhyātā dhyānam samabhyaset sahaja āgantukam pāpam asthi vāc udbhavam tathā jñāna agniḥ dahate kṣipram suṣka indhanam iva analaḥ jñānāt parataram na asti sarva pāpa vināśanam abhyaset ca sadā jñānam sarva saṅga vivarjitaḥ jñāninaḥ sarva pāpāni jīryante na atra saṃśayaḥ yathā tathā dhyānam tasmāt dhyānam samabhyaset dhyānam nirviṣayam proktam ādau sa viṣayam tathā ṣaṣ prakāram samabhyasya cutaḥ ṣaṣ daśabhiḥ tathā tathā dvādaśadhā ca eva punar ṣoḍaśadhā kramāt śuddha jāmbūnada ākāram vadhūma aṅgāra saṃnibham ahiṃsakaḥ satya vādī asteyī sarva yatnāt saṃtuṣṭaḥ śauca saṃpannaḥ svādhyāya nirataḥ sadā na budhyati tathā dhyātā sthāpya cittam dvijottamāḥ na ghrāti na śṛṇoti eva līnaḥ sva ātmani yaḥ svayam na ca sparśam vijānāti sa vai samarasaḥ smṛtaḥ kālarudra ākhyaḥ vāyu tattve maheśvaraḥ suṣire sa śivaḥ sākṣāt kramāt evam vicintayet tau śarvaḥ smṛtaḥ devaḥ hi apām bhave iti smṛtaḥ bhīmaḥ suṣira nāke asau bhāskare maṇḍale sthitaḥ īśānaḥ soma biṃve ca mahādevaḥ iti smṛtaḥ puṃsā paśupatiḥ devaḥ ca aṣṭadhā aham vyavasthitaḥ kāṭhinyam yat tanau sarvam pārthivam parigīyate yat saṃcarati tat vāyuḥ suṣiram yat dvijottamāḥ tat ākāśam ca vijñānam śabda jam vyoma saṃbhavam tathā eva viprāḥ vijñānam sparśa ākhyam vāyu sambhavam rūpam vāhneyam iti uktam āpyam rasa mayam dvijāḥ gandha ākhyam pārthivam bhūyas cintayet bhāskaram kramāt netre ca dakṣiṇe vāme somam hṛdi vibhum dvijāḥ bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bahni tattvam syāt lalāṭa antam dvijottamāḥ vāyavyam vai lalāṭa ādyam vyoma ākhyam vā śikhā agrakam na jīvaḥ prakṛtiḥ sattvam rajaḥ ca atha tamaḥ punar mahant tathā abhimānaḥ ca tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca vyoma ādīni ca bhūtāni na eva iha paramārthāt vyāpya tiṣṭhat yatas viśvam sthāṇuḥ iti abhidhīyate dadhāti bhūmiḥ ākāśam avakāśam dadāti ca tad ājñayā tatam sarvam tasmāt vai cintayet dvijāḥ tena eva adhiṣṭhitam tasmāt etat sarvam dvijottamāḥ saṃsāra viṣa taptānām jñāna dhyāna amṛtena vai pratīkāraḥ samākhyātaḥ na anyathā dvijasattamāḥ jñānam dharma udbhavam sākṣat jñānāt vairāgya saṃbhavaḥ vairāgyāt paramam jñānam paramārtha prakāśakam yoga siddhyā vimuktiḥ syāt sattva niṣṭhasya na anyathā sattva śaktim samāsthāya śivam abhyarcayet dvijāḥ sarvatas dharma niṣṭhaḥ ca sadā utsāhī samāhitaḥ mṛju svabhāvaḥ satatam svastha cittaḥ mṛduḥ sadā amānī buddhimān śāntaḥ tyakta spardhaḥ dvijottamāḥ sadā mumukṣuḥ dharma jñaḥ sva ātma lakṣaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ ṛṇa traya vinirmuktaḥ pūrva janmani puṇya bhāj jarā yuktaḥ dvijaḥ bhūtvā śraddhayā ca guroḥ kramāt anyathā vā api śuśrūṣām kṛtvā kṛtrima varjitaḥ āsādya bhāratam varṣam brahma vid jāyate dvijāḥ samparkāt jñānam āsādya jñāninaḥ yoga vid bhavet kramaḥ yam mala pūrṇasya jñāna prāpteḥ dvijottamāḥ tasmāt anena mārgeṇa tyakta saṃgaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ saṃsāra kālakūṭa ākhyāt mucyate muni puṃgavāḥ evam saṃkṣepāt proktam mayā vaḥ acyutam jñānasya eva iha māhātmyam prasaṃgāt iha śobhanam evam pāśupatam yogam kathitam tu īśvareṇa tu na deyam yasya kasya api śiva uktam muni puṃgavāḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api saṃsāra śamanam naraḥ sa yāti brahma sāyujyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge saṃsāraviṣakathanam nāma ṣaḍaśītimaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca niśamya te mahā prājñāḥ kumāra ādyāḥ pinākinam procuḥ praṇamya vai bhītāḥ prasannam parameśvaram uvāca evam uktaḥ prahasya īśaḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ prāhatām ambikām prekṣya praṇipatya sthitān dvijān akārtajñaḥ paśuḥ jīvaḥ vibhuḥ bhoktā hi aṇuḥ pumān māyī ca māyayā baddhaḥ karmabhiḥ yujyate tu saḥ jñānam dhyānam ca bandhaḥ ca mokṣaḥ na asti ātmanaḥ dvijāḥ eṣā vidyā hi aham vedyaḥ prajñā eṣā ca śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ dhṛtiḥ eṣā mayā niṣṭhā jñāna śaktiḥ kriyā tathā icchā ākhyā ca tathā hi ajñā dve vidye na ca saṃśayaḥ na hi eṣā prakṛtiḥ jaivī vikṛtiḥ ca vicārāt purā mama ajña mad vaktrāt samutpannā sanātanī tad pañcavaktrā mahābhāgā jagantām abhaya pradā tām ājñām saṃpraviśya aham cintayan jagatām hitam saptaviṃśat prakāreṇa sarvam vyāpya anayā śivaḥ uvāca evam uktvā tadā apaśyat bhavānīm parameśvaraḥ bhavānī ca tam ālokya māyām aharat avyayā te māyā mala nirmuktāḥ munayaḥ prekṣya pārvatīm prītāḥ babhūvuḥ muktāḥ ca tasmāt eṣā parā gatiḥ umā śaṃkarayoḥ bhedaḥ na asti eva paramārthāt dvidhā asau rūpam āsthāya sthitaḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ yadā vidvān asaṃgaḥ syāt ājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ tadā muktiḥ kṣaṇāt eva na anyathā karma koṭibhiḥ bhūta vivṛddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ prasādena kṣaṇāt muktiḥ pratijñā eṣā na saṃśayaḥ garbha sthaḥ jāyamānaḥ vā bālaḥ vā taruṇaḥ api vā vṛddhaḥ vā mucyate jantuḥ prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ prasādāt devadevasya na atra kāryā vicāraṇā eṣaḥ eva jagannāthaḥ bandha mokṣa karaḥ śivaḥ bhūḥ bhūvaḥ svar mahaḥ ca eva janaḥ sākṣāt tapaḥ svayam satya lokaḥ stathā aṇḍānām koṭi koṭi śatāni ca tathā anyeṣu ca lokeṣu vasanti ca cara acarāḥ sarve bhava aṃśa jāḥ nūnam gatiḥ tu eṣām saḥ eva vai viśvam bhūtam tathā jātam bahudhā rudraḥ eva saḥ rudra ājñā eṣā sthitā devī hi anayā muktiḥ ambikā iti evam khecarāḥ siddhāḥ jajalpuḥ prīta mānasāḥ yadā avalokya tān sarvān prasādāt anayā ambikā tadā tiṣṭhanti sāyujyam prāptāḥ te khecarāḥ prabhoḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge munimohaśamanam nāma saptāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ uvāca tad ṣaḍviṃśat śakti saṃyuktam aṣṭadhā ca dvijottamāḥ tatas ṣoḍaśadhā ca eva punar dvādaśadhā dvijāḥ aṣṭa śakti samāyuktam aṣṭamūrtim ajam prabhum tābhiḥ ca aṣṭavidhāḥ rudrāḥ catuḥṣaṣṭividhāḥ punar śaktayaḥ ca tathā sarvāḥ guṇa aṣṭaka samanvitāḥ evam pāśupatam yogam mokṣa siddhi pradāyakam tasya aṇina ādayaḥ viprāḥ na anyathā karma koṭibhiḥ tatra aṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam yoginām samudāhṛtam prākāmyam ca eva sarvatra īśitvam ca eva sarvatas tat ca api trividham jñeyam aiśvaryam sārvakāmikam sāvadyam nāma yat tatra pañcabhūta ātmakam smṛtam indriyāṇi manaḥ ca eva ahaṅkāraḥ ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ tatra sūkṣma pravṛttiḥ tu pañcabhūta ātmakā punar indriyāṇi manaḥ citta buddhi ahaṅkāra saṃjñitam punar aṣṭaguṇaḥ ca api sūkṣmeṣu eva vidhīyate tasya rūpam pravakṣyāmi yathā āha bhagavān prabhuḥ aṇima ādyam tathā avyaktam sarvatra eva pratiṣṭhitam trailokye sarva bhūtānām duṣprāpyam samudāhṛtam śīghra tvam sarva bhūteṣu dvitīyam tu padam smṛtam prākāmān viṣayān bhuṅkte tathā apratihataḥ kvacid vaśyāni ca asya bhūtāni trailokye sa carācare aṇu tvāt tu paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣma tvāt apavargikaḥ vyāpakaḥ tu apavargāt ca vyāpakāt puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ sūkṣma bhāvāt tu aiśvarye parame sthitaḥ aiśvaryam ca apratīghātam prāpya yogam anuttamam evam pāśupatam yogam jñātavyam muni puṃgavāḥ svarga apavarga phala dam śiva sāyujya kāraṇam athavā gata vijñānaḥ rāgāt karma samācaret rājasam tāsamam vā api bhuktvā tatra eva mucyate tasmāt sthānāt punar śreṣṭhaḥ mānuṣyam upapadyate pariśramaḥ hi yajñānām mahatā arthena vartate bhūyas mṛtyu vaśam yāti tasmāt mokṣaḥ param sukham dṛṣṭvā tu puruṣam divyam viśva ākhyam viśvatomukham viśva pāda śiraḥ grīvam viśveśam viśva rūpiṇam viśva gandham viśva mālyam viśva ambara dharam prabhum kavim purāṇam anusāsitāram sūkṣmāt ca sūkṣmam mahataḥ mahāntam aliṅginam nirguṇam cetanam ca nityam sadā sarva gam sarva sāram paśyanti yuktyā hi acala prakāśam tad bhāvitāḥ tejasā dīpyamānam hi atīndriyaḥ vā api su sūkṣmaḥ ekaḥ paśyati acakṣuḥ sa śṛṇoti akarṇaḥ na ca asti abuddham na ca buddhiḥ āsti tanām sarva gatām sūkṣmām prasava dharmiṇīm prakṛtim sarva bhūtānām yuktāḥ paśyanti yoginaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādam tat sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutiman loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati puruṣam sarva bhūtānām tam vidvān na vimuhyati bhūtātmānam mahātmānam paramātmānam avyayam strī puṃsoḥ saṃprayoge hi jāyate hi tatas prabhuḥ kālena kalalam ca api budvudam saṃprajāyate mṛd piṇḍaḥ tu yathā cakre cakra āvartena pīḍitaḥ evam ādhyātmikaiḥ yuktāḥ vāyunā saṃprapūritaḥ yāvat hi vaiṣṇavaḥ vāyuḥ jāta mātram na saṃspṛśet tāvat kālam mahādevam arcayāmi iti cintayet mānuṣaḥ tatra yathārūpam yathāvayas jalāt saṃbhavati prāṇaḥ prāṇāt śukram vivardhate rakta bhāgāḥ trayastriṃśat retaḥ bhāgāḥ caturdaśa pituḥ śarīrāt pratyaṅgam rūpam asya upajāyate tatas asya mātuḥ āhārāt pīta līḍha praveśanāt nābhi deśena vai prāṇāḥ te hi ādhārāḥ hi dehinām nava māsāt parīkliṣṭaḥ saṃveṣṭita śirodharaḥ praveśanaḥ nava māsa uṣitaḥ ca api yoni chidrāt avāṅmukhaḥ tāḍanam bhakṣaṇam ca eva pūya śoṇita bhakṣaṇam yathā hi apaḥ tu saṃchinnāḥ saṃśleṣmam upayānti vai tathā chinnāḥ ca bhinnāḥ ca yātanā sthānam āgatāḥ evam jīvāḥ tu tebhiḥ pāpaiḥ tapyamānāḥ svayaṅkṛtaiḥ prāpnuyuḥ karmabhiḥ śeṣaiḥ duḥkham vā yadi vā itarat te nityam yama viṣyeṣu saṃpravṛttāḥ krośantaḥ satatam aniṣṭa saṃprayogaiḥ śuṣyante su bhṛśam ananta yātanābhiḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā yat abhīkṣṇam niṣevate tad abhyāsaḥ harati enam tasmāt kalyāṇam ācaret anādimān prabandhaḥ syāt pūrva karmaṇi dehinaḥ saṃsāram tāmasam ghoram ṣaḍvidham pratipadyate mānuṣyāt paśu bhāvaḥ ca paśu bhāvāt mṛgaḥ bhavet mṛga tvāt pakṣi bhāvaḥ ca tasmāt ca eva sarīsṛpaḥ sarīsṛpa tvāt gacchet vai sthāvara tvam na saṃśayaḥ iti evam hi manuṣya ādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sthāvarātikaḥ sāttvikaḥ ca api saṃsāraḥ brahma ādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ piśāca antaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ svarga sthāneṣu dehinām caturdaśānām sthānānām madhye viṣṭaṃbhakam rajaḥ saṃsāraḥ pūrva dharmasya bhāvanābhiḥ praṇoditaḥ mānuṣam bhajate nityam tasmāt dhyānam samācaret nityam samārabhet dharmam saṃsāra bhaya pīḍitaḥ tathā samārabhet yogam yathā ātmānam sa paśyati eṣaḥ āpaḥ param jyotiḥ eṣa setuḥ anuttamaḥ vivṛtyāḥ hi eṣa saṃbheda adbhutānām ca eva śāśvataḥ hṛdistham sarva bhūtānām upāsīta maheśvaram tathā antar saṃsthitam devam sva śaktyā parimaṇḍitam aṣṭadhā ca aṣṭadhā ca eva tathā ca aṣṭavidhena ca sṛṣṭi artham saṃsthitam vahnim saṃkṣipya ca hṛdi sthitam dhyātvā yathāvat deveśam rudram bhuvana nāyakam hutvā pañca āhutīḥ samyak tad cintā gata mānasaḥ vaiśvānaram hṛdistham tu yathāvat anupūrvaśas apaḥ pūtāḥ sakṛt prāśya tūṣṇīm hutvā hi upāviśan prāṇāya iti tatas tasya prathamā hi āhutiḥ smṛtāḥ apānāya dvitīyā ca vyānāya iti tathā parā udānāya syāt samānāya uti pañcamī svāhākāraiḥ pṛthak hutvā śeṣam bhuñjīta kāmatas apaḥ punar sakṛt prāśya ācamya hṛdayam spṛśet prāṇānām granthiḥ asya ātmā rudraḥ hi ātmā viśa antakaḥ prāṇe niviṣṭaḥ vai rudraḥ tasmāt prāṇa mayaḥ svayam mām īśa svāhā brahma ātmane svayam evam pañca āhutīḥ ca eva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ tvam devānām asi cyeṣṭhaḥ rudraḥ tvam ca purovṛṣā iti evam kathitam sarvam guṇa prāpti viśeṣāt savasya jagataḥ ca eva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ tvam devānām asi jyeṣṭhaḥ rudraḥ tvam ca puras vṛṣā iti evam kathitam sarvam guṇa prāpti viśeṣāt yoga ācāraḥ svayam tena brahmaṇā kathitaḥ purā evam pāśupatam jñānam jñātavyam ca prayatnāt yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet vā dvijottamān iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge homa ādi varṇanam nāma aṣṭāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi śauca ācārasya lakṣaṇam yat anuṣṭhāya śuddha ātmā paretya gatim āpnuyāt brahmaṇā kathitam pūrvam sarva bhūta hitāya vai saṃkṣepāt sarva veda artham saṃcayam brahma vādinām udaya artham tu śaucānām munīnām uttamam padam māna avamānau dvau etau tau eva āhuḥ viṣa amṛte prāpya anujñām tatas ca eva jñāna yogam anuttamam cakṣuḥ pūtam caret mārgam vastra pūtam jalam pibet satya pūtam vadet vākyam manaḥ pūtam samācaret matsyagṛhyasya yat pāpam ṣaṣ māsa abhyantare bhavet eka aham tad samam jñeyam a pūtam yat jalam bhavet aghora lakṣaṇam mantram tatas śuddhim avāpnuyāt athavā pūjayet śaṃbhum ghṛta srāna ādi vistaraiḥ tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śuddhyate na atra saṃśayaḥ tathā yuktam caret bhaikṣyam satām dharmam a dūṣayan bhaikṣyam caret vanastheṣu yāyāvara gṛheṣu ca śreṣṭhā tu prathamā hi iyam vṛttiḥ asya upajāyate atas ūrdhvam gṛhastheṣu śīlīneṣu caret dvijāḥ śraddadhāneṣu dānteṣu śrotriyeṣu mahātmasu atas ūrdhvam punar ca api aduṣṭa apatiteṣu ca bhaikṣyam yavāgūḥ takram vā payaḥ yāvakam eva ca phala mūla ādi pakvam vā kaṇa piṇyāka saktavaḥ māhārāḥ teṣu siddheṣu śreṣṭham bhaikṣyam iti smṛtam ap vindum yaḥ kuśa agreṇa māsi māsi samaśnute nyāyāt yaḥ caret bhaikṣyam pūrva uktāt saḥ viśiṣyate dadhi bhakṣāḥ payaḥ bhakṣāḥ ye ca anye jīva kṣīṇakāḥ sarve te bhaikṣya bhakṣasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm bhasma śāyī bhavet nityam bhikṣā cārī jita indriyaḥ yaḥ icchet paramam sthānam vratam pāśupatam caret yoginām ca eva sarveṣām śreṣṭham cāndrāyaṇam bhavet ekam dve trīṇi catvāri śaktitas vā samācaret mahā bhikṣūṇām ahiṃsā paramā tu iha akrodhaḥ guru śuśruṣā śaucam āhāra lāghavam nityam svādhyāyaḥ iti ete niyamāḥ parikīrtitāḥ yathā dvipaḥ iva araṇye manuṣyāṇām vidhīyate devaiḥ tulyāḥ sarva yajña kriyāḥ tu yajñāt jāpyam jñānam āhuḥ ca jāpyāt jñāna ddhyānām saṅga rāgāt apetam tasmin prāpte śāśvatasya upalaṃbhaḥ damaḥ śamaḥ satyam akalmaṣa tvam maunam ca bhūteṣu akhileṣu ca ārjavam atindriyam jñānam idam tathā śivam prāhuḥ tathā jñāna viśuddha buddhayaḥ samāpnuyāt yogam imam mahātmā mahā ṛṣayaḥ ca evam anindita amalāḥ prāpyate abhimatān deśān aṅkuśena nivāritaḥ etad mārgeṇa śuddhena dagdha bījaḥ hi akalmaṣaḥ sat ācāra ratāḥ śāntāḥ svadharma paripālakāḥ pitāmahena upadiṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ sākṣāt sanātanaḥ sarva loka upakāra artham śṛṇudhvam pravadāmi vaḥ guru upadeśa yuktānām vṛddhānām krama vartinām abhyutthāna ādikam sarvam praṇāmam ca eva kārayet aṣṭāṅga praṇipātena tridhā nyastena suvratāḥ jyeṣṭha anye api ca te sarve vandanīyāḥ vijānatā bhaṅgam na kurvīta yadi icchat siddhim uttamām varjayet sarva yatnāt kaitavam vitta śāṭhyam ca paiśunyam varjayet sadā ati hāsam avaṣṭambham līlā sva icchā pravartanam yatīnām āsanam vastram daṇḍa ādyam pāduke tathā mālyam ca śayana sthānam pātram chāyām ca yatnatas yajña upakaraṇa aṅgam ca na spṛśet vai padena ca kṛtvā pramādāt viprāḥ praṇavasya ayutam japet saṃdhyā lope kṛte vipraḥ tris āvṛttya eva śuddhi ati laṅghane samayānām tu abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe kāka ulūka kapotānām pakṣiṇām api ghātane śatam aṣṭa uttaram japtvā mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ smaraṇāt śuddhim āpnoti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na evam ātma vidām asti prāyaścittāni codanā yoga dhyāna eka niṣṭhāḥ ca nirlepāḥ kāñcanam yathā śuddhānām śodhanam na asti viśuddhāḥ brahma vidyayā uddhṛta an uṣṇapena ābhiḥ pūtābhiḥ vastra cakṣuṣā paṅka aśma dūṣitam ca eva sāmudram palvala udakam sa śaivālam tathā anyaiḥ vā doṣaiḥ duṣṭam vivarjayet vastra śauca anvitaḥ kuryāt sarva kāryāṇi vai dvijāḥ namaskāra ādikam sarvam guru śuśrūṣaṇa ādikam vastra śauca vihīna ātmā hi aśuciḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ deva kārya upayuktānām pratyaham śaucam iṣyate itareṣām hi vastrāṇām śaucam kāryam mala āgame kauśa yāvikayoḥ rukṣaiḥ kṣaumāṇām gaurasarṣapaiḥ śrīphalaiḥ aṃśupaṭṭānām kutapānām ariṣṭakaiḥ carmaṇām vidalānām ca vetrāṇām vastra vat matam valkalānām tu sarveṣām chatra cāmarayoḥ api bhasmanā kāṃsyam kṣāreṇa āyasam ucyate haimam adbhiḥ śubham pātram raupya pātram dvijottamāḥ maṇi aśma śaṅkha muktānām śaucam taijasa vat smṛtam rasāṇām iha śuddhiḥ utplavanam smṛtam tṛṇa kāṣṭha ādi vastūnām śubhena abhyukṣaṇam smṛtam uṣṇena vāriṇā śuddhiḥ tathā sruc sruvayoḥ api tathā eva yajña pātrāṇām muśala ulūkhalasya ca śṛṅga asthi dāru dantānām takṣaṇena eva śodhanam saṃhatānām mahābhāgāḥ dravyāṇām prokṣaṇam smṛtam asaṃhatānām dravyāṇam pratyekam śaucam ucyate abhukta rāśi dhānyānām eka deśasya dhūṣaṇe tāvat mātram samuddhṛtya prokṣayet vai kuśa ambhasā śāka mūla phala ādīnām dhānya vat śuddhiḥ iṣyate go nivāsena vai śuddhā secanena dharā smṛtā bhūmi stham udakam śuddham vaitṛṣṇyam yatra gauḥ vrajet vatsaḥ śuciḥ prasravaṇe śakuniḥ phala pātane svādārāsyam gṛhasthānām ratau bhāryā abhikāṅkṣayā hastābhyām kṣālitam vastram kāruṇā ca yathāvidhi kuśa aṃbunā su saṃprokṣya gṛhṇīyāt dharma vittamaḥ paṇyam prasāritam ca eva varṇa āśrama vibhāgaśaḥ śuciḥ ākara jam teṣām śvā mṛga grahaṇe śuciḥ chāyā ca vipluṣaḥ viprāḥ makṣikā ādyāḥ dvijottamāḥ rajaḥ bhūḥ vāyuḥ agniḥ ca medhyāni sparśane sadā suptvā bhuktvā ca vai viprāḥ kṣuttvā pītvā ca vai tathā ṣṭhīvitvā adhyayana ādau ca śuciḥ api ācamet punar pādau spṛśanti ye ca api para ācamana bindavaḥ kṛtvā ca maithunam spṛṣṭvā patitam kukkuṭa ādikam sūkaram ca eva kāka ādi śvānam uṣṭram kharam tathā yūpam cāṇḍālaka ādyān ca spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati rajasvalām sūtikām ca na spṛśet antyajām api sūtikā śauca saṃyuktaḥ śāva aśauca samanvitaḥ saṃspṛśet na rajaḥ tāsām spṛṣṭvā snātvā eva śudhyati na eva aśaucam yatīnām ca vanastha brahmacāriṇām naiṣṭhikānām nṛpāṇām ca maṇḍalīnām ca suvratāḥ tatas kārya virodhāt hi nṛpāṇām na anyathā bhavet vaikhānasānām viprāṇām patitānām asaṃbhavāt a saṃcaya dvijānām ca snāna mātreṇa na anyathā tathā saṃnihitānām ca yajña artham dīkṣitasya ca ekāha ādi ajña yājīnām śuddhiḥ uktā svayambhunā tatas tu adhīta śākhānām caturbhiḥ sarva dehinām tam bāndhavānām dvijottamāḥ tatas ṛtu trayāt arvāk eka ahaḥ parigīyate sapta varṣāt tatas ca arvāk tri rātram hi tatas param daśa aham brāhmaṇānām vai prathame ahani vā pituḥ daśa aham sūtikā aśaucam mātuḥ api evam avyayāḥ arvāk tri varṣāt snānena bāndhavānām pituḥ sadā aṣṭa abdāt eka rātreṇa śuddhiḥ syāt brāndhavasya tu dvādaśa abdāt tatas ca arvāk tri rātram strīṣu suvratāḥ daśa ahe tu tri rātram aśuciḥ bhavet tatas saṃnihitaḥ vipraḥ ca arvāk pūrvam tat eva vai saṃvatsare vyatīte tu snāna mātreṇa śudhyati spṛṣṭvā pretan tri rātreṇa dharma artham snānam ucyate dāhakānām ca netṝṇām snāna mātram abāndhave anugamya ca vai snātvā ghṛtam prāśya viśudhyati maraṇe ca eva tri rātram śrotriye mṛte mātulānām ca sodarāṇām ca vā dvijāḥ bhūpānām maṇḍalīnām ca sadyas nīrāṣṭra vāsinām kevalam dvādaśa ahena kṣatriyāṇām dvijottamāḥ na abhiṣiktasya ca aśaucam saṃpramādeṣu vai raṇe vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśa ahena śūdraḥ māsena śudhyati aśaucam ca ānupūrvyeṇa yatīnām na eva vidyate tretā prabhṛti nārīṇām māsi māsi ārtavam dvijāḥ prayānti ca mahābhāgāḥ bhāryābhiḥ kuravaḥ yathā varṇa āśrama vyavasthā ca tretā prabhṛti suvratāḥ bhārate dakṣiṇe varṣe vyavasthā na itareṣu atha mahāvīte suvīte ca jaṃbūdvīpe tathā aṣṭasu śākadvīpa ādiṣu proktaḥ dharmaḥ vai bhārate yathā rasollāsā kṛte vṛttiḥ tretāyām gṛha vṛkṣa jā sā eva ārtava kṛtāt doṣāt rāga dveṣa ādibhiḥ nṛṇām yava ādyāḥ saṃprajāyante grāmya āraṇyāḥ caturdaśa oṣadhyaḥ ca rajaḥ doṣāḥ strīṇām rāga ādibhiḥ nṛṇām akāla kṛṣṭāḥ vidhvastāḥ punar utpāditāḥ tathā prathame ahani cāṇḍālī yathā avajyā tathā aṅganā snātvā ardha māsāt saṃśuddhā tatas śuddhiḥ bhaviṣyati mūtra vat śaucam iṣyate pañca rātram tathā aspṛśyā rajasā vartate yadi sā viṃśat divasāt ūrdhvam rajasā pūrvavat tathā snāne śaucam tathā gānam rodanam hasanam tathā yānam abhyañjanam nārī dyūtam ca eva anulepanam divāsvapnam viśeṣeṇa tathā vai dantadhāvanam maithunam mānasam vā api vācikam devatā arcanam rajasvalā aṅganā sparśa saṃbhāṣe ca rajasvalā saṃtyāgam ca eva vastrāṇām varjayet sarva yatnatas snātvā anya puruṣam nārī na spṛśet tu rajasvalā īkṣayet bhāskaram devam brahmakūrcam tatas vibet kevalam pañcagavyam vā kṣīram vā ca ātma śuddhaye caturthyām strī na gamyā tu gata ulpa āyuḥ prasūyate vidyā hīnam vrata bhraṣṭam patitam pāradārikam dāridrya arṇava magnam ca tanayam sā prasūyate rakta ādhikyāt bhavet nārī śukra ādhikye bhavet pumān ṣaṣṭhyām gamyā mahābhāgā sat putra jananī bhavet pum iti narakasya ākhyā duḥkham ca narakam viduḥ puṃsaḥ trāṇa anvitam putram tathābhūtam prasūyate aṣṭamyām sarva saṃpannam tanayam saṃprasūyate navamyām dārikā daśamyām paṇḍitā bhavet ekādaśyām tathā nārīm janayet sā eva pūrvavat dvādaśyām dharma tattva jñam śrauta smārta pravartakam trayodaśyām jaḍām nārīm sarva saṃkara kāriṇīm caturdaśyām yadā gaccet sā putra jananā bhavet pañcadaśyām ca dharmiṣṭhām ṣoḍaśyām jñāna pāragam strīṇām vai mathune kāle vāma pārśve prabhañjanaḥ caret yadi bhavet nārī pumāṃsam dakṣiṇe labhet strīṇām maithuna kāle tu pāpa graha vivarjite ukta kāle śuciḥ bhūtvā śuddhām gacchet śuci smitām iti evam saṃprasaṅgeṇa yatīnām dharma saṃgrahe sarveṣām eva bhūtānām sat ācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ yaḥ paṭhet śūṇuyāt vā api sat ācāram śuciḥ naraḥ śrāvayet vā yathānyāyam brāhmaṇān dagdha kilbiṣān iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sadācārakathanam nāma okonanavati tamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atha ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi yatīnām iha niścitam prāyaścittam śiva proktam yatīnām pāpa śodhanam pāpam hi trividham jñeyam vāc manaḥ kāya saṃbhavam satatam hi divā rātrau yena idam veṣṭyate jagat tad karmaṇā vinā api eṣa tiṣṭhati iti parā śrutiḥ kṣaṇam evam prayojyam tu āyuṣyam tu vidhāraṇam na hi yogāt param kiñcid narāṇām dṛśyate śubham tasmai dyogam praśaṃsaṃti dharma yuktāḥ manīṣiṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā aparāvaram dhīrāḥ param gacchanti tat padam yāni bhīkṣūṇām tathā eva upavratāni ca ekaika atikrame teṣām prāyāścittam vidhīyate upetya tu striyam kāmāt prāyaścittam vinirdiśet prāṇāyāma samāyuktam caret sāṃtapanam vratam tatas carati nirdeśāt kṛcchram ca ante samāhitaḥ punārāśramam āgatya caret bhikṣuḥ atandritaḥ na dharma yuktam anṛtam hinasti iti manīṣiṇaḥ tathā api na ca kartavyam prasaṃgaḥ hi eṣa dāruṇaḥ ahorātra apavāsaḥ ca prāmāyāma śatam tathā hiṃsā hi eṣā parā sṛṣṭā stainyam vai kathitam tathā yat etat draviṇam nāma prāṇāḥ hi ete bahiścarāḥ evam kṛtvā su duṣṭa ātmā bhinna vṛttaḥ vratāt cyutaḥ bhūyas nirvedam āpannaḥ caret cāndrāyaṇam vratam vidhinā śāstra dṛṣṭena saṃvatsaram iti śrutiḥ tatas saṃvatsarasya ante bhūyas prakṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ ahiṃsā sarva bhūtānām karmaṇā manasā girā akāmāt api hiṃseta yadi bhikṣuḥ paśūn kṛmīn kṛcchrātikṛcchram kurvīta cāndrāyaṇam atha api vā tena dhārayitavyāḥ vai prāṇāyāmāḥ tu ṣoṭaśa tri rātram upavāsāḥ ca prāṇāyāma śatam tathā rātrau skannaḥ śuciḥ snātvā dvādaśā eva tu dhāraṇā prāṇāyāmena śuddha ātmā virajāḥ jāyate dvijāḥ eka annam madhu māṃsam vā a śṛta annam tathā eva ca abhojyāni yatīnām tu pratyakṣa lavaṇāni ca ekaika atikramāt teṣām prāyaścittam vidhīyate prājāpatyena kṛcchreṇa tatas pāpāt pramucyate vyatikramāḥ ca ye kecid vāc manaḥ kāya saṃbhavāḥ caret hi śuddhaḥ sama loṣṭha kāñcanaḥ samasta bhūteṣu ca sat samāhitaḥ sthānam dhruvam śāśvatam avyayam tu param hi gatvā na punar hi jāyate iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge yatiprāyāścittam nāma navatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi ariṣṭāni nibodhata yena jñāna viśeṣeṇa mṛtyum paśyanti yoginaḥ arundhatīm dhruvam ca eva soma chāyām mahāpatham pāvakam yaḥ paśyati na jīvet vai māsāt ekādaśāt param vamet mūtram purīṣam ca suvarṇam rajatam tathā pratyakṣam athavā svapne daśa māsān na jīvati paśyet pratorpa śācān ca nava māsān sa jīvati prakṛteḥ ca nivarteta ca aṣṭau māsan ca jīvati agratas pṛṣṭhatas vā api khaṇḍam yasya padam bhavet pāṃsuke kardame vā api sapta māsān sa jīvati kākaḥ kapotaḥ gṛdhraḥ vā nilīyet yasya mūrdhani kravyādaḥ vā khagaḥ yasya ṣaṣ māsān ativartate gacchet vāyasa paṅktībhiḥ pāṃsu varṣeṇa vā punar svacchāyām vikṛtām paśyet catuḥ pañca sa jīvati anabhre vidyutam paśyet dakṣiṇām diśam āsthitām udake dhanuḥ aidram vā trīṇi dvau vā sa jīvati apsu vā yadi vā ādarśe yaḥ hi ātmānam na paśyati aśiraskam tathā paśyet māsāt vā ūrdhvam na jīvati yasya vai snāta mātrasya hṛdayam pariśuṣyati dhūmam vā mastakāt paśyet daśa ahān na saḥ jīvati spṛṣṭaḥ na hṛṣyeta tasya mṛtyuḥ upasthitaḥ ṛkṣa vānara yuktena rathena āśām ca dakṣiṇām kṛṣṇa ambara dharā śyāmā gāyantī vā api atha aṅganā yam nayet dakṣiṇām āśām svapne saḥ api na jīvati chidram vā svasya kaṇṭhasya svapne yaḥ vīkṣate naraḥ nagnam vā śramaṇam dṛṣṭvā vidyāt mṛtyum upasthitam dṛṣṭvā tu tādṛśam svapnam sadyas eva na jīvati bhasma aṅgārān ca keśān ca nadīm śuṣkām bhujaṅgamān paśyet yaḥ daśa rātram tu na saḥ jīvati tādṛśaḥ puruṣaiḥ udyata āyudhaiḥ pāṣāṇaiḥ tāḍyate svapne yaḥ sadyas na sa jīvāti sūrya udaye prati uṣasi pratyakṣam yasya vai śivāḥ yasya vā snāta mātrasya hṛdayam pīḍyate bhṛśam jāyate dantaharṣaḥ ca tam gata āyuṣam ādiśet bhūyas bhūyas traset yaḥ tu rātrau vā yadi vā divā rātrau ca indradhanuḥ paśyet divā nakṣatra maṇḍalam para netreṣu ca ātmānam na paśyet na saḥ jīvati ca nāsā bhavati vijñeyaḥ gata jīvitaḥ yasya kṛṣṇā kharā jihvā padma ābhāsam ca vai mukham gaṇḍā iva piṇḍikā rakte tasya mṛtyuḥ upasthitaḥ mukta keśaḥ hasan ca eva gāyan nṛtyan ca yaḥ naraḥ yasya śveta vana ābhāsā śveta sarṣapa saṃnibhā uṣṭrāḥ vā rāsabhāḥ vā abhiyuktāḥ svapne rathe śubhāḥ dve vā atha parame ariṣṭe ekībhūtaḥ param bhavet ghoṣam na śṛṇuyāt karṇe jyotiḥ netre na paśyati na ca uttiṣṭhati yaḥ śvabhrāt tad antam tasya jīvatam ūrdhvā ca dṛṣṭiḥ na ca saṃpratiṣṭhā raktā punar saṃparivartamānā mukhasya śoṣaḥ suṣirā ca nābhiḥ ati uṣṇa mūtraḥ viṣama sthaḥ eva divā vā yadi vā rātrau pratyakṣam yaḥ nihanyate yaḥ tu prāvaraṇam śuklam svakam paśyati mānavaḥ tyaktvā khedam viṣādam ca upekṣet bruddhimān naraḥ prācīm vā yadi vā udīcīm diśam niṣkramya vai śuciḥ udak mukhaḥ prāc mukhaḥ vā svaśthaḥ ca ācāntaḥ eva ca yathā dīpaḥ nivāta sthaḥ na iṅgate sā upamā smṛtā prāc udak pravaṇe deśe tathā yuñjīta śāstra vid kāmam vitarkam prītim ca sukha duḥkhe ubhe tathā ghrāṇe ca rasane nityam cakṣuṣī sparśane tathā kālakarmāṇi vijñāya samūheṣu eva nityaśas dvādaśa adhyātmam iti evam yoga dhāraṇam ucyate śatam ardhaśatam vā api dhāraṇām mūrdhni dhārayet khinnasya dhāraṇā yogāt vāyuḥ ūrdhvam pravartate tatas ca āpūrayet deham oṃkāreṇa samanvitaḥ tathā uṅkāra mayaḥ yogī akṣare tu akṣarī bhavet atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi oṃkāra prāpti lakṣaṇam eṣa tri mātraḥ vijñeyaḥ vyañjanam ca atra ca īśvaraḥ mātrā dvitīyā tāmasī smṛtā tṛtīyām nirguṇām ca eva mātrām akṣara gāminīm gāndhārī ca eva vijñeyā gāndhara svara sambhavā pipīlikā gati sparśā prayuktā mūrdhni lakṣyate yathā prayuktaḥ oṃkāraḥ pratiniryāti mūrdhani praṇavaḥ dhanuḥ śaraḥ hi ātmā brahma lakṣaṇam ucyate om iti ekākṣaram hi etat guhāyām nihitam padam viṣṇu kramāḥ trayaḥ tu ete ṛc sāmāni yajūṃṣi ca mātrā ca ardham ca tisraḥ tu vijñeyāḥ paramārthāt akāraḥ hi akṣaraḥ jñeyaḥ ukāraḥ sahitaḥ smṛtaḥ makāra sahita uṅkāraḥ tri mātraḥ iti saṃjñitaḥ oṃkāraḥ tu trayaḥ lokāḥ śiraḥ tasya triviṣṭapam mātrā pādaḥ rudra lokaḥ hi amātram tu śivam padam evam jñāna viśeṣeṇa tat padam samupāsyate upāsyam hi prayatnena śāśvatam sukham icchatā tatas plutavatī ca eva tṛtīyā ca upadiśyate etāḥ tu mātrāḥ vijñeyāḥ yathāvat anupūrvaśas indriyāṇi manaḥ buddhim dhyāyan ātmani yaḥ sadā māsemāse aśvamedhena yaḥ yajeta śatam samāḥ tena yat prāpyate puṇyam mātrayā tat avāpnuyāt na tathā tapasā ugreṇa na yajñaiḥ bhūri dakṣiṇaiḥ yat phalam prāpyate samyak mātrayā tat avāpnuyāt tatra ca eṣā tu yā mātrā plutā nāma upadiśyate eṣā eva bhavet kāryā gṛhasthānām tu yoginām ca eva viśeṣeṇa aiśvarye hi aṣṭa lakṣaṇe tu vijñeyā tasmāt yuñjīta tām dvijāḥ evam hi yoga saṃyuktaḥ śuciḥ dātaḥ jita indriyaḥ bhātmānam vidyate yaḥ tu sa sarvam vindate dvijāḥ tasmāt pāśupataiḥ yogaiḥ ātmānam cintayet budhaḥ ātmānam jānate ye tu śucayaḥ te na saṃśayaḥ ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni veda upaniṣadaḥ tathā yoga jñānāt avāpnoti brāhmaṇaḥ adhyātma cintakaḥ yoni saṃkramaṇam tyaktvā yāti vai śāśvatam padam yathā vṛkṣāt phalam pakvam pavanena samīritam namaskāreṇa rudrasya tathā pāpam praṇaśyati tasmāt tris pravaṇam yogī upāsīta maheśvaram avimukteśvaram gatvā vārāṇasyām tu śodhanam saṃtyajet sa yāti śiva sāyujyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā avimuktam param kṣetram jantūnām mukti dam sadā seveta satatam dhīmān viśeṣāt maraṇa antike iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge ariṣṭakathanam nāma ekanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ evam vārāṇasī puṇyā yadi sūta mahāmate vaktum arhasi ca naḥ tad prabhāvam hi sāṃpratam vistareṇa yata anyāyam śrotum kautūhalam hi naḥ uvāca vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ samyak vārāṇasyāḥ su śobhanam vistareṇa mayā vaktum brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā devaḥ purā kṛta udvāhaḥ śaṅkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ vārāṇasīm anuprāpya darśayāmāsa śaṃkaraḥ avimukteśvaram liṅgam vāsam tatra cakāra saḥ vārāṇasī kurukṣetra śrīparvata mahālaye haimavatyāḥ svayam devaḥ sa nandī parameśvaraḥ uktavan parameśānaḥ pārvatyāḥ prīyate bhavaḥ praphulla nānāvidha gulma śobhitam latā prātāna ādi manoharam bahis virūḍha puṣpaiḥ paritas priyaṅgubhiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiḥ ca ketakaiḥ aśoka punnāga
