śataiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ dvirepha mālā ākula puṣpa saṃcayaiḥ kvacid praphulla ambuja reṇu bhūṣitaiḥ vihaṃgamaiḥ ca anukala praṇādibhiḥ matta sārasa cakravākaiḥ pramatta dātyūha varaiḥ ca sarvatas kvacid ca kekā ruta nāditam śubham kvacid ca kāraṇḍava nāda nāditam kvacid ca matta ali kula ākulīkṛtam mada ākulābhiḥ bhramara aṅganā ādi bhī niṣevitam cāru sugāndhi puṣpakaiḥ kvacid su paṣpaiḥ sahakāra vṛkṣaiḥ latā upagūḍhaiḥ tilakaiḥ ca gūḍham pragīta vidyādhara siddha cāraṇam pravṛtta nṛtta anugata apsaraḥ gaṇam prahṛṣṭa nānāvidha pakṣi sevitam pranṛtta hārīta kula upanāditam mṛgendra nāda ākula matta mānasaiḥ mada mudita vihaṃgam prāpta nāda abhīrāmam kusumita taru śākhā ālīna matta dvirepham nava kisalaya śobhā śobhitam prāṃśu śākham kvacid ca dantakṣata cāru vīrudham kvacid latā āliṅgi ta cāru vṛkṣakam kvacid vilāsa alasa gāminībhiḥ niṣevitam kiṃpuruṣa aṅganābhiḥ pārāvata dhvani vikūjita cāru śṛṅgaiḥ abhraṃkaṣaiḥ sita manohara cāru rūpaiḥ tuṅga agraiḥ nila puṣpaiḥ tabaka bhara nata prāṃśu śākhaiḥ aśokaiḥ delā prānta anta līna śruti sukha janakaiḥ bhāsita antam manojñaiḥ haṃsānām pakṣa vāta pracalita kamala svaccha vistīrṇa toyam coyānām tīra jāta pracakita kadala cāṭu nṛtyat mayūram māyūraiḥ pakṣa candraiḥ kvacid avani gataiḥ rañjita kṣmā pradeśam deśe deśe vilīna pramudita vilasat matta hārīta vṛndam hṛṣṭabhiḥ kvacid api kinnara aṅganābhiḥ viṇābhiḥ sa madhura gīta nṛtta kaṇṭham saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacid upalipta kīrṇa puṣpaiḥ āvāsaiḥ parivṛta pādapam munīnām ramyam priyaṅgu taru mañjarī sakta bhṛṅgam bhṛṅga āvali kavalita āmra kadamba puṣpam gulma antara prasabha bhīta mṛgī samūham vāta īritam tanubhṛtām apavarga dātṛ candra aṃśu jāla śablaiḥ tilakaiḥ manojñaiḥ sindūra kuṅkuma kusumbha nibhaiḥ aśokaiḥ cāmīkara dyuti samaiḥ atha karṇikāraiḥ puṣpa utkaraiḥ upacitam su viśāla śākhaiḥ kvacid kāñcana saṃkāśaiḥ puṣpaiḥ ācita bhū talam sakala bhuvana bhartā lokanāthaḥ tadānīm tuhinaśikhara putryā sārdham iṣṭaiḥ gaṇeśaiḥ vividha taru viśālam matta hṛṣṭa anna puṣṭaiḥ upavanam ati ramyam darśayāmāsa devyāḥ puṣpaiḥ vanyaiḥ śubha śubhatamaiḥ kalpitaiḥ divya bhūṣaiḥ devīm divyām upavana gatām bhūṣayāmāsa śarvaḥ sā ca api enam tuhināgiri sutā śaṅkaram devadevam puṣpaiḥ divyaiḥ śubhataratamaiḥ bhūṣayāmāsa bhaktyā saṃpūjya pūjyam saṃprekṣya ca udyāna ramyam gaṇa īśvaraiḥ nādi mukhaiḥ ca sārdham uvāca devam praṇipatya devī uvāca udyānam darśitam deva prabhayā parayā yutam uvāca mad ambhojam tadā āha girijām hasan śrī bhagavant uvāca idam guhyatamam kṣetram sadā vārāṇasī mama sarveṣām eva jantūnām hetuḥ mokṣasya sarvadā asmin siddhāḥ sadā devi madīyam vratam āsthitāḥ nānā liṅga dharāḥ nityam mama loka abhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇe nānā vihaga sobhite kamala utpala puṣpa āḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṅkṛte rocate me sadā vāsaḥ yena kāryeṇa tat śṛṇu kāmam hi atra mṛtaḥ devī jantuḥ mokṣāya kalpate atas param idam kṣetram parā ca iyam gatiḥ mama vimuktam na mayā yasmāt mokṣyate vā kadācana naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre gaṅgādvāre ca puṣkare snānāt saṃsevanāt vā api na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yatas prayāgāt api tīrtha agryāt avimuktam idam śubham kāmam bhuñjan svapan krīḍan kurvan hi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ kṛtvā pāpa sahasrāṇi piśāca tvam varam nṛṇām na tu śakra sahasra tvam svarge kāśi purīm vinā jaigīṣavyaḥ parām siddhim gataḥ yatra mahā tapāḥ asya kṣetrasya māhātmyāt bhaktyā ca mama bhāvitaḥ jaigīṣavya guhā śreṣṭhā yoginām sthānam iṣyate dhyāyantaḥ tatra mām nityam yoga agniḥ dīpyate bhṛśam manaḥ ca eva sāyujyam īpsitam sthānam eva ca kṣetra saṃsevanāt eva gaṇeśa tvam avāpa ha iha eva ārādhya mām devi siddhim yāsyati anuttamām parāśara sutau yogī ṛṣiḥ vyāsaḥ mahā tapāḥ brahmā deva ṛṣibhiḥ sārdham viṣṇuḥ vā api divākaraḥ anye api yoginaḥ divyāḥ channa rūpāḥ mahātmanaḥ ye punar nirmamāḥ dhīrāḥ sattva sthāḥ vijita indriyāḥ vratinaḥ ca nirāraṃbhāḥ sarve te mayi bhāvitāḥ devadevam samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṅga varjitāḥ gatāḥ iha param mokṣam prasādāt mama suvrate janma antara sahasreṣu yam na yogī samāpnuyāt goprekṣakam idam kṣetram brahmaṇā sthāpitam purā tat kailāsa bhavanam ca atra paśya divyam varānane goprekṣakam ayā āgamya dṛṣṭvā amām atra mānavaḥ kapilāḥ hraham iti evam tathā vai brahmaṇā kṛtam atra api svayam eva aham vṛṣadhvajaḥ iti smṛtaḥ sāṃnadhyam kṛtavan devi sadā aham dṛśyate tavyā gaccha upaśamam īśaiḥ iti upaśāntaḥ śivaḥ tathā atra aham brahmaṇā ānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā brahmaṇā ca api saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punar brahmaṇā api tatas viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvigna cetasā mayā ānītam idam liṅgam kasmāt sthāpitavān asi tam uvāca punar viṣṇuḥ brahmanam kupita ānanam dṛṣṭvā enam api deveśam mama lokam vrajet naraḥ sthāpayāmāsa vidhivat bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ svarlīneśvaraḥ iti evam atra aham svayam āgataḥ ananyā sā gatiḥ tasya yoginām ca eva yā smṛtā vyāghra rūpam samāsthāya nihataḥ darpitaḥ balī na punar durgatim yāti dṛṣṭvā enam vyāghram īśvaram ādau atra aham āgamya prasthitaḥ gaṇapaiḥ saha jyeṣṭhasthānam idam tasmāt etat mama puṇya darśanam devaiḥ saṃmatāt etāni liṅgāni stāpitāni atas mama priya hitam sthānam jñātvā liṅgam pratiṣṭhitam śaileśvaram iti khyātam dṛśyatām iha ca ādarāt nadī eṣā varuṇā devi puṇyā pāpa pramocanī kṣetram etat alaṅkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā sthāpitam brahmaṇā ca api saṃgame liṅgam uttamam sagameśvaram iti evam khyātam jagati dṛśyatām saṃgame devanadyā hi yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ idam manye mahā kṣetram nivāsaḥ yoginām param kṣetra madhye ca yatra aham svayam bhūtvā agram āsthitaḥ siddhānām sthānam etat hi madīya vrata dhāriṇām yoginām mokṣa lipsūnām jñāna yoga rata ātmanām dṛṣṭvā enam madhyameśānam janma prati na śocati sthāpitam liṅgam etat tu śukreṇa bhṛgu sūnunā nāmnā śukreśvaram nāma sarva siddha amara arcitam mṛtaḥ ca na punar jantuḥ saṃsārī tu bhavet naraḥ purā jambuka rūpeṇa asuraḥ deva kaṇṭakaḥ brahmanaḥ hi varam labdhvā gomāyuḥ bandha śaṅkitaḥ dṛṣṭvā enam api deveśam sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt grahaiḥ śukra purogaiḥ ca etāni sthāpitāni ha paśya puṇyāni liṅgāni sarva kāma pradāni tu evam etāni puṇyāni mad nivāsāni pārvati kathitāni mama kṣetre guhyam ca anyat idam śṛṇu yojanam viddhi cāru aṅge mṛtyu kāle amṛta pradam gaṇa tvam labhate dṛṣṭvā hi asmin mokṣaḥ hi avāpyate gāṇapatyam labhet yasmāt yatas sā muktiḥ uttamā tatas mahālayāt tasmāt kedārāt madhyamāt api smṛtam puṇyatamam kṣetram avimuktam varānane kedāram madhyamam kṣetram sthānam ca eva mahālayam mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamam tu idam yatas sṛṣṭāḥ tu ime lokāḥ tatas kṣetram idam śubham avimukteśvaram liṅgam mama dṛṣṭvā iha mānavaḥ sadyas pāpa vinirmuktaḥ paśu pāśaiḥ vimucyate śaileśam saṃgameśam ca svarlīnam madhyameśvaram hiraṇyagarbham īśānam goprekṣam vṛṣabhadhvajam upaśāntam śivam ca eva jyeṣṭhasthāna nivāsinam śukreśvaram ca vikhyātam vyāghreśam jambukeśvaram dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkha sāgare uvāca tatas pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma abhyaṅga sita prabhāḥ māheśvarāḥ mahātmānaḥ tathā vai niyata vratāḥ punar nirīkṣya yogeśam dhyāna yogam ca kṛtsnaśas tasthuḥ ātmānam āsthāya līyamānāḥ iva īśvare sthitānām saḥ tadā teṣām devadevaḥ umāpatiḥ sa bibhrat paramām mūrti babhūva puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ tasya tām paramām mūrtim āsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ na śaśāka punar draṣṭum hṛṣṭa romā girindrajā tatas tu adṛṣṭam ākāram budhvā sā prakati sthitam prakṛteḥ mūrtim āsthāya yogena parameśvarī tam śaśāka punar draṣṭum harasya ca mahātmanaḥ viviśuḥ hṛdayam sarve dagdha saṃsāra bījinaḥ pañcākṣarasya vai bījam saṃsmarantaḥ su śobhanam sarva pāpa haram divyam purā ca eva prakāśitam tam dṛṣṭvā śailajā prāha hṛṣṭa sarva tanūruhā tām uvāca suraśreṣṭhaḥ tadā devīm giradrijām śrī bhagavant uvāca yaiḥ yaiḥ yogāḥ iha abhyastāḥ steṣām ekena janmanā tasmāt etat mahat kṣetram brahma ādyaiḥ sevitam tathā pratimāsam tathā aṣṭamyām pratimāsam caturdaśīm ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ devi vārāṇasyām upāsyate śaśi bhānu uparāge ca kārttikyām ca viśeṣataḥ pṛthivyām sarva tīrthāni vārāṇasyām tu jāhnavīm uttara pravahām puṇyām mama mauli viniḥsṛtām pituḥ te girirājasya śubhām himavantaḥ sutām puṇya sthāna sthitām puṇyām puṇya diś pravahām sadā saṃnihatya kurukṣetram sārdham tīrtha śataiḥ tathā puṣkaram nimipam ca eva prayāgam ca pṛthūdakam drumakṣetram kurukṣetram naimiṣam tīrtha saṃyutam kṣetrāṇi sarvatas devī devatāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā saṃdhyā ca ṛtavaḥ ca eva sarvāḥ nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca samudrāḥ sapta ca eva atra deva tīrthāni kṛtsnaśas avimukteśvaram dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā ca eva triviṣṭapam kālabhairavam āsādya dhūta pāpāni sarvaśas pṛthivyām yāni puṇyāni mahānti āyatanāni ca avimuktam kṣetra varam mahā pāpa nibarhaṇam kedāre ca eva yat liṅgam yat ca liṅgam mahālaye madhyamesvara saṃjñam ca tathā pāśupateśvaram maṅkukarṇeśvaram ca eva gokarṇau ca tathā hi ubhau sthāneśvaram tathā ekāgram kāleśvaram ajeśvaram bhairaveśvaram īśānam tathā uṅkāraka saṃjñitam amareśam mahākālam jyotiṣam bhasmagātrakam yāni ca anyāni puṇyāni sthānāni mama bhū tale aṣṭaṣaṣṭi samākhyāni ruḍhāni anyāni kṛtsnaśas tāni sarvāṇi aśeṣāṇi vārāṇasyām viśanti mām snātasya ca eva gaṅgāyām dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe sarva yajña phalaiḥ tulyam iṣṭaiḥ śata sahasraśas su dṛṣṭam kuru deveśi avimuktam gṛham mama darśayāmāsa bhagavān śrīparvatam anuttamam śrīparvatam anuprāpya devyā deveśvaraḥ haraḥ kṣetrāṇi darśayāmāsa sarva bhūta patiḥ bhavaḥ kuṇḍiprabhe ca paramam divyam vaiśravaṇeśvaram māśāliṅgam ca deveśam divyam yat ca bileśvaram rāmeśvaram ca paramam viṣṇunā yat pratiṣṭhitam dakṣiṇa dvāra pārśve tu kuṇḍaleśvaram īśvaram vivṛddham giriṇā sārdham devadeva namaskṛtam tat ca vara dam devaiḥ pūrvam pratiṣṭhitam karmeśvaram ca vipulam kārya artham brahmanā kṛtam śrīmat siddhavaṭam ca eva sadā āvāsaḥ mama avyaye ajena nirmitam divyam sākṣāt ajabilam śubham tatra śṛṅgāṭaka ākāram śṛṅgāṭa acala madhyame śṛṅgāṭakeśvaram nāma śrī devyā tu pratiṣṭhitam rajeśvaram ca paryāye rajasā su pratiṣṭhitam ca koṭīśvaram mahā tīrtham rudra koṭi gaṇaiḥ purā dvidevakula saṃjñam ca brahmaṇā dakṣiṇe śubham uttare sthāpitam ca eva viṣṇunā ca eva śailajam mahā pramāṇa liṅgam ca mayā pūrvam pratiṣṭhitam iti uktvā tad gṛhe tiṣṭhat alaṅgṛham iti smṛtam tatra api tīrtham tīrtha jñe vyomaliṅgam ca paśya me gomaṇḍaleśvaram ca eva nanda ādyaiḥ su pratiṣṭhitam devaiḥ sarvaiḥ tu śakra ādyaiḥ stāpitāni varānane śrīmat devahrada prānte sthānāni imāni pasya me tvayā hitāya jagatām hārakuṇḍam idam kṛtam alaṅkṛtam mayā brahma purastāt muni bhaḥ siha caṇḍikeśvarakam devi caṇḍikeśā tava ātmajā caṇḍikā nirmitam sthānam ambikātīrtham uttamam rucikeśvarakam ca eva dhārā eṣā kapilā śubhā eteṣu devi sthāneṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣu ca pūjayet mām sadā bhaktyā mayā sārdham hi modate śrīśaile saṃtyajet daṃham brāhmaṇaḥ dagdha kilbiṣaḥ mahāsnānam ca yaḥ kuryāt ghṛtena vidhinā eva tu sa yāti mama sāyujyam sthāneṣu eteṣu suvrate snānam pala śatam jñeyam abhyaṅgam pañcaviṃśatyām palānām dve sahasre tu mahāsnānam prakīrtitam snāpya liṅgam madīyam tu gavyena eva ghṛtena ca saṃmārjya śata yajñānām snānena prayutam tathā pūjayā śata sāhasram anantam gīta vādinām mahāsnāne prasaktam tu snānam aṣṭaguṇam smṛtam śami puṣpam ca vidhinā bilva pattram ca paṅkajam anyāni api ca puṣpāṇi bilva pattram na saṃtyajet catur droṇaiḥ mahādevam aṣṭa droṇaiḥ atha api vā daśa droṇaiḥ tu naivedyam aṣṭa droṇaiḥ atha api vā śata droṇa samam puṇyam āḍhake api vidhīyate vitta hīnasya viprasya na atra kāryā vicāraṇā bherī mṛdaṅga muraja timirā paṭaha ādibhiḥ sa bhṛtya putra dāraiḥ ca tathā saṃbandhi bāndhavaiḥ sārdham pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā pārthayet liṅgam uttamam dravya hīnam kriyā hīnam śraddhā hīnam sureśvaraiḥ kṛtam vā na kṛtam vā api kṣantum arhasi śaṃkara japitvā evam mahābījam tathā pañcākṣarasya vai tat phalam samavāpnoti vārāṇasyām yathā mṛtaḥ tathā eva mama sāyujyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ uvāca niśamya vacanam devī gatvā vārāṇasīm purīm avimukteśvaram liṅgam payasā ca ghṛtena ca arcayāmāsa deveśam rudram bhuvana nāyakam tatra andhakam mahā daityam hiraṇyākṣa sutam prabhuḥ anugṛhya gaṇa tvam ca prāpayāmāsa līlayā yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api kṣetra māhātmyam uttamam śrāvayet vā dvijān sarvān kṛta śaucān jita indriyān iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vārāṇasīśailamāhātmyakathanam nāma dvinavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ damitaḥ tu katham lebhe gāṇapatyam maheśvarāt vaktum arhasi ca asmākam yathāvṛttam yathāśrutam uvāca ca eva mandare śoṣaṇam tathā vara lābham aśeṣam ca pravadāmi samāsatas prasādāt brahmanaḥ sākṣāt avadhya tvam avāpya ca līlayā ca aprayatnena trāsayāmāsa vāsavan bādhitāḥ tāḍitāḥ baddhāḥ pātitāḥ tena te surāḥ viviśuḥ mandaram bhītāḥ nārāyaṇa purogamāḥ evam saṃpīḍya vai devān andhakaḥ api mahā asuraḥ tatas te samāḥ tāḥ suredrāḥ sa sādhyāḥ sureśa maheśam purā iti āhuḥ evam drutam ca alpa vīrya prabhinna aṅga bhinnāḥ vayam daitya rājasya śastraiḥ nikṛttāḥ jaya iti vācā bhagavan damūcuḥ kirīṭa baddha añjalayaḥ samantāt atha aśeṣa asurān tasya koṭi koṭi sataiḥ tatas bhasmīkṛtya mahādevaḥ nirbibheda andhakam tadā śūlena śūlinā protam dagdha kalmaṣa kañcukam dṛṣṭvā andhakam nanāda īśam praṇamya sa pitāmahaḥ tad nāda śravaṇāt neduḥ devāḥ devam praṇamya tam nanṛtuḥ munayaḥ sarve mumuduḥ gaṇa puṃgavāḥ sasṛjuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi devāḥ śambhoḥ tadā upari dagdha ugninā ca śūlena protaḥ pretaḥ iva andhakaḥ sāttvikam bhāvam āsthāya cintayāmāsa cetasā mayā śaṃbhuḥ purā sākṣāt maheśvaraḥ yaḥ smaret manasā rudram prāṇānte sakṛt eva vā sa yāti śiva sāyujyam kim punar bahuśas smaran brahmā ca bhagavant viṣṇuḥ sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ śaraṇam prāpya tiṣṭhanti tam eva śaraṇam vrajet evam saṃcintya tuṣṭa ātmā saḥ undhakaḥ ca andhaka ardanam sa gaṇam śivam īśānam astuvat puṇya gauravāt hiraṇyanetra tanayam śūla agra stham sureśvaraḥ provāca dānavam prekṣya ghṛṇayā nīlalohitaḥ tuṣṭaḥ asmi vatsa bhadram te kāmam kim karavāṇi te śrutvā vākyam tadā śaṃbhoḥ hiraṇyanayana ātmajaḥ harṣa gadgadayā vācā provāca idam maheśvaram pradadau durlabhām śraddhām daitya indrāya mahā dyutiḥ praṇemuḥ tam suredra ādyāḥ gām apatye pratiṣṭhitam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrve bhāge andhakagāṇapatyātmakaḥ nāma trinavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham asya pitā daityaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ su dāruṇaḥ viṣṇunā sūditaḥ viṣṇuḥ vārāha tvam katham gataḥ tasya śṛṅgam maheśasya bhūṣaṇa tvam katham gatam etat sarvam viśeṣeṇa sūtaiḥ vaktum iha arhasi uvāca hiraṇyakaśipoḥ bhrātā hiraṇyākṣaḥ iti smṛtaḥ purā andhaka asura īśasya pitā kāla antaka upamaḥ devān jitvā atha daityandraḥ baddhvā ca dharaṇīm imām nītvā rasātalam cakre bandīm indīvara prabhām tatas sa brahmakāḥ devāḥ parimlāna mukha śriyaḥ bādhitāḥ tāḍitāḥ hiraṇyākṣeṇa tena vai praṇamya śirasā viṣṇum daitya koṭi vimardanam sarve vijñāpayāmāsuḥ dharaṇī bandhanam hareḥ śrutvā etat bhagavant viṣṇuḥ dharaṇī bandhanam hariḥ bhūtvā yajñavarāhā asau yathā liṅga udbhave tathā daityaiḥ ca sārdham daitya indram hiraṇyākṣam mahā balam daṃṣṭra agra koṭyā hatvā enam reje daitya anta kṛt prabhuḥ kalpa ādiṣu yathāpūrvam praviśya ca rasātalam bahis tatas tuṣṭāva eveśam devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ śakra ādyaiḥ sahitaḥ bhūtvā girā śāśvatāya varāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe daṇḍine namaḥ nārāyaṇāya sarvāya brahmaṇe paramātmane kartre netre suredrāṇām śāstre ca sakalasya ca tavyā kṛtam sarvam idam prasīda sureśa lokeśa varāha viṣṇo tathā eka daṃṣṭra agra mukha agra koṭi bhāga eka bhāga ardhatamena viṣṇo hatāḥ kṣaṇāt kāma da daitya mukhyāḥ sva daṃṣṭra koṭyā saha putra bhṛtyaiḥ tvayā uddhṛtā deva dharā dharā īśa dharādhara ākāra dhṛtā agra daṃṣṭre tvayā eva deveśa vibho kṛtaḥ ca jayaḥ surāṇām asura īśvaṇām aho vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhatas sakala tārakā ādayaḥ nihitā rasātala gatā vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhatas sakala tārakā ādayaḥ jagatām hitāya bhavatā vasuṃdharā bhagavān rasa atasa puṭaṅga tā tadā atha tām uddhṛtām tena dharām devāḥ muni īśvarāḥ mūrdhni āropya namaścakruḥ cakriṇaḥ saṃnidhau tadā kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa kāryeṇa śata hastena viṣṇunā lokānām dhāriṇī tvam hi mṛttike hara pātakam manasā karmaṇā vācā avara de vārija īkṣaṇe tvayā hatena pāpena jīvāmaḥ tvad prasādāt iti uktā sā tadā devī dharā devaiḥ adha abravīt vārāha rūpam anagham cacāla ca dharā punar tasya devadevasya dhīmataḥ yadṛcchayā bhavaḥ paśyan jagāma jagat īśvaraḥ daṃṣṭrām jagrāha dṛṣṭvā tām bhūṣaṇa artham atha ātmanaḥ devāḥ ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sa indrāḥ devadevasya vaibhavam dharā pratiṣṭhitā hi evam devadevena līlayā bhūtānām saṃplave ca api viṣṇoḥ ca eva kalevaram brahmaṇaḥ ca tathā anyeṣām devānām api līlayā katham vimuktiḥ viprāṇām tasmāt daṃṣṭrī maheśvaraḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge varāhaprādurbhāvaḥ nāma caturnavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ nṛsiṃhena hataḥ pūrvam hiraṇyākṣa agrajaḥ śrutam uvāca hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahrādaḥ iti viśrutaḥ dharma jñaḥ satya saṃpannaḥ tapasvī ca abhavat sudhīḥ janma prabhṛti deveśam pūjayāmāsa ca avyayam tam ādipuruṣam bhaktyā para brahma svarūpiṇam brahmaṇaḥ adhipatim sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāra kāraṇam saḥ upi viṣṇoḥ tathābhūtam dṛṣṭvā putram samāhitam stuvantam prāha deva arīḥ pradahan iva pāpa dhīḥ prahrāda vīra duṣputra dvija deva ārti kāraṇam kaḥ viṣṇuḥ padmajaḥ vā api śakraḥ ca varuṇaḥ athavā vāyuḥ somaḥ tathā īśānaḥ pāvakaḥ mama yaḥ samaḥ mām eva arcaya bhaktyā ca svalpam nārāyaṇam sadā prahrāda jīvite vāñchā tava eṣā śṛṇu ca asti ced śrutvā api tasya vacanam hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sudhīḥ prahrādaḥ pūjayāmāsa namaḥ nārāyaṇa iti ca namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti sarva daitya kumārakān adhyāpayāmāsa ca tām brahma vidyām su śobhanām durlaṅghyām ca ātmanaḥ dṛṣṭvā śakra ādibhiḥ api svayam putreṇa laṅghitām ājñām hiraṇyaḥ prāha dānavān kṣīra vārinidhi śāyinaḥ prabhoḥ niṣphalam tu atha babhūva tejasā tatra eva āvirabhūt hantum nṛsiṃha ākṛtim āsthitaḥ jaghāna ca sutam prekṣya pitaram dānava adhamam bibheda tad kṣaṇāt eva karajauḥ niśitaiḥ śataiḥ pīḍayāmāsa daitya indram yuga anta agniḥ iva aparaḥ ā brahma bhuvanāt viprā pracacāla ca suvratāḥ dṛṣṭvā sura asura mahā uraga siddha sādhyāḥ tasmin kṣaṇe hari viriñci mukhāḥ nṛsiṃham dhairyam balam ca samavāpya yayuḥ visṛjya ādiṅmukha antam asura akṣaṇa tatparāḥ ca tatas taiḥ gataiḥ saḥ eṣa devaḥ nṛsiṃhaḥ sahasra ākṛtiḥ sarva pād sarva bāhuḥ sahasra īkṣaṇaḥ soma sūrya agni netraḥ tadā saṃsthitaḥ sarvam āvṛtya māyī tam tuṣṭuvuḥ sura śreṣṭhāḥ lokāḥ loka acale stitāḥ sa brahmakāḥ sa sādhyāḥ ca sa yamāḥ sa marūt gaṇāḥ jyotiṣām tu paran jyotiḥ paramātmā jagat mayaḥ sthūlam sūkṣmam su sūkṣmam ca śabdabrahma mayaḥ śubhaḥ yajñabhuj yajñamūrtiḥ tvam yajñinām phala daḥ prabhuḥ bhavān matsya ākṛtiḥ kaurmam āsthāya jagati sthitaḥ vārāhim ca eva tām saiṃhīm āsthāya iha vyavasthitaḥ devānām deva rakṣā artham nihatya ditija īśvaram dvija śāpa chalena evam avatīrṇaḥ asi līlayā na dṛṣṭam yat tvad anyam hi bhavān sarvam carācaram bhavān viṣṇuḥ bhavān rudraḥ bhavān eva pitāmahaḥ māyayā bahudhā saṃstham advitīya mayam prabho toṣyāmaḥ tvām katham bhāsi devadeva mṛgādhipa na jagāma dvijāḥ śāntim mānayan yonim ātmanaḥ yaḥ nṛsiṃha stavam bhaktyā paṭhet vā artham vicārayet śravayet vā dvijān sarvān viṣṇu loke mahīyate tad antare śivam devāḥ sa indrāḥ sa brahmakāḥ prabhum saṃprāpya tuṣṭavuḥ sarvam vijñāpya mṛga rūpiṇaḥ tatas brahma ādayaḥ tūrṇam saṃstūya parameśvaram ātma trāṇāya śaraṇam jagmuḥ parama kāraṇam mandara stham mahādevam krīḍamānam saha umayā sevitam gaṇa gandharvaiḥ siddhaiḥ apsarasām gaṇaiḥ praṇamya daṇḍa vat bhūmau tuṣṭāva parameśvaram namaḥ śivāya rudrāya śaṃkarāya śivāya te ugraḥ asi sarva bhūtānām niyantā asi śivaḥ asi naḥ namaḥ śivāya śarvāya śaṃkarāya ārti hariṇe mayaskarāya viśvāya viṣṇave brahmaṇe namaḥ hiraṇyabāhave sākṣāt hiraṇyapataye namaḥ śarvāya sarva rūpāya puruṣāya namaḥ namaḥ sat asat vyakti hīnāya mahataḥ kāraṇāya te nityāya viśvarūpāya jāyamānāya te namaḥ mahudhā loke prabhūtāya namaḥ namaḥ kālāya kāla pūpāya namaḥ kāla aṅga hāriṇe devāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ mahīyase namaḥ tubhyam hantre deva arīṇām sadā tārāya ca sutārāya tāraṇāya namaḥ namaḥ harikeśāya devāya śaṃbhave paramātmane devānām śambhave tubhyam bhūtānām śambhave namaḥ śaṃbhave haimavatyāḥ ca manyave rudra rūpiṇe kapardine namaḥ tubhyam kālakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ hiraṇyāya maheśāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namaḥ namaḥ bhasma digdha śarīrāya daṇḍa muṇḍī īśvarāya ca namaḥ hrasvāya dīrghāya vāmanāya namaḥ namaḥ bhīmāya bhīma rūpāya bhīma karma ratāya te sadyāya sadya rūpāya sadyojātāya te namaḥ vāmāya vāma rūpāya vāma netrāya te namaḥ aghora rūpāya vikaṭāya vikaṭa śarīrāya te nāmaḥ puruṣa rūpāya puruṣa eka tatpuruṣāya vai namaḥ puruṣa artha pradānāya pataye parameṣṭhine īśānāya namaḥ te īśvarāya namaḥ namaḥ brahmaṇe brahma rūpāya namaḥ sākṣāt śivāya te sarva viṣṇuḥ nṛsiṃhasya rūpam āsthāya viśva kṛt daitya indraiḥ bahubhiḥ sārdham hita artham jagantām prabhuḥ saiṃhīm samānayan yonim bādhate nikhilam jagat ugraḥ asi sarva duṣṭānām niyantā asi śivaḥ asi naḥ trāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān śukram tu vṛttam viśveśa krīḍāḥ vai kevalam vayam tava unmeṣa nimeṣābhyām asmākam pralaya udayau saṃtaptāsmaḥ asmaḥ vayam deva hariṇā amita tejasā uvāca vijñāpitaḥ tathā devaḥ prahasan prāha tān surān abhayam ca dadau teṣām haniṣyām iti tam prabhuḥ saḥ api śakraḥ suraiḥ sārdham praṇipatya yathāgatam paraḥ brahmā tathā anye ca sura uttamāḥ atha utthāya mahādevaḥ śārabham rūpam āsthitaḥ yayau prānte nṛsiṃhasya garvitasya mṛga āśinaḥ apahṛtya tadā prāṇān śarabhaḥ sura pūjitaḥ siṃhāt tatas naraḥ bhūtvā jagāma ca yathākramam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyat vā api saṃstavam śārvam uttamam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge nārasiṃhe pañcanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham devaḥ mahādevaḥ viśva saṃhāra kārakaḥ śarabha ākhyam mahā ghoram vikṛtam rūpam āsthitaḥ kiṅkim dhairyam kṛtam tena brūhi sarvam aseṣataḥ uvāca ātmanaḥ bhairavam rūpam mahāpralaya kārakam mad ājagāma purā sadyas gaṇānām agratas hasan nṛsiṃha rūpaiḥ ati ugraiḥ koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ krīḍadbhiḥ ca mahā dhīraiḥ brahma ādyaiḥ kundukaiḥ iva a dṛṣṭa pūrvaiḥ anyaiḥ ca veṣṭitaḥ vīra vanditaḥ ātta śastraḥ jaṭā jūṭe jvalat bāla indu maṇḍitaḥ bāla indu dvitaya ākāra tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭra aṅkura dvayaḥ maṇḍaladhanuḥ khaṇḍa saṃnibha bhrū latā yutaḥ mahā pracaṇḍa huṅkāra badhirīkṛta diṅmukhaḥ nīla megha añjana ākāra bhīṣaṇa śmaśruḥ adbhutaḥ vādakhaṇḍam akhaṇḍābhyām bhrāmayan triśikham muhur vīrabhadraḥ api bhagavān vīra śakti vijṛṃbhitaḥ svayam vijñāpayāmāsa kim atra smṛti kāraṇam mayi śrī bhagavant uvāca sa nṛsiṃha agniḥ śamaya enam durāsadam sāṃtvayan bodhaya ādau tam tena kim na upaśāmyati sūkṣmam sūkṣmeṇa saṃhṛtya sthūlam sthūlena tejasā vaktram ānaya kṛttim ca vīrabhadra mama ājñayā iti ādiṣṭaḥ gaṇādhyakṣaḥ praśānta vapuḥ āsthitaḥ uvāca vākyam īśānaḥ pitāputram iva aurasam uvāca jantu cakram bhagavantā rakṣitam matsya rūpiṇā bibharṣi kūrma rūpeṇa vārāheṇa uddhṛtā mahī tvam eva sarva bhūtānām prabhāvaḥ prabhuḥ avyayaḥ yadā yadā hi lokasya duḥkham kiñcid prajāyate tadā tadā avatīrṇaḥ tvam kariṣyasi nirāmayam tvayā dharmāḥ ca vedāḥ ca śubhe mārge pratiṣṭhitāḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ śāntayā girā śrī nṛsiṃhaḥ uvāca idānīm saṃhariṣyāmi jagant etat carācaram saṃharttuḥ na hi saṃhāraḥ svatas vā paratas api vā aham hi sarva śaktīnām pravartaka nivartakaḥ devatā parama artha jñāḥ mama eva paramam viduḥ mad aṃśāḥ śakti saṃpannāḥ brahma śakra ādayaḥ surāḥ mad nābhi paṅkajāt jātaḥ purā brahmā caturmukhaḥ rajasā adhiṣṭhitaḥ sraṣṭā rudraḥ tāmasaḥ ucyate viśva adhikaḥ svatantraḥ ca kartā hartā akhila īśvaraḥ idam tu mad param tejaḥ kaḥ punar śrotum icchati atas mām śaraṇam prāpya gaccha tvam vigata jvaraḥ avehi paramam bhāvam idam bhūta mahā īśvaraḥ kāle asmi aham kāla vināśa hetuḥ lokān samāharttum aham pravṛttaḥ mṛtyoḥ mṛtyum viddhi mām vīrabhadra jīvanti ete mad prasādena devāḥ uvāca sa ahaṅkāram idam śrutvā hareḥ āmata vikramaḥ vihasya uvāca sa avajñam tatas visphurita adharaḥ uvāca kim na jānāsi viśveśam saṃhartāram pinākinam asat vādaḥ vivādaḥ ca vināśaḥ tvayi kevalaḥ tava anyonya avatārāṇi kāni śeṣāṇi sāṃpratam kṛta aniyena kena api kathā śeṣaḥ bhaviṣyati doṣam tvam paśya etat tvam avasthām īdṛśīm gataḥ tena saṃhāra dakṣeṇa kṣaṇāt saṃkṣayam eṣyasi tvad nābhi paṅkajāt jātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ sṛṣṭi arthena jagant pūrvam śaṃkaram nīlalohitam tad lalāṭāt abhūt śaṃbhoḥ sṛṣṭi artham tat na dūṣaṇam aṃśaḥ ūham devadevasya mahābhairava rūpiṇaḥ evam rakṣaḥ vidārya eva tvam śakti kalayā yutaḥ upakāraḥ hi asādhūnām apakārāya kevalam adya api tava nikṣiptam kapālam kūrma rūpiṇaḥ vismṛtam kim tad aṃśena daṃṣṭra utpātana pīḍitaḥ dakṣa yajñe śiraḥ chinnam mayā te yajña rūpiṇaḥ adya api tava putrasya brahmaṇaḥ pañcamam śiraḥ tad aṃśam tasya tad valam kaṇḍūyamāne śirasi katham tat vismṛtam tvayā kutas prāptam kṛtam kena tvayā tat api vismṛtam te mayā sakalāḥ lokāḥ gṛhītāḥ tvam payonidhau nidrā paravaśaḥ śeṣe sa katham sāttvikaḥ bhavān tvad ādiḥ tam vaṣarī antam rudra śakti vijṛṃbhitam tad tejasaḥ api mahātmyam yuvam draṣṭum na hi kṣamau sthūlāḥ ye hi prapaśyanti tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam dyāvāpṛthivyāḥ indra agni yamasya varuṇasya ca dhvānta udare śaśāṅkasya janitvā parameśvaraḥ tvam mahākālaḥ kāla kālaḥ maheśvaraḥ sthiradhanvā kṣayaḥ vīraḥ vīraḥ viśva adhikaḥ prabhuḥ upahastāḥ jvaram bhīmaḥ mṛga pakṣi hiraṇmayaḥ śāstā aśeṣasya jagataḥ na tvam na eva caturmukhaḥ ittham sarvam samālokya saṃhāra ātmānam ātmanā no ced idānīm krodhasya mahābhairava rūpiṇaḥ vajra aśaniḥ iva sthāṇoḥ tu evam mṛtyuḥ patiṣyati uvāca atra antare mahā ghoram vipakṣa bhaya kāraṇam vīrabhadrasya tat rūpam tad kṣaṇāt eva dṛśyate na tāt hiraṇmayam saumyam na sauram na agni saṃbhavam tadā tejāṃsi sarvāṇi tasmin līnāni śāṅkare rudra sādhāraṇam ca eva cihnita vikṛta ākṛti tatas saṃhāra rūpeṇa su vyaktaḥ parameśvaraḥ paśyatām sarva devānām jaya śabda ādi maṅgalaiḥ sahasra bāhuḥ jaṭilaḥ candra ardha kṛta śekharaḥ sa mṛga ardha śarīreṇa pakṣābhyām cañcunā dvijāḥ ati tīkṣṇa mahā daṃṣṭraḥ vajra tulya nakha āyudhaḥ kaṇṭhe kālaḥ mahā bāhuḥ catuṣpād vahni saṃbhavaḥ yuga anta udyata jīmūta bhīma gambhīra niḥsvanaḥ samam kupita vṛtta agni vyāvṛtta nayana trayaḥ spaṣṭa daṃṣṭra udhara uṣṭhaḥ ca huṅkāreṇa yutaḥ haraḥ atha vibhramya pakṣābhyām nābhi pādebhiḥ udārayan pādau ābadhya pucchena bāhubhyām bāhu maṇḍalam uḍḍīya uḍḍīya bhagavān pakṣa āghāta vimohitam harim harantam vṛṣabham viśva īśānam tam īśvaram anuyānti surāḥ sarve namaḥ vākyena tuṣṭuvuḥ nīyamānaḥ para vaśaḥ dīna vaktraḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ tuṣṭāva parameśānam hariḥ tam lalita akṣaraiḥ śrī nṛsiṃhaḥ uvāca namaḥ rudrāya śarvāya mahāgrāsāya viṣṇave namaḥ bhavāya śarvāya śaṃkarāya śivāya te kāla kālāya kālāya mahākālāya mṛtyave vīrāya vīrabhadrāya kṣayadvīrāya śūline mahādevāya mahate paśūnām pataye namaḥ ekasmai nīlakaṇṭhāya śrīkaṇṭhāya pinākine parasmai parameśāya parātparatarāya te parātparāya viśvāya namaḥ te viśvamūrtaye namaḥ viṣṇu kalatrāya viṣṇu kṣetrāya bhānave kaivartāya kirātāya mahā vyādhāya śāśvate bhairavāya śaraṇyāya mahābairava rūpiṇe namaḥ nṛsiṃha saṃhartre kāma kāla purāraye mahā pāśa ogha saṃhartre viṣṇu māyā anta kāriṇe tryaṃbakāya tryakṣarāya śipiviṣṭāya mīḍhuṣe mṛtyuṃjayāya śarvāya sarvajñāya makha araye makha īśāya vareṇyāya namaḥ te vahni rūpiṇe mahā ghrāṇāya jihvāya prāṇa apāna pravarttine triguṇāya triśūlāya guṇa atītāya yogine saṃsārāya pravāhāya mahā yantra pravartine vara dāya avatārāya sarva kāraṇa hetave amoghāya agni netrāya lakulīśāya śambhave bhiṣaktamāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine yoga rūpiṇe meghavāhāya devāya pārvatīpataye namaḥ sthāṇave kṛtti vāsāya namaḥ pañcārtha hetave yogi īśvarāya nityāya satyāya parameṣṭhine uvāca nāmnām aṣṭaśatena evam stutvā amṛta mayena tu punar tu pārthayāmāsa nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabha īśvaram yadā yadā mama ajñānam ati ahaṃkāra dūṣitam evam vijñāpayan prītaḥ śaṃkaram narakesarī nanu aśaktaḥ bhavān viṣṇo jīvitāntam parājitaḥ tad vaktra śeṣa mātra antam kṛtvā sarvasya vigraham tadā maṅgam vīrabhadraḥ kṣaṇāt tatas ūcuḥ atha brahma ādayaḥ sarve varībhadra tvayā dṛśā jīvitāḥ smaḥ vayam devāḥ parjanyena iva pādapāḥ vātaḥ vāti ca sosi tvam mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ yat avyaktam param vyoma kalā atītam sadāśivam na viddhi paramam dhāma rūpa lāvaṇya varṇane upasargeṣu sarveṣu trāyasva asmān gaṇādhipa bhagavant vartate rūpavān haraḥ īdṛśān te avatārāṇi dṛṣṭvā śiva bahūn tamaḥ kadācid saṃdihet na asmān tvad cintā astamayā tathā guñja giri vara taṭa amita rūpāṇi sarvaśas gamyam te na nītavyam parāparā dve tanū tava tudrasya veda jñāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ viduḥ ghorā api anyā śivā api anyā te pratyekam anekadhā iha asmān pāhi bhagavan iti ahata mahā balaḥ brahma viṣṇu īndra candra ādi vayam ca pramukhāḥ surāḥ sura asurāḥ saṃprasūtāḥ tvattaḥ sarve maheśvara brahmā ca indraḥ viṣṇuḥ ca yama ādyāḥ na sura asurān atas asmān pāhi bhagavant surā dānaiḥ abhīpsitaiḥ uvāca tān surān devaḥ mahā ṛṣiḥ ca purātanān yathā jale jalam kṣiptam kṣīram kṣīre ghṛtam ghṛte ekaḥ eva tadā viṣṇuḥ śiva līnaḥ na ca anyathā eṣaḥ eva nṛsiṃha ātmā sa darpaḥ ca mahā balaḥ jagat saṃhāra kāreṇa pravṛttaḥ narakesarī etāvat uktvā bhagavān vīrabhadraḥ mahā balaḥ apaśyān sarva bhūtānām tatra eva antaradhīyata nṛsiṃha kṛtti vasanaḥ tadā prabhṛti śaṅkaraḥ vaktram tat muṇḍa mālāyām nāyaka tvena kalpitam tatas devāḥ nirātaṅkāḥ kīrtayantaḥ kathām imām yaḥ idam param ākhyānam puṇyam vedaiḥ samanvitam paṭhitvā śṛṇute ca eva sarva duḥkha vināśanam dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam ārogyam puṣṭi vardhanam apamṛtyu praśamanam mahā śānti karam śubham tatas duḥsvapna śamanam sarva bhūta nivāraṇam śeṣa lokasya sopānam vāñchita artha eka sādhanam eva idam tu śarabha ākāram param rūpam pinākinaḥ ca taiḥ eva paṭhitavyam ca śrotavyam ca śiva ātmabhiḥ śiva utsaveṣu sarveṣu caturdaśī aṣṭamīṣu ca paṭhet pratiṣṭhā kāleṣu śiva sannidhi kāraṇam cora vyāghra hi siṃha antakṛtaḥ rāja bhayeṣu ca atra anya utpāta bhūkaṃpa davāgni pāṃsu vṛṣṭiṣu ulkā pāte mahā vāte vinā vṛṣṭyā ativṛṣṭiṣu yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api stavam sarvam anuttamam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śarabhaprādurbhāvaḥ nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ uvāca āsīt antaka saṃkāśaḥ tapasā labdha vikramaḥ tena devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ brahmānam vai jalaṃdharaḥ mad deva devaśam viṣṇum viśva haram gurum provāca idam dityāḥ putrān nyāya dhīḥ jetum īśvaram tam jitvā sarvam īśānam gaṇapaiḥ nadinā kṣaṇāt vāsava tvam ca vaḥ dāsye dānava puṃgavāḥ jalandhara vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānava adhamāḥ jagarjuḥ uccais pāpiṣṭhāḥ mṛtyu darśana tatparāḥ bhavaḥ api dṛṣṭvā daitya indram meru kūṭam iva sthitam brahmaṇaḥ vacanam rakṣan rakṣakaḥ jagantām prabhuḥ sa aṃbaḥ sa nandī sa gamaḥ provāca prahasan iva kim kṛtyam asura īśāna yuddhena anena sāṃpratam jalandharaḥ api tat vākyam śrutvā śrotra vidāraṇam vākyena alam mahā bāho devadeva vṛṣadhvaja candra aṃśu sannibhaiḥ śastraiḥ hara yoddhum iha āgataḥ niśamya āsya vacaḥ śūlī pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā mahā ambhasi cakāra āśu rathāṅgam raudram āyudham kṛtvā arṇava ambhasi sitam bhagavant rathāṅgam smṛtvā jagattrayam anena hatāḥ surāḥ ca balavān yadi ca uddhartum tiṣṭha yoddhum na ca anyathā gadām uddhṛtya hatvā ca nandinam tvām ca śaṃkara hatvā lokān suraiḥ sārdham ḍuṇḍubhān garuḍaḥ yathā indra agni yama vitteśa vāyu vārīśvara ādayaḥ samastān parvatān prāpya gharṣitāḥ ca gaṇeśvara giri indraḥ mandaraḥ śrīmān nalaḥ meruḥ su śobhanaḥ bāhu daṇḍena kaṇḍū noda artham āpatat gaṅgā niruddhā bāhubhyām līlā artham himavat girau nārīṇām mama bhṛtyaiḥ ca vajraḥ baddhaḥ divaukasām vaḍabāyāḥ mukham bhagnam gṛhītvā vai kareṇa tu tad kṣaṇāt eva sakalam ca ekārṇavam abhūt idam airāvata ādayaḥ nāgāḥ kṣiptaḥ sindhu jala upari garuḍaḥ api mayā baddhaḥ nāgapāśena viṣṇunā urvaśī ādyāḥ mayā nītāḥ nāryaḥ kāra gṛha antaram kathañcid labdhavān śakraḥ śacīm ekām praṇamya mām mām na jānāsi daitya indram jalaṃdharam umāpate uvāca mahān te devāḥ śakti musalaiḥ sāyakaiḥ nata parvabhiḥ parājitāḥ tadā devāḥ devadeva īśvaram harim praṇemuḥ tam sureśānam śoka saṃvigna mānasāḥ tān samīkṣya atha bhagavān devadeva īśvaraḥ hariḥ vatsāḥ dhātrī īśaḥ śākalyaḥ śarvarīpatiḥ parama artha guruḥ dṛṣṭiḥ guruḥ āśrita vatsalaḥ rasaḥ rasajñaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva sattva avalambanaḥ uvāca evam nāmnām sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam snāpayāmāsa ca vibhuḥ pūjayāmāsa paṅkajaiḥ parīkṣā artham hareḥ pūjā kamaleṣu maheśvaraḥ gopayāmāsa kamalam tadā ekam bhuvaneśvaraḥ pūjayāmāsa bhāvena nāmnā tena jagadgurum tatas tatra vibhuḥ dṛṣṭvā tathābhūtam haraḥ harim tasmāt avatatāra āśu maṇḍalāt pāvakasya ca koṭi bhāskara saṃkāśam jaṭā mukuṭa maṇḍitam jvālā mālā vṛtam divyam tīkṣṇan daṃṣṭram bhayaṃkaram śūla ṭaṅka gadā cakra kunta pāśa dharam haram itthaṃbhūtam tadā dṛṣṭvā bhavam bhasma vibhūṣitam hṛṣṭaḥ namaścakāra āśu devadevam janārdanaḥ tadā prāha mahādevaḥ prahasan iva śaṃkaraḥ saṃprekṣya praṇayāt viṣṇum kṛta añjali puṭam sthitam jñātam mayā idam adhunā deva kāryam janārdana sudarśana ākhyam cakram ca dadāmi te śobhanam yat rūpam bhavatā dṛṣṭam sarva loka bhayaṃkaram śāntam raṇa ajire viṣṇo devānām duḥkha sādhanam śāntasya ca astram śāntasya ācchāntena astra īma kim phalam śāntasya samare ca astram śāntiḥ eva tapasvinam yoddhuḥ śāntyā bala chedaḥ parasya bala vṛddhi daḥ devaiḥ aśāntaiḥ yat rūpam madīyam bhāvaya avyayam kim āyudhena kāryam vai yoddhum deva ari sūdanaiḥ kṣamā yudhi na kāryam vai yoddhum deva ari sūdana tadā prabhṛti tam prāhuḥ padmākṣam iti suvratam dattvā enam nayanam cakram viṣṇave nīlalohitaḥ pasparśa ca karābhyām vai su śubhābhyām uvāca ha vara doham vara śreṣṭha varān varaya ca īpsitān bhaktyā vaśīkṛtaḥ nūnam tvayā aham puruṣottama tat śrutvā vacanam tasya dayāvān sutarām bhavaḥ pasparśa ca dadau tasmai śraddhām śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ prāha ca evam mahādevaḥ paramātmānam acyutam mātaram pitaram dakṣam bhaviṣyati sureśvarī bhaginīm te kalyāṇām devīm haimavatīm umām mad saṃbandhī ca lokānām madhye pūjyaḥ bhaviṣyasi mām divyena ca bhāvena tadā prabhṛti śaṅkaram ayācata mahādevam munibhiḥ samam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet vā dvijottamān ghṛta ādyau snāpayet rudram stālyā vai kalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ nāmnām sahasreṇa anena śraddhayā śivam īśvaram tasmāt nāmnām sahasreṇa dvijāḥ japet nāmnām sahasram ca sa yāti paramām gatim iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge sahasranāmabhiḥ pūjanāt viṣṇu cakra lābhaḥ nāma aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ saṃbhavaḥ sūcitaḥ devyāḥ tvayā sūta mahāmate menā ja tvam mahādevyāḥ dakṣa yajña vimardanam viṣṇunā ca katham dattā devadevāya śambhave kalyāṇam vā katham tasya vaktum arhasi sāṃpratam teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇika uttamaḥ saṃbhavam ca mahādevyāḥ prāha teṣām mahātmanām uvāca yuṣmābhiḥ vai kumārāya tena vyāsāya dhīmate vacanāt vaḥ mahābhāgāḥ praṇamya umām tathā bhavam sā bhaga ākhyā jagaddhātrī liṅga mūrteḥ tri vedikā liṅgaḥ tu bhagavān dvābhyām jagat sṛṣṭiḥ dvijottamāḥ liṅga vedi samāyogāt ardhanārīśvaraḥ bhavat prāhiṇoti sma tasya eva jñānam jñāna mayaḥ haraḥ viśva adhikaḥ asau bhagavant ardhanārīśvaraḥ vibhuḥ hiraṇyagarbham tam devaḥ jāyamānam apaśyata saḥ upi rudram mahādevam brahmā apaśyata śaṃkaram tam dṛṣṭvā saṃsthitam devam ardhanārīśvaram prabhum tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ vara dam vārija udbhavaḥ vibhajasva iti viśveśam viśvātmānam ajaḥ vibhuḥ sasarja devīm vāma aṅgāt patnīm ca eva ātmanaḥ samām śraddhā hi asya śubhā patnī tatas puṃsaḥ surātanī sā eva ājñayā vibhoḥ devī dakṣa putrī babhūva ha satī saṃjñā tadā sā vai rudram eva āśritā patim dakṣam vinindya kālena devī hi abhūt punar nāradasya eva dakṣaḥ api śāpāt evam vinindya ca an ādṛtya kṛtim jñātvā satī dakṣeṇa tad kṣaṇāt bhasmīkṛtvā ātmanaḥ deham yoga mārgeṇasā punar babhūva pārvatī devī tapasā ca gireḥ prabhoḥ jñātvā etat bhagavant bhargaḥ dadāha ruṣitaḥ prabhuḥ viṣṇunā lokapālān ca śaśāpa ca muni īśvaraḥ vināśaḥ vai kṣaṇāt eva māyayā śaṃkarasya vai iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge devīsaṃbhavaḥ nāma navanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ vijitya viṣṇunā sārdham bhagavant parameśvaraḥ uvacā dakṣa yajñe su vipule devān viṣṇu purogamān dadāha bhagavant rudraḥ sarvān muni gaṇān api bhadraḥ nāma gaṇaḥ tena preṣitaḥ parameṣṭhinā saḥ sṛjat vīrabhadraḥ ca gaṇeśān roma jān śubhān gaṇa īśvaraiḥ samāruhya ratham bhadraḥ pratāpavān gaṇa īśvarāḥ ca te sarve vividha āyudha pāṇayaḥ yajña vāṭaḥ tathā tasya gaṅgādvāra samīpatas tad deśe ca eva vikhyātam śubham kanakhalam dvijāḥ dagdhum vai preṣitaḥ ca asau bhagavān parameṣṭhinā tadā utpātaḥ babhūva atha lokānām bhaya śaṃsanaḥ parvatāḥ ca vyaśīryanta pracakaṃpe vasuṃdharā marutaḥ ca api aghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makara ālayaḥ grahāḥ ca na prakāśyante na devāḥ na ca dānavāḥ tatas kṣaṇāt praviśya eva yajña vāṭam mahātmanaḥ roma jaiḥ sahitaḥ bhadraḥ kālāgniḥ iva ca aparaḥ samparkāt eva dakṣa ādya munīn devān pinākinā dagdhum saṃproṣitaḥ ca aham bhavantam sa muni īśvaraiḥ iti uktvā yajña śālām tām dadāha gaṇa puṃgavaḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ ca saṃkruddhāḥ yūpān utpāṭya cikṣipuḥ gṛhītvā gaṇapāḥ sarvān gaṅgā srotasi cikṣipuḥ vyaṣṭaṃbhayat adīna ātmā tathā anyeṣām divaukasām bhagasya netre ca utpāṭya karaja agreṇa līlayā nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaḥ ca evam nyapātayat tathā candramasam devam pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā gharṣayāmāsa bhagavān vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān vahneḥ hasta dvayam chittvā jihvām utpāṭya līlayā jaghāna mūrdhani pādena vīrabhadraḥ mahā balaḥ jaghāna devam īśānam triśūleṇa mahā balam trayaḥ ca tri śatam teṣām tri sāhasram ca līlayā trayam ca eva suredrāṇām jaghāna ca muni īśvarān anyān ca devān devaḥ usau sarvān yuddhāya saṃsthitān jaghāna bhagavant nudraḥ khaḍga muṣṭi ādi sāyakaiḥ atha viṣṇuḥ mahādejāḥ cakram udyamya mūrchitaḥ viṣṇoḥ yoga balāt tasya divya dehāḥ su dāruṇāḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā hastāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ ca jajñire tān sarvān api nihatya gadayā viṣṇum tāḍayāmāsa mūrdhani tatas ca urasi tam devam līlayā eva raṇa ajire papāta ca tadā bhūmau visaṃjñaḥ puruṣottamaḥ krodha rakta īkṣamaḥ śrīmān atiṣṭhat puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ vyaṣṭaṃbhayat adīna ātmā kara stham na cacāla saḥ atiṣṭhat staṃbhitaḥ tena śṛṅgavant iva niścalaḥ tribhiḥ ca dharṣitam śārṅgam tridhā bhūtam prabhoḥ tadā śārṅgam koṭi prasaṅgāt vai ciccheda ca śiraḥ prabhoḥ vāyunā preritam ca eva prāṇa jena pinākinā pradīpita mahā śālam dṛṣṭvā yajñaḥ api dudruve te tadā mṛga rūpeṇa dhāvantam gaganam prati vīrabhadraḥ samādhāya viśiraskam atha akarot ariṣṭaneminam vīraḥ bahu putram muni īśvaram munīm aṅgirasam ca eva kṛṣṇāśvam ca mahā balaḥ nikṛtya karaja agreṇa varibhadraḥ pratāpavān bhadram āha mahā tejāḥ prārthayan praṇataḥ prabhuḥ saḥ api bhadraḥ prabhāveṇa brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ śamam jagāma śanakais śāntaḥ tasthau tad ājñayā sa gaṇaḥ sarva daḥ śarvaḥ sarva loka maheśvaraḥ hatānām ca tadā teṣām pradadau pūrvavat tanum dakṣasya ca muni indrasya tathā anyeṣām maheśvaraḥ vāgīśyāḥ ca eva nāsā agram devamātryāḥ tathā eva ca naṣṭānām jīvitam ca eva varāṇi vividhāni ca kalpayāmāsa vai vaktram līlayā ca mahān bhavaḥ dakṣaḥ api labdha saṃjñaḥ ca samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ tuṣṭāva devadeveśam śaṅkaram vṛṣabhadhvajam stutaḥ tena mahā tejāḥ pradāya vividhān varān gām apatyam dadau tasmai dakṣāya akliṣṭa karmaṇe devāḥ ca sarve deveśam tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavān tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ devaḥ deveśam nīlakaṇṭham vṛṣadhvajam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge śivakṛddakṣayajñavidhvaṃsanaḥ nāma śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham himavataḥ putrī babhūva aṃbā satī śubhā katham vā devadeveśam avāpa patim īśvaram uvāca sā menā tanum āśritya sva icchayā eva vara aṅganā tadā haimavatī jajñe tapasā ca dvijottamāḥ ca dvādaśe ca tadā varṣe pūrṇe haimavatī śubhā tapaḥ tepe tayā sārdham anujā ca śubha ānanā ṛṣayaḥ ca tadā sarve sarva loka maheśvarīm tuṣṭuvuḥ tapasā devīm samāvṛtya samantataḥ jyeṣṭhā hi aparṇā hi anujā ca ekaparṇā śabhānanā tṛtīyā ca vārārohā tathā ca eva ekapāṭalā tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ parvātyāḥ parameśvaraḥ vaśīkṛtaḥ mahādevaḥ sarva bhūta patiḥ bhavaḥ tārā ātmajaḥ mahā tejāḥ babhūva diti nandanaḥ tasya putrāḥ trayaḥ ca api tārakākṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ vidyunmālī ca bhagavān kamalākṣaḥ ca vīryavān pitāmahaḥ tathā ca eṣām tāraḥ nāma mahā balaḥ tapasā labdha vīryaḥ ca prasādāt brahmanaḥ prabhoḥ vijitya samare pūrvam viṣṇum ca jitavan asau divyam varṣa sahasram tu divārātram aviśramam sa ratham viṣṇum ādāya cikṣepa śata yojanam tāreṇa vijitaḥ saṃkhye dudrāva garuḍadhvajaḥ tāraḥ varān śataguṇam labdhvā śataguṇam balam deva indra pramukhān jitvā devān deva īśvara īśvaraḥ taiḥ devan sarva lokeṣu māyayā devatāḥ ca saha indreṇa tārakāt bhaya pīḍitāḥ na śāntim lebhire śūrāḥ śaraṇam vā bhaya arditāḥ tadā amarapatiḥ śrīmān saṃnipatya amara prabhuḥ uvāca aṅgirasam devaḥ devānām api saṃnidhau bhagavan tārakaḥ nāma tārajaḥ dānava uttamaḥ yāni amoghāni āyudhāni aṅgiraḥ vara tāni moghāni jāyante prabhāvāt amaradviṣaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi dviguṇāni bṛhaspate viṣṇunā yodhitaḥ yuddhe tena api na ca sūditaḥ yaḥ tena anirjitaḥ yuddhe viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā evam uktaḥ tu śakreṇa jīvaḥ sārdham sura adhipaiḥ sahasrākṣeṇa ca vibhum saṃprāpya āha kuśadhvajam saḥ upi tasya mukhāt śrutvā praṇayāt praṇata ārti hā devaiḥ aśeṣaiḥ sa indraiḥ tu jīvam āha pitāmahaḥ jāne vā ūrtim suredrāṇām tathā api śṛṇu sāṃpratam vinindya dakṣaiḥ yā devī satī rudra aṅga sambhavā tasyāḥ ca eva iha rūpeṇa yūyam devāḥ sura uttamāḥ tayoḥ yogena saṃbhūtaḥ skandaḥ śakti dharaḥ prabhuḥ bhujaḥ senā nīḥ pāvakiḥ prabhuḥ svāheyaḥ kārtikeyaḥ ca gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhāmajaḥ devaḥ śākhaḥ viśākhaḥ ca naigama īśaḥ ca vīryavān senāpatiḥ kumāra ākhyaḥ sarva loka namaskṛtaḥ līlayā eva mahāsenaḥ prabalam tāraka asuram evam uktaḥ tadā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā śikharam āsādya smaram sasmāra suvrataḥ ratyā samam samāgamya namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ sa śakram āha tam jīvam jagajjīvaḥ dvijottamāḥ smṛtaḥ yat bhavatā jīva saṃprāptaḥ ham tava antikam śaṃkareṇa ambikām adya saṃyojaya yathāsukham tena mārgeṇa mārgasva patnyā ratyā anayā saha saḥ api tuṣṭaḥ mahādevaḥ pradāsyati śubhām gatim viprayuktaḥ tayā pūrvam tām girijām umām devadeva āśramam gantum matim cakre tayā saha gatvā tad aśraye śaṃbhoḥ saha ratyā mahā balaḥ nayanena tṛtīyena sa avajñam tam eva aikṣata adahat tad kṣaṇāt eva lalāpa karuṇam ratiḥ ratyāḥ pralāpam ākarṇya devadevaḥ vṛpadhvajaḥ kṛpayā parayā prāha kāma patnīm nirībhya ca yadā viṣṇuḥ ca bhavitā vāsudevaḥ mahā yaśāḥ śāpāt bhṛgoḥ mahā tejāḥ sarva loka hitāya vai sā praṇamya tadā rudram kāmapatnī śuci smitā iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge madanadāhaḥ nāma eka adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ hitāya ca āśramāṇām ca krīḍā artham bhagavant bhavaḥ jagāma sa svayam brahmā marīci ādyaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ tapaḥ vanam mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ padam saṃbhavaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca tām devīm sa jagatoraṇīm tapasā lokān saṃtāpayasi śailaje tvayā sṛṣṭam jagat sarvam mātar tvam mā vimāśaya tvam hi saṃdhāraye lokān imān sarvān sva tejasā saḥ evam parameśānaḥ svayam ca varayiṣyati vara de yena sṛṣṭā asi na vinā yaḥ tvayā ambike iti uktvā tām namaskṛtya muhur saṃprekṣya pārvatīm bhāga anugraham karttum dvija rūpeṇa ca āśramam sā ca dṛṣṭvā māhadevam dvija rūpeṇa saṃsthitam pratibhā ādyaiḥ prabhum jñātvā nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam saṃpūjya vara dam devam brāhmaṇa chadmanā gatam tuṣṭāva parameśānam pārvatī parameśvaram kula dharma āśrayam rakṣan bhūdharasya mahātmanaḥ krīḍā artham ca saṃtām madhye sarva deva patiḥ bhavaḥ āsthāya rūpam yat saumyam sameṣya iham saha tvayā iti uktvā tām samālokya devaḥ divyena cakṣuṣā jagāma iṣṭam tadā divyam sva puram prayayau ca sā dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭaḥ tadā devīm menayā tuhinācalaḥ āliṅgya āghrāya saṃpūjya putrīm sākṣāt tapasvinīm svayaṃvaram tadā devyāḥ sarva lokeṣu aghoṣayat atha brahmā ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sākṣāt janārdanaḥ tvaṣṭā aryamā vivasvant ca yamaḥ varuṇaḥ eva ca vāyuḥ somaḥ tathā īśānaḥ rudrāḥ ca munayaḥ tathā aśvinaḥ dvādaśa ādityāḥ gandharvāḥ garuḍaḥ tathā yakṣāḥ sādhyāḥ daityāḥ kimpuruṣa uragāḥ samudrāḥ ca nadāḥ vedāḥ mantrāḥ stotra ādayaḥ kṣaṇāḥ nāgāḥ ca parvatāḥ sarve yajñāḥ sūrya ādayaḥ grahāḥ trayastriṃśat ca devānām trayaḥ ca tri śatam tathā apsarobhiḥ pranṛttābhiḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaiḥ vandibhiḥ stūyamānā ca sthitā śailasutā tadā sita ātapatram ratna aṃśu miśritam ca avahat tathā mālinī giriputryāḥ tu saṃdhyā pūrṇa indu maṇḍalam cāmara āsakta hastābhiḥ divya strībhiḥ ca saṃvṛtā vijayā vyajanam gṛhya sthitā devyāḥ samīpa gā mālām prahṛhya devyām tu sthitāyām deva saṃsadi śiśuḥ bhūtvā mahādevaḥ krīḍā artham pṛṣabhadhvajaḥ atha dṛṣṭvā śiśum devāḥ tasyāḥ utsaṅga vartinam staṃbhitaḥ śiśu rūpeṇa devadevena līlayā vajram kṣeptum na śaśāka bāhum cālayitum tathā vahnim śaktim tathā kṣeptam na śaśāka tathā sthitaḥ yamaḥ api daṇḍam khaḍgam ca nirṛtiḥ muni puṃgavāḥ varuṇaḥ nāgapāśam ca dhvaja yaṣṭim samīraṇaḥ somaḥ gadām dhaneśaḥ ca daṇḍam daṇḍa bhṛtām varaḥ īśānaḥ ca tathā śūlam tīvram udyamya saṃsthitaḥ rudrāḥ ca śūlam ādityāḥ muśalam vasavaḥ tathā śiraḥ prakaṃpayan viṣṇuḥ cakram udyamya saṃsthitaḥ tasya api śirasaḥ bālaḥ sthira tvam pracakāra ha cakram kṣeptum na śaśāka bāhūn cālayitum na ca pūṣā dantān daśan dantaiḥ bālam aikṣata mohitaḥ tasya api daśanāḥ petuḥ dṛṣṭa mātrasya śambhunā brahmā parama saṃvignaḥ dhyānam āsthāya śaṃkaram sa buddhvā devam īśānam śīghrām utthāya vismitaḥ sa buddhva devam īśānam śīghram utthāya vismitaḥ buddhiḥ tvam sarva lokānām ahaṅkāraḥ tvam īśvaraḥ bhūtānām indriyāṇām ca tvam eva īśa pravartakaḥ tava aham dakṣiṇāt hastāt sṛṣṭaḥ pūrvam purātanaḥ iyam ca prakṛtiḥ devī sadā te sṛṣṭi kāraṇa patnī rūpam samāsthāya jagat kāraṇam āgatā prasādāt te deveśaiḥ niyogāt ca mayā prajāḥ deva ādyāḥ tu imāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ mūḍhāḥ tvad yoga mohitāḥ kuru prasādam eteṣām yathāpūrvam bhavantu ime uvāca vijñāpya evam tadā brahmā devadevam maheśvaram san tantitān tadā tena bhagavant āha padmajaḥ devatāḥ sarvāḥ na eva budhyata śaṃkaram gacchadhvam śaraṇam śīghram devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ sa nārāyaṇakāḥ sarve munibhiḥ śaṃkaram prabhum sārdham mayā eva deveśam paramātmānam īśvaram praṇemuḥ manasā sarve sa nārāyaṇakāḥ prabhum yathāpūrvam cakāra āśu vacanāt brahmanaḥ prabhuḥ tejasā tasya devāḥ te sa iṃdra candra divākarāḥ sa brahmakāḥ sa sādhyāḥ ca sa nārāyaṇakāḥ tathā sa yamāḥ ca sa rudāḥ ca cakṣura prāthayan vibhum tebhyaḥ ca paramam cakṣuḥ sarva dṛṣṭau ca śaktimat dadau ambā patiḥ śarvaḥ bhavānyāḥ ca calasya ca labdhvā cakṣuḥ tadā devāḥ indra viṣṇu purogamāḥ brahma ādyāḥ nemire tūrṇam bhavānī ca giriśvaraḥ munayaḥ ca mahādevam gaṇeśāḥ śiva saṃmatāḥ sasarjuḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭim ca khecarāḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ jaguḥ gandharva mukhyāḥ ca nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ mumuhuḥ gaṇapāḥ sarvam mumoda ambā ca pārvatī tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣam tridivaukasām pādayoḥ stāpayāmāsa mālām divyām sugandhinīm saha devyāḥ namaścakruḥ śirobhiḥ bhū tala āśritaiḥ sarve sa brahmakāḥ devāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge umāsvayaṃvaraḥ nāma dvi adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atha brahmā mahādevam abhivandya kṛtāñjaliḥ udvāhaḥ kriyatām devaḥ iti uvāca maheśvaram tasya tat vacanam śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ yathā iṣṭam iti loka īśam prāha bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ udvāha artham maheśasya tad kṣaṇāt eva suvratāḥ brahmaṇā kalpitam divyam puram ratna mayam śubham atha aditiḥ ditiḥ sākṣāt danuḥ kadruḥ sukālikā siddhiḥ māyā kriyā durgā devī sākṣāt sudhā svadhā sāvitrī veda mātā ca rajanī dakṣiṇā dyutiḥ svāhā svāhā matiḥ vuddhiḥ ṛddhiḥ vṛddhiḥ sarasvatī rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī devī anumati tathā dharaṇī dhāraṇī ca ilā śacī nārāyaṇī tathā etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca devānām mātaraḥ patnayaḥ tathā udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasya iti jagmuḥ sarvāḥ mudā anvitāḥ uragāḥ garuḍāḥ yakṣāḥ gandharvāḥ kinnarāḥ gaṇāḥ sāgarāḥ girayaḥ meghāḥ māsāḥ saṃvatsarāḥ tathā vedāḥ mantrāḥ tathā yajñāḥ stomāḥ dharmāḥ ca sarvaśas huṅkāraḥ praṇavaḥ ca eva pratihārāḥ sahasraśas koṭiḥ apsarasaḥ divyāḥ tāsām ca paricārikāḥ yāḥ ca sarveṣu dvīpeṣu deva lokeṣu nimnagāḥ tāḥ ca strī vigrahāḥ sarvāḥ saṃjagmuḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ gaṇapāḥ ca mahā bhāgāḥ sarva loka namaskṛtāḥ udvāhaḥ śaṃkarasya iti tatra ājagmuḥ mudā anvitāḥ abhyayus śaṅkha varṇāḥ ca gaṇa koṭyaḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ daśabhiḥ kekara akṣaḥ ca vidyutā uṣṭābhiḥ eva ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā viśākhāḥ ca navabhiḥ pāra yātrikaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvātakaḥ śrīmān tathā eva vikṛta ānanaḥ jvālā keśaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ koṭibhiḥ gaṇa puṃgavaḥ saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmān dundubha uṣṭābhiḥ eva ca pañcabhiḥ ca kapālī īśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃdārakaḥ śubhaḥ koṭi koṭibhiḥ eva iha gaṇḍakaḥ kumbhakaḥ tathā eva iha gaṇapaḥ sarva sattamaḥ pipalaḥ ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaḥ ca tathā dvijāḥ bhiḥ sapta candratāpanaḥ mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnām gaṇapaḥ vṛtaḥ kuṇḍī dvādaśabhiḥ vīraḥ tathā parvatakaḥ śubhaḥ ca kālakaḥ ca eva mahākālaḥ śatena vai āgnikaḥ śata koṭyā vai koṭyā agnimukhaḥ eva ca mūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā ca eva dhana āvahaḥ sannāmaḥ ca śatena eva kumudaḥ koṭibhiḥ tathā amoghaḥ kokilaḥ ca eva koṭi koṭyā sumantrakaḥ kākapāṭaḥ aparaḥ ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā saṃtānakaḥ prabhuḥ mahābalaḥ ca navabhiḥ madhupiṅgaḥ ca piṅgalaḥ koṭīnām ca eva saptatyā caturvaktraḥ mahā balaḥ koṭi koṭi sahasrāṇām śataiḥ viśātibhiḥ vṛtāḥ vīrabhadraḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā roma jāḥ ca eva koṭibhiḥ karaṇaḥ ca eva viṃśatyā navatyā kevalaḥ śubhaḥ kāṣṭhakūṭaḥ catuḥ ṣaṣṭyā sukeśaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ tathā virupākṣaḥ ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ tāluketuḥ ṣaṣ āsyaḥ ca pañca āsyaḥ ca sanātanaḥ saṃvartakaḥ tathā caitraḥ lakulīśaḥ svayam prabhuḥ loka antakaḥ ca tathā daitya antakaḥ prabhuḥ mṛtyu hṛt kāla hā kālaḥ mṛtyuṃjaya karaḥ tathā devaḥ bhṛṅgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadeva priyaḥ tathā aśanīḥ bhāsakaḥ ca eva catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahasrapād ete ca anye ca gaṇapāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ mahā balāḥ sarve sahasra hastāḥ ca jaṭā mukuṭa dhāriṇaḥ candra rekhā avataṃsāḥ ca nīla kaṇṭhāḥ tri locanāḥ hāra kuṇḍala keyūra mukuṭa ādyaiḥ alaṅkṛtāḥ brahma indra viṣṇu saṃkāśāḥ aṇima ādi guṇaiḥ vṛtāḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśāḥ tatra ājagmuḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ pātāla cāriṇaḥ ca eva sarva loka nivāsinaḥ tumbaruḥ nāradaḥ hāhā hūhūḥ ca eva tu sāma gāḥ ratnāni ādāya vādyān ca tatra ājagmuḥ tadā puram ṛṣayaḥ kṛtsnaśas tatra deva gītāḥ tapodhanāḥ puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān japuḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ girijām tām alaṅkṛtya svayam eva śuci smitām puram praveśayāmāsa svayam ādāya keśavaḥ sadasi āha ca deveśam nārāyaṇam ajaḥ harim vāma aṅgāt asya rudrasya dakṣiṇa aṅgāt aham prabho mad mūrtiḥ tuhinādri īśaḥ yajña artham sṛṣṭaḥ eva hi eṣā haimavatī jajñe māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ śrauta smārta pravṛtti artham udvāha artham iha āgataḥ atas asau jagatām dhātrī dhātā te mama api ca kṣmā ap agni kha indu sūrya ātma pavana ātmā yatas bhavaḥ eṣā hi ajā śukla kṛṣṇā lohitā prakṛtiḥ bhavān śreyaḥ api śailarājena saṃbandhaḥ ayam tava api ca mad aṃśasya asya śailasya mama api ca guruḥ bhavān uvāca devāḥ ca munayaḥ sarve devadevaḥ ca śaṅkaraḥ tatas ca utthāya vidvāḥ saḥ padmanābhaḥ praṇamya tām pādau prakṣālya devasya karābhyām kamala īkṣaṇaḥ tvadīyā eṣā vivāha artham menajā hi anujā mama iti uktvā sa udakam da tvā devīm deveśvarāya tām atha sarve muni śreṣṭhāḥ sarva veda artha pāragāḥ ūcuḥ dātā gṛhītā ca phalam dravyam vicārāt eṣa devaḥ haraḥ nūnam māyayā hi tatas jagant iti uktvā tam praṇemuḥ ca prīti kaṇṭākita tvacaḥ sasṛjuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddha cāraṇāḥ deva dundubhayaḥ neduḥ nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ brahmaṇā munibhiḥ sārdham devadevam umāpatim devaḥ api devīm ālokya sa lajjām himaśailajām na tṛpyati anavadya aṅgī sā ca devam vṛṣadhvajam vara daḥ asmi iti tam prāha harim saḥ upi āha śaṃkaram dadāsi mama yadi ājñām karttavyaḥ hi akṛtaḥ vidhiḥ yat yat iṣṭam suraśreṣṭhaiḥ tat kuruṣva yathā īpsitam tatas praṇamya hṛṣṭa amāḥ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ānītān viṣṇunā viprāḥ saṃpūjya vividhaiḥ varaiḥ tris ca tam jvalanam devam kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam suraiḥ ca mānavaiḥ sarvaiḥ prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā tatas pādyam tayoḥ da tvā śambhoḥ ācamanam tathā madhuparkam tathā gām ca praṇamya ca punar śivam bhṛgo adya munayaḥ sarve ca akṣataiḥ tila taṇḍulaiḥ sūrya ādayaḥ samabhyarcya tuṣṭuvuḥ vṛṣabhadhvajam samāpya āropya ca yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api bhava udvāham śuci smitaḥ śrāvayet vā dvijān śuddhān veda vedāṅga pāragān yatra ayam kīrtyate vipraiḥ tāvat āste tadā bhavaḥ tasmāt saṃpūjya vidhivat kīrtayet na ayathā dvijāḥ udvāhe ca dvijendrāṇām kṣatriyāṇām dvijottamāḥ kṛta udvāhaḥ tadā devyā haimavatyā vṛṣadhvajaḥ sa gaṇaḥ nandinā sārdham sarva deva gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ purīm vārāṇasīm divyām ājagāma mahā dyutiḥ avimukte sukha āsīnam praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam apṛcchat kṣetra māhātmyam bhavānī harṣita ānanā vaktum mayā sureśāni ṛṣi saṃgha abhipūjitam pāpinām yatra muktiḥ syāt mṛtānām eka janmanā anyatra tu kṛtam pāpam vārāṇasyām vyapohati vārāṇasyām kṛtam pāpam paiśācya naraka āvaham kṛtvā pāpa sahasrāṇi piśāca tvam varam nṛṇām na tu śakra sahasra tvam svarge kāśi purīm vinā oṃkāra īśaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ mṛtānām na punarbhavaḥ uktvā kṣetrasya māhātmyam saṃkṣepāt śaśiśekharaḥ darśayāmāsa ca udyānam parityajya gaṇeśvarān yathāśrutam mayā sarvam prasādāt vaḥ su śobhanam iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge pārvatīvivāhavarṇanam nāma tri adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham vināyakaḥ jātaḥ gajavaktraḥ gaṇeśvaraḥ uvāca dharma vighnam tadā karttum daityānām abhavan dvijāḥ asurāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca rākṣasāḥ krūra karmiṇaḥ tāmāsāḥ ca tathā ca anye rājasāḥ ca tathā bhuvi brahmānam ca harim viprāḥ labdha īpsita varāḥ yatas tatas asmākam sura śreṣṭhāḥ sadā vijaya saṃbhavaḥ putra artham ca eva nārīṇām narāṇām karma siddhaye vighneśam śaṃkaram sraṣṭum gaṇapam stotum arhatha iti uktvā anyonyam anagham tuṣṭuvuḥ śivam īśvaram namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyam sarvajñāya pinākine anaghāya viriñcāya devyāḥ kārya artha dāyine akāyāya artha kāyāya hareḥ kāya apahāriṇe te kṛta ādi bheda kālāya kālavegāya te namaḥ dharma ādi aṣṭa padāya ca kālī viśuddha dehāya kālikā kāraṇāya te kālakaṇṭhāya mukhyāya vāhanāya varāya te hiraṇyaretase ca eva namaḥ śarvāya śūline kapāla daṇḍa pāśa asi carma aṅkuśa dharāya ca pīta śuklāya rakṣā artham surāṇām kṛṣṇavartmane pañcamāya mahā pañca yajñinām phala dāya ca pañcāsya phaṇi hārāya pañcākṣara mayāya te pañcākṣara dṛśe tubhyam parātparātarāya te bhū svara vajra aṅga vaktrāya akṣaya rūpiṇe pañcaka hastāya ca ādi hastāya te namaḥ ṭā ādi pādāya rudrāya ta ādi pādāya te namaḥ pādi meṇḍhrāya yadi aṅga dhātu saptaka dhāriṇe śānta tma rūpiṇe sākṣāt kṣa danta krodhine namaḥ lava repha hala aṅgāya niraṅgāya ca te namaḥ sarvaṣām eva bhūtānām hṛdi niḥsvana kāriṇe bhruveḥ ante sadā sadbhiḥ dṛṣṭāya atyanta bhānave bhānu soma agni netrāya paramātma svarūpiṇe guṇatraya upari sthāya tīrtha pādāya te namaḥ tīrtha tattvāya sārāya tasmāt api parasmai te mad jayuḥ sāmavedāya oṃkārāya namaḥ namaḥ oṅkāre trividham rūpam āsthāya upari vāsine pītāya kṛṣṇa varṇāya raktāya atyanta tejase sthāna pañcaka saṃsthāya pañcadhā aṇḍa bahis kramāt brahmaṇe viṣṇave tubhyam kumārāya namaḥ namaḥ ambāyāḥ parameśāya sarva upari cāraya te mūla sūkṣma svarūpāya sthūla sūkṣmāya te namaḥ sarva saṃkalpa śūnyāya sarvasmāt rakṣitāya te bhādi madhya anta śūnyāya cit saṃsthāya namaḥ namaḥ yama agni vāyu rudra ambu soma śakra niśācaraiḥ nityam sa gaṇaiḥ pūjitāya te sarvaṣu sarvadā sarva mārge saṃpūjitāya te maheśvarāya dhīrāya namaḥ sākṣāt śivāya te makha madana yama agni dakṣa yajña kṣapaṇa vicitra vicoṣṭitam kṣamasva uvāca yaḥ paṭhet tu stavam bhakyā śakra agni pramukhaiḥ suraiḥ ca kīrtitam śrāvayet vidvāḥ saḥ yāti paramām gatim iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge devastutiḥ nāma catur adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca yadā sthitāḥ sura īśvarāḥ praṇamya ca evam īśvaram tadām bikāpatiḥ bhavaḥ pinākadhṛk maheśvaraḥ dadau nirīkṣaṇam kṣaṇāt bhavaḥ sa tān sura uttamān praṇemuḥ ādarāt haram surāḥ mudā ārdra locanāḥ bhavaḥ sudhā amṛta upamaiḥ nirīkṣaṇaiḥ nirīkṣaṇāt tat āha bhadram astu vaḥ sura īśvarān maheśvaraḥ sura artham īśa vīkṣyate surāḥ gṛham gatāḥ tu ime praṇamya ca āha vākpatiḥ patim nirīkṣya nirbhayaḥ surā pakāra kāriṇām iha eṣaḥ eva naḥ varaḥ tatas tadā niśamya vai pinākadhṛk sureśvaraḥ gaṇeśvaram sureśvaram vapuḥ dadhāra saḥ śivaḥ gaṇa īśvarāḥ ca tuṣṭuvuḥ surevarāḥ maheśvaram samasta loka sambhavam bhava ārtti hāriṇam śubham triśula pāśa dhāriṇam samasta loka saṃbhavam gajānanam tadā aṃbikā daduḥ puṣpa varṣam hi siddhāḥ muni indrāḥ tathā khecarāḥ deva saṃghāḥ tadānīm tadā tuṣṭuvuḥ ca ekadantam sura īśāḥ praṇemuḥ gaṇeśam maheśam vitandrāḥ vicitra vastra bhūṣaṇaiḥ alaṅkṛtaḥ gajānano mātram sutam dṛṣṭvā cakāra bhagavant bhavaḥ gajānanāya kṛtyān tu sarvān sarveśvaraḥ svayam ādāya ca karābhyām ca su sukhābhyām bhavaḥ svayam āliṅgya āghrāya mūrdhānam mahādevaḥ jagadguruḥ tava avatāraḥ daityānām vināśāya mama ātmaja devānām upakāra artham dvijānām brahma vādinām yajñaḥ ca dakṣiṇā hīnaḥ kṛtaḥ yena mahī tale adhyāpanam ca adhyayanam vyākhyānam karma eva ca yaḥ anyāyatas karoti asmin tasya prāṇān sadā hara varṇāt cyutānām nārīṇām narāṇām nara puṃgava svadharma rahitānām ca prāṇān apahara prabho yāḥ striyaḥ tvām sadā kālam puruṣāḥ ca vināyaka yajanti tāsām teṣām ca tvad sāmyam dātum arhasi yauvana sthān ca vṛddhān ca iha amutra ca pūjitaḥ saṃpūjyaḥ vandanīyaḥ ca bhaviṣyasi na sa śaṃyaḥ mām ca nārāyaṇam vā api putraka tvām an abhyarcya kalyāṇam śrautam smārtam ca laukikam kurute tasya kalyāṇam akalyāṇam bhaviṣyati brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ ca eva gajānana saṃpūjya sarva siddhi artham bhakṣya bhojya ādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ te ca arcanīyāḥ śakra ādyaiḥ bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ ajam harim ca mām vā api śakram anyān surān api sasarja ca tadā vighna gaṇam gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ gaṇaiḥ sārdham namaskṛtvā api atiṣṭhat tasya ca agratas daityānām dharma vighnam ca cakāra asau gaṇeśvaraḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet vā sukhībhavet iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge vināyakotpattiḥ nāma pañca adhi ka śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ nṛtya āraṃbhaḥ katham śambhoḥ kimartham vā yathātatham vaktum arhasi ca naḥ śrutaḥ skanda agraja udbhavaḥ uvāca sūdayāmāsa kālāgniḥ iva devān dvijottamān dārukeṇa tadā devāḥ tāḍitāḥ pīḍitāḥ bhṛśam brahmānam ca tathā īśānam kumāram viṣṇum eva ca bādhitāḥ tena te sarve brahmāṇam prāpya vai dvijāḥ saṃprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve pitāmaha purogamāḥ brahmā prāpya ca deveśam praṇamya bahu dhānataḥ dāruṇaḥ bhagavān dāruḥ pūrvam tena vinirjitāḥ brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhaga netra hā bhavatīm prārthayāmi adya hitāya jagatām śubhe ekena aṃśena deveśam praviṣṭāḥ deva sattamam na viveda tadā brahmā devāḥ ca indra purogamāḥ girijām pūrvavat śambhoḥ dṛṣṭvā pārśva sthitām śubhām māyayā mohitaḥ tasyāḥ sarvajñaḥ api caturmukhaḥ sā praviṣṭā atanum tasya devadevasya pārvatī kaṇṭha sthena viṣeṇa asya tanum cakre tadā ātmanaḥ tām ca jñātvā tathābhūtām tṛtīyena īkṣaṇena vai sasarja kālīm kāmāriḥ kāla kaṇṭhīm kapardinīm jātā yadā kāli kāla kaṇṭhī jātā tadānīm vipulā jaya śrīḥ devetarāṇām ajayaḥ tu asiddhyā tuṣṭiḥ bhavānyāḥ parameśvarasya mā jātām tadānīm sura siddha saṃghāḥ dṛṣṭvā bhayāt dudruvuḥ āgni kalpām kālīm gara alaṅkṛta kāla kaṇṭhīm upedandra padmodbhava śakramukhyāḥ tathā eva jātam nayanam lalāṭe sitāṃśu lekhā ca sirasi udagrā kaṇṭhe karālam niśitam triśūlam kare karālam ca vibhūṣaṇāni sārdham divya aṃbarāḥ devyāḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ siddha indra siddhāḥ ca tathā piśācāḥ jajñire punar ājñayā dārukam tasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvarī dānavam sūdayāmāsa sūdayantam sura adhipān saṃraṃbha ati prasaṅgāt vai tasyāḥ sarvam idam jagat krodha agninā ca vipra indrāḥ saṃbabhūva tadā āturam bhavaḥ api bāla rūpeṇa śmaśāne preta saṃkule ruroda māyayā tasyāḥ krodha agnim pātum īsvaraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā bālam īśānam māyayā tasya mohitā utthāpya āghrāya vakṣojam stanam sā pradadau dvijāḥ stana jena tadā sārdham kopam asyāḥ papau punar krodhena anena vai bālaḥ kṣetrāṇām rakṣakaḥ abhavat mūrtayaḥ aṣṭau ca tasya api kṣetrapālasya dhīmataḥ evam vai tena bālena kṛtā sā krodha mūrchitā kṛtam asyāḥ prasāda artham devadevena tāṇḍavam saṃdhyāyām sarva bhūta indraiḥ pretaiḥ prītena śūlinā pītvā nṛtya amṛtam śambhoḥ ākaṇṭham parameśvarī tatra sa brahmakāḥ devāḥ sa indra upendrāḥ samantataḥ praṇemuḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ kālīm punar devīm ca pārvatīm evam saṃkṣepāt proktam tāṇḍavam śūlinaḥ prabhoḥ yoga ānandena ca vibhoḥ tāṇḍavam ca iti ca apare iti śrī liṅgadṛ pūrvadṛ śivatāṇḍavakathanam nāma ṣaṣ adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ purā upamanyunā sūta gāṇapatyam maheśvarāt kṣīrārṇavaḥ katham labdhaḥ vaktum arhasi sāṃpratam uvāca kumāraḥ iva tejasvī krīḍamānaḥ yadṛcchayā kadācid kṣaram alpam ca pītavān mātula āśrame mātula sutaḥ hi apibat kṣīram uttamam pītvā sthitam yathākāmam dṛṣṭvā provāca mātaram gavyam kṣīram ati svādu na alpam uṣṇam namāmi aham uvāca upalālitā evam putreṇa putram āliṅgya sa ādaram duḥkhitā vilalāpa ārtā smṛtvā nairdhanyam ātmanaḥ smṛtvā smṛtvā punar kṣīram upamanyuḥ api dvijāḥ dehi dehi iti tām āha rodamānaḥ mahā dyutiḥ uñcha vṛttyā ajintān vījān svayam viṣṭvā ca sā tadā tat āloḍya toyena kala bhāṣiṇī āliṅgya ādāya duḥkha ārtā pradadau kṛtrimam payaḥ pītvā ca kṛtrimam kṣīram mātrā dattam dvijottamaḥ na etat kṣīram iti prāha mātaram ca ati vihvalaḥ duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha saṃprekṣya āghrāya mūrdhani taṭinī ratna pūrṇāḥ te svarga pātāla gocarāḥ bhāgya hīnāḥ na paśyanti bhakti hināḥ ca ye śive rājyam svargam ca mokṣam ca bhojanam kṣīra saṃbhavam na labhante priyāṇi eṣām no tuṣyati sadā bhavaḥ kṣīram tatra kutas asmākam mahādevaḥ na pūjitaḥ bālaḥ api mātaram prāha praṇipatya tapasvinīm cirāt vā hi acirāt vā api kṣīrodam sādhayāmi aham uvāca tam āha mātā śuśubham kurvi iti sutarām sutam himavat parvatam prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ śrutvā teṣām tadā vākyam bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ kim idam tu iti saṃcintya jñātvā tad kāraṇam ca saḥ mandaram tūrṇam maheśvara didṛkṣayā dṛṣṭvā devam praṇamya evam provāca idam kṛtāñjaliḥ kṣīra artham adahat sarvam tapasā tam vivāraya mahā śakra rūpam samāsthāya gantum cakre matim tadā vāmena śacyā sahitam sura indram kareṇa ca anyena sita ātapatram rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakra rūpī sadāśivaḥ āsthāya evam hi śakrasya sva rūpam parameśvaraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā parameśānam śakra rūpa dharam śivam praṇamya śirasā prāha muniḥ muni varāḥ svayam pāvitaḥ ca āśramaḥ ca ayam mama deveśvaraḥ svayam prāptaḥ śakraḥ jagannāthaḥ bhagavān bhānunā prabhuḥ evam uktvā sthitam vīkṣya kṛta añjali puṭam dvijam prāha gambhīrayā vācā śakra rūpa dharaḥ haraḥ varayāmi śive bhaktim iti uvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ prāha sa vyagram īśānaḥ śakra rūpa dharaḥ svayam mām na jānāsi deva ṛṣe deva rājānam īśvaram tatas śakrasya vacanam śrutvā śrotra vidāraṇam upamanyuḥ idam prāha japan pañcākṣaraiḥ śubham bhava antara kṛtam pāpam śrutā nindā bhavasya tu śrutvā nindām bhavasya atha tad kṣaṇāt eva saṃtyajet sva deham tam nihatya āśu śiva lokam sa gacchati yaḥ vācā utpāṭayot jihvām śiva nindā ratasya tu mama icchāyāḥ kṣīram prati sura adhamam purā mātrā tu kathitam tatthyam eva na saṃśayaḥ bhasma ādhārāt mahā tejāḥ bhasma muṣṭim pragṛhya ca dagdhum svada iha mā āgneyīm dhyātvā vai dhāraṇām tadā atiṣṭhat ca mahā tejāḥ śuṣka indhanam iva avyayaḥ hārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇām tasya yoginaḥ atharva astram tadā tasya saṃhṛtam candrikeṇa tu ca idam niyogāt nandinaḥ tathā sva rūpam eva bhagavān āsthāya parameśvaraḥ darśayāmāsa viprāya bāla indu kṛta śekharam kṣīra dhārā sahasram ca kṣīroda arṇavam eva ca dadhi ādeḥ arṇavam ca eva ghṛta uda arṇavam eva ca phala arṇavam ca bālasya bhakṣya bhojya arṇavam tathā apūpa girayaḥ ca eva tathā atiṣṭhan samantataḥ girijā avalokya sa smitām sa ghṛṇam prekṣyatu tam tadā ghṛṇī bhuṅkṣva bhogān yathākāmam bāndhavaiḥ paśya vatsa me upamanyo mahābhāga tava ambā eṣā hi pārvatī mayā putrīkṛtaḥ asi adya dattaḥ kṣīrodadhiḥ tathā madhunaḥ ca arṇavaḥ ca eva dadhnaḥ ca arṇavaḥ eva ca ājya udana arṇavaḥ ca eva phala lohya arṇavaḥ tathā apūpa girayaḥ ca eva bhakṣya bhojya arṇavaḥ punar pitā tava mahādevaḥ pitā vai jagatām mune mātā tava mahābhāgā jaganmātrī na saṃśayaḥ amara tvam mayā dattam gāṇapatyam ca śāśvatam varān varaya dāsyāmi na atra kāryā vicāraṇā evam uktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyām upagṛhya tam yoga aiśvaryam tadā tuṣṭāḥ brahma vidyām dvijottamāḥ saḥ upi labdhvā varam tasyāḥ kumāra tvam ca sarvadā tuṣṭāva ca mahādevam harṣa gadgadayā girā varayāmāsa ca tadā vareṇyam viraja īkṣaṇam kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā praṇipatya punar punar prasīda devadeveśa tvayi ca avyabhicāriṇī iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge upamanyucaritam nāma sapta adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ asau vāsudevena kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā katham labdham tadā jñānam tasmāt kṛṣṇena dhīmatā tām sūta kathām pātaka nāśinīm uvāca sva icchayā hi avatīrṇaḥ api vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ nindayan eva mānuṣyam deha śuddhim cakāra saḥ manyoḥ ca upamanyoḥ vai dṛṣṭavan tatra tam munim namaścakāra tam dṛṣṭvā dhaumya agrajam aho dvijāḥ bahu mānena vai kṛṣṇaḥ tris kṛtvā vai pradakṣiṇam tasya avalokanāt eva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ naṣṭam eva malam sarvam kāya jam karma jam tathā divyam pāśupatam jñānam pradadau prīta mānasaḥ muneḥ prasādāt mānyaḥ asau kṛṣṇaḥ pāśupate dvijāḥ tapasā tu eka varṣa ante dṛṣṭvā devam maheśvaram sa ambam sa gaṇam avyagram labdhavan putram ātmanaḥ tadā prabhṛti tam kṛṣṇam munayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve tasthuḥ saṃvṛtya sarvadā anyam ca kathayiṣyāmi mukti artham prāṇinām sadā sauvarṇīm mekhalām kṛtvā ādhāram daṇḍa dhāraṇam sauvarṇam piṇḍikam ca api vyajanam daṇḍam eva ca naraiḥ striyā atha vā kāryam maṣi bhājana lekhanīm ca api atha pātram atha api vā pāśupatāya dātavyam bhasma uddhūlita vigrahaiḥ sauvarṇam rājatam vā api tāmram vā atha nivedayet mad vitta anusāreṇa yoginam pūjayet budhaḥ te sarve pāpa nirmuktāḥ samasta kula saṃyutāḥ yānti rudra padam divyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yoginām saṃpradānena śivaḥ kṣipram prasīdati rājyam putram dhanam bhavyam aśvam yānam atha api vā adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvam sādhyam prayatnāt bhavyam pāśupatam nityam saṃsāra arṇava tārakam etat vaḥ kathitam sarvam saṃkṣepāt na ca saṃśayaḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati iti śrī liṅga mahāpurāṇe pūrva bhāge aṣṭottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ca ayam pūrva bhāgaḥ śrī śaṃkara arpaṇam astu iti śrī saṭīka liṅga mahāpurāṇa pūrva bhāgaḥ samāptaḥ
